Who was manipulating things from behind the scenes?

Silver light flowed through the night, enveloping the immortal palace. But it didn’t obscure the immortal music and twittering chatting and laughter coming from the Hundred Flowers Palace. It drifted into the ears of Li Mengtu, who was waiting outside of Young Aurora Hall in his role as Zhong Chi.

Inside the main hall, Xu Qing also heard it. Xu Qing looked up at the person standing outside. Li Mengtu is acting strangely today....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. Normally speaking, his study partner would leave at night, unless otherwise ordered to stay. It was rare to see him around at this hour. With such thoughts on his mind, Xu Qing waved his hand to produce a Go board.

“Zhong Chi,” he said.

His study partner hurried into the hall, saying, “Your humble servant is here, Young Lord.”

“Play Go with me.” Xu Qing looked down at the Go board.

“Sure thing.” Nodding, Li Mengtu hurried over.

Xu Qing took a game piece and put it on the board. Game pieces descended. The sound of the wind grew stronger.

***

The wind that night was cold as it screamed through the Scourgebolt Palace. Sir Vilespirit was hurrying through it in the guise of the middle-aged corrections officer whose identity he had taken.

Someone must have figured out who I really am. That’s why everything happening in the Scourgebolt Palace today has me so on edge. And that’s why it took until today to get all the details about the other three true monarchs.

As he walked along, his mind was filled with thoughts of the current situation. I’m getting the feeling that if I don’t act tonight, I’ll never get the chance. This whole thing is very strange....

His narrowed eyes glittered with a strange light. Someone is using me as bait. They’re trying to force me to take action tonight. But there’s no doubt that the information I just got is time-sensitive. If I don’t act quickly enough, it won’t count as a betrayal of the immortal palace. And the waves won’t be suitable for my needs.

So no matter how I look at it, tonight is my last chance to do anything. And when you add in those rumors that have been spreading lately....

Sir Vilespirit looked thoughtful. Is the person using me as bait the person who spread the rumors? Or is it the subject of the rumors? If Fourth True Monarch is the fisherman, then his goal is obviously to lure out whoever spread the rumors.

Of course, there’s always the possibility that Fourth True Monarch himself is the source of the rumors. Maybe he’s just trying to sow confusion, and trick everyone into thinking there’s some other mastermind working in opposition to him. That could theoretically lead the rest of us into making some big mistakes.

His eyes glittered as he pondered this possibility. In the end, it doesn’t matter. Given that they’ve targeted me in their plot, I suppose I’ll have to—.

His expression flickered as his train of thought was interrupted. He stopped in place. Expression somber, he clasped hands and bowed.

“Master.”

A person walked out of the night. It was a dignified old man wearing the daoist robes of the Scourgebolt Palace. As his eyes fell on Sir Vilespirit, he frowned slightly. “What are you doing scurrying around so late at night?”

Sir Vilespirit tensed inwardly. This person was his host’s Master, and he was also an honor guard in the Scourebolt Palace. He had a lot of power and authority, and normally treated his apprentice coldly. At the same time, the host’s memories were telling him that the man was nothing short of awe-inspiring. In fact, he had already second-guessed his choice of identity a few times because of it. He knew he had to be extremely careful. freewebnovel.com

“Master,” Sir Vilespirit said, “my thunderlight has recently developed an excess of yang energy. I’m planning to take a trip to the lightning pond and extract some gloomthunder serum to stabilize it.”[1]

The old man’s eyes glittered like electricity as he looked his apprentice up and down. As his gaze pierced into the depths of his apprentice, he confirmed that there was indeed an excess of yang energy present. He nodded slightly.

“There have been some rumors going around the immortal palace lately,” the old man said. “However, the Immortal Lord, the palace lords, and the elders haven’t put much stock into them. As a result, I haven’t been looking too deeply into the matter. That said, if you hear anything actionable, bring it to me immediately.”

“Yes, sir,” said Sir Vilespirit.

With that, the old man turned and vanished into the night.

Sir Vilespirit waited a moment, then hurried on his way.

After he was gone, the old honor guard appeared again. He looked at the disappearing form of the corrections officer, and seemed to be lost in thought.

***

That gaze caused Sir Vilespirit to feel as if great weight was bearing down on him from behind. Thankfully, it didn’t last for long. When it was gone, he breathed a sigh of relief and hurried away a bit faster.

His true destination was actually a long-distance teleportation portal located next to the lightning pond. He currently had everything he needed to activate the portal. As long as he got into the portal and left, then he could send the information to the buyer. That action would be the betrayal he required.

That was his dao. He needed to betray the palace, regardless if that was not how things played out historically. After all, this was just a reflection of history, so what did it matter? His canon treasure, the broken sword within him, would get the nourishment it needed for a major transformation.

Of course, I have to make it out alive first!

He was wrapped up in such thoughts as he neared the lightning pond.

As he did, fluctuations began to roll out that could only be sensed by someone with space-time canon. And they were getting increasingly intense, making them like torches on a bright night.

***

Xu Qing sensed the fluctuations but didn’t react visibly. He placed a game piece onto the board. He had no idea what Fourth True Monarch was up to this night, but Li Mengtu’s unusual behavior had got him thinking. Besides, he had been waiting for days now to see what would happen because of the rumors he had spread. Now, the space-time fluctuations he had been waiting for had finally appeared....

“Zhong Chi,” he suddenly said, “I can tell something’s on your mind. You’re not focusing on the game. What’s going on?”

Li Mengtu hesitated briefly, but seeing that Young Lord Aurora was looking at him, he smiled wryly.

“I guess I can’t keep anything hidden from you, Young Lord. Ai.... Yesterday I confessed my love to Little Hui over at the Spiritguiding Palace. She didn’t exactly reject me, but she did say she needed to think about it. So... I guess I just can’t stop thinking about that whole situation.”

Xu Qing smiled and waved his hand dismissively. “Since you have something like that on your mind, there’s no need to keep this game going. Please go find Fourth True Monarch and invite him to come play with me. A game with Elder Brother Fourth right now would be much more meaningful.”

Something seemed odd to Li Mengtu, but he didn’t put too much thought into it. After all, his memories were telling him that Young Lord Aurora and Fourth True Monarch had a good relationship and were known to play Go together regularly. It was only because of the imminent inauguration of Immortal Lord Aurora that the immortal palace was so busy. Considering there was only one true monarch left behind, he and the young lord hadn’t had many opportunities to play Go like they had before.

Maybe this is an opportunity.... Wouldn’t it be ironic if I could get the young lord to help deal with Fourth True Monarch?

As that thought occurred to him, he made sure to look suddenly hesitant.

Xu Qing frowned slightly. “What’s wrong?”

“Young Lord, I doubt the true monarch has free time today...” Li Mengtu said.

Xu Qing looked up at him.

Mind racing, Li Mengtu continued, “Young Lord, I heard that the true monarch is doing something very important tonight.”

Xu Qing’s jaw nearly dropped. “Oh? Who told you that? And what important thing is he up to?”

“That’s just what people are saying. You heard about those recent rumors, right? Well, word has spread from True Monarch Hall that Fourth True Monarch went out to arrest someone tonight.” Li Mengtu was picking his words very carefully.

Xu Qing’s smile faded away, and his eyes glinted aggressively. “Rumors are nothing but fabrications. How could anyone believe such hearsay? And the people who benefit the most are the people who start them! That’s especially true of these rumors about Elder Brother Fourth.

“Considering he has such a high position in the immortal palace, it’s no wonder there are people who don’t like him. They just want to hurt him! I thought people would just have a good laugh and then move on. I never imagined the rumors were still circulating!

“Tomorrow I want you to send out orders from me forbidding anyone from spreading rumors. And that counts even more for you! I don’t want you running your mouth!”

Li Mengtu sighed inwardly. Given his observations and insight, he was convinced that Young Lord Aurora was being very serious. And now it was obvious that it would probably be impossible to get the young lord to help deal with Fourth True Monarch.

“Yes, sir,” he said, nodding fervently.

Xu Qing’s expression softened a bit. “That said, Zhong Chi, it seems like you’re really on top of the latest news. I suppose you’re good at digging up information?”

Li Mengtu only hesitated for a moment. “I can get information very quickly if it’s for you, Young Lord!”

Xu Qing smiled. “Alright, I’ll keep that in mind. You know, you’ve been at my side for years now, and I feel like I really know you. You’ve had it rough recently. Look how pale your complexion has been getting! Why don’t you go and rest up. Tomorrow I can help you out with Little Hui.”

Li Mengtu plastered a grateful look onto his face, bowed deeply, then left, all the while sighing inwardly.

Xu Qing watched Li Mengtu leave, then shifted his gaze in the direction of the lightning pond. That was where the space-time fluctuations were coming from. To Xu Qing’s eyes, those fluctuations looked like a sea of fire.

It looks like this is the response from Fourth True Monarch that I’ve been waiting for. Someone is changing history over there. So, should I go over there, or should I stay here...? If I stay, and Fourth True Monarch gets history back on track, then I’ll have lost one of my rocks.

Xu Qing looked down at the game board. The pieces were already in endgame formation. He put another piece onto the board.

Outside, the night wind grew louder. A game was underway, and someone... was playing a piece.

***

Sir Vilespirit raced along through the wind. Faster and faster he moved, passing the lightning pond and moving right toward the teleportation portal. He was almost there.

But just when he was about to enter the portal, everything shook violently as an invisible sealing enveloped the area. Something very cold came with it. In the blink of an eye, it became raw killing intent that locked down on the heart and mind.

Then a calm voice spoke. “I’ve been waiting for you a while now, Sir Vilespirit.”

Out of nowhere appeared a host of chains that represented law and order. In the middle of them was Sir Star Ring in the guise of Fourth True Monarch. With every step he took, terrifying pressure mounted. The countless chains vibrated and clanked. The sounds were like words of order that caused space-time to thrum, and brought everything out of a state of chaos.

“Sir Star Ring!” growled Sir Vilespirit. “So what if your canon and Fourth True Monarch’s canon are the same?”

Even as the words left his mouth, a fierce sword energy erupted from within him, causing a broken iron sword to appear behind him. In an instant, a devastating killing intent surged.

***

In the Scourgebolt Palace, the honor guard who was the Master of Sir Vilespirit’s host... suddenly looked in the direction of the teleportation portal, his eyes glittering.

Mouth curving into a cold smile, he murmured, “You were on a fishing expedition, Sir Star Ring. But did you know that, all the while, I was fishing for you?”

1. I think because of the author’s health and the slower release rate, he has been making more mistakes than usual lately. Or maybe mistakes isn’t the right word. Inconsistencies. He very frequently will introduce things (names of characters, skills, items), only to bring them up later with a different name. I am striving to maintain continuity as I edit so that everything flows well and makes sense. This paragraph is one such instance. Some of the terms here are called something else later. This was a particularly egregious instance, so my translation of this paragraph wouldn’t match the Chinese if you checked it, but it does match the story as a whole. Hopefully that makes sense. In some cases going forward, I’ll include footnotes to explain such edits, but in most cases I’ll just make the edits without explanations, otherwise there would be way too many footnotes clogging up the chapters. ☜

All of the important players’ focus was now gathered at that teleportation portal. Viewed from afar, nothing seemed out of the ordinary. The teleportation portal stood there just like always, and it wasn’t possible to see the corrections officer or Fourth True Monarch. freewebnovel.com

In the guise of Fourth True Monarch, Sir Star Ring was using a special spell formation as well as space-time fluctuations to cut off the area from outside view. Only very unusual and special people could detect what was going on, and Sir Star Ring had notified all of them in advance of what was to come. The peace and calm visible from the outside was an illusion. If you stepped past that, you would immediately hear the sound of order, which was like heavenly thunder.

Sir Star Ring stood there, overflowing with power and majesty; his mere gaze seemed able to latch onto any deviant behavior and force it to revert to normalcy. When he spoke, his voice seemingly became substantive. It transformed into countless glittering magical symbols that swirled around to form a majestic spell formation.

Silver light seemed to inundate heaven and earth in the area. It was as if daytime had come. This was... a dao voice turning into order itself!

The spell formation sent dazzling light out as Fourth True Monarch’s canon erupted, weighing down on everything with crushing might. It was like a sea in the sky, weighing down on everything below.

And it was all focused on... Sir Vilespirit.

Mountain-toppling, sea-draining energy made Sir Vilespirit like a lone rowboat in an angry sea, tossed about by tsunami waves. But his eyes didn’t show even a hint of surrender. Rather, his battle spirit spiked, and the huge broken sword behind him emanated a very aggressive aura. The moment the shocking silver spell formation appeared, veins had bulged on his face, and they quickly made the shape of a ghost face, malevolent and infinitely gruish.

He reached out and touched the spell formation. In the blink of an eye, the spectacular broken sword began emanating heaven-shaking, earth-shattering sword reverberations. Shimmering light then flowed out across the sword, filling in the missing pieces.

In the blink of an eye, it was whole. Sir Vilespirit took the hilt, and then... slashed it toward the spell formation that represented order.

The sword and the spell formation hit each other. A deafening boom rang out. The formation was powerful, but the broken sword was stronger. It was like a violent criminal who would allow order to be imposed only to slash it apart with a sword! The spell formation crumbled into fragments.

Sir Vilespirit shivered from head to toe, all while coughing up gobs of blood. As he staggered backward, it seemed as if much of his life force and soul had been absorbed by the broken sword. That was the price he had to pay to use it.

But he obviously couldn’t worry too much about that now. Taking advantage of the time the sword had bought, he shot closer to the teleportation portal. He was nearly there.

Of course, there was no way Sir Star Ring had run out of options. He had hardly put any thought to what he did moments ago. In fact, his expression remained completely calm as he waved his hand. That movement caused the chains to writhe like silver snakes, swirling through heaven and earth to form an even more astonishing spell formation. Whether it was in terms of aura, momentum, pressure, or complexity, it was far superior to the previous ones. These chains had become pure order.

The formation immediately shot toward Sir Vilespirit.

Sir Vilespirit’s face fell. Although he had never fought Sir Star Ring before, he knew that Sir Star Ring was strong. After all, he was known as the number one chosen in the eastern planetary system. And yet, finding out firsthand how strong he was still came as a surprise.

Of course, he still had more cards to play. His eyes glinted ferociously, and veins bulged on his face as the ghost face completely overtook his facial features. It was like he had become a different person, and he was now pulsing with a terrifying aura.

Even as the spell formation descended, he reached back and grabbed the sword. Allowing it to draw deeply on his life force, he stabbed it toward the spell formation. The dome of heaven went dark. The broken sword hit the spell formation with unstoppable momentum, but as they made contact, both ceased to move.

An instant later, the tip of the sword pierced through the formation. However... it stopped at the tip! It wasn’t that the sword wasn’t up to the task. Rather, the wielder couldn’t sustain its use. Blood sprayed out of his mouth as his body withered significantly.

Sir Star Ring was on the other side of the spell formation, looking as calm as ever. Looking coldly at Sir Vilespirit, he waved his hand. A boundless power surged from the spell formation.

Sir Vilespirit spasmed as he tumbled backward before flopping onto the ground, blood oozing out of his eyes, ears, nose, and mouth. He couldn’t even hold the broken sword. It spun off to the side, where it stabbed into the ground emanating a regretful thrumming sound. Everything was over.

“With battle prowess like that, the fact that you’ve been at odds with Zhou Zhengli for so many years indicates that Zhou Zhengli really has been feigning weakness. He’s clearly pushed that ability to the highest level of perfection.”

Sir Star Ring reached out toward Sir Vilespirit. No amount of struggling did any good on the part of Sir Vilespirit. He was hoisted up to dangle in midair. Chains swept forth and surrounded him. The canon symbols formed from sound swept forth like sealing marks.

“Considering how you’ve misbehaved, I’m going to strip your consciousness out of this world and send you back.”

The canon of order surged. He had a unique canon. But after he came to the fourth world, it changed. Perhaps it had been blessed by order itself, or perhaps it was because his canon was the same as that of his host. But either way, it gained the power to destroy! His canon of order could destroy the consciousness of an opponent. It was like an explosive purification.

The body of the corrections officer began to shake violently and let loose shaky screams. The canon of order swept through him, destroying all remnants of Sir Vilespirit. The process didn’t take long. Soon, the purification was complete. The consciousness had been destroyed.

The dead corrections officer flopped to the ground, and the sword off to the side disappeared.

During the entire fight, Sir Star Ring’s expression hadn’t changed at all. But now he reacted with surprise.

My order isn’t something deadly. Normally speaking, after driving out Sir Vilespirit’s consciousness and destroying it, the host should have gone back to normal. Instead... he actually died?[1]

Sir Star Ring looked off into the distance, his eyes gleaming coldly.

There can be only one explanation. This person was Sir Vilespirit. But at the same time, he wasn’t Sir Vilespirit!

Put precisely, he deeply believed himself to be Sir Vilespirit. Combined with the fact that the sword within him was real, it obscured his own senses. Even when dying, he believed himself to be Sir Vilespirit. Therefore, after driving the will out, Sir Vilespirit died, and he died. And that was because the traces of Sir Vilespirit within him were part of who he truly was.

The actual Sir Vilespirit is still alive!

Sir Star Ring scowled. There were a lot of people putting game pieces into play. There was more than one person fishing in the pond.

There was one game board, but pieces were being played onto it by Xu Qing, Sir Star Ring, and others.

It was virtually impossible for someone to reach this level of cultivation without being able to plot and scheme. And even people who came across as being simple-minded only used that as camouflage. What people could see on the outside meant nothing. Any who trusted what they saw at first sight were only moments away from disappearing forever. Whether it was covert plotting or overt plotting, whether it was playing Go or fishing, there are always ways to deal with any situation.

Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered. Though he wasn’t dealing with simpletons, he would still crush them all. And even if he slipped up somehow, he had the ability to set things back on course.

With that, he reached out toward the spot where the sword had disappeared. Instantly, an energy appeared that had nothing to do with order. It was the aura of the broken sword, and by using it, Sir Star Ring planned to track down the real Sir Vilespirit. Unfortunately, the aura wouldn’t stick around for much longer. It was already fading.

That’ll be enough time. I want one more kill!

Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered with killing intent as he prepared to shoot off in the direction indicated by the sword. However, that was when something very dramatic happened.

Colors suddenly flashed in the sky. Then a tempest raged into being around the teleportation portal. Grains of sand shot up from the ground, joining the tempest to create... a sandstorm.

In the blink of an eye, Sir Star Ring... was prevented from leaving. As intense rumbling sounds filled the area, Sir Star Ring floated up into the air, his hair and robes whipping around him, his eyes glinting aggressively. He was currently looking at a figure emerging within the vast sandstorm.

It was a woman dressed in a voluminous black robe, whose face was hidden behind a mask. Of course, physical appearances could be faked, so that in itself meant nothing.[2]

“So, you actually showed up,” Sir Star Ring said, his eyes glittering as he sensed the unfamiliar aura.

His plan had involved two major goals. The first was to crush Sir Vilespirit and thus quell chaos and restore order. The other... was to fish out the person who had been spreading rumors behind the scenes. Because that person had targeted him, it seemed most likely that they had differing goals. That person was not interested in maintaining order, which meant... that if they didn’t show up after what happened with Sir Vilespirit, it would count as a win. And if they did show up... then Sir Star Ring would get the clues he needed to determine their identity.

He had put his opponent in a no-win situation. That said, this person had come at a very inopportune time, just when Sir Star Ring needed to go track down Sir Vilespirit.

Therefore, Sir Star Ring simply turned to leave. After all, the sword aura was disappearing. And most importantly, Sir Vilespirit had obviously been doing some fishing of his own, using the fake version of himself as bait. He was clearly trying to make an opportunity to betray the palace without allowing Sir Star Ring to make things right. There was no time to waste.

Unfortunately, it was obvious that this black-garbed woman wasn’t going to back down from a fight just because Sir Star Ring wanted to leave.

The moment Sir Star Ring started moving, the black-garbed woman waved a hand, and the sandstorm issued intense rumbling sounds as a huge pair of eyes appeared. The eyes were gray. They seemed apathetic and emotionless as they stared at Sir Star Ring....

He couldn’t move. He got the sense that, as soon as the eyes looked at him, he had no body, and his consciousness was being separated and turned into countless grains of sand. And within each grain of sand was an individual consciousness.

“How interesting....”

Eyes flashing, Sir Star Ring waved his hand, causing numerous chains to fly out. They quickly formed a vortex in front of him, out of which emerged thirteen silver coffins. The coffins were of varying sizes and shapes, and all of them pulsed with an aura of order.

They did not open. It was as if it didn’t matter whether or not Sir Star Ring occupied the body of Fourth True Monarch, his will alone could not do this. This was an ability that came from the real Fourth True Monarch!

1. This is an important point which is said almost in passing, so I’m putting this footnote here to make sure readers notice it. Normally speaking, killing one of the possessed people will result in the consciousness of the outsider being expelled. Then the possessed person will go back to normal and continue along the normal track of history. This is one of the main explanations why everyone is trying to achieve their goals via intrigue as opposed to overt action. ☜

2. In reality, the gender of this person is not revealed until later. That’s easy to do in Chinese. Unfortunately, when you have extended scenes, it becomes almost impossible to keep the gender hidden in English. I mean, it’s possible, but at a certain point it becomes extremely awkward, and also obvious. So rather than bend over backward to hide the gender, I’m just revealing it a bit early. ☜

Fourth True Monarch cultivated the canon of order. And thus, over the years, he had tracked down everyone who competed with him by cultivating the same canon, and killed them. Thus, the canon became his own. His dao of order became completely and utterly unique.

Unless he died, it would be impossible for anyone else in existence to take the canon of order. As of this moment, thirteen canons had appeared, yet only three canonical orders emerged from within the coffins. freewebnovel.com

“Wind cannot exist here!”

The moment the words drifted out, all wind in heaven and earth vanished. Countless grains of sand began to fall to the ground.

“Sand cannot exist here!”

The grains of sand stopped moving, then turned into absolutely nothing.

Up in midair, the black-garbed woman looked on, eyes narrowed.

Then came the third and last canonical order. “Other than me, no one from outside this space-time can exist here!”

A terrifying force descended as if to purify the area and drive everything away. When it hit the black-garbed woman, who shivered from head to toe, her consciousness started peeling away. Then, the eyes behind the mask turned crimson. Laughter rang out. It was a sinister, disdainful laughter.

“You’re not the real Fourth True Monarch, nor the Immortal Lord. So you order things not to happen, and you think they just won’t?”

There was a sudden boom as the black-garbed woman exploded, turning into a host of sand grains that weren’t permitted to exist. Then the woman forcefully reappeared, whereupon everything in the area was different.

Simultaneously, back in Young Aurora Hall, Xu Qing tilted the game board, causing all the pieces to slide off onto the ground. A clattering sound filled the hall. It was as if heaven and earth were transforming completely.

The independent dimension surrounding the teleportation portal had turned into a desert! Sand spread out infinitely in all directions. Within that desert was an invisible hand, drawing the outlines of various images.

An eagle spread its wings, letting loose a piercing cry as it shot toward Sir Star Ring. A rhino stepped out, threw its head back, and bellowed as it rushed in the same direction. A shapeless mass, like the outline of heavenly soldiers and commanders, formed and charged forth.

It was like a mural made from sand. The images came one after another!

Next, a blazing sun appeared in the mural of the desert, drawn by the invisible hand. Within it was a sun god. A bright moon rose, and a moon god was in it, looking down at all heaven and earth. Words appeared that turned into a story, which became a thread that formed the outline of another figure. The mural of the desert was transforming.

A figure bearing a sword materialized, surrounded by raging sword energy. He wore an imperial robe and crown, and was none other than the past life origin of the three souls Sunfire, Starfire, and Moonfire. This was the human emperor of that world that existed outside of the Revered Ancient mainland![1]

The desert rumbled as Sir Star Ring tumbled backward. At the same time, the desert world began to collapse and disperse. It was turning back into a teleportation portal!

Sir Star Ring’s face was still very grim, but as everything from before faded away, he realized that he still had a bit of the aura from Sir Vilespirit’s broken sword!

Time was up.

Up in midair, the black-garbed woman’s aura was weak. She backed up, and was on the verge of fading into nothing.

Eyes glittering coldly, Sir Star Ring said, “Well, you came here intending to throw my order into chaos. In that case....”

He reached out toward the black-garbed woman in a clutching motion. The sound of his voice transformed into a majestic spell formation. Chains whipped out, becoming a formation of order. And then, both formations glittered with silver light as they connected. As they spun, the power of order turned into a purifying force that swept over the black-garbed woman. In the blink of an eye, chains flew out of the spell formation to wrap up the figure in black. Then the sounds of order became magical symbols that flowed over the black robes.

As they poured into her, her consciousness started to be peeled away. Yet this black-garbed woman was no ordinary individual. Though she was in a weak state and in a bad situation, she still had a trump card to play.

All of a sudden, golden light surged out from the woman in black. Then the world changed again. It became nothing but sea and sky. The unusual thing was that the sky was below, the sea was overhead. Strangely, fish were swimming in the sky and birds were flying in the water. Everything was inverted. An enormous clay figure sat cross-legged in the sea, and was reflected in the sky. The clay figure’s eyes opened. One was real. One was false. It was a case of something true and something bogus. This was the godly authority of Starfire, which could invert the real and false![2]

An instant later, everything vanished, including the black-garbed woman. Only the chains remained, except they had nothing to latch onto, and could only clank around aimlessly. The peeling away had succeeded, but had also failed.

It was a success because the peeling method actually worked. But it was a failure because what it peeled away was false. An illusion.

Unfortunately, after such an interchange, the true identity of the black-garbed figure couldn’t be hidden from Sir Star Ring.

The fox maiden!

Sir Star Ring turned to look in the direction of Young Aurora Hall, his expression profoundly forbidding. Then he looked away. He had a more troublesome issue to deal with at the moment, thanks to the interference of the fox maiden. And there was nothing he could do about it.

An enraged figure had just appeared in the canopy of heaven, surrounded by boundless waves of lightning. It was none other than the Master of the middle-aged corrections officer who had just died. He was an honor guard in Scourgebolt Palace! He was glowering viciously, although inside he was actually laughing coldly.

That was because he was actually the real Sir Vilespirit! Because he had arrived in the fourth world a bit late, he had worked very hard to stay hidden. Using a secret magic known only to him, he had altered the perceptions of his apprentice, forcing the apprentice to believe himself to be Sir Vilespirit. He had even secretly put his canon treasure, the sword, into the apprentice to make him the perfect double, and also the perfect bait.

Then he had stayed hidden in the shadows to wait for his apprentice to foster the proper karma. That was why the apprentice, believing himself to be the real Sir Vilespirit, had done the things that Sir Vilespirit would have done. For example, betray the palace.

The real Sir Vilespirit had planned all along to operate from within the shadows and within the light at the same time. In that manner, he pinned down Fourth True Monarch while simultaneously making it possible for him to actually betray the palace. That had been his plan from the beginning.

However, based on how things played out, he eventually changed his mind. He came up with an even more ingenious plan.

As the lightning crackled, he rushed forward loudly and with great purpose so that he attracted a lot of attention. Moving at top speed, he shot toward the area protected by the spell formation, within which was the teleportation portal. He slammed into the formation. A huge boom rang out that filled the immortal palace.

“Exalted True Monarch, why did you murder my apprentice??” he shouted. Instantly, the immortal palace was thrown into an uproar.

Countless streams of divine will converged on the teleportation portal. The spell formation shattered, revealing Fourth True Monarch as well as the furious old honor guard from the Scourgebolt Palace. In addition, there on the ground was... the corpse of the corrections officer.

Sounding completely furious, Sir Vilespirit said, “My apprentice went out to collect some gloomthunder serum, only to be brutally executed right here. Look, he has lineaments of order on him! That’s obviously evidence that you killed him, True Monarch!

“You need to tell me right now what crime my apprentice committed that gave you the right to cut him down in cold blood! Don’t tell me he perpetrated some heinous act against the immortal palace! If that’s the case, then I’ll accept the matter without objection!

“But if you can’t provide a good explanation, then that means you murdered an innocent person. Not even you, True Monarch, can do something like that without providing compensation and accepting punishment. At the very least, you’ll be locked up, and depending on the severity, you could face the death penalty.”

Sir Star Ring said nothing in response. He knew that he had been boxed into a corner. Even if he had thought to get rid of the corpse sooner, it wouldn’t have done any good. It would be a simple matter to look back through time to see what happened. He really had killed the apprentice. Besides, there were other things that happened that he didn’t want anyone to see.

There were basically two options here. One would be to claim that the apprentice committed a crime worthy of death. The other option would be to say that he didn’t commit a crime.

If he had committed such a crime, then the killing could be justified. However, whatever crime he claimed had been committed, it needed to count as a betrayal in order to satisfy the honor guard. If that happened, then it would validate Sir Vilespirit’s betrayal, and it would cause significant waves in space-time. That, in turn, would mean that Sir Star Ring had failed to maintain order.

If the apprentice did not commit a crime, then Sir Star Ring would have no way to explain the killing!

Personal grudges or other enmities couldn’t be a good explanation. If Sir Star Ring admitted to killing for that reason, then it would raise the ire of the masses, and he would definitely be jailed. If that happened, then he would be trapped for the next half-month, and would have no way to prevent other outsiders from creating waves in space-time. That would amount to him losing the entire game of Go.

If you considered which of the two options was worse, it meant that there was really only one choice to make. And that was to claim that the apprentice had committed some crime that harmed the interests of the immortal palace.

How ruthless!

Sir Star Ring sighed inwardly. All of this was happening thanks to the interference of the fox maiden. If that hadn’t happened, he would have had time to deal with Sir Vilespirit, and would not be facing such a dilemma.

He could claim that the apprentice had been possessed. Unfortunately, Sir Vilespirit had already made a very persuasive argument, and unless he got what he wanted, it was obvious that he would demand hard evidence to prove any claim true or false.

Besides, claiming the apprentice had been possessed wouldn’t necessarily justify killing him. If anything, it would make people suspect that he had been killed to keep him quiet. After all, interrogation was the best option in a case like that, not execution.

If it wasn’t for the recent rumors, this situation might not be so serious. But the rumors were still circulating, and Fourth True Monarch was at the center of them all. People were saying that he had been possessed. That made things all the more dangerous. It was easy to imagine a scenario in which he tried to explain things away only to end up implicating himself.

Finally, Sir Star Ring looked up, first at Sir Vilespirit hovering in midair, and then at the distant Young Aurora Hall. Finally, he floated up into the air, his face completely expressionless.

“This person betrayed the palace! He has a classified jade slip on him with all the proof. That’s why I had no choice but to kill him!”

Sir Vilespirit trembled, and was visibly struggling to breathe steadily. He could sense the broken sword calling out excitedly to him. The connection between him and the sword was now closer than ever. Space-time was whipping up into a tempest. It was becoming a timescape vortex that no one else could see or even sense. Unheard-of waves were rolling out.

Over in Young Aurora Hall, Xu Qing was in the middle of picking up all the game pieces that had fallen down. He suddenly looked up and smiled faintly.

He was holding a handful of sand. It was time sand, and each grain represented a law of time. Every grain that entered into him could significantly bolster his space-time canon! That was how he had benefited from Sir Vilespirit stirring up waves in space-time.[3]

2. This reflects what we saw in chapter 663 and 706. ☜

3. The relation between time and sand seems to echo what happened in chapter 1117. ☜

It was a momentous night in the immortal palace. A member of the Scourgebolt Palace tried to betray the immortal palace but failed. Fourth True Monarch killed him at the teleportation portal, arousing the suspicions of that person’s Master, Gongsun Qingmu. Then, when it was revealed that there really was a classified jade slip on the victim, the matter was settled.[1]

That said, some people found it very suspicious that Fourth True Monarch proclaimed that the matter was resolved.

Young Lord Aurora’s wedding was quickly approaching, and the Immortal Lord would soon be inaugurated. As a result, some important things became unimportant, while certain unimportant things became extremely important. Everyone understood how that worked. At the moment, there was nothing that could compare to those two approaching events.

Even if there were some suspicious things going on, they would have to wait until later to be resolved. They couldn’t be allowed to interfere with what was slated to happen in half a month.

***

An hour passed. Dawn had not yet come, and yet the immortal palace had already calmed back down.

However, the events that had just played out were like a tempest in the minds of the outsiders. All were complicated and intelligent people who were adept at analyzing situations and hatching schemes. What was more, they had the memories of their hosts, and thus, it was easy for them to figure out what was going on.

There’s no definitive proof that the honor guard from the Scourgebolt Palace is Sir Vilespirit. But that’s highly likely to be the case. If it really is Sir Vilespirit, then the other guy was probably Sir Star Ring! And the third person is probably the one who started those rumors. All three were fighting! Obviously, Sir Star Ring made out very badly! Not only did he not kill Sir Vilespirit, but he was forced to confirm that the palace was betrayed. Sir Vilespirit is a genius! And so is that mysterious person who started the rumors! Now it begs the question of what Sir Star Ring is going to do going forward....[2]

As undercurrents bubbled, Fourth True Monarch appeared in True Monarch Hall, face expressionless as he strode up to the top of the highest tower in the complex. There, the night air blew strongly as he looked at the distant Young Aurora Hall. A thin moon cast its glow down, but the dark clouds seem to swallow up the light. Everything was gloomy and visibility was almost nonexistent.

Just like Sir Star Ring’s mood. He had suffered a big defeat this night, and he wasn’t used to losing. In fact, as far as he could remember, he had never lost this badly before. As he stood looking at Young Aurora Hall, his eyes glittered mysteriously.

Time passed. Perhaps because of the heavy clouds, dawn seemed to arrive a bit later than usual. That was when Zhou Zhengli arrived behind Sir Star Ring. He bowed deeply.

“For the first half of the night,” Zhou Zhengli said quietly, “Zhong Chi was in Young Aurora Hall. When he left, he went straight to his residence and didn’t come out again. Young Lord Aurora was inside Young Aurora Hall the entire time. He never came out. The music in the Hundred Flowers Palace never stopped. Unless there were others there who I had no means to detect, it seems... that nobody left Young Aurora Hall at all.”

He was obviously aware of Sir Star Ring’s big loss, as well as the fact that his own nemesis had been part of the clash. Originally, he had been planning to take action along with Sir Star Ring. However, Sir Star Ring had been so confident that he could resolve the situation that he forbade him from coming along. Instead, he sent Zhou Zhengli to Young Aurora Hall to stake it out.

Inside, Zhou Zhengli was laughing coldly. Was it self-confidence? Or was it arrogance? Does he really look down on the other Shining Stars that much...?[3]

The people who ended up among the Shining Stars weren’t nobodies.

“I clearly underestimated them,” Sir Star Ring said.

His words caused Zhou Zhengli’s pupils to constrict. He was fully aware of how proud and conceited Sir Star Ring was. It wasn’t an easy thing for arrogant people to admit when they were wrong. Because of that, he suddenly realized that these hidden enemies must be a lot more complicated than he had assumed.

“That said,” Sir Star Ring continued, “I already know who one of them is.”

Up in the dome of heaven, the clouds clashed, causing lighting to flash and thunder to rumble. All of a sudden, Sir Star Ring’s eyes were clearly visible.

“Unfortunately, although many signs point to the identity of the hidden conspirator, I’m not going to make the same mistake again. I’m not going to look down on them like before. Therefore... I have to assume it’s possible that the enemy is using multiple identities, and the one I dealt with earlier is only the first layer of many. The true mastermind is likely still hiding out there in the night.”

More lightning flashed, illuminating the darkness.

Zhou Zhengli didn’t offer a response. He could tell that Sir Star Ring was really just thinking out loud. After some thought, he decided to go into more detail about what he had learned earlier that night.

“Exalted one, based on my observations of Zhong Chi tonight, combined with your earlier analysis of his goals, I’d say that your previous speculation about him is correct. He’s definitely Li Mengtu. And he’s most likely trying to place his poison canon into the space-time here.

“That said, he’s not attempting to immediately change history. He wants to take advantage of the time here to add the depth of time into his poison. Ultimately, he’s probably planning to poison his host body to death right before the historical calamity. In doing so, his poison canon will gain both karma and a more complex function.

“Regardless of whether waves in this version of history will affect reality, he’ll have a foundation for his canon. And that foundation... will be clearly visible to his Master in history.”

“All that matters is that we stop him at the right time,” Sir Star Ring said calmly.

Zhou Zhengli nodded and said nothing further. As dawn broke, he left quietly, all in line with his usual strategy of feigning weakness.

Finally, dawn light seeped through the dark clouds, spreading through the lands. It was daytime.

As the light spread, Sir Star Ring murmured, “There aren’t many game pieces left on the side of order....”

***

In Young Aurora Hall, Xu Qing had long since picked up all the fallen game pieces and was now putting them back on the board. He was carefully recreating the same game layout from before. In fact, he was just now placing the last piece down on the board. As he did, he heard soft laughter from behind him.

“Brilliantly played, Young Lord!”

A very charming and seductive voice reached Xu Qing’s ears. Starfire strolled in, clad in a sheer garment that perfectly accentuated hēr curves. Shē sat down opposite Xu Qing.

Skin as fair as snow formed a perfect contrast to hēr garment, making hēr seem even more attractive. Shē reached down with her fair hand, picked up a game piece with two fingers, and put it down on the board. Shē looked up seductively and licked hēr lips.

“Fourth True Monarch tricked me. Your humble slave girl got hurt. In fact, I almost didn’t make it back here. What’s more, someone was staking out Young Aurora Hall. It wasn’t easy to come and go without being noticed. And that means... your humble slave girl needs a reward!”

Placing one hand on the game board, shē leaned forward, placing hēr astoundingly beautiful face much closer to Xu Qing. She exhaled softly.

“Oh, Young Lord, please reward your humble slave girl. Pretty please?”

Xu Qing looked up from the game board and into hēr eyes. “You’ve taken a liking to my host? If you’re not worried about the possibility of being killed by the Immortal Lord, I can take my consciousness out for a day and give you a chance.”

Starfire was temporarily struck speechless. Shē had assumed that Xu Qing would respond the way he usually did. Never could shē have guessed that he would offer such a crafty retort. Shē was so surprised hēr jaw nearly dropped. Cursing him silently for being such a blockhead, shē leaned back and tucked a stray hair behind hēr ear.

“You blew your cover tonight,” Xu Qing said calmly. “Are you ready to deal with the ramifications?”

“No, I’m not!” shē snapped in irritation. Shē snorted coldly.

Xu Qing began picking up the pieces from the board one by one. “I know full well you’ve already thought things through,” he said coolly. “The task I want you to accomplish tonight falls in line with your own plan. I don’t care how you do it. But let me remind you that Sir Star Ring will be targeting you for the next step of his plan!”

Starfire blinked hēr beautiful eyes a few times. “Ooh, are you worried about your humble slave girl, Young Lord? Have any advice for me?”

Xu Qing put the game board away. “Today isn’t the appropriate time to go see Sir Vilespirit. Go tomorrow. As for whether or not you get that identity you want, well, that’ll be up to you.”

Starfire covered hēr mouth as shē laughed softly. “You know what I like most about you, Xu Qing? Your intelligence.”

Xu Qing closed his eyes and said nothing further.

Smiling just as before, Starfire stretched, revealing more of hēr beautiful curves. Then shē turned and left.

The day passed uneventfully.

Xu Qing never left Young Aurora Hall. He spent all his time studying the sand of time. It was marvelous. The only downside was that he didn’t have much of it. He currently had two options. One was to absorb all of it immediately. The other option....

I could use this sand to create even bigger waves in space-time. And then I could ultimately get a lot more of it!

It didn’t take long for him to make a decision.

By the time night fell, nothing noteworthy had played out. It was almost as if nothing had happened the previous night. People went about their business. Apparently, that event was a much more sensitive topic than the rumors from before. Hardly anyone was even talking about it. There was an unspoken agreement among everyone to simply not mention it.

Night came and went.

***

Around dawn, a knock could be heard on the door of the residence of the honor guard Gongsun Qingmu, who had just lost his dear apprentice.

The door quietly opened, whereupon a black-garbed and masked figure entered.

Gongsun Qingmu looked coldly at the visitor. He said nothing.

The figure in black looked around, then laughed softly. “You weren’t pleased with my gift from last night, Sir Vilespirit?”

Sir Vilespirit’s expression remained the same as ever. Voice raspy, he said, “What do you want?”

“You lost an apprentice. But you gained one too.” The figure in black laughed.

Sir Vilespirit’s heart started pounding. How could he have ever guessed that this person wanted this? An identity?

A moment passed, whereupon Sir Vilespirit said, “Just who exactly are you?”

The figure in black didn’t answer the question. “It’s not important who I am. What’s important is that, going forward, you have an ally. And we... can work together. By doing so, you can betray the palace even more dramatically than before.”

Sir Vilespirit said nothing for a long moment. When he finally spoke, he said, “I need to think about it.”

The figure in black laughed, then departed.

***

A similar scene was playing out in a guest hall in the south of the immortal palace.

“I need to think a bit about your offer, True Monarch,” Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix said softly.

Sir Star Ring in the guise of Fourth True Monarch nodded expressionlessly. “It wasn’t easy for you to get that identity, was it? You paid a high price. And you want to use it to see history play out as intended. You want to marry the Young Lord, whereupon the karma created with the immortal palace will put you halfway to becoming its owner. Of course you have more complicated plans than that. But it doesn’t matter. That doesn’t conflict with me.”

He turned and walked to the entrance, where he stopped and looked back at her. “Your host is the only one who can really drive all the courtesans out of the Hundred Flowers Palace. Including that fox maiden. Once you do, I’ll make sure you reach your goal!”

1. Gongsun Qingmu: Gongsun is a compound surname. Compound surnames are not very common nowadays. They were more common in ancient times. That said, among compound surnames, Gongsun is pretty common, at least in the works of Er Gen. It gives a person’s name an old-timey feel, and in the case of this one, it sounds like someone associated with the government. Qingmu is made of Qing which means “blue/green/cyan” and is the same character from Xu Qing’s name. Mu means “wood/tree.” This is the same set of characters that I translated as Greenwood earlier in the novel. It first came up in chapter 888, where I also mentioned that the term came up in ISSTH. There is no indication that Gongsun Qingmu is connected to any of those things. ☜

2. This bit of thought dialogue has no attribution. Based on the context, it’s obviously one contiguous thought, not a conversation. But it’s never attributed to a specific person. I think it’s supposed to represent the general thoughts of the various outsiders. ☜

3. Linguistic note here that has no relevance but is cool. In Chinese, the terms for self-confidence and arrogance are very similar, so it makes for a much better contrast. Self-confidence is a fairly direct correlation to the English term, as it combines the characters for “self” and “belief/faith/confidence.” Meanwhile, arrogance also starts with the “self” character, to be followed by the “big” character. Because both of them start with “self,” it makes for a little bit of wordplay that doesn’t come across in English. ☜

It was halfway through the twelfth month of the year 2999 in the Dao Finale of the Nineshores calendar. That meant there was only half a month left until Immortal Lord Nineshores stepped down and Immortal Lord Aurora was inaugurated. It also meant that the wedding day of Young Lord Aurora and the daughter of Immortal Lord Nineshores was just around the corner.

Ordinarily speaking, that wedding would be a major event in the Fifth Star Ring, and would cause countless cultivators to make the long journey to the court to offer respects. In fact, all of the Immortal Lords would come as well, along with their apprentices and followers. However, it was a sensitive time, and not an occasion for ostentatious displays. Therefore, Immortal Lord Aurora refused to have any visiting guests, and would instead have a limited number of attendees to a ceremony held in the immortal palace itself.

That said, it was only natural that there would be gifts and decorations. Lanterns were being hung throughout the palace, and colorful banners were put up everywhere. All of the ladies dressed up. That was especially true in Young Aurora Hall.

All of these were things that had happened historically speaking, but interfering with them wouldn’t have done much. So Xu Qing just let the master of ceremonies continue with all the decorations and other preparations for the wedding.

He was currently in the main hall furthering his study of the sand of time. If situations arose outside that needed to be handled, he would send Zhong Chi out to deal with them.

Time passed slowly. Eventually, the setting sun cast its warm glow into the sky. Within Young Aurora Hall, the master of ceremonies was putting the last wedding decorations into place.

Zhong Chi was making a final inspection of everything.

Pointing at the embroidered balls hanging from the eaves, he frowned, looked at the master of ceremonies, and said, “There’s something wrong with the color of the balls. At first glance they look like they’re made entirely from shivering immortal roses. But in the light of the setting sun, you can clearly see that they have imperfections. What’s more, the total number is inauspicious! There needs to be an even number! Take them down immediately![1]

“And look at the red silk banners! They’re not shiny enough. The magical techniques and immortal power aren’t flowing through them naturally. Take them down! Also....”[2]

Li Mengtu as Zhong Chi was being very responsible and diligent. He felt that it was important to put on a good show. After all, just the day before, Young Lord Aurora really had said some nice things about him to Little Hui from the Spiritguiding Palace. Given his host’s personality, it made sense that he would be profoundly grateful. That said, Li Mengtu was sighing inwardly, as he knew that, historically speaking, the wedding... would turn out to be a bloodbath.

In half a month, the young lord will die violently in this place.... In fact, nobody will make it out alive. Given all the time I’ve spent with Young Lord Aurora recently, I have to admit that he’s a nice person. He’s somewhat given to lust, true. But given who he is, that fact that he’s only somewhat given to lust... makes him nearly perfect.

Li Mengtu sighed. He had been increasingly struck with the sensation that life in the immortal palace was nice. He didn’t have much pressure at all. All he needed to do was take care of the young lord and keep him safe. After all, out in the real world, he had far too many responsibilities. He had to constantly struggle to turn things around, both for his clan, and for himself.

Given that he was one of the Shining Stars, it was no surprise that he had noticed his Master seemed to have sinister intentions. But he couldn’t reveal such thoughts. All he could do was work secretly from the shadows to try to change things. If he had to compare the two identities, there was no doubt... that he preferred being Zhong Chi.

As such thoughts ran through his head, he suddenly noticed a floor tile that had a chip in it. Brow furrowed, he opened his mouth to say something about it. However, that was when a brilliant light shone in the evening sky. Then he heard the cries of phoenixes.

All of a sudden, an imperial carriage being pulled by nine phoenixes appeared in midair over Young Aurora Hall. The exquisitely decorated chariot glittered blindingly, illuminating every corner of Young Aurora Hall. The nine phoenixes pulling the chariot were as red as fire, as if the burning sunset had painted them that color.

The chariot was flanked by over a hundred guards with spears in their hands, all of them somber-looking in their black armor. They were Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s honor guard, tasked with keeping her safe.

When the carriage appeared, the master of ceremonies clasped hands and bowed.

Li Mengtu’s eyes narrowed slightly, but his expression was one of respect as he hurried forward and offered formal greetings. “Well met, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix.”

A cold snort drifted out from the carriage. Shortly after, two handmaidens lifted the curtain, and a beautiful woman emerged.

She was none other than Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, the daughter of Immortal Lord Nineshores! She was not acting like she had been back at the Scourgebolt Cliffs, when her softness was hidden beneath a veneer of anger. Instead... her eyes were piercing, as if she could peer into the depths of one’s thoughts. Her expression was calm, but there was a tempest within it.

She was not dressed like usual. She wore gorgeous blue-and-white palace attire. That, coupled with her furious expression, made her seem like someone nobody would dare to mess with. It was as if her mere presence was enough to prevent anyone from acting rashly. freewebnovel.com

She walked out of the carriage and into Young Aurora Hall. Once inside, she seemed even more majestic than before. That was because she knew her value and position. She also understood how to use her power to safeguard her own dignity and rights. She had a gaze that seemed capable of seeing through lies instantly. And that gaze was now focused on Li Mengtu in his guise as Zhong Chi.

“Has the Hundred Flowers Palace been torn down yet?” she said in a low, powerful voice. Every word seemed like a hammer blow to the heart.

Everyone else present kept their heads bowed. Even Li Mengtu felt the pressure weighing down on him thanks to her words.

It’s only been a few days, but this person has definitely acclimated to this identity. There are no clues like there were on the first day. In fact, if this was our first meeting, I would be hard-pressed to be able to guess she’s really an outsider.

Quickly collecting his thoughts, Li Mengtu said, “The young lord gave orders a few days ago for the Hundred Flowers Palace to be torn down. Unfortunately, your humble servant has been so busy with your wedding decorations, ma’am, that the whole matter of tearing down the palace skipped my mind.... Your humble servant will start the work tomorrow.”

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix glowered at him. “There’s no need to wait until tomorrow. It can be torn down today.”

With that, she strode forward.

Li Mengtu seemed like he wanted to offer a further explanation, and even took a step forward to get closer to her. But her guards pushed him away. All he could do was send a quick voice message to Young Lord Aurora, then hurry after Spirit Phoenix.

“Young Lady,” he cried, “this is manual labor we’re talking about. Let me handle it!”[3]

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix just continued onward furiously. She had already spotted the Hundred Flowers Palace, and as she and her retinue neared, they were like oppressive black clouds that caused the evening sky to turn dark. A great wind had picked up, blowing through the Hundred Flowers Palace, and causing all the flowers therein to sway back and forth.

And yet... there was a peony there, lounging in the spot that belonged to the young lord. She wore sheer garments which barely obscured her body beneath. Coupled with the languid expression on her face, she seemed to exude flirtatiousness. Hardly paying any attention to the wind from outside the palace, she sighed.

“Keep singing and dancing, girls.”

The hundred flowers laughed. The immortal music swelled.

Outside the palace, Li Mengtu saw what was happening, and his eyes narrowed. He took a few steps back, doing nothing to interfere.

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix's eyes were full of rage, but her voice was as cold as ice. “Wipe this filthy place out of existence!”

The black-armored guards around her surged with frigid energy as they advanced toward the Hundred Flowers Palace. They didn’t even need to launch an attack. The frigid energy roiling off of them caused everything to freeze over. And after it was frozen, it crumbled into ashes. As they walked forward, everything crumbled around them.

The master of ceremonies, Li Mengtu, and the Young Aurora Hall guards... did nothing to interfere. That was because, normally speaking... the only person in the Aurora Immortal Palace who had the right to tear down the Hundred Flowers Palace was Immortal Lord Aurora. Not even his four apprentices could do it.

But today... someone new showed up who did have that right. And that was the young lady who was about to be married to their young lord! In fact, she had more right to tear down the Hundred Flowers Palace than even the Immortal Lord. After all, the Immortal Lord himself had previously said that the place should be torn down.[4]

In other words, there wasn’t a single person who had the right to stop what Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix was doing.

Thus, her guards marched forward. Rumbling sounds echoed out nonstop. Thanks to the actions of the guards, the Hundred Flowers Palace crumbled into ashes starting from the exterior and then moving in.

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix stood off to the side, watching coldly.

Li Mengtu sighed inwardly. Young Lord. Ah, Young Lord. I wish I could have done something.

As Li Mengtu stood there ruefully, the guards reached the interior of the palace. Now visible was the pond, the hundred flowers, and the fox maiden.

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix saw all of them. She saw the colorful gauze garments. She saw the debauchery. She saw the endless curves and long legs. Some of the women were enticing, some were seductive, some were pure, some were mature, and some were simply gorgeous. There were even some nonhumans....

Grinding her teeth, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix said, “Filthy. Obscene. Dirty. You harlots offend public morality! How utterly shameless, you depraved hags!”

The hundred flowers bristled in rage.

But the fox maiden, looking very calm and composed, simply picked up a grape, put it in her mouth, and looked at Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. She laughed softly.

“Aren’t you quite the beauty? Unfortunately, fate is a cruel mistress. If you weren’t the daughter of Immortal Lord Nineshores, I’m afraid you would have ended up just like us. A wonderful morning glory like you would have ended up right here in the Hundred Flowers Palace, vying with the rest of us to attract the attention of our lord and master.” The fox maiden sighed as if with regret.[5]

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s eyes became incredibly aggressive. Whether it was she or her host, they were the same in that, from the time they were small until now, no one had ever spoken to them in such a filthy and sarcastic way. The morning glory suddenly didn’t seem very much like a morning glory. Glaring at the fox maiden, she suddenly thought back to what Fourth True Monarch had told her.

“A place as filthy as this,” she said coldly, “and people as perverse as this... should be driven out of the immortal palace immediately!”

1. Embroidered balls are traditional decorations that are usually made from silk. Here’s what they looked like. ☜

2. Red silk banners are another thing you see at Chinese weddings. Here’s what they looked like. They often have red flowers made of silk attached to them. The flowers aren’t specifically mentioned in this passage, but it would make sense to me that they do have those. ☜

3. The title used (young lady) here is the title she would bear as the wife of the young lord. It’s more like “young (lord’s) wife” if you directly parsed it out. ☜

4. In chapter chapter 1147 the Immortal Lord said to tear down the Hundred Flowers Palace. ☜

5. There is some wordplay here that doesn’t come out in English. In Chinese “morning glory flower” is literally a “cow-leading flower.” The “cow-leading” is a reference to the Cowherd from the folktale of the Cowherd and the Weaver Girl. The Cowherd is the male love interest in that story, so there are some obvious implications there. What is literally said is that “you would be a morning glory, who ‘leads the cow’ for our lord and master.” ☜

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s eyes burned with rage, and her face was grim and fierce. She was really not used to hearing obscene talk. Although the person possessing Spirit Phoenix did not come from as prestigious a background as the real Spirit Phoenix, she was still from a rich and noble family. And thus, killing intent was raging in her heart.

It wasn’t that she wanted to kill the hundred flowers. Nor did she want to kill the fox maiden. She wanted to kill... the consciousness that was possessing the fox maiden!

Fourth True Monarch had explained that, just like her, the fox maiden had been possessed by an outsider. She wasn’t sure exactly who it was. But she was determined to find out for sure after she left this place.

In response to her orders, the black-armored guards surged with killing intent and martial auras as they advanced. Instantly, a tempest screamed in all directions, with the goal of crushing everything in its path and destroying all of the hundred flowers.

However, the ladies of the Hundred Flowers Palace, though seemingly delicate, had all been selected directly by Young Lord Aurora. And all of them were extraordinary individuals. They didn’t just have good looks. They had dazzling talent, and none of them had weak cultivation bases. If they did, they couldn’t deserve to be named among the ‘hundred flowers.’

And what was even more noteworthy was that the fox maiden was in charge. Almost as soon as the black-armored guards unleashed their baleful auras, the ample-chested fox maiden sat up and crossed her legs.

Glaring, she said, “Every single one of us girls is a chosen cultivator. And every single one of us has been taken good care of by the young lord. We who live in the Hundred Flowers Palace are able to stand aloof from worldly affairs. How could a morning glory like you possibly claim that we’re filthy?

“Who cares if you’re getting married to the young lord? It’s not a real marriage, anyway! So how can you drive us away to anywhere? I’m very curious to see how you plan to get rid of us. Do you intend to just slaughter us right here and now??”

The fox maiden snorted coldly, whereupon the cultivation bases of all of the surrounding hundred flowers surged. Magical techniques and divine abilities formed in an instant. All of a sudden, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and her retinue found themselves facing stiff opposition. The proverbial swords were drawn and arrows nocked. Killing intent flared. Things looked like they were about to get violent very quickly.

Some distance away, Li Mengtu shivered as a voice spoke into his mind. It was Xu Qing. After getting his instructions, Li Mengtu rushed forward to stand in between the two parties.

“The young lord has given orders!”

All eyes shifted to stare at him.

Taking a deep breath, he said, “The young lord says the following: ‘I am too ashamed to come in person. As I think back to the years of immortal music, and the company of the hundred flowers, I sigh in my heart. But all good things come to an end.... My father’s orders cannot be disobeyed....

“‘However, the hundred flowers have done nothing wrong. All fault lies with me. No one is to cause any harm to my hundred flowers. And each of the hundred flowers will be bestowed with 100,000,000 pieces of immortal jade, 100,000 immortal pills, 100 immortal treasures, and 10 pieces of immortal destiny....

“‘I wish all hundred flowers a safe and happy future. And now, you may take your leave.’”

After Zhong Chi delivered the message in full, he was left with a racing heart. He knew what had happened in real history. The Hundred Flowers Palace had been torn down and all the women departed. In some ways, the big wedding ended up giving them a chance to survive calamity. The history books didn’t go into detail about how many actually left the immortal palace and thus escaped death.

However, Li Mengtu did know that, historically speaking, the Hundred Flowers Palace didn’t end up being torn down until four days before the wedding. But now, it was happening much earlier than that.

After the young lord’s message was delivered, the hundred flowers stood there silently. Soon, a feeling of grief filled the area.

Finally, the fox maiden sighed and looked around. “The young lord is being generous with us. Considering his sincerity, and the fact that the wedding approaches, plus the orders of the Immortal Lord, all of you... should leave his forsaken place. Now we follow through with the plan. There is no Hundred Flowers Palace here anymore, but there will be a Hundred Flowers Palace out in the Fifth Star Ring!”

Instantly, space-time began to ripple. In real history, the Hundred Flowers Palace had only existed in Young Aurora Hall in the immortal palace. It had never existed anywhere else. Considering what Starfire was capable of, and how long shē had spent in the Hundred Flowers Palace, there was no way shē was unaware of that fact. Obviously, shē had worked out a plan with the hundred flowers.

If the Hundred Flowers Palace ended up torn down, then they wouldn’t really just disperse in defeat. They would go into the outside world and form their own sect.

And the name of that sect would be... the Hundred Flowers Palace! There would always be a Hundred Flowers Palace that belonged to Young Lord Aurora. And in the records of the Hundred Flowers Palace, the fox maiden would be listed as the first palace lord of the place! The story would pass down through the generations!

As a result of this, waves were spreading in space-time. And though Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix had canon, she couldn’t detect that. But she was fully aware of the significance of these words in terms of historicity. Her expression suddenly became very serious.

Meanwhile....

Xu Qing stood in Young Aurora Hall, his hands clasped behind his back as he looked out the window, a melancholy expression on his face. Of course, inside, he was completely calm.

Although he didn’t know history as well as Spirit Phoenix or the person playing the role of Spirit Phoenix. But he could sense the waves in space-time. From the moment Spirit Phoenix arrived, space-time had been rippling, which made it obvious that history was changing. That said, the changes were minimal.

At that point, he came to realize that Fourth True Monarch was probably behind the whole thing. He could allow some minor waves in space-time if it meant he could seize the initiative. His target had obviously been the fox maiden.

But now, the space-time waves were much larger. And Xu Qing knew why; it was Starfire’s doing. Starfire obviously wasn’t going to bet everything on Sir Vilespirit.

“How interesting...”

A quiet voice drifted through the hall behind Xu Qing.

He wasn’t surprised at all to hear it. He slowly turned around.

A figure was materializing out of thin air. He had eyebrows like swords and eyes like stars. Clad in a violet-gold robe, he stood as tall and straight as a pine tree. Atop his head was a violet-gold crown inlaid with jewels and decorated with lifelike dragons and phoenixes. There was an otherworldly air to him. He was none other than Fourth True Monarch!

“What are you doing here, Elder Brother Fourth?” Xu Qing said with a wry smile. “Don’t tell me you’re here to make fun of me.”

“This is all due to Master’s orders, little Junior Brother,” Fourth True Monarch said warmly. “There was nothing I could do to stop it. I just came to keep you company. I was worried you would be upset.”

He didn’t seem to be acting aggressively in any way, and in fact, came across as very sincere.

Of course, in reality, Sir Star Ring was closely scrutinizing the young lord. That was just how he acted on instinct.

Looking depressed, Xu Qing shook his head and declined to say anything.

“That said, little Junior Brother, I have to admit that fox maiden you won from Li the Chosen was quite intriguing....” Sir Star Ring seemed to randomly look at Xu Qing’s eyes. He had known from the very beginning that many outsiders would focus their attention on the young lord, so it was no surprise that the fox maiden ended up with him. He also knew that it was impossible for the consciousness of an outsider to possess either the young lord or Immortal Lord Aurora. However, after his previous failure, he couldn’t help but start wondering if that was true.

With a stunned expression, Xu Qing looked Sir Star Ring up and down in his guise of Fourth True Monarch.

That reaction caused Sir Star Ring to similarly react with shock. He was just about to say something, but Xu Qing beat him to it.

“Elder Brother Fourth,” Xu Qing whispered, “you never paid attention to anyone in the Hundred Flowers Palace before. But now you’re talking like that...?”

Sir Star Ring’s guard instantly went up. The rumors about him were still circulating, so the last thing he wanted was people from this space-time to start suspecting him of something.

But then Xu Qing laughed. “Elder Brother Fourth, don’t tell me you’ve suddenly set your heart on mundane matters? Well, that’s fine. To tell you the truth, the hundred flowers have accompanied me for so long that I can’t bear to part with any of them. But the fox maiden just arrived. If you like her, then you can have her. Take her as a handmaiden.”

Although Xu Qing was speaking casually, there was no way Sir Star Ring could accept the offer!

First of all, it wasn’t something Fourth True Monarch would do. What was more, the fox maiden wasn’t fated to do that.

That said, even he was tempted. If he had the fox maiden as a handmaiden, then he could drive the outside consciousness from her to forestall future misfortune. However, even as such thoughts passed through his mind, he realized Young Lord Aurora was looking at him closely....

He shivered inwardly. In my host’s memories, Young Lord Aurora doesn’t act this simplistic. Is it because he’s suspicious of me now...? It’s true that I’m not exactly acting like a true monarch.

Having reached this point in his train of thought, Sir Star Ring laughed. “Please, I hope you never make a suggestion like that again.”

Xu Qing also laughed. “For a second there, I thought... that you were going to say yes!”

He really was Young Lord Aurora. And Fourth True Monarch was really no one else other than Fourth True Monarch!

After the young lord’s message was delivered to the Hundred Flowers Palace, the entire situation was defused. All of the gifts the young lord had said to be delivered were taken from the inner court of Young Aurora Hall. The fox maiden calmed everyone down, and they left. freewebnovel.com

Before long, the fox maiden was the only one left behind in Hundred Flowers Palace. She lounged there lazily, looking like she had no intention of leaving.

Frowning, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix looked at her. “If you don’t get the hell out of the immortal palace within ten breaths of time, then I’ll have you cast out with force!”

Starfire smiled charmingly. “Oh honey, you look so cute when you’re mad! No wonder the young lord was willing to kick the rest of them out.”

Spirit Phoenix stewed in her rage for ten breaths of time. Then she turned and left. Along the way, she ordered, “Escort her out!”

The black-armored guards advanced. From the majestic pressure that emanated from them, they were obviously about to take action.

But then, a cold voice erupted like thunder outside of Young Aurora Hall.

“What do you think you’re doing to my apprentice??” All of a sudden, Gongsun Qingmu from the Scourgebolt Palace appeared in midair. Looking very angry, he continued, “That fox spirit is my apprentice! This is her identity medallion, which has already been officially registered at Scourgebolt Palace!”

The fox maiden grinned, stood, and bowed to him. “Master.”

Spirit Phoenix stopped in her tracks. The black-armored guards froze in place. None of them had the power to drive someone out of the immortal palace who was officially registered there!

Even stronger space-time waves rolled out.

Looking in the direction of Young Aurora Hall, Sir Vilespirit in the guise of Gongsun Qingmu coldly said, “I know you’re there, True Monarch. You just killed one of my apprentices. And now you’re causing trouble for another of my apprentices? Why does it seem like you’re targeting me over and over again?”

In Young Aurora Hall, Xu Qing looked surprised. He turned to Sir Star Ring.

Sir Star Ring’s expression did not change, but inside, he was uncharacteristically uneasy. He suddenly felt more loathing than ever for Sir Vilespirit.

Once this thing is over, and we’re back in the eastern planetary system, I’m going to personally track him down and kill him!

The situation with the Hundred Flowers Palace was resolved by the time the sun set. The hundred flowers had been dismissed, and were already long gone, pursuing their collective dream.

But the fox maiden... was still around. She was now an apprentice of Gongsun Qingmu, and thus had an identity medallion from the Scourgebolt Palace. What was more, she would soon be the palace lord of the Hundred Flowers Palace.

With those dual identities, Starfire was very close to accomplishing hēr goal. As of now, shē was free to come and go as shē pleased at Young Aurora Hall. As an official cultivator of the immortal palace, it was nothing out of the ordinary for hēr to pay a visit if shē wanted, unless Xu Qing expressly forbade it.

Considering shē was an old friend of Young Lord Aurora, the only thing Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix could do now was flick her sleeve and stalk off. She seemed angry, but that was only half-real. The half of it that was real came because of the things the fox maiden had said to her. The other half was an act for the sake of the agreement she had made with Fourth True Monarch. It was business, nothing more.

Regardless of how things worked out, thanks to that agreement, she was now under the protection of Fourth True Monarch. As for whether or not Fourth True Monarch got what he wanted out of the deal, that didn’t really have anything to do with her.

In the guise of Fourth True Monarch was Sir Star Ring, who briefly pulsed with a dangerous aura before saying a few random words and leaving Young Aurora Hall. He was planning to temporarily refrain from doing anything further regarding this matter.

And then, the space-time waves made more sand of time in front of Xu Qing. Not exactly very much.
