He scooped up the sand and looked at the spot where Fourth True Monarch had just left. His eyes glittered.

I need to get rid of him. Soon. He’s smart, and considering he's been beaten twice in a row, his third move... is going to be difficult to deal with. If he’s still around on the wedding day, he might cause too much trouble for me to handle. That said, it won’t be hard to take care of him.

He rolled the sand in his palm as he considered the matter. So, how do I drive the outsider’s consciousness from his body....

***

Five days passed. There were now only ten days left until the wedding.

As the end of the month neared, the sky over the Fifth Star Ring didn’t just feature the rosy glow during evening. Nor was it dark only at night. Sometimes, the sun would set almost as soon as it rose. And sometimes, rosy clouds would obscure the sun at high noon, making it seem like evening.

At the moment, the sky was bright on one side and dark on the other. Strangely, there was no moon on the dark side and no sun on the bright side. The sun and moon no longer cycled regularly. There were similar oddities in the weather patterns.

Mortals found the whole thing to be shocking, confusing, and even terrifying.

It was different with the cultivators. Although not all of them had experienced such things before, the ancient records provided a clear explanation. When one epoch led into another, and Immortal Lord succession occurred, the star ring would shift course and fundamentally restart. It would last ten days before the restart and seven days after, for a total of seventeen days in which the heavenly bodies blurred and the workings of heaven were thrown into chaos.

During the first ten days, everything sank into a state similar to primal-chaos. It was a time in which thoughts blurred and daos could not be sought. During the final seven days, heaven and earth were reestablished. All living beings benefited from immense blessings, being cleansed and able to bask in auspicious signs. The transformations to heaven and earth signified that the handover process was reaching a conclusion.

The dao of Immortal Lord Nineshores was being stripped away from the Fifth Star Ring, while the dao of Immortal Lord Aurora was being fused into it. That was the cause of all the strange phenomena.

During those seventeen days, all divination methods became less effective, and all forms of cognition grew weak. Omniscience did not function properly. That was why this time in history was so full of secrets. There was simply no way for people outside of that time period to truly know what went on then.

At the moment, everyone was looking up into the sky. That included Hordeslayer and Rampart in the sword furnace, Sir Star Ring as Fourth True Monarch in True Monarch Hall, Sir Vilespirit as Gongsun Qingmu in Scourgebolt Palace, Li Mengtu as Zhong Chi, and others whose true identities were not known, such as Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix in the south guest hall and Li the Chosen, who was still in seclusion.

There were also other people who were in hiding and had not yet been revealed as being outsiders. All of them could sense that the workings of heaven were degenerating. The great and unstoppable wheel of history was grinding onward.

Sir Star Ring laughed softly. This was the day he had been waiting for. The power of order would rise to the occasion.

In Young Aurora Hall, Xu Qing stood looking at the mixed darkness and light in the sky.

As the workings of heaven were thrown into chaos, and as the inevitability of history continued, he could sense that the ‘lake waters’ of this portion of space-time were deeper and weightier than ever. If he wanted to make waves, he couldn’t just rely on rocks. He needed a gale-force wind. And that was because there was more working against the waves than outside forces. The water of the lake itself was also resisting.

After coming here and doing so much work and study into time itself, I now have a much better understanding of how space-time works. Some parts of history aren’t that difficult to change. They can simply be rewritten.... But other things cannot be altered. If you even touch them, you’ll suffer a major backlash! And the most important thing right now... is going to happen on the day of the wedding!

Xu Qing looked down from the sky to the collection of sand in his hand. He was just about to turn around and call for the fox maiden to be brought for an audience when he heard a stern voice speaking in his mind.

“Come to Aurora Palace to see me!”

Xu Qing stopped in place and bowed his head respectfully. “Yes, sir.”

The voice belonged to Immortal Lord Aurora!

Aurora Palace was in the direct center of the immortal palace, underneath the Aurora Grand Hall. It was the location of Immortal Lord Aurora’s sleeping quarters as well as his secluded meditation facilities. Normally speaking, no one was allowed to even set foot there. The Immortal Lord’s four apprentices were no exception. Not even his son was allowed to go inside.

Therefore, when Xu Qing heard the Immortal Lord summoning him to Aurora Palace, he couldn’t help but take it seriously. He also knew that he couldn’t afford any delays, so he quickly left Young Aurora Hall and headed directly toward Aurora Grand Hall.

Before long, a complex of buildings appeared ahead. There was an enormous public square, paved with perfectly uniform limestone tiles that made the place glisten like a mirror. Magnificent jade towers lined the square on either side, making it look like a scene from a painting.

Going down the middle of the huge square were numerous imposing buildings. And in the very center of all of them was the biggest building of all. It had a very unique architectural style. It was towering and beautiful, with red walls and golden roof tiles that glittering resplendently. That building was none other than Aurora Grand hall.

Terrifying auras pulsed out of that building, causing Xu Qing to inhale sharply as he flew closer. The auras scanned him, then retracted, offering no obstacle to him. However, he could imagine what would have happened if it had been someone other than himself approaching.

Eventually, Xu Qing stepped in through the main door of Aurora Grand Hall. He immediately bowed at the waist.

Then a mysterious and majestic force descended. His vision blurred briefly, and when he could see again, he was no longer in the hall. He was in a long corridor.

Silent, flickering candles lined the corridor on either side. Thanks to their dim light, he could see greenish-black stairs in front of him, leading down into the darkness. The sound of metal clanking against stone reached his ears.

This was Aurora Palace. Based on his host’s memories, Xu Qing was actually familiar with this place. He remembered coming here when he was young. After growing up, though, he had rarely visited. Taking a deep breath, he started walking down the stairs.

The clanking sounds grew clearer and louder as he descended. After the time it takes an incense stick to burn, they were thunderous. What was more, waves of heat battered at him without cease. Eventually, he reached the end of the stairs.

There was a chamber there.

In the middle of it, a constant stream of earthflame shot up from the ground. Immortal Lord Aurora stood at the flame, using a shining silver hammer to pound a sheet of iron. Every blow he struck caused a deafening boom, and sent waves of heat out in all directions.

Immortal Lord Aurora wasn’t using his cultivation base. Instead, he relied solely on fleshly body power. His expression was one of pure concentration.

Xu Qing took the scene in, then approached quietly and watched the Immortal Lord work. He had no idea why he had been summoned, nor did he have any idea what the Immortal Lord was doing. As far as he could tell, the piece of iron didn’t seem unusual in any way. At most, it was... very hard.

As the forging process went on, the iron began to flicker with golden light. Time passed. The iron shone more and more brightly. Eventually, it was a pure golden color, and instead of being a random lump, it had a definite shape.

To Xu Qing, it looked like a golden plaque.

Immortal Lord Aurora stopped working. Picking up the golden-colored plaque, he studied it closely, and gradually, a look of satisfaction appeared on his face. Using his finger, he started writing.

Two families are now united in marriage by this covenant that never ends. From the moment this agreement is reached, the couple face a happy future of affinity. They are predestined to grow old together, and will be by each other’s side until the sea does wither up and stone rots. You will put your union above all else, and will have many prosperous and famous descendants

Let this marriage agreement be for all eternity; it is beautiful like rosy leaves, forever inscribed here as the happy couple always abides by its romantic tidings.

And thus, the agreement is confirmed.[1]

Immortal Lord Aurora’s style of calligraphy was as flamboyant as dancing dragons and swirling phoenixes. Every character seemed like a living thing crying out with joy and happiness.[2]

What was more, they had been peeled away from the mortal word, forming text that was backed with law and canon. They were words that could only apply to a son and daughter-in-law! It was a marriage contract!

Xu Qing felt enlightened just reading the words.

Only at this point did Immortal Lord Aurora turn to look at Xu Qing. “A name needs to go on here. Your name. Are you going to write it, or shall I?”

Xu Qing felt as if the question had struck him senseless. And that was because something completely and utterly outrageous had just occurred to him! He did not know, nor could he remember, the actual name of Young Lord Aurora! It didn’t exist in his memories! Xu Qing was shaken to the core. Up to this point, he hadn’t even thought about this. No one had ever spoken his name. Xu Qing said nothing.

Immortal Lord Aurora looked deeply at Xu Qing for a long moment, then coolly said, “I’ll handle it for you, okay?”

His hand moved as he inscribed the name onto the golden plaque.

Mi Ming.[3]

The moment Xu Qing looked at the name, his mind started spinning. A very strange feeling welled up within him as he realized that, at that very moment, a name now existed in his memories. For some reason, the name seemed very weighty. In fact, it was so weighty that the ground beneath his feet cracked and crumbled. He was shaking physically.

It was such a profound moment that Xu Qing couldn’t help but say, “Father, this—”

“It's nothing abnormal. After all, a marriage contract binds you for life.” Immortal Lord Aurora took out a jade box and put the marriage contract inside, then suspended it above the earthflame. He seemed about to say something further, but before he could, the firelight suddenly dimmed.

Immortal Lord Aurora frowned and waved his hand. “You can leave now. I called you here because I heard about what happened with the Hundred Flowers Palace and wanted you to witness the oath on the marriage contract. The contract will remain suspended here, untouchable by anyone save the two of us. Ten days from now, on your wedding day, I’ll come get it.”

Xu Qing’s vision blurred again, and when the sensation passed, he was outside of the chamber.

***

At the exact same moment that Xu Qing left, the firelight in the chamber grew even dimmer. Pulses of living black pulsed out of Immortal Lord Aurora.

More and more of it appeared until it created a shadowy figure. If Xu Qing had been there, he would have recognized it instantly. That shadowy figure was the exact same thing he had seen reflected beneath Immortal Lord Aurora that day at the lake!

The dark figure looked at the spot where Xu Qing had just stood and then spoke in a raspy voice. “In the time of the succession, when the workings of heaven in the Fifth Star Ring are the most chaotic, you took away the name of the sun and moon. You made sure that the people of the world forgot the name of the sun and moon without even realizing it. That includes the Immortal Lords and the Immortal Paragon. Your skill, combined with the chaos in the heavenly workings, ensures that, temporarily at least, the matter will not be noticed.

“Most ingenious is that you used the name of the sun and moon to replace your son’s name. This is really going to be a lovely surprise to your father, the Immortal Paragon.”[4]

Aurora looked expressionlessly at the dark figure. “You used the wrong form of address. You’re me. And I’m you. That’s our father.”

1. The text is full of idioms and metaphors that are understandable to Chinese readers based on context and culture, but which have little meaning to average English readers when translated directly. For instance, it uses “mandarin ducks” a few times. I’m sure many of you readers would understand that mandarin ducks are a reference to a married couple, but I’m also sure there are readers who would have no idea what that meant. And this entire passage is full of such flowery and poetic stuff. I wanted the meaning to be clear without use of footnotes, so my translated version is a bit more direct. Yes, it takes away some of the poetic flair, but in this context I feel it’s important. Beyond that (minor spoilers here), there is later wordplay I had to take into account, in which the meaning is very important, so, on multiple levels, this more direct version is necessary.... ☜

2. The idiom dancing dragons and swirling phoenixes is used to describe Chinese calligraphy that has a certain dramatic look and feel. There are different styles of calligraphy, but I did a quick Baidu search for calligraphy described in this way. Here are a few images to give you an idea of what the calligraphy might look like. ☜

3. Mi Ming: Mi is not a common surname. It’s a rather literary word that means “to seek, look for.” Ming means many things, but primarily “bright, brightness.” ☜

4. I’m sure some of you might be wondering if the name Mi Ming has anything to do with the names of the sun and moon that were previously mentioned in chapter 1155 and 1153. Since I translated those names instead of transliterated, it’s not obvious. But the answer is no. None of the names share the same characters. In fact, the characters aren’t even similar, nor do they have similar pronunciations. THAT SAID, the character Ming, brightness, is literally made up of the two characters for sun and moon. Sun is 日 and moon 月 while ming/brightness is 明. So take that for what you will.... ☜

Time passed. Six days. There were only four more days until the wedding!

The workings of heaven grew increasingly unstable. As the day of succession neared, the cycles of the sun and moon became more chaotic. In even just one day, it would go back and forth between darkness and light dozens of times. The entire world was affected. Sometimes, it was impossible to see the moon during the night and the sun during the day. Occasionally, everything would get mixed up, and a bright moon would be visible during the day, while a black sun came out at night!

It was pure confusion. Just like Zhou Zhengli’s thoughts at the moment. He stood in the highest tower in True Monarch Hall, his head bowed as he spoke to Sir Star Ring, who stood in front of him with his hands clasped behind his back.

“Back in the eastern planetary region,” Zhou Zhengli said, “you occupied such a high position that you could remain separated from the affairs of the world, thinking about the dao. At that time, Sir Vilespirit was like a bug to you. As a result, you were not really aware of his despicable and wicked deeds. But I was out there clashing with him constantly. So I understand him a bit more.

“Since you’ve inquired about him, exalted one, I’ll explain a bit of what I know. He has not gained enlightenment of any canon. His canon comes from the evil broken sword inside of him. That sword has a name: Betrayal!

“And that’s why everything he does revolves around the concept of betrayal. He’s betrayed sects. He’s betrayed his own beliefs. He’s betrayed everything....” Zhou Zhengli seemed to be saying some things by not saying them. Looking at Sir Star Ring, he decided to stop for a moment to let him think.

Sir Star Ring turned and looked down at the bowing Zhou Zhengli. “In other words, he’ll even betray an ally! His dao is that of betrayal, and therefore, to him, it doesn’t matter who he betrays as long as he betrays someone!”

Zhou Zhengli sighed with regret. “You fully deserve to be called the number one Shining Star, exalted one. All it took was a brief explanation from me, and you understand the complete picture. In contrast, it took me years of fighting and a lot of contemplation to wrap my mind around it.”

Sir Star Ring glanced at Zhou Zhengli. Zhou Zhengli had a very respectful look on his face and didn’t dare to make eye contact. He just kept bowing. The tower was silent for a time.

Then Sir Star Ring said, “I know you’re talented, Zhou Zhengli. And I know you’re a schemer as well. You fought with Sir Vilespirit for years, to the point where he views you as his archenemy. How could you possibly be deemed mediocre?”

Sir Star Ring looked off at the horizon and calmly said, “Maybe feigning weakness is your dao. Or maybe you just work hard at it. But... if you keep it up, then I’ll just peel your consciousness out of that body. It makes little difference to me if you’re at my side. Therefore, what you’ve said so far about Sir Vilespirit isn’t enough. I need you to give me a good reason to get rid of him right now.”

Sometimes, overwhelming power can defeat someone even ten times as skilled. This was just such a case. It didn’t matter how Zhou Zhengli planned or schemed. If he didn’t provide a good reason right then and there, Sir Star Ring would do just as he had said. He was perfectly willing to send Zhou Zhengli away. That was the simplest way to do away with his scheming.

Zhou Zhengli smiled wryly and then sighed. “Exalted one, you misunderstand me. Truth be told, sir, it’s not that I didn’t try hard. It’s just that your brilliance is so dazzling I fear I might burn myself.... Since you brought it up, I can briefly outline the problem here. If you notice any faulty logic, sir, please point it out.

“Originally, we had the initiative in this little conflict. But we lost the initiative to them. From what I can tell, the main problem is that we’re looking at things from too high of a vantage point.

“When you occupy such a high position, the plots and schemes of nobodies are hard to notice. You need to get on the same level as them. Only then will you realize how wily and ruthless they are. Only then can you guard against their machinations. After all, we’re in the right here. They’re the evil ones. This reality is something that I only recently started to realize, and it all became clear thanks to this conversation today.

“It might seem like there aren’t many people on our side, but I think... that we actually have the most people on our side. With the exception of certain outsiders, everyone in the immortal palace... is on the side of order, right?

“They’re all historical figures who have no idea what fate has in store for them. They’ll automatically follow the proper course in space-time.... And that’s order, correct? Exalted one, if I can understand such things, then obviously you do too. You wanted me to say it out loud so that... I would be bound by karma, and wouldn’t consider abandoning your service.

“But, sir, you really misunderstand me. Following you has long been a dream of mine. The reality is that I’m not very smart, and I’m worried about making bad decisions. That’s why I’ll always follow your lead, exalted one.”

With that all said, Zhou Zhengli kept his head bowed and said nothing further.

Sir Star Ring closed his eyes for a while. When he opened them, they shone brightly. He looked at Zhou Zhengli.

“After all of this is over and we’re back in the eastern planetary region, come find me at the Star Ring Pagoda.” Having said that, he turned and walked off.

“Many thanks, Milord!” Zhou Zhengli bowed deeply. Eyes narrowed, he watched as Sir Star Ring left.

Sir Star Ring’s advantage is that he’s strong and brave. His weakness is that he’s obstinate and self-opinionated. All I had to do was push a little here and there, and he’s raring to fight. Let’s just hope it turns out to be a good show.

***

Thunder rumbled above. A moment ago, the skies were clear and blue. But now the rain was pouring down.

However, that rainfall didn’t produce so much as a ripple on the lake of space-time in the immortal palace. As the workings of heaven became more chaotic, and as the day of succession drew near, space-time grew more solid than ever.

Xu Qing was able to sense that thanks to his space-time canon. He knew that it was getting more and more difficult to create any waves. It wasn’t some sudden development. It was just how things worked historically speaking.

I’m afraid this is the opportunity Fourth True Monarch has been waiting for.

He stood in Young Aurora Hall, looking up as the sky suddenly switched from darkness to light. At the same time, the pouring rain transformed into hail. The pitter-patter turned into a thunderous crashing sound. A frigid aura spread, weighing down heavily on everything, eventually becoming a powerful wind that stirred Xu Qing’s hair. As the wind blew, he could sense the unstoppable flow of history approaching.

***

The current arrived. And along with it came a minor incident that shook the immortal palace! It could be called minor because it was something that was subject to change at any moment, and was insignificant enough that it was easy to overlook or misunderstand. But that supposedly minor incident still affected the whole immortal palace.

It was an order issued by Fourth True Monarch. He personally called on the immortal palace’s Law Enforcement Bureau to launch an investigation into Gongsun Qingmu, Li the Chosen, the fox maiden, and Zhong Chi.

According to him, Gongsun Qingmu, an honor guard from the Scourgebolt Palace, was conspiring to betray the immortal palace. The evidence was the jade slip from Gongsun Qingmu’s apprentice, as well as information about his background and other details. All of it implicated his Master. That was why Fourth True Monarch suspected that Gongsun Qingmu's apprentice had been planning to betray the palace on orders from his Master!

As for the fox maiden, Fourth True Monarch revealed the details of her life before coming to the immortal palace. That, coupled with the fact that Gongsun Qingmu had taken her in as an apprentice, cast her in suspicion. And though there was no clear indication of her motive, Fourth True Monarch claimed that he knew the truth. She was after Young Lord Aurora! She had intentionally gotten close to the young master to earn status and avoid being expelled. Given how things turned out, it was obvious that she knew Gongsun Qingmu, otherwise he would never have taken her as an apprentice without having any previous contact. All of it proved that she was conspiring against Young Lord Aurora!

As for Li the Chosen, he had intentionally tried to get Young Lord Aurora to take in the fox maiden. He had offered her as the stakes of a bet knowing full well that he would lose. It was all to get her close to the young lord. It was the act of an accomplice!

Meanwhile, Zhong Chi had been a companion of Young Lord Aurora for years. He had seemed very loyal, but for unknown reasons had a change of heart. The proof was the poison inside of him, which he himself had ingested! No one would intentionally poison themselves, and thus, Fourth True Monarch believed that the poison was part of a secret magic being used to poison and kill Young Lord Aurora.

Fourth True Monarch’s accusations shook the whole immortal palace. In the blink of an eye, countless people were paying attention to the situation. None of these accusations were made behind closed doors. By peeling back the lid on the entire thing, and letting everyone in the immortal palace see what was going on, order could be preserved.

With everyone as witnesses, the entire affair was out in the open for all to see. That way, if Fourth True Monarch was telling the truth, the matter could be handled swiftly. Everything could conform to order.

And if Fourth True Monarch was wrong, all he had to do was apologize and say it was all a misunderstanding. In that case, if there were any waves in history, they would be very weak. After all, the matter wouldn’t affect the larger course of history.

To Sir Vilespirit and the others involved, it was a ruthless blow that they had no way to avoid or block.

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix paid close attention to the matter from the beginning. In order to make sure no suspicion was cast on her, she stayed in Young Aurora Hall constantly.

What was more, the situation with driving the fox maiden out of Young Aurora Hall left Li Mengtu no choice but to leave the service of the young lord. Before departing, he had come to visit Xu Qing one last time. Thinking back to everything they had done together left Li Mengtu feeling quite moved. Looking at the young lord, he suddenly felt reluctant to leave. It was an experience he would never forget. After bowing one last time, he made a sudden decision. freewebnovel.com

“Young Lord, your humble servant had a strange dream last night.... I dreamed of your wedding, only a few days from now. There was a lot of noise and excitement, and the atmosphere in the immortal palace was jubilant. Unfortunately... in the moment when you and your wife bow to heaven and earth, a great catastrophe struck. You never finished bowing.... The world became drenched in blood.”

With that, he bowed one last time and walked out.

Xu Qing watched him leave, his eyes glittering. This counterattack from Fourth True Monarch came as no surprise. There was a conflict between people who wanted to maintain order and those who wanted to change history. Everyone had their own dao. And Xu Qing knew that the only reason he had come out on top in the past was that he was so well hidden. When fighting from the shadows, it was easy to come out on top against people in the light.

Because of that circumstance, the opponent was focused on Sir Vilespirit and the fox maiden. Unfortunately, the victories he had won from the shadows were minor, and didn’t affect the big picture. History was going to unfold as normal without much changes. All he had changed were minor details. The other side had always had the advantage. It was just that they had forgotten about that thanks to his string of small successes. But they would remember eventually.

I’m just waiting for the moment that you do remember and then take the initiative.

He had just put a very important game piece onto the board. It was a piece that would cause a great tempest to rise up. Unfortunately, he wasn’t strong enough to play this game alone. He didn’t have enough allies, and what was more, the other side of the conflict needed to participate. That was how to make a big stir!

After all, when the side of order took the initiative to act, it would result in waves. They would be small, but... it was still something!

It’s getting windy.

Rumbling filled the outside world as the wind erupted into a tempest, sending debris flying through the air.

Xu Qing’s eyes turned cold.

It was time to use the wind to climb to the heights of heaven!

On that night, the heavenly workings were causing dramatic transformations. The wind kept picking up, thunder boomed, and lightning illuminated the darkness. Rumbling shook the immortal palace, reaching the ears of everyone, including Sir Vilespirit, who was playing the role of Gongsun Qingmu in the Scourgebolt Palace.

Lightning illuminated the hall in which he stood as Sir Star Ring stepped out thin air in the guise of Fourth True Monarch. Instantly, killing intent surged within him, all as a frigid coldness swept out, enveloping the hall in winter. Snowflakes drifted everywhere, and ice crystals began to build up inside Sir Vilespirit, filling his body and threatening to wipe out his consciousness.

“Stay? Or go?” Sir Star Ring said calmly. “Do you really want to be my enemy? Or will you join me? You already accomplished your goal, haven’t you? So what is your decision??”

His clearly enunciated words turned into swords of ice, filled with the might of order. And all were pointed at Sir Vilespirit. Ice chains clinked into being, sweeping through the hall to become a mysterious spell formation, pulsing with brilliant mightiness.

Sir Vilespirit slowly looked up at the figure standing in front of him. He smiled a very wicked smile.

“What exactly did my old nemesis Zhou Zhengli say to you, oh exalted one? He understands me better than anyone. In truth, ever since leaving Young Aurora Hall, I’ve just been waiting for you to come. As for my decision....”

He lifted his hand, within which appeared a jade medallion. It was the fox maiden’s identity medallion! Sir Vilespirit’s eyes glittered mysteriously as he forcefully crushed it. A cracking sound rang out as the jade medallion crumbled into pieces.

“Upon investigation, I came to realize that Qiu Lingshan harbored evil intentions. She infiltrated the immortal palace in order to commit criminal acts. I’m willing to punish myself for failing to realize it sooner. I immediately stripped her of her status. As for whether she deserves the death penalty, I’ll let you decide, True Monarch.”[1]

Qiu Lingshan was the true name of the fox maiden in this space-time. With that jade medallion crushed, her status as an apprentice and member of the Scourgebolt Palace was revoked.

This was Sir Vilespirit’s dao. Betrayal. That included betrayal of organizations and betrayals of allies. As far as he was concerned, it didn’t matter who he betrayed, as long as he betrayed someone. That was how things were in this space-time. Everyone was plotting against each other. The fox maiden was plotting against him, and he was plotting against her.

The moment he had an identity and some allies, he had the foundation for betrayal. And just as he had said, he really had been waiting for Sir Star Ring to show up. The frigid coldness, ice swords, and chains faded away.

Sir Star Ring turned to leave. He had accomplished what he wanted to accomplish.

However, just before he stepped out, Sir Vilespirit spoke from behind him. “Exalted one, I’ve been fighting Zhou Zhengli for years now, and though he understands me, I also understand him. So I’ll give you a little advice. That guy... believes great good to be evil, and believes great evil to be good. He’s more complicated than you think!”

Sir Star Ring stood in the doorway, his expression unchanging. “Everybody says that if you take the Shining Stars and put them out in the world, they’ll become ambitious and ruthless. That’s why I care about what people do, not what their ideals are. As long as I’m the strongest, then I don’t care what someone’s ideals are. If they obey me, so be it. If they disobey, I kill them.”

With that, he strode out and became an electric bolt of light that disappeared an instant later.

Sir Vilespirit chuckled. This whole fourth world thing has been very interesting. Sir Star Ring from the east rarely goes out into the world, so he’s only now finding out how difficult it is to deal with the other Shining Stars. That’s why the arrogant fellow just can’t stop from calling himself the strongest. Interesting. Very interesting.

Sir Vilespirit smiled, and this time it was both wicked and deranged. Strangely, though, the laughter that accompanied it didn’t come out of his mouth. It came from the broken sword inside of him.

***

Sir Star Ring was now outside of the Scourgebolt Palace in front of a courtyard. It was a courtyard that had been set up for subordinates of the palace. After the incident with Spirit Phoenix at Young Aurora Hall, the fox maiden had taken up residence here.

Those two psychos think they’ve figured me out and know how to manipulate me. Little do they know that there’s a reason they’re both Shining Stars in the eastern planetary system. They’re both dao fruits that I’ll use to nourish my canon of order in the future!

The moment Sir Star Ring appeared, the doors of the courtyard opened. The fox maiden leaned up against the door frame and looked at him languidly.

“That lousy Master of mine really isn’t reliable at all, is he? He crushed my identity medallion. He sold me out, through and through. And now you’ve come here to kill me, is that right?” She laughed softly. “You’re very clever, True Monarch. Now that I have no status in the immortal palace, I’m superfluous, and can be killed freely. It won’t cause any waves at all. After all... historically speaking, I shouldn’t even be in the immortal palace anymore. Well, aren’t you going to do it? I already did what I wanted to do here. I’m ready to leave at any time.”

Shē smiled broadly, as if this visit from the true monarch wasn’t a surprise to hēr at all.

But Sir Star Ring didn’t attack hēr. Instead, he calmly took a step forward. “You’re right. But if you did what you wanted to do, why haven’t you left yet? No, I’d say you probably have another plan you’re working on.” He took another step forward. “Is it that you’ve come to realize you can’t just leave?”

He continued walking the whole time, so that by the time he was finished, he was inside the courtyard, only a few meters away from hēr. He stopped walking.

Starfire was smiling, but inside, hēr guard was up, and shē sensed great danger. It was exactly as he had just said. When Sir Star Ring had blown everyone’s cover, shē’d tried to separate hēr consciousness from the fox maiden’s body, but had come to find that shē couldn’t. In the past, shē had been able to, but now there was some intangible force preventing hēr from doing it. That said, shē was an adept schemer, and thus, shē didn’t let that show on hēr face.

Before shē could respond, Sir Star Ring continued speaking. “Am I right, unknown god??”

His last words struck like a lightning bolt. Starfire was stunned to the core. In hēr previous clash with him, shē had worked hard to conceal the truth, and had believed shē had done a good job. After all, shē was half a step away from being an Altar God, and had plenty of secret magics at hēr disposal.

And everything that happened after that had seemed to indicate that Sir Star Ring had not detected anything unusual during their interactions. But now....

“If it was anyone else,” he continued, “they wouldn’t have been able to tell. But I’m from the Star Ring Pagoda in the eastern planetary region. Do you know why it’s named after the star ring...? Did you really think that you could fight with someone like me and that I wouldn’t notice you were working so hard to conceal your godly aura? The reason I didn’t say anything before is that... I wanted to see who else was working with you!”

He waved his hand, and a silver medallion appeared.

Astonishingly, the name Qiu Lingshan was visible on the medallion.

“This is a god-branding medallion. They’ve been used since ancient times in the Fifth Star Ring to subdue gods. As you would expect, you can get them here in the immortal palace. With this medallion sealing you, your consciousness can’t escape this place unless I permit it!”

He casually pushed his finger down onto the medallion. A sealing force specifically designed to target gods suddenly shot out, causing Starfire to shiver and gasp.

“I think it’s best if you stay right here for now. Tonight we’re going to see whether or not you have someone backing you. Will they come to your rescue? If they don’t show up by daybreak... you’ll find out what happens when I use this god-branding medallion on your true form. And therefore, I suggest you send a message asking for help.”

Sir Star Ring sat down with a smile on his face to wait for dawn.

Meanwhile, Starfire was trembling, hēr eyes bloodshot already thanks to the power of the god-branding medallion.

***

The wind blew stronger and stronger. It swept through the immortal palace all the way to Young Aurora Hall.

Xu Qing’s hair stirred. He was walking through the wind.

Many things had taken place. First was Fourth True Monarch blowing the cover of so many people. Then Starfire explained that hēr consciousness couldn’t leave the fourth world after shē was expelled from Young Aurora Hall. Next came Li Mengtu’s apology. Finally, Spirit Phoenix moved into Young Aurora Hall.

If this was a game of Go, then his opponent’s pieces would have him surrounded, left with no option other than to be devoured.

But all of it... has just helped me to see things clearly!

He looked off in the direction of the sword furnace, and then at Starfire’s residence.

As for the game situation.... Playing one piece the right way can revitalize the board completely. freewebnovel.com

He took another step and disappeared. When he reappeared... he had not left Young Aurora Hall, but instead, was in one of the side halls. This was where Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix had taken up residence! The moment he appeared, the black-armored guards surged with energy.

“Back down!” Xu Qing said quietly.

The might and power of Young Lord Aurora weighed down, and the streams of energy backed away. The guards had no choice but to allow Xu Qing to walk into the hall, bringing the wind and rain with him. There inside was Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, seated cross-legged and looking straight at him.

The moment their eyes met, Spirit Phoenix’s heart thumped in her chest. However, she didn’t reveal that on her face. Instead, she took control of the conversation by saying, “What is it? Here to interrogate me because I kicked out the fox maiden?”

Xu Qing ignored her outburst, walked over the window, and looked out at the sky. “Zhong Chi just left. Before he did, he said he had a dream. He dreamed that before we could complete the kneeling ritual in our wedding, catastrophe arrived and everything ended up soaked in blood.”

Spirit Phoenix snorted coldly. “Vicious lies! He should die for that!”

Without even turning to look at her, he said, “Vicious lies? You mean like the recent rumors? Supposedly some outsiders showed up recently. So... are you one of them?”[2]

“You’re not acting like yourself today,” Spirit Phoenix said, her heart racing, but a frown on her face.

Xu Qing smiled. He didn’t turn around. But what he said next struck Spirit Phoenix like a bolt of lightning. “I don’t care if you’re Yuanshan Su or somebody else. Either way, your goal is simply to be connected by karma to my host. And you want to use that to become half-owner of the immortal palace. So the question is, do you want the marriage to succeed? Or do you want it to fail?”

As he finished speaking, he slowly turned around and looked her straight in the eyes, his gaze bright and aggressive.

His words were like 10,000,000 bolts of heavenly lightning striking her down to the core of her being. Shaking, she shot to her feet and took a few steps back. Her mind was being battered with waves of shock so intense she was struck as senseless as a wooden chicken. All she could do was stare at Xu Qing as if he was a ghost.

“Wh-who... who are you?” she stammered in astonishment. Never in her wildest imagination would she have even considered guessing that Young Lord Aurora would actually say her name.

It was enough to make everything clear. He was an outsider! Young Lord Aurora was actually an outsider. She was in daze, and even wondered if what was happening was real. It overturned everything she thought was true. It subverted all her expectations. In fact, it surpassed the level of ‘astonishing.’ Yet, there was no denying what was right in front of her.

“You....” Yuanshan Su’s face was ashen, and her thoughts were in complete chaos. She couldn’t even speak, as she didn’t know what to say.

Xu Qing remained as calm as ever as he looked at her. “My guess is that you want the marriage to succeed. That will make it more possible for you to reach your goal. Therefore, I suggest we work together to make sure the marriage happens. But if you refuse to work with me, then on the wedding day, I’ll reject you in front of everyone. That will change history in a dramatic way, and cause some big waves! You need to give me your answer before I walk out of here.”

He turned and walked toward the door. Step by step, he got closer.

Yuanshan Su couldn’t breathe steadily. She couldn’t calm down. All she could do was watch him walking away from her, her heart pounding. Just when he was about to walk out, she took a deep breath, a complicated expression on her face.

“I’ll work with you!” There was no way she could refuse. In the final analysis, her entire plan revolved around the young lord. He was key to it all. That was why, from the very beginning, she had never considered Fourth True Monarch to be an actual ally. All it took were those handful of words spoken by the young lord for her to defer to him!

Xu Qing was at the door. He was not surprised at all at her response. He had known from the beginning that once he revealed that he was an outsider, she would have no other option than to join him. That was a foregone conclusion, given her goal.

Voice cool, he said, “Good. Go keep the fox maiden safe tonight, no matter how you do it.”

With that, he stepped outside into the wind. Looking in the direction of the fox maiden’s residence, he sighed inwardly.

You want to fight, Elder Brother Fourth? Well, tonight we’re going to fight!

The wind screamed faster and faster, rapidly turning into a tempest!

1. You might remember that Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s real name is Zhou Linshan. This name here, Qiu Lingshan, is a different name. I just wanted to clarify this, because even when I was reading it, I was temporarily confused about whose name it was. The third character is shared with Qiu Lingshan, but the second character is not. The names are not connected. ☜

2. There is some word play that doesn’t translate. The specific characters for what I’m rendering “vicious lies” have the exact same pronunciation as the word for “rumors.” So what he actually says is something like “you saying the word ‘vicious lies’ makes me think of the recent ‘rumors,’” which makes perfect sense in Chinese, but doesn’t have the same ring in English. In reality, this play on words wouldn’t work in spoken Chinese, because you have to be able to see the characters to differentiate between them. It would be like wordplay involving the letter Y and the word why? If you said something like, “Do you mean why? Or do you mean Y?” it obviously wouldn’t make any sense without further context or being able to see the word. ☜

The wind roared through the immortal palace. As lightning flashed and thunder boomed, Xu Qing advanced through the wind. The workings of heaven were in chaos, but his heart was utterly calm. Wild colors flashed in the dome of heaven, but no expression flashed across his face.

As of tonight, it was obvious what he had to do. The game piece he had played in the form of Yuanshan Su was the clarion call marking his comeback. And to go along with that call, he needed a spear.

And thus, he appeared in the complex of buildings outside of Aurora Grand Hall in the very middle of the immortal palace. There, terrifying divine will kept watch, yet he didn’t slow down at all. He shot right through the public square to appear.... right in front of Aurora Grand Hall.

The storm grew stronger. Curtains of rain fell, and the wind scraped through the air and across the green limestone. Water splashed everywhere.

Amidst all that, Xu Qing ducked his head, clasped hands, and bowed.

“Father!” he said loudly. “There are a few things I need to do tonight. And I need to use the marriage contract!”

Thunder crashed, but it wasn’t capable of drowning out Xu Qing’s voice. After all of his observations and calculations, he was confident that his request would be granted. And that was because the marriage contract fundamentally belonged to the young lord.

Originally, he had been hesitant. But after everything that happened... he was convinced that there was no way the Immortal Lord didn’t know about everything going on in the palace, including the situation with the outsiders! This section of history was a mere space-time reflection, but... the entities inside this space-time had extremely high personhood. Xu Qing refused to believe that the old-timers in the palace hadn’t noticed the signs of what was going on!

And yet, for this entire time, they had remained silent. They had not interfered! They were not providing either assistance or obstruction to the side of order or the side of change. And that lack of interference amounted to a tacit approval! They approved of everything that was happening!

Thus, having combined the implications of all his observations and analyses, Xu Qing had come here tonight!

His voice entered the hall and reached a figure seated cross-legged there. The figure opened his eyes and looked outside. His left eye was black, while his right eye glittered like a jewel.

A moment later, the storm went still. The thunder and lightning ceased. And a golden beam of light glided out of Aurora Grand Hall toward Xu Qing.

It was a golden plaque, upon which was inscribed the marriage agreement. It was none other than the marriage contract for Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. As the contract floated over, the voice of Immortal Lord Aurora emerged from the hall.

“Due to various reasons, I cannot help you with the matter you seek to handle. You’ll have to do it yourself. When it’s done, make sure to get some rest as soon as possible.”

“Yes, sir,” Xu Qing said, keeping his head bowed.

After taking the marriage contract, he turned and left. Rain poured down behind him. The storm raged in front of him.

As Xu Qing left, the storm grew more intense. By the time lightning had struck three more times, Xu Qing had appeared outside the immortal palace’s university.

Thanks to the memories of his host, Xu Qing was familiar with the place. It was composed mostly of small buildings constructed from immortal timber. The roofs were made of black tiles, and the grounds were filled with immortal trees. It was a beautiful and secluded place, complete with bridges spanning flowing streams. This place was truly suited to learning.[1]

Unfortunately, it was night, and it was raining hard, so the scenery was a bit different. The trees swayed back and forth wildly, and the streams weren’t even visible. The bridges were obscured by the sheets of falling water, and the windows of the buildings glowed with soft light that seemed to separate the interior from the outside world.

Xu Qing walked right into the university. He entered the haze and the soft light without obstruction, as if the warding spells protecting this place didn’t even exist to him. He was the young lord, and thus, though a few places in the immortal palace were restricted to him, the university wasn’t one of them.

He quickly arrived at a multi-storied building with the address #317. This building served as the university’s secluded meditation facilities, as well as a place to serve sentences after being punished. Thus, it was backed by the might of the palace, and was not a place that could be easily broken into or out of.

There was currently someone seated cross-legged inside #317. He noticed Xu Qing’s arrival, and opened his eyes. When he turned and looked outside, he looked surprised.

“You—”

At that exact moment, lightning fell, casting bright light everywhere and illuminating both people. On the outside was Xu Qing. On the inside was Li the Chosen.

“Young Lord!” said Li the Chosen. He blinked a few times, looking chagrined. He had been extremely nervous in recent days, but had been too scared of Fourth True Monarch to do anything.

Thanks to how Fourth True Monarch had interfered, Li the Chosen had failed to get close to the young lord. His original plan had been to watch the young lord closely to see how history would play out. That would conform to his canon, which was that of mist and obfuscation. It was no ordinary mist, though. It came from history. The mist of history was the substructure of his canon. The more clearly he saw history, the more he could dispel the mist of history. And that dispelled mist would be absorbed by his own canon, strengthening it.

Sadly, he had been foiled before he could even take the first step down the path of his plan. All he could do was wait here, sealed, until everything ended. He could have simply left the fourth world early, but he wasn’t willing to do that.

Upon seeing the young lord, he bitterly said, “Young Lord, it’s not that I didn’t want to go to your beast ranch. Someone plotted against me and got me sentenced to this place.... I—”

“Li the Chosen,” Xu Qing interrupted coolly. He had no time for chit-chat. “You were willing to cause space-time waves to get close to me, all in the hopes of slightly altering the trajectory of established history. That was the first step of your plan, right? Well, I don’t care who you really are or what your goal is. I merely want to know: do you want to succeed? Do you want to get out of there?”

Xu Qing’s calm voice hit Li the Chosen’s ears harder than heavenly lightning, shaking him to the depths of his soul. His pupils constricted, and his wry expression disappeared completely, replaced by a look of pure incredulity.

“Who are you?” Li the Chosen said, struggling to keep his cool as he looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing didn’t answer the question. He turned and started walking away. At the same time, he waved his hand, and the door that had been sealing Li the Chosen this whole time quietly swung open.

The wind blew inside, along with Xu Qing’s voice.

“I don’t care what your goal is here in the fourth world. I can help you succeed. Or I can make sure you fail. Right now, I need you to do something for me. Assassinate Fourth True Monarch. And make sure he cuts off one of your arms in the process.”

Xu Qing left.

Li the Chosen sat silently inside #317. A moment later, he looked up, his heart racing. The fact that the young lord was actually an outsider was so astonishing that he wasn’t sure how to react.

The young lord’s words had contained a threat. If anyone else had spoken those words, they would have been nothing but that: a threat. The question would have been whether there would be follow-through. But considering the threat came from Young Lord Aurora....

I have no choice but to believe he’ll do it....

Li the Chosen took a deep breath. Eyes flashing with cold light, he walked out of the open door!

***

A big wave had kicked up in space-time!

A person who was supposed to be locked in seclusion when catastrophe hit was now freed. He was now a trusted aide to the young lord. No longer locked up in seclusion, he was now plotting how to assassinate Fourth True Monarch, and have his arm cut off in the process. A wave like this was going to totally alter the course of history.

That’s just the first wave tonight. Next is Li Mengtu.

Xu Qing left the university that stormy night. Next he appeared... outside Zhong Chi’s residence.

***

Outside the Scourgebolt Palace, in the fox maiden’s residence, Starfire was trembling and hēr eyes were bloodshot. The god-branding medallion had hēr completely suppressed, and shē could sense how terrifying its power was. Given that this type of medallion was the Fifth Star Ring’s primary way of keeping gods under control, it was no wonder its power was beyond comparison.

Even shē, who was almost an Altar God, could do nothing but tremble in the face of a god-branding medallion. In fact, shē even got the sense that the god-branding power could be applied to hēr true form.

Sir Star Ring was currently seated in front of her cross-legged, looking very calm. Looking coldly at the fox maiden, he said, “We’re halfway through the night. I’m very curious to see if I’ve correctly guessed who your backer is. And... hmm?”

He suddenly looked in the direction of the university. A chaotic wave in that direction had attracted his attention. And then, almost at the exact same time that he noticed it, he looked... at the entrance of the courtyard.

Thunderous rumbling sounds echoed out as Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s imperial carriage raced through the storm. As soon as it arrived, Yuanshan Su stepped out in the guise of Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. She looked very angry. Before Sir Star Ring could say a thing, she gained the upper hand.

“True Monarch, what exactly do you think you’re doing to my Elder Sister??” As the words left her mouth, a host of black-armored guards fanned out into the courtyard.

Sir Star Ring’s eyes flickered with uncharacteristic surprise. “I wasn’t expecting you to show up.”

Eyes radiating fury, Yuanshan Su spoke with decisiveness that could sever nails and chop iron. “The fox maiden is the apprentice of my Master. Therefore, she’s my Elder Sister. It’s no surprise at all that I would show up when she’s in trouble!”

“When did she get that status?” Sir Star Ring asked. He had taken advantage of Sir Vilespirit’s betrayal to strip the fox maiden of her status. But now it seemed that Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix had given her a new status.

“A long time ago,” Yuanshan Su said. “If you don’t believe me, go talk to my father. But what’s more important is that I said so.”

She stepped forward to the fox maiden and waved her hand, using the power of her host’s body to negate the god-branding medallion.

Starfire breathed a sigh of relief and then laughed softly. “Milady, your humble slave girl was almost convinced you wouldn’t come to help.”

Yunashan Su ignored hēr.

Sir Star Ring watched all of this happening and laughed softly. Then he slowly rose to his feet, looking a bit absent-minded. Voice hoarse, he said, “I really could never have guessed that you would show up to save hēr! That said, your arrival has really cleared up the mystery.

“You might be the mastermind I’ve been waiting for. But if you’re not, then I think I have a good idea of who the real mastermind is. This is definitely unexpected. Very unexpected. Somebody got the identity that no one is supposed to be able to get....”

1. The black roof tiles mentioned here are a traditional type of Chinese roof. Nowadays they can be made from more modern materials like plastic or whatever. Incidentally, remember a while ago how I mentioned that the character Qing from Xu Qing’s name can mean blue, green, cyan or even black? Well, this is one case in which the character means black when used as part of this specific combination of characters. As you can see from these pictures, the tiles are indeed black, or perhaps a charcoal color. ☜

Sir Star Ring got an answer to his question, but it only scratched the surface of the mystery. The arrival of Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix cleared away enough fog for him to see things clearly. Unfortunately, not all the fog was gone, so no matter how he studied the situation, things weren’t completely and utterly clear. It was like looking at flowers in the fog.

That said, given what he could see thanks to his canon, he felt strongly that he was correct. After all, it was human nature to believe what you wanted to believe. And Sir Star Ring was human. That was the reason he looked absent-minded and spoke in a hoarse voice.

What was more, he knew that if it was as he suspected, then... there was no chance he could win this war in the end. And given the events that had played out, his opponent had only just begun to fight!

Maybe I can’t win. But there’s a possibility... I might not lose!

Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered as killing intent rose within him. Ignoring Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and the fox maiden, he turned to leave. The two of them weren’t important to him now.

At the moment, the most crucial element to him was time. And therefore, he wasn’t going to waste any time on these people.

Starfire looked at him and was inclined to block his path. Unfortunately, the pressure from the god-branding medallion made it so that all shē could do was look at Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. “He seems to be in a hurry, Junior Sister. What do you say we slow him down?”

Yuanshan Su’s eyes glittered, but in the end... she chose not to block his path. All he told me to do was protect the fox maiden.

Eyes narrowing, she watched Fourth True Monarch walk out of the courtyard and disappear into the wind and rain.

Thunder rumbled.

RUUUUUUUMMMMBLE!

As Xu Qing appeared outside of Zhong Chi’s residence, he heard the crash of thunder. He walked inside. Everything blurred. There were spell formations and warding spells designed to keep people out, but they didn’t do a thing to Xu Qing.

In the blink of an eye, he was standing right over Li Mengtu, who sat there cross-legged and meditating in the guise of Zhong Chi. A flash of lightning lit up heaven and earth outside, and the light reached inside. Li Mengtu opened his eyes and looked confused.

“Young Lord?” He had not been expecting Young Lord Aurora to show up. He quickly got to his feet and prepared to bow, but before he could, a gentle force emanated from Xu Qing that prevented him from bowing.

Xu Qing walked to the window and looked out at the storm. The wind blew and the thunder boomed.

“Li Mengtu!” he said calmly.

As he spoke the words, thunder crashed outside, and the sound of it slammed into Li Mengtu’s heart. Mind spinning, his face fell. He couldn’t have been more astonished, and though he opened his mouth to speak, it was Xu Qing whose words rang out in the room.

“I know what you’re trying to do. You’re using your canon to slowly infect the body you’ve possessed. You’re trying to poison it to death!

“However, the presence of your own consciousness combined with the extraordinary nature of the body is making it difficult for you to meet the requirements to poison it to death. Therefore, you’re hoping to take advantage of a key moment in history, and the mighty waves it will generate, to make your canon of poison more effective.

“Your host is supposed to die in the coming catastrophe, but you’re hoping to kill him with poison. If you do that, then your poison will have the weight of history behind it. And technically speaking, it will have appeared in history before your own Master.

“As a result, it won’t matter that this is only a reflection of history. It will still be an effective weapon for your inevitable fight with your Master in the future. If this history becomes real, then your canon of poison will have a foundation in reality. If this history remains a mere reflection, then you’ll be able to have a foundation of an illusion.

“Either way, it will benefit your future cultivation. An ingenious plan!” Xu Qing turned to look at Li Mengtu.

The words caused Li Mengtu’s heart to pound so loudly it was almost deafening. He was breathing heavily, and the look of respect in his eyes had changed into something fierce and aggressive. Yet within that aggression there was a profound and obvious incredulity.

He was thinking the very same thing that went through the minds of Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, Li the Chosen, and Fourth True Monarch earlier. A person who was supposedly impossible to possess had indeed been possessed.... The result was confusion and astonishment.

In the blink of an eye, his canon poison surged within him. Staring at Xu Qing, he suppressed his astonishment and quickly regained his cool.

A thousand thoughts running through his head, he said, “Who are you?”

“You likely guessed who I am the moment I said your name,” Xu Qing said calmly.

Li Mengtu said nothing. He was indeed able to make an educated guess, considering that he had told Patriarch Diling about his identity, and instructed him to pass the information to Xu Qing. But then he thought back to all of his interactions with Young Lord Aurora, and he wasn’t totally sure. That was especially true considering that it wouldn’t be too difficult to figure out who he was. After all, poison... was his defining attribute in real life. He was about to explain all of this when thunder crashed outside.

Xu Qing noticed it and looked outside. He had a lot to do tonight, and it was going to take time to explain everything to Li Mengtu.

“I have a better way to accomplish your goal!” Xu Qing took out a special jade slip and was about to imprint it with information. Before he did, he stopped and looked at Li Mengtu. “Pick a fundamentally defining name for your poison canon!”

Li Mengtu’s eyes flashed. Given that Zhong Chi was the study partner of the young lord, he recognized what kind of jade slip that was. It was a jade slip of decree. His heart was already racing as he realized what the young lord was about to do. It was something he had dreamed of accomplishing, but had been unable to do.

Though he was still unsure of who exactly he was dealing with, he didn’t hesitate to say, “Poison of Mengtu!”[1]

Xu Qing nodded, then pinched the jade slip as he imprinted it with divine will.

“Zhong Chi, disciple of the immortal palace, will use the canon Poison of Mengtu to protect and safeguard the young lord! Therefore, Zhong Chi is hereby authorized to create the Department of Poison in Young Aurora Hall, to further the study of his poison and permanently enshrine it as an aspect of the immortal palace. Let his proclamation be heard worldwide!”

Li Mengtu’s mind was spinning more dramatically than it ever had in his life. He knew full well... that this was a righteous bestowal![2]

His identity was receiving a righteous bestowal, as was the foundation of his poison canon. This was clearly a far more direct way to reach his goal than poisoning himself, and it was also far more impressive! In fact, the two different methods couldn’t even be compared with each other.

As the decree was being imprinted, space-time waves rolled out dramatically, vying with the thunder outside in terms of intensity.

Upon sensing the space-time waves, Xu Qing flicked the jade slip into the air and sent it flying to Li Mengtu. “Wait until tomorrow morning. Then come to Young Aurora Hall to officially set up the Department of Poison.”

Li Mengtu caught the jade slip. He wanted to say something, but at the moment was at a complete loss for words.

“Finally,” Xu Qing said, “take some of your poison and give it to me.... It needs to be strong, otherwise how could you use it to protect me?”

He looked calmly at Li Mengtu.

Li Mengtu didn’t hesitate for a moment. Reaching up, he viciously sliced open his chest, causing blood to spray out. It was pure black. Next, he sent some of his will into the blood to catalyze the poison canon to the proper level. He put it in a bottle, and then he gave it to Xu Qing.

Xu Qing took it and examined it. “It seems to me that your understanding and mastery of plants and vegetation is imperfect. From the time I gave the poison canon back to you until now... you haven’t improved it much.”

Shaking his head, he walked out and disappeared into the wind and rain.

Inside, Li Mengtu exhaled slowly. As the words the young lord had just spoken seemed to echo in his ears, he smiled wryly.

You hid yourself very well, Xu Qing....

The storm got more intense in the immortal palace. Rain poured down, and the chaos in the workings of heaven grew more obvious. Half of the sky was suddenly red like evening. The other half was still pitch black!

In the pitch-black part, Sir Star Ring was flying at top speed toward Zhong Chi’s residence. The waves coming from there were like flames in the night. But even as he shot forward, a fog suddenly appeared out of nowhere in the darkness, blocking his path! Sir Star Ring stopped in place.

Li the Chosen slowly walked out of the fog, his eyes gleaming with the desire to do battle. “You seem like you’re in a hurry, Sir Star Ring. Where are you going?”

Intense fighting was playing out in the darkness.

At first, when he changed the direction of Li the Chosen, the waves were minor. But they picked up when events played out at the fox maiden’s residence. freewebnovel.com

Then he went to Li Mengtu and issued a decree, and the waves grew more forceful.

Next comes Li the Chosen’s severed arm. That needs to become a reality. After that, the decree’s contents will become effective, and the space-time waves will really kick up. Unfortunately... all of that won’t be enough.

Xu Qing sent his divine will to the poisoned blood in his hand. Other than Li Mengtu’s Master, there was only one person who could possibly understand his poison canon. And that person was Xu Qing. At the moment, he was focusing his powers of understanding on the poisoned blood, hoping to use the body of his host to augment it and... make it stronger.

Before long, he arrived at Scourgebolt Palace, and Gongsun Qingmu’s residence.

Inside was Sir Vilespirit in the form of Gongsun Qingmu. Opening his eyes, he looked in surprise at the entrance. He could sense who was there. He had been ready for someone to come looking for him, and was very confident in being able to deal with whoever it was. But how could he have ever guessed that the person to come... would be Young Lord Aurora?? Just like everyone else, he was shaken to the core.

The storm raged, and as red light shone everywhere, thunder boomed.

Xu Qing did not show any trace of politeness as he stepped forward. The door exploded, and as the wind and rain entered, so did he.

Looking down, he said, “Your dao is that of betrayal. But that’s not going to work on me.”

1. Just a quick reminder that the Mengtu from Li Mengtu’s name contains the characters for “dream” and “earth/soil.” So if you translated the name of the poison, it would be Poison of Dreaming of Earth/Soil. In all likelihood, someone who didn’t know the background of the name of the poison would think of it in that way. But all of the ‘outsiders,’ who of course are familiar with Li Mengtu, would instantly associate it with his name. And I think the meaning, in this case, is related to him as a person, rather than the implication of his name. So in this case, I’m choosing to render the poison name with his name instead of the translation of the meaning. ☜

2. The term here is a fairly unique term. The characters are the same as the ability used by Meng Hao in ISSTH, but it’s not intended to relate to that character or novel. The term does not exist in dictionaries, and interestingly, when you search for it on the Chinese internet, the top results are all explanations of how it works in cultivation novels. Essentially, it’s a magical way of authenticating something as being official. ☜

Sir Vilespirit had no choice but to take the fluctuations very seriously. He looked up at the young lord. He had not predicted this outcome. There were many people he assumed might come to him this night, but he hadn’t even considered the possibility that it would be Young Lord Aurora, who, up to this point, had not acted strangely in any way. What was more, the young lord’s words struck him to the core like a sharp blade.

Simultaneously, the seeming fact that Young Lord Aurora was an outsider was causing a tempest of astonishment to rage inside Sir Vilespirit.

But Xu Qing wasn’t done adding on pressure. Dropping down into a squat, he stared Sir Vilespirit in the eyes.

Given that time frame... don’t you think I can make sure that all of your betrayals fail, whether they be in the past, present, or future?”

As Xu Qing’s words hammered into Sir Vilespirit, the dangerous look in his eyes grew stronger. Eventually, the air behind him started to ripple and blur as a terrifying iron sword took shape. At the same time, an explosive sword will surged.

Xu Qing’s expression remained completely calm. He hardly seemed to notice Sir Vilespirit’s aura change as he seemed to prepare to take action. However, he did look over at the broken sword.
