Remember, I could issue orders to have you locked up all the way until the wedding and the catastrophe. To put it bluntly, the only way your betrayal will work is if I permit it to.”

Sir Vilespirit sat there scowling and not saying a word. The pressure on him just continued to build, until finally he spoke. “Young Lord, surely you didn’t come here just to say all that.”

As thunder rumbled, Xu Qing reached out toward the broken sword behind Sir Vilespirit.

Sir Vilespirit hesitated briefly about what to do, but in the end, chose not to stop him.

Xu Qing made a grasping motion, and the sword flew over to him. He gripped the blade with his thumb and forefinger. After examining it, he spoke through the sound of the thunder from outside.

“What if your sword was stained with my blood, and I said you had tried to assassinate me...? Could there be any more ultimate betrayal here other than killing the Immortal Lord himself? The betrayal of assassinating the young lord would definitely be very beneficial to you.”

Xu Qing ran his finger along the edge of the blade, causing a drop of blood to fall onto the sword. The sword vibrated excitedly. The space-time waves in the area immediately grew more intense.

Of course, there was no true success yet. However, Sir Vilespirit’s heart was already racing. He could sense that if a betrayal of this level succeeded, it would be immensely helpful to him. Struggling to control his breathing, he looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing looked back at him coldly. “That was how I had planned to help you succeed at your betrayal, and survive the process. But sadly for you, you made a mistake.”

Sir Vilespirit didn’t respond. He knew exactly what mistake he had made. He had mistakenly revoked the fox maiden’s status as an apprentice. Unfortunately, he knew there was nothing he could do now. How could he ever have guessed that someone would take an identity that should have been impossible to take?

As of now, he knew that regardless of who this outsider was, Sir Star Ring... had almost no chance of coming out on top. Without any hesitation, he rose to his feet and bowed deeply to Xu Qing.

“How can I make up for this, Young Lord?”

Xu Qing tossed him the bottle with Li Mengtu’s poisoned blood in it. Then he took out a jade slip of decree and imprinted it with divine will.

“Gongsun Qingmu of the Scourgebolt Palace conspired with outside enemies to betray the immortal palace and assassinate me, the young lord. Thanks to the safeguard of the poison created personally by Zhong Chi, Gongsun Qingmu’s assassination attempt failed, and he was poisoned to death!

“Given how many years Gongsun Qingmu prepared, it’s no surprise he has a clone outside of the immortal palace. Therefore, notices will be put up throughout the Fifth Star Ring naming Gongsun Qingmu... wanted dead or alive!”

After that, he sent the blood-stained sword back, then left without casting another glance at Sir Vilespirit. As for Sir Vilespirit... he had no choice about what to do next. He sighed, and with a bitter expression, opened the bottle and drank the poison.

He had no other options. If he didn’t cooperate, there were simply too many ways for the young lord to force him to fail. It didn’t matter if Fourth True Monarch had declared his apprentice’s actions to be a betrayal. If the young lord wanted to... he could overturn the entire game board.

Sir Vilespirit was not really in a position to fight back. And that meant he had only one path going forward. As the poison spread through him, Sir Vilespirit trembled, and his skin gradually turned black. That poison was Li Mengtu’s canon, and had been augmented by Xu Qing, making it astounding. Sir Vilespirit could do nothing to save himself from it.

As Xu Qing disappeared into the storm, lightning flashed, illuminating the hall and revealing that Sir Vilespirit was seated cross-legged, with his head drooping down onto his chest. He was dead! His dao was gone, and his mind perished. Sir Vilespirit’s consciousness had been driven out of the fourth world!

As Xu Qing had said, he could stay behind if he wanted, but had picked the wrong path. Thus, his only true choice had been to ingest the poison. The moment he died... two huge space-time waves surged through the immortal palace!

The first came because Gongsun Qingmu’s assassination betrayal had a foundation and was settled conclusively. That situation caused a huge wave. The other came from Zhong Chi. As of that moment, the decree Xu Qing had given to Zhong Chi became a closed loop! He had successfully safeguarded the young lord! The space-time tempest became like a vortex, or a blooming flower within the wind and rain.

As it spun, Xu Qing continued on his way. His next destination was... the sword furnace where Hordeslayer and Rampart were! That was his last place to visit that night.

As he neared, the space-time waves coming from everyone else grew stronger. Eventually, those coming from Li the Chosen grew incredibly dramatic!

Xu Qing turned and looked in that direction. Li the Chosen’s arm was just severed.

Large amounts of space-time sand began to form around Xu Qing, shining with dazzling light that almost made him seem illusory. Looking away from it, he continued on his way.

Step by step, he got closer to the sword furnace. Soon, he caught sight of it.

The sword furnace, located in the middle of a spell formation, was pitch black and emanated unspeakable might. There was more thunder here than anywhere else, as lightning bolts similar to heavenly tribulation fell constantly and hit the sword furnace. Every bolt of lightning sent sparks exploding out and showering down. Even from a distance, it was a majestic and mysterious sight.

The constantly showering sparks were sucked in by the spell formation and turned into a sea of electricity. Aggressive sword energy was building up in the sword furnace, and it seemed just on the verge of erupting out!

“You two have a much simpler hiding spot than everyone else,” Xu Qing said coolly. “You possessed sword embryos. If it weren’t for the increase in waves recently, I wouldn’t have been able to find you very easily. Most interesting of all is that the two of you are taking advantage of your situation to emerge early.”

When Hordeslayer and Rampart heard his words, they trembled in shock. But then Xu Qing spoke again.

“Well, that’s fine. It will just make it easier to realize who’s in charge!” The moment the words ‘who’s in charge’ were spoken, lightning crashed off in the distance.

Amidst the silver lightning bolts was Sir Star Ring, who shot toward the sword furnace in a beam of prismatic light as Fourth True Monarch, his expression grim and his killing intent raging.

Lightning and thunder went wild as Sir Star Ring shot through the air in the form of Fourth True Monarch. He pierced through heaven and earth like a spear, moving with mountain-toppling, sea-draining momentum....

Nothing could block his path! Amidst intense rumbling sounds, he smashed through the outer wall of the building that contained the sword furnace. As the rubble rained down and rain fell... he landed right next to the furnace! He was standing right in front of Xu Qing! His incredible momentum caused a virtual tempest to whip up around him.

Xu Qing’s garments flapped, and his hair whipped about. But he stood as firm as a mountain, not taking even a single step backward.

His expression remained the same as ever as he looked coolly at Sir Star Ring. “You seem to be in a good mood tonight, Elder Brother Fourth.”

“As I expected, it’s you!” replied Sir Star Ring, a complicated look in his eyes.

Endless bolts of lightning flowed across his entire body, eventually streaming down his legs to spread out into the surroundings. As for his eyes... when they locked onto Xu Qing, all traces of doubt within him were wiped out. As his thoughts went wild, his expression became incomparably grim, and massive killing intent built up within him.

“It’s truly a surprise you hid yourself so well...” he said, taking a step toward Xu Qing. “You were the one who spread those rumors! I set up the situation with Sir Vilespirit to try to draw you out, but you sent the fox maiden in your stead.”

He took another step forward. “I arranged for Yuanshan Su to interfere, but thanks to your alliance with Sir Vilespirit, you got her a new status, and my efforts to drive her away failed. After I blew everyone’s cover, you made sure Sir Vilespirit’s betrayal worked. Then... you cowed Yuanshan Su, helped Li Mengtu succeed, got Sir Vilespirit to kill himself, and sent Li the Chosen to block my path.

“I have to admit that you’re very, very clever! You have an identity that makes you impervious to everyone. And that indicates that I have no way of winning this war. After all, if I make a move here... it will cause waves! I suppose that was a factor in your plans.”

Sir Star Ring took a third step forward. He was fully aware that because of the identities held by himself and his opponent, there was no historical basis for them to fight. If he started a fight, it would cause the very waves he was trying to prevent. And protracted fighting would lead to injuries that would make the waves even bigger.

“But... I still have an option other than losing!” When he took his fourth step, his energy surged. Thunderous rumblings surrounded him as a terrifying aura erupted from him. Eyes burning with killing intent, he shot toward Xu Qing!

His way of not losing was to drive Xu Qing’s consciousness out! If he did that, then even though he would fail to maintain order, at least he could get rid of his opponent, and thus, not lose to him. Afterward, there was always the possibility he could smooth everything out! After all, the wedding day was the most important event of this fourth world space-time!

As his voice rang out and his energy surged, he shot forward, all while tens of thousands of chains made of canon swept out around him. They filled heaven and earth with dazzling light, causing the dark sky over the sword furnace to turn as bright as day. It even outshone the lightning, causing everything to dim in relation to the pure order.

And yet, there was more. A host of spell formations rumbled into being behind Sir Star Ring. There were nine layers, each layer complex and majestic, and all of them shining with a different color of light.

There were a total of seven colors, plus black and white. Nine colors. Nine formations. As they spun, they emanated a terrifying pressure that could shake heaven and earth. That force, along with the tens of thousands of chains, and Fourth True Monarch’s strength, was all closing in directly on Xu Qing. When Sir Star Ring attacked... he didn’t hold anything back!

Inside the sword furnace, Hordeslayer and Rampart, who were still reeling from Xu Qing’s words, could sense the dramatic events outside.

“It doesn’t matter if Young Lord Aurora is an outsider like us....”

“Right now, this is the best opportunity we could have!”

“We should take advantage of their fighting to try to form the immortal swords!”

“Whatever happens here beyond that has nothing to do with us. Even if they destroy space-time and throw everything into chaos, it won’t have any karmic connection to us!”

“We’re going to get our fourth world good fortune without any hitch at all!”

Hordeslayer and Rampart took advantage of the moment, holding back none of their strength as they tried to catalyze the immortal swords into being as quickly as possible. In the blink of an eye, sword energy raged within the furnace. The immortal swords were about to come into the world!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he saw what was happening to the sword furnace. He knew instantly that they were taking advantage of his fight with Sir Star Ring to form the swords early and avoid karma.

He also knew that if this was happening in the real world, there was no way he could fight Sir Star Ring. Sir Star Ring was number one among the Shining Stars, and had gained enlightenment of his own mighty and mysterious canon. What was more, he was at the absolute peak of Imperial Sovereign, and was half a step into the Grand Emperor level. He had even defeated an actual Grand Emperor in combat....

But this was the fourth world. The body of Xu Qing’s host could make up for the weakness of his actual cultivation base. And even if Sir Star Ring took advantage of Fourth True Monarch’s body to unleash power superior to his own, the reality was that the space-time waves in the fourth world were a weapon for Xu Qing. The fourth world was really the best battlefield for him at the moment. What was more... his host’s status could also be used as a weapon.

Therefore, Xu Qing waved his hand, and an invisible space-time tempest immediately rumbled out explosively.

As a result, the incoming chains started to blur.

Then Xu Qing waved his hand again, and space-time sand floated out, surrounding him and causing him to fuse into space-time. He immediately became blurry.

“You set things up ingeniously. But you’re still lacking because... you’re too weak!” Sir Star Ring kept his eyes on Xu Qing as he pointed a finger up into the sky.

Instantly, the nine-layered spell formation began to spin rapidly, becoming a vortex out of which spewed an ancient aura. Next, a green stone stele began to emerge from the vortex, and the sensation of ancient time grew vastly more intense.

Unreadable text and magical symbols flowed across the surface of the stone stele, making it look infinitely mysterious. The chains of orders began to vibrate, all while explosively unleashing the power of order. Apparently, this stone stele was one of the origins of order!

Sir Star Ring had summoned it to be the heart of the spell formation. Then he pushed his hand in Xu Qing’s direction.

“Be expelled by order!”

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Winds screamed. The green stone stele rumbled loudly. And as the vortex of the formation spun, the mightiness of the aura raged out, along with an expelling will that crushed down on Xu Qing. It looked like the space-time waves were about to disperse.

Not even Xu Qing, fused as he was with space-time, could hide himself from them. He was on the verge of being totally crushed. Then Xu Qing looked up.

“Elder Brother Fourth, just you coming here was too much.... You’ve already entered into my chaotic sea of space-time.”

As the words left his mouth, he gently waved his hand. The sand of time in the area was swept about, causing the sand to disperse through heaven and earth. The friction of the sand rubbing against itself and floating about caused one timeline after another to appear. They were timelines of chaos.

It wasn’t just about time flowing faster, being reversed, or stopping. There was something more profound going on. It was like a formless river that was everywhere at the same time. And yet it wasn’t set rigidly in one place. The power of the outside world, or alterations, could bring about different transformations.

A good example was the Desert of Time, which was the manifestation of the life essence treasure of Immortal Lord Aurora’s wife. What it revealed was subsidiary branches of time.

“Any who enters my chaotic sea will sustain the effects of time,” Xu Qing said, his eyes turning cold. “Your every movement will create chaotic timelines. You will be hit by countless timelines, causing you to either die or go insane! Enter the sea and find bitterness. Experience tribulation. Time comes to cease. It is... Infinite Timelessness!”[1]

As his voice echoed out, all of the chains present, all of the symbols in the spell formation, the green stone stele, and Fourth True Monarch’s body... were hit by the spreading space-time sand, whereupon countless timelines appeared. All were wrapped up. And then, the chains, the spell formation, the stone stele, and Fourth True Monarch began to ripple, distort, and blur.

The chaotic sea of space-time erupted. Chaos was being used to counter order!

Sir Star Ring looked at the countless timelines covering him within the sea of chaos, and his eyes sharpened.

“So this is how you’re breaking order.... If this was happening in real life, it would cause me some trouble. But do you know why I chose to possess Fourth True Monarch?”

Sir Star Ring lifted his foot, and when he stepped forward, ripples flowed across the sea of space-time chaos. But when ripples appeared on a sea of chaos, those ripples represented order!

“It’s because Fourth True Monarch was the original founder of the Star Ring Pagoda! Though he perished in the catastrophe that befell the immortal place, the Order Pagoda was built outside of the palace. It continued on after that, until it was eventually renamed the Star Ring Pagoda!

“I inherited the name Star Ring, and I gained enlightenment of order. Therefore... I am completely in unison with Fourth True Monarch here, and I can unleash Fourth True Monarch’s essence of order!”

Sir Star Ring’s eyes suddenly shone as if with starlight. Astonishingly, his eyes seemed to contain twin seas of stars! Each sea of stars contained millions upon millions of heavenly bodies, and all of them were shining brightly and arranged in a specific sequence....

Then a majestic voice echoed in heaven and earth.

“Order is another word for rules. Without rules, nothing can be accomplished. But the word ‘rules’ is made from two characters. The first is the character for the compass. The second is the character for the carpenter’s square.

“As they say, you can lay the square down to measure a piece of rope, or stand it upright to measure height. Invert the square and you can measure depths, or place it vertically to measure distance. Bend it to measure something circular, flatten it to measure something flat.”[2]

As the words were spoken, they formed a dao resonance. At the same time, the sea of stars in Sir Star Ring’s left eye rearranged themselves into the shape of a carpenter’s square! Within his right eye, the stars took the shape of a measuring compass!

This was... using the square to set life and death, while using the compass to depict reincarnation!

1. This dialogue is almost exactly the same as what was said in chapter 1117. ☜

2. The saying “without rules, nothing can be accomplished” is from the Mencius. Because it’s a famous saying from real life, I want to keep the common translation. But there is some significant wordplay to address. Much of it I conveyed by spelling things out more overtly than in Chinese. But some elements require additional explanation. The second part of the saying from the Mencius, which is generally rendered as “nothing can be accomplished,” is more literally “cannot form the fangyuan.” Fangyuan is made from two characters. One character means, among other things, “flat/square” while the other means “circular.” This combination of characters can mean different things, among them: circumference, neighborhood, surrounding area, radius, general area, etc. Add to that the fact that the square and circle have implications in Chinese mythology (specifically, I'm talking about the square from fangyuan, not the square from “carpenter's square,” which is a different character altogether). This was something that caused a lot of trouble for me when I first started translating xianxia. Long story short, the square represents earth and the circle represents heaven. Given that, it kind of makes sense to think of the square and circle as representing “everything/anything,” as the combination essentially represents heaven and earth, in other words, everything. Readers of ISSTH might remember a scene very early in the novel when there was a section about the square and circle motif being inverted, which was said to be an inversion of the natural order of things. So this entire passage, and by extension the ability, has multiple levels of wordplay and meaning. I wouldn’t be surprised if there are some elements that didn’t occur to me about the symbology and whatnot. But at least now you get a general feeling for it. In the next chapter, the square and circle aspect will become important. ☜

As of this moment, Sir Star Ring was revealing the true nature of Fourth True Monarch’s power. Similar to the situation with the thirteen coffins, he couldn’t manipulate them perfectly. But on a fundamental level, and in terms of personhood, they were a dramatically awesome force.

A sound rang out that surpassed any sounds of nature. It was greater than any dao resonance, as if it represented the order of the universe and the rules of the starry sky. The moment it happened, the carpenter’s square made of millions upon millions of stars in his left eye became manifest externally, revealing the power of order!

It was laid down to form the boundary of the world. It stood upright to outline the upper limit. It was inverted to determine the depth of the world. It was placed vertically to establish distance! Gradually, all of that converged into a square around Xu Qing. It became... a square world around Xu Qing.[1]

Within that independent world, chains began to flow, almost as if it were a prison isolated from the outside world. Xu Qing was being cut off from the local space-time! And that would leave him without a foundation! This was the way to vanquish his sea of chaos!

A very serious expression appeared in Xu Qing’s eyes as he realized that he couldn’t block this manifestation of order. Within this world, his consciousness was like a mortal being suffocated. It felt very uncomfortable.

That was because as he was separated from the space-time of the fourth world, he lost the augmentation of space-time, and he was losing the foundation he needed to keep his consciousness inside of Young Lord Aurora. All of a sudden, images appeared around him. They were blurry versions of himself, and they represented his consciousness, which had come and fused into Young Lord Aurora. But now... he was being separated, and so was his consciousness.

And yet, things weren’t over yet. Next, the circular compass in Sir Star Ring’s right eye manifested outside, and began to draw a circle around Xu Qing!

When the circle appeared, rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth, and great daos trembled. Within that circle was an infinitude of circles, layer upon layer all with a beginning but no end, creating life and death. This was reincarnation!

All of the circles were spinning at different rates, creating a terrifying gravitational force! It weighed down on Xu Qing, and combined with the previous force of expulsion to make it even stronger. It was going to fully drive Xu Qing’s consciousness out of the body of Young Lord Aurora, and expel it from this space-time.

Inside, Xu Qing sighed regretfully. In this version of history, Fourth True Monarch was truly a formidable person with great potential. He knew that he was no match for this. Yet he wasn’t flustered; from the moment he had decided to fight Sir Star Ring, he had begun preparing thoroughly.

As the images around him began to disperse, he reached up and rubbed his lips. That caused thunder to rumble. Countless lightning bolts converged, and cracking sounds rang out as they turned into the hand of an old man. When that hand appeared, everything in existence went still.

Next, the fingers of the hand formed an incantation sign. The sign created a resonance with heaven and earth. Everything trembled as the natural and magical laws of the world were affected, including all order and rules.

This was Young Lord Aurora’s canon... Three-Karmas Ten-Evils Seal! Black karma fire erupted all over Xu Qing, then spread out in all directions. The fire was so intense it could burn anything it touched, and in the blink of an eye, the world that was separating him from everything else turned into a sea of flames. Then it swept back inside of Xu Qing, filling him and turning into a sealing mark!

When the mouth could not speak, when the karma of the mouth was pure, when the body was at peace, when one was fully without concern, ten thousand thoughts could flourish! Sealing one’s own mouth would seal one away from death! This was sealing the karma of the mouth![2]

This sealing was resisting the force of expulsion! The world trembled as black karma fire covered Xu Qing. Then he looked up at Sir Star Ring, his eyes glittering. The hand of lightning went into a different incantation sign. Thunder rumbled.

As was said, the body could not tread a vile path, could not harm life, could not kill, steal, or be obscene. The karma of the body was absolutely pure. When the body was pure, nothing in existence could defile it. No wickedness could stain it. This was the second of the three karmas. The karma of body sealing!

When the body does not move, and was not within karma, it could not be expelled. It was as if it didn’t exist, and thus there was nothing to expel. This karma supported reincarnation!

Xu Qing stood there like a reef amidst crashing waves. No matter how the wind and rain raged, he stood tall. How could his reincarnation be expelled?

The square world trembled. The circle of reincarnation shook. The sound of it spread in all directions.

Seeing this, Sir Star Ring’s heart filled with determination. He knew that this fight was going to be his last chance. Eyes glittering, he extended the index and middle fingers of his right hand and pushed them against his eyes, one on each eye! The eyes turned crimson, as if the seas of stars within them had become soaked in blood. Within the blood-red seas of stars, the power of order emanated a blood-red glow that turned into punishment that rumbled toward Xu Qing.

“Punishment!”

The square world and circle of reincarnation were bolstered by the power. Blood-red light raged, causing the force of expulsion to start working even more dramatically.

Xu Qing shivered from head to toe, and felt more clearly than ever that he was being expelled. In fact, he felt like he was almost completely separated from Young Lord Aurora’s fleshly body. Above that body appeared... a projection of his true image.

“As I expected, it’s you!” When Sir Star Ring saw the true manifestation of Xu Qing’s consciousness, his killing intent raged. Holding nothing back, he went all out to expel him from the world.

But then, the projection of Xu Qing, as well as Young Lord Aurora’s fleshy body, raised their hands. And up above, the hand of lightning went into another sign.

It was the third of the three karmas from Three-Karmas Ten-Evils Seal. It was... sealing the karma of will!

Thoughts and actions could be both righteous or evil. The good would be kept, and the evil would be expelled! Good karma could include refraining from greed, anger, or unorthodox opinions. It could bless the body, become boundless benevolence, and illuminate anything and everything with great auspiciousness. Bad karma could include embracing greed, anger, or unorthodox opinions. It could lead one to worship false deities, make one as dark as a wretched devil, take away light, and bring misfortune.

This seal did not lock down the body or bind the mouth. It put fetters on canon! You could say that the first two karmas affected oneself, while the third karma would be directed at the enemy!

As it appeared, it bound order and restricted rules. What was more, it completely enveloped Sir Star Ring.

Afterimages sprang up around him as the projected image of his consciousness was locked onto by evil karma. Clearly... the sealing of the karma of will was driving his consciousness out of his body! Both of them were trying to expel each other!

The projected consciousnesses of Sir Star Ring and Xu Qing were visible above the heads of Fourth True Monarch and Young Lord Aurora. Xu Qing faced the pressure of reincarnation and the square world. Sir Star Ring was being burned by karma fire, and his evil karma could not be tolerated by heaven and earth, and thus, he was being expelled. They were both fighting back viciously against the other!

This was a clash of canon. It was a clash between Fourth True Monarch and Young Lord Aurora. It was a clash of order versus eternity. And most of all, it was a fight between Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring!

As the clash went on, the expelling force from the square world began to weaken. The driving away caused by the circle of reincarnation slowed down. But they did not disappear. They could be slowed, but similar to how a torrential downpour could be blocked temporarily, they could not be reversed.

As Sir Star Ring saw that, and as the karma fire burned around him, he fought back against the force of expulsion to raise his hand. At the same time, his eyes shone with determination. He would pay whatever price he had to in order to drive the consciousness of his enemy away.

Xu Qing’s eyes shone brightly as he prepared to take out the marriage contract.... That was his ultimate trump card in this fight; if utilized at the right time, it could completely reverse the situation.

But just as Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring were both about to go all out to defeat each other... the sword furnace down below began to rumble loudly!

An aggressive will, like none other in the world, erupted from inside the sword furnace! It was a sign the immortal swords were about to come out into the world.

Hordeslayer and Rampart had fused their consciousnesses with the sword embryos, and had previously intended to let the process go along naturally and come out into the world on the wedding day. But given how things were progressing, they suddenly felt a lot of pressure. That was especially true considering that Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring were fighting right in front of them. That... got them very nervous.

Therefore, they had done everything in their power, even if it meant changing history and causing waves, to come out into the world that very night. It meant coming out early, and that could result in complexities with the others. But they didn’t care.

It didn’t matter to them if Sir Star Ring won or lost. And they couldn’t care less if Xu Qing lived or died. Even if the two of them bashed each other’s brains out at the same time, or if space-time got turned completely upside-down. It would have nothing to do with Hordeslayer and Rampart. All they cared about were their own goals!

As of this moment, the space-time waves got even more intense. For the immortal swords to come out into the world now... was a significant change to history! freewebnovel.com

Sir Star Ring’s expression flickered. He chose this location with the express purpose of forcing them to do this!

Unfortunately, he was locked in such close combat with Xu Qing that he couldn’t interfere.

The sky dimmed as countless lightning bolts shot toward the sword furnace. One after another, they slammed down onto the furnace. All of a sudden, sword light erupted from inside, creating a multicolored beam that shot high into the sky.

Within that beam of light... emerged two immortal swords that were both black and white in color! The immortal swords had come out into the world! The lightning then turned black and white as it encircled the two swords. A thrumming sound echoed out, reaching deafening proportions, and a sword might weighed down, so immense it seemed it could shatter heaven and earth.

From within all that came the excited laughter of Hordeslayer and Rampart.

“Sir Star Ring, and you, the unknown, detestable cultivator, we brothers must thank you. If it weren’t for your little game and the stimulus it provided, we wouldn’t have been as confident in gaining enlightenment.”

“In fact, our enlightenment might have failed. But thanks to the help from you two, we not only came into the world early, but also, we gained deeper enlightenment!”

“And now, our canon has become even more impressive!”

Laughter rang out from the two immortal swords. Hordeslayer and Rampart were clearly very excited, and they were about to send their consciousnesses back to the outside world. But before they left, they had more to say.

“Have fun playing around, kids. Grandpa isn’t gonna stick around! If the two of you have the chance, come to the north and see how outstanding we are in real life. After all, you performed a real service to us here!”

“That’s especially true of you, you unknown, detestable, shameless, unreasonable idiot who possessed the young lord. I can’t believe you dared try to tell us what to do! Keep on dreaming, why don’t you?”

Xu Qing looked at the two immortal swords, and he heard the words being directed at him. His eyes narrowed.

The next instant... a pure white jade slip flew out from his host! It was the very same betrothal gift that Immortal Lord Aurora had given to Immortal Lord Nineshores. It was blank, but could be imprinted with divine will to allow any item from the immortal palace to transfer ownership to the bearer!

On that occasion days earlier, Nineshores had accepted the other betrothal gifts, but had not taken the jade slip that allowed the user to take any treasure from the immortal palace. He had given that to Xu Qing. All in all, he was giving away his daughter’s hand in marriage, and given his personality, was not the type of person to covet the belongings of a family friend.[1]

That jade slip was now a trump card for Xu Qing to play in a key moment. Originally... Xu Qing had been ambivalent about the use of the jade slip.

And when he picked the sword furnace as the location to fight Sir Star Ring, he didn’t do it with the intention of forcing the two swords to be bonded to him. His original goal had been to ensure that the clash between order and chaos would put pressure on to the two swords in the furnace, and thus give Hordeslayer and Rampart no choice about what to do. They would be forced to take advantage of the moment to complete the swords ahead of schedule. They would be in a very passive position.

If Sir Star Ring won, then their future success would all be contingent on his approval. After all, suppression itself was an act of maintaining order. If the young lord won... then all he would have to do was order them to be bonded to him. That also gave Hordeslayer and Rampart a spectacular motivating force.

In the end, they really had no choice but to speed up. Only by putting everything on the line could they catalyze their sword bodies and come out into the world early. That was the only way to come out on top. It was their only chance at success. And that was what Xu Qing wanted. It was an overt plot.

According to his plan, as long as the two swords came out into the world early, it would result in space-time waves that would help him going forward. But... the words spoken by the two swords before their departure were overly excited.

Therefore, Xu Qing decided that forcing a bond would be a significant departure from history. And that would be great for him. Even as the excited words echoed out, and the consciousnesses within them stirred in preparation to leave the fourth world....

Xu Qing took out the blank jade slip and threw it up into the air. It rose above him. Dazzling, endless light shone out.

Xu Qing sent out his divine will at the exact moment that the consciousnesses of Hordeslayer and Rampart were about to leave... and he branded them into the jade slip.

“A pair of immortal swords have come into the world today. I hereby assign them names. One is Hordeslayer. The other is Rampart... and they will be my personal swords!”

As his divine will spread out, rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth. It was like the resonance of a great dao as magical law stirred, and a binding order formed.

It could be called a fatal blow. Not only did it determine who the swords belonged to, but it also gave them names.... Those names, Hordeslayer and Rampart, instantly created an extremely strong bond of karma! Because of that karma, the pair of black-and-white immortal swords vibrated as countless immortal symbols appeared on their surface.

They had been created in the immortal palace, and had been born out of the immortal palace’s sword furnace. In every respect imaginable, the pair of swords were utterly and thoroughly objects of the immortal palace.

Then, the immortal symbols from the jade slip responded to Xu Qing and formed an extremely tight bond. It could not be resisted, could not be blocked, and could not be rejected! Inside of them, Hordeslayer and Rampart, who were just like spirit automatons now, had no time to react. They had been overwhelmed with excitement, and hadn’t even considered that Xu Qing would do something like he did.

The moment Xu Qing branded the swords with the immortal symbols, the two swords shivered, and Hordeslayer and Rampart were struck numb with shock. An instant later, an incredibly majestic force surged out of the immortal palace, pouring into the immortal swords and into their consciousnesses....

Massive waves rose up within their divine will. They were undergoing a righteous bestowal that was turning them into spirit automatons and bonding them to an owner.

As of this moment... they were truly spirit automatons. The sealing marks which would force spirit automatons to acknowledge their master... had appeared on them.

And because Xu Qing had given them names... the karma in the sealing marks wouldn’t just affect this specific instance of space-time. It was highly likely... that they would apply in the outside world as well!

The astonishment within Hordeslayer and Rampart surpassed all imagination. They felt like their minds were being ravaged by countless bolts of heavenly lightning. It was just like the saying great joy begets sorrow.

“Th-this... this....”

“But this... I...”

Their effort to leave the fourth world had been interrupted. Karma bound them. They had to acknowledge they were owned by someone else. And they had been officially named.... It became a binding force that they couldn’t fight against. Their consciousness absolutely could not leave now!

As they reeled to the core, Xu Qing lifted his left hand. He beckoned at them.

“Come here.”

The two black-and-white immortal swords vibrated and issued a thrumming call.... And then, as Hordeslayer and Rampart felt madness overwhelming them, the swords they had possessed, turned around and soared gracefully toward Xu Qing!

They had no choice but to obey. Their consciousnesses wished to weep and rave. But they couldn’t. Deep inside, they realized that, as the swords’ excitement built, so did their own. It was beyond their control.

Meanwhile, because the immortal swords came into the world early, and because Xu Qing had bound them and forced them to acknowledge him, the space-time waves grew even more intense!

Combined with everything that happened up to this point, the waves surged like heaven-shaking, earth-shattering tsunamis! In fact, it was totally correct to say that the space-time waves had reached tsunami level!

Waves came because of Li the Chosen, Gongsun Qingmu, the fox maiden, Zhong Chi, and then the two swords.... A raging tsunami hit the viscous surface of the space-time lake, causing the water to spin and seethe.

Xu Qing’s consciousness was already back inside his host’s body, and he was standing atop the tsunami! He could clearly sense that order had been crushed!

He waved his hand, and the two swords shot toward him and then started orbiting around him. It didn’t matter how Hordeslayer and Rampart struggled. Their madness did nothing to change the situation. They had to respond to Xu Qing’s divine will, unleashing the power of the swords to form a fierce and consummate sword energy that slashed at the reincarnation and the world square!

Rumbling echoed out in shocking fashion. The world square crumbled. The circle of reincarnation fell to pieces! Order shattered loudly.

Sir Star Ring shivered from head to toe, and two streams of blood seeped out of his eyes. The seas of millions upon millions of stars in his eyes collapsed. The compass and the carpenter’s square became nothing but dust. Most important of all was that his canon was shaken violently.

The two swords’ intense momentum continued. After destroying the world square and circle of reincarnation, they shot into the sky, becoming an intersection of black and white as they headed directly toward Sir Star Ring.

Killing intent raged.

Inside the swords, Hordeslayer and Rampart could do nothing but ignore their bitterness and madness, and throw caution to the wind as they pushed the swords to the limit of their strength. After all, they were also furious with Sir Star Ring.

Sir Star Ring’s face fell, and he fell back at top speed. Thousands and thousands of thoughts ran through his mind, and all of them were full of rage toward Xu Qing. As those thoughts combined, Sir Star Ring took a deep breath and suddenly lifted his right hand. Extending his index finger, he pushed down on his forehead.

When he pulled his finger away, a dazzling chain of gold emerged from his forehead. He swept it out in front of him. The chain wasn’t very long, as it was only made from 99 links. It was one short of 100. Every single link in the chain was covered with densely packed magical symbols, each of which represented order.

The moment it appeared, the power of order became incredibly clear, and it formed a strong resonance with Sir Star Ring’s consciousness. That was because the golden chain was not something that belonged to Fourth True Monarch. It... was the foundation of Sir Star Ring’s canon!

Once the chain acquired its 100th ring, he would break out of the Imperial Sovereign level and become a Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor. That was why he was intent on maintaining order in the fourth world.

As of this moment, he was throwing caution to the wind. As he took out his own canon, thirteen coffins manifested around him. The coffins were different sizes and made of different materials, but all of them emanated a strong aura of order. The moment they appeared, brightly colored light flashed in heaven and earth. The coffins contained corpses of canon, which were all that remained of the rivals Fourth True Monarch had killed.

Originally, Sir Star Ring had only been strong enough to use three of the coffins. But he knew that three coffins wouldn’t be enough to do anything to the immortal swords, much less Xu Qing on his tsunami of space-time. Therefore, he catalyzed his canon, forcing it to a higher level in the hopes of turning everything around at this key moment! He quickly performed an incantation gesture, his face distorting as the golden chain glittered, wrapped around the thirteen coffins, and sent golden light flooding into them.

Instantly, the thirteen coffins started shaking. Their lids did not open, but thunderous banging sounds started echoing out from inside of them. Sounds of thumping and pounding filled the air. At the same time, thirteen voices echoed out, grimly crying out in voices that surpassed sounds of nature or dao reverberations!

“Order and judgment; bones of sycophants; dig down to the Yellow Springs; be executed immediately!”

It was a total of fifteen words, and they became a judgment of order, transforming into an ancient stone stele that rumbled toward Xu Qing atop the tsunami of space-time.

Xu Qing looked up, his expression calm, but his eyes gleaming with unprecedented ferocity.

“The space-time waves have become a tsunami,” he said calmly. “That should be enough to cover some of the words. And that... means this fight is about to end.”

All of a sudden, a golden plaque flew out from Xu Qing’s robe and hovered in front of him.

As soon as it appeared, heaven and earth went still. Space-time became calm. The waves stopped. Everything became peaceful. Auspicious signs and propitious blessings emerged from within.

The plaque was, of course, the marriage contract. Immortal Lord Aurora had personally created it, imbued it with his will, his consciousness, and his blessing. And it contained all of the well wishes he could give to his son. The words on the plaque had been penned directly by him. They represented his will!

Two families are now united in marriage by this covenant that never ends. From the moment this agreement is reached, the couple face a happy future of affinity. They are predestined to grow old together, and will be by each other’s side until the sea does wither up and stone rots. You will put your union above all else, and will have many prosperous and famous descendants.

Let this marriage agreement be for all eternity; it is beautiful like rosy leaves, forever inscribed here as the happy couple always abides by its romantic tidings.

And thus, the agreement is confirmed.

Xu Qing extended his hand, and the space-time power from the tsunami covered most of the words, causing them to blur away so that only sixteen words were left visible. Those sixteen words linked together to form a sentence.

This covenant ends, this predestined affinity. You wither up, like rotting leaves. Thus, it is confirmed.[2]

Xu Qing pointed at Sir Star Ring in the form of Fourth True Monarch! The sixteen words from the marriage contract shone with majestic light as the space-time tsunami surged. In the blink of an eye, the predestined affinity between Sir Star Ring and Fourth True Monarch was ended!

His consciousness suddenly withered up. It was like a rotting leaf!

Sir Star Ring’s face fell dramatically.

Sir Star Ring’s heart swelled with astonishment. He felt like an infinitude of lightning bolts were smashing into him, causing him to struggle to breathe.... He could clearly sense an unstoppable force slowly peeling his consciousness away from his host’s body. It was completely irreversible!

The so-called predestined affinity was the main reason why he had chosen Fourth True Monarch as his host. Right now, that foundation was collapsing! The unstoppable force was causing his consciousness to desiccate and rot. It even affected the surrounding world, like rotting leaves rapidly withering away.

At the same time, orders and natural laws alike fell into nothing. That included the golden chain that was the manifestation of Sir Star Ring’s canon. As Sir Star Ring’s consciousness withered, the chain... broke! Rings cracked apart, causing indescribable pain to Sir Star Ring’s consciousness.
