The words that had been spoken formed canon and materialized, but now they were sent spinning away until they didn’t exist. The might of an Immortal Lord surpassed all else in existence.

It wasn’t just Sir Star Ring who was flabbergasted. So were the two immortal swords. Hordeslayer and Rampart hovered in midair, trembling. The scene playing out in front of them surpassed anything they could have imagined possible. In fact, event after event on this day had surpassed anything they could conceive. Some mysterious person had acquired an identity that should have been impossible to acquire. In an inconceivable twist, they had been forced to be bonded to him.

And now... that marriage contract appeared! Contrary to expectation, the words written on the contract had been put to use.

As a result, Hordeslayer and Rampart were deeply, deeply shaken.

In this space-time, the marriage contract was above everything else in terms of position and significance. It was paramount! Contained within it were blessings from Immortal Lord Aurora to his son. Those blessings contained a will. The will permeated each word in the contract, making each word canon in this space-time. They were law! When canon flowed, order had to bow its head, and rules had to conform. Acting in contradiction would amount to acting in contradiction to the will of Immortal Lord Aurora.

In all of the immortal palace, there were only two people who could use such an item, and they were Aurora and his son. Therefore, the moment the marriage contract appeared, the conclusion of this event was set in stone and could not be changed.

The reason Xu Qing could cover some of the words on the contract in order to make it conform to his needs of the moment... was that written up on it was the name of the young lord who he had possessed! It went without saying that he qualified!

There was just one element he needed, and that element... was space-time waves. And the space-time waves needed to reach a certain level before they would be effective.

That was why Xu Qing had forced everyone to change history in order to reach their goals. All of that led to the dramatic changes to space-time that he needed. He needed the space-time waves to reach the level of a tsunami! By doing so, he would have the strength he needed to cover over some of the words on the marriage contract.

It might seem like a simple thing, but the reality was that, to make it happen required a host of complicated steps that all had to be accomplished properly. The level of difficulty was astonishing.

Thunder boomed in the sky. Sky-obfuscating, land-enshrouding mightiness weighed down on the location of the sword furnace. Looking up, it was possible to see a net of electric sparks connecting to the tsunami of space-time. A figure stood on the tsunami, hair flowing, energy surging, and a fierce gleam in his eyes, as if his gaze could pierce the depths of the world.

He was looking at Sir Star Ring in the form of Fourth True Monarch. The sixteen words on the marriage contract shone with dazzling, endless light.

The glow of it illuminated the twisted, distorted face of Fourth True Monarch. His entire body was emanating black smoke. The smoke swirled together into the form of Sir Star Ring, which immediately began to dissipate.

All defiance within him was meaningless. None of his struggling did a single thing.

The sixteen words on the marriage contract were unstoppable. Maybe he was the number one Shining Star on the outside, but that didn’t mean he could stop what was happening. All he could do... was wait to be expelled!

His predestined affinity with Fourth True Monarch had been severed. He had been filled with a power of withering that was immensely harmful. Previously, he had expelled other people. But now, he was being expelled.

The foundation of his canon had been broken. Not only had he failed to benefit from coming to the fourth world, but also, he had been seriously hurt.

As he was disappearing, he glared at Xu Qing with killing intent in his gaze.

“I admit that you beat me this time. But... our fight isn’t over. I’m going on to the fifth world, a place you can never go to, and there, I’ll become a Quasi-Immortal! And to repay you for blocking me from completing my canon... I’ll just wait until the immortal palace event is over. Then, when you don’t have the identity from this space-time, and are back outside, I’ll kill you in an instant!”

Then Sir Star Ring’s consciousness crumbled into ashes. He had been expelled from this space-time. In the game between order and chaos, order had been thoroughly defeated. There was no possibility for order to make a comeback.

Sir Star Ring’s final words had been full of deadly threats. But the stage had already been set, so Xu Qing wasn’t going to let deadly threats affect him.

By the time the immortal place event is over, I won’t have the same cultivation base I do now!

Xu Qing looked over at Fourth True Monarch’s body. Without Sir Star Ring’s consciousness in it, Fourth True Monarch was like a bubble that just popped and disappeared. A thoughtful expression appeared on Xu Qing’s face.

Now that order had been defeated, space-time was thrumming. It was like a wild horse that had been freed of any reins, or raging waters free of a dam. In an instant, the space-time waves surpassed anything from before. Massive amounts of space-time sand appeared out of nowhere, flying from all the living beings in the immortal palace and congregating around Xu Qing like rain.

This was a hundred times more than anything he had seen before! The scintillating grains of sand fell constantly, forming together until they made the shape of an hourglass! And it came to float right in front of Xu Qing![1]

The moment the hourglass formed, heaven and earth shook. The immortal palace trembled. The world rippled. Dazzling light shone out that could suppress all things. This was a precious treasure of space-time!

Xu Qing’s heart raced. By means of his own canon, he could sense that this hourglass would only work for fifteen minutes.[2]

Put precisely, it could transcend this space-time for fifteen minutes! He could use the hourglass whenever he wanted. It could be used in the past, or in any time. And whatever happened then would be permanent. Whatever happened... existed outside of time and beyond the timescape![3]

At the same time, the moment Xu Qing gained enlightenment of the hourglass, his personal canon advanced. Innumerable bits of enlightenment regarding time filled his consciousness, bolstered his canon, and nourished his laws. As a result, in a very short time, his canon advanced in a way that would normally take countless years. He instantly reached the peak of the eighth extreme!

As his canon advanced, Xu Qing’s aura, battle prowess, and cultivation base all rose dramatically. He was now on the very cusp of being a nine-world Smoldering God!

My reserve powers are more than sufficient. When I make that final advancement and reach the nine-world level, I will become an Imperial Sovereign! Not only will I be stronger than ordinary Imperial Sovereigns, but thanks to all of my accumulated knowledge and advanced preparation, the Imperial Sovereign level... will be nothing but a stepping stone! I’m just around the corner from being a Quasi-Immortal!

Xu Qing took a deep breath and looked off at the horizon. Because the workings of heaven were in chaos, the horizon was blurry. Yet it was just barely possible to see... the rising sun. It was daytime. Sunlight pierced the clouds, landing on the sword furnace as well as Xu Qing. He looked away from the horizon and at the sword furnace.

“Come out,” he said coolly.

Distortions appeared as a figure took shape. It was a young man clad in white. He didn’t seem very special, but his face was kindly, and he smiled in a very unthreatening manner as he bowed to Xu Qing.

“Well met, Young Lord. It is I, Zhou Zhengli. Whether in terms of strategy or actions, Young Lord, you were spectacular in this fight. It was like immortal might shocking the world. You are truly a dragon amongst men, sir!”

This young man was of course, Zhou Zhengli, who had been working with Sir Star Ring this entire time! His expression was calm and sincere, his smile rueful but admiring.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered coldly.

The moment Sir Star Ring’s consciousness had been expelled, Zhou Zhengli had arrived. Though he had remained hidden, his aura made it obvious that he was waiting for someone to notice him. Each and every one of the Shining Stars was an extraordinary individual. But during the entire fight between Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring, he had remained completely out of sight.

It would be easy to discount someone like that. Yet despite the fact that Sir Star Ring was gone... he was still here. That was suspicious.

Furthermore, as Xu Qing had dealt with Sir Vilespirit, and came to know how conniving he was, he had come to some conclusions about the person Sir Vilespirit considered his nemesis, Zhou Zhengli. Zhou Zhengli was a sneaky person, who liked to hide his true strength, his true thoughts, and of course... his true goals!

“You aren’t actually trying to maintain order, are you?” Xu Qing said. “I suppose I owe you some thanks for how things ended with Sir Star Ring.”

If Sir Star Ring had been around to hear such words, he would have been shaken to the core.

Xu Qing sounded very certain of his conclusion. If Zhou Zhengli had also been devoted to order, then Sir Star Ring’s departure wouldn’t have resulted in such monumental space-time waves. But Sir Star Ring’s departure had felt like a complete and utter defeat. There was only one explanation.

“Brilliant, Young Lord,” Zhou Zhengli said in a soft, obsequious voice. “I have no intention of being an enemy of you, sir, neither here nor in the outside world. The fact you acquired a seemingly impossible identity indicates that you... are no ordinary individual. You’re obviously someone I want to get along with, sir.

“Sir Star Ring is obstinate and self-opinionated. To be honest, I couldn’t do much other than nudge him a bit in one direction or another. That was my goal. The moment I realized that Young Lord Aurora was not who he should be, my goal... was to make friends with you.

“The truth is that it doesn’t matter to me which side I’m on in the fourth world. I could try to maintain order, I could stay neutral, or I could try to make waves. That is my canon. My dao.” With that, Zhou Zhengli bowed his head in a very obsequious way.

Eyes glittering, Xu Qing said, “You certainly went into a lot of detail just now.”

Zhou Zhengli didn’t seem ruffled. Maintaining his bow, he said, “I want to make friends with you, and I want to stay in the fourth world. If you don’t understand me thoroughly, then I doubt you’d agree to be friends, and you certainly wouldn’t let me stick around.”

1. For the sand to make an hourglass shape makes more sense in Chinese, as the word for hourglass in Chinese is literally “sand filter.” ☜

2. In reality, the hourglass will work for ‘the time it takes an incense stick to burn.’ For a number of reasons, I’m going to render it as, simply, fifteen minutes. One reason is that the word ‘time’ is important, and the characters for “incense stick of time” do not actually contain the character for time. I generally render it as ‘time it takes an incense stick to burn’ for clarity’s sake. But I want to avoid unnecessary wordplay elements in this part of the story. Generally speaking, Er Gen uses ‘incense stick of time’ to mean something roughly between fifteen to thirty minutes (I asked him about this in person once). I’m going to go with fifteen minutes for ease of reading. What’s important here is not the specific number of minutes involved. It could be 15, 20, or 30. All would work. The important thing is that it’s a relatively short time. ☜

3. This is yet another instance in which “time” and “timescape” are clearly different terms that are either synonymous or near-synonymous. And yes, this is a title drop as the author uses the exact characters from the title of the series. ☜

“That’s not good enough,” Xu Qing said as he hovered in midair, looking down at Zhou Zhengli, who was still maintaining a humble bow.

Zhou Zhengli seemed harmless. But the reality was that harmlessness was a mere veneer. On the inside he was like a deadly viper. He had manipulated Sir Star Ring, and had certainly played a role in his ultimate downfall.[1]

Xu Qing didn’t want to fall into the same trap. Of course, his cautious nature would dictate his choices. Therefore, it didn’t matter that Zhou Zhengli claimed he wanted to be friends. Unless he provided an excellent reason, Xu Qing was not inclined to keep him around. And given how powerful Xu Qing was right now, if he didn’t want to keep him around, Zhou Zhengli would not stick around.

The wind was cold, so cold that not even the sunlight provided any warmth. As it blew, Zhou Zhengli looked up at Xu Qing.

“Exalted one, there are only four days left until the wedding. Someone needs to keep an eye on Zhong Chi’s poison, otherwise it could cause trouble in the four remaining days. Someone should also keep tabs on Li the Chosen to ensure he doesn’t get any ideas. Sir, you have a lot to keep track of. Well, I’m very familiar with Jiang Fan, so I can handle that.[2]

“Someone should also take time to record the details of the fox maiden identity to pass on to later generations. And, of course, the same goes for my identity. I’m the palace’s official historian. What’s more, sir, as the young lord, you need another study partner.

“All of those things can cause waves. There are many things I could help you with over the next four days, Young Lord. I can help you, not just to keep things going as they are, but to make even more waves. In addition, there are three people still in hiding. I’ve been keeping a close eye on everything, and I already uncovered their identities. You don’t need to waste your time on them, Young Lord. I can take care of one per day for you.

“That way, by the time we get to the wedding day, there won’t be any unknown factors to deal with. In the end, Young Lord, if you think the space-time waves aren’t sufficient, then just give the order, and I’ll die publicly to change history. Of course, every additional day that I live will benefit me.

“Sir, those are the reasons you should let me stay.” Zhou Zhengli once again bowed and waited for Xu Qing to make a decision.

Xu Qing looked coldly at Zhou Zhengli for a long moment. Then he waved his hand, and the shining marriage contract flew back into the fold of his robe. Then, another wave of his hand caused the immortal swords with Hordeslayer and Rampart in them to leap over to him and hover on either side, shining with immortal light and emitting immortal fluctuations.

Then Xu Qing ignored Zhou Zhengli as he walked over to the door leading away from the sword furnace. Just before leaving, he spoke over his shoulder to Zhou Zhengli.

“Have you ever eaten snake meat before? The more venomous the snake, the more tender the meat.” Xu Qing left.

Zhou Zhengli remained stock-still for a long moment. After everything was quiet for a time, he slowly straightened up and looked at the spot where Xu Qing had just departed. His expression became very serious.

He and Sir Star Ring have similarities and differences. He’s more cautious and more ruthless. He thinks of me as a venomous snake. But... to me, and probably to Sir Star Ring as well, isn’t he also a venomous snake...?

He sighed deeply. More than ever, he wanted to avoid making an enemy out of this person.

***

As the wedding day approached, and as the Aurora Epoch neared, the chaos in the workings of heaven grew more intense. The transitions between day and night grew more frequent, and there were constant changes in weather. And yet... nobody seemed to have been paying attention to the events of the previous night. It was as if the wind had blown everything away.

Fourth True Monarch appeared again, and this time, he got along perfectly with Xu Qing. Their initial meeting was one of chatting and laughter, and the familiar mannerisms and tone of voice resonated perfectly with the Fourth True Monarch from the memories of Xu Qing’s host. Apparently, his Elder Brother Fourth had no memories about what had played out the night before. And he also had no idea that he had been possessed by another consciousness.

That got Xu Qing thinking. After all, he had personally witnessed Fourth True Monarch disappear after the fight by the sword furnace.

Does it mean...?

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he looked up at the sky. Then he bade farewell to Fourth True Monarch and headed back to Young Aurora Hall. He did not come out again.

The four days went by quickly.

Zhou Zhengli did exactly as he said he would, and worked very hard during the four days. He recorded all of the information about the fox maiden identity, not just her status as a disciple of Nineshores, but everything else as well. As a result, she became an established figure in history.

He monitored Li the Chosen as well. As a result, Li the Chosen felt hemmed in, and had no chances to cause trouble. Zhou Zhengli even urged him to just accept how things were. He helped Zhong Chi with his poison work, working hard to ensure that the Poison Department was fully established, and that the Poison of Mengtu became common in the immortal palace.

He even tapped into the power of the immortal palace to cause three successive waves in space-time, all of which were the result of him expelling other outsiders who had remained hidden the entire time. He accomplished that by means of beheadings. The result was that Xu Qing got even more space-time sand.

Zhou Zhengli did only those things and nothing else. After all, he didn’t want to do anything to cause a misunderstanding with Xu Qing. He was extremely respectful.

And thus, time passed during the final four days before the wedding. There were no setbacks. And at long last, the day came for Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and Young Lord Aurora to be married.

When the day began, the heavenly daos were no longer in motion. The heavenly workings went still. Both sun and moon were visible in the dome of heaven, shining radiantly. When you looked up into the sky, everything seemed bright and auspicious.

Just as before, the immortal palace was full of bright lanterns and colorful decorations. Everyone was smiling, and the atmosphere was lively. There was a bustle of noise and excitement. Lively chatting and expressions of praise could be heard everywhere.

Xu Qing was flanked by a host of ceremonial officials as he walked out of Young Aurora Hall. Cheers filled the air.

Xu Qing was not wearing the same clothes he usually wore. He had a brightly-colored robe embroidered with nine golden dragons, all of which were so lifelike they seemed like they might fly up into the air at any moment. The collar and cuffs of the robe were decorated with exquisite immortal jade and spirit shells, all of which were befitting the son of an Immortal Lord. He wore a spirit crown inset with immortal jade that glittered in the light that shone down from the sky above.

Wherever he went, people offered cries of joy, approval, and blessing.

“Congratulations, Young Lord!”

“Hahaha! It’s the young lord’s wedding day! The young lord and young lady are really a match made in heaven!”

“Young Lord, after the wedding, you can’t go back to your old ways. I’ve watched you grow up, and now that you’re getting married, I can only hope to see the day you take up the position of Immortal Lord.”

“Good luck, Young Lord! I hope your journey of life is full of love and happiness. You’ll definitely grow old with the young lady, and be united for all eternity!”

Xu Qing heard wonderful words of blessing and anticipation coming from all sides. Although he had been expecting this to happen, he was a bit taken aback by it all.

Eventually, the sound of bells could be heard through the clamoring crowd. That was when he arrived at Aurora Grand Hall. A huge banquet had been laid out, though there were no guests from outside, only cultivators from the immortal palace. It was a bustling, luxurious event.

Xu Qing looked around and spotted Zhong Chi smiling, one-armed Li the Chosen sitting there with a wooden expression, and Zhou Zhengli looking modest and humble. He even spotted the fox maiden, who looked somewhat irritated.

At the highest spot in the banquet stood Immortal Lord Aurora. He normally had a grave expression on his face, but right now, he was smiling. That said, he was meticulously dressed in the most orthodox manner, and was obviously taking this day very seriously. When he caught sight of Xu Qing, he waved him to approach.

Xu Qing took a deep breath, settled his thoughts, and hurried over.

As soon as he reached the Immortal Lord, Aurora smiled kindly and helped Xu Qing to straighten his red wedding gown.

Immortal Lord Aurora sighed. “If your mother could see you right now, she would be so happy.”

Xu Qing looked like he was about to say something, but Immortal Lord Aurora tousled his hair and smiled kindly. “No need to go into all that. Look, your wife’s here.”

Off in the distance, red light shone boundlessly as Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix appeared, clad in her wedding gown, flanked by her handmaidens.

The wedding gown was exquisite. It was made of dark red silk, and was embroidered with golden phoenixes and clouds. It looked like the sunrise itself, and was a perfect indication that she would become the official wife of the young lord. Her hair was coiled into a bun, which surrounded her phoenix crown and then tumbled down her back filled with glistening spirit pearls. As she walked, her dress swayed back and forth, making her look like a blooming peony as she approached Xu Qing.

Xu Qing hesitated. The Immortal Lord then pushed him from behind, and he took a step forward.

Every step he took was accompanied by loud cheering. Every step he took brought auspicious signs.

Countless gazes were fixed on the two of them as they neared each other.

***

Outside of the space-time of the immortal palace, in the real world, not very far away from the Fallen Immortal Moors, was the God Blood River. The river water churned as a black boat glided across its surface.

No one knew exactly how many ferry boats operated on the God Blood River. But one thing was for sure. Those few people who ever took a ferry twice in their life would rarely see the same ferry pilot.

There was no passenger aboard the ferry boat. There was only the ferry pilot, clad in a woven rush raincoat, whose ancient and wrinkled hand guided the oar and kept the boat on a forward course. The pilot seemed used to time passing by, year after year, seemingly with no beginning or no end.

But today was different. As the wind blew across the river, the ripples it created seemed to tug desolately on the ferry pilot’s heartstrings....

The pilot slowly looked up. The aurora above rippled, shining down onto the boat. The face beneath the wide bamboo hat... was the wrinkled face of a very old woman. This ferry pilot was actually a woman! She was looking off in the direction of the Fallen Immortal Moors, and she seemed to be lost in memories. In the end, she sighed.

“You came back....”

The wind blew, stirring the woven rush raincoat. And beneath it, it was just possible to see... a very ancient red wedding dress.

1. The contrast between “harmless” and “viper” is better in Chinese, because harmless literally means “without poison/venom.” Meanwhile, the term I’m rendering as deadly viper literally is “hyper-venomous snake.” ☜

2. Jiang Fan was introduced in chapter 1136. Based on clues in chapters 1152 and 1167, we readers could have deduced that Jiang Fan was Li the Chosen. But there was never any 'onscreen' evidence of other characters figuring out who he was. In fact, in chapter 1149, Zhou Zhengli specifically said that he didn’t know who Jiang Fan was. I guess if he was playing Sir Star Ring the entire time, it would make sense that he withheld the information, or perhaps he found out later. ☜

The sun and moon were in the sky simultaneously, reflecting each other’s brilliance, and creating a unified glow of dazzling light. It shone down on the lands of this space-time, almost like wedding garments gifted by heaven itself.

As countless cultivators looked on... two people approached each other step by step. A man and woman, each clad in wedding garments, got closer and closer to each other, one coming from the east, the other from the west.

The woman wore a dazzling wedding dress that looked like living flame. Her smile was a touch bashful, but her eyes contained a longing for the future. As she advanced, her beautiful face seemed to fill with a rosy glow, whether because of the rising sun or her own emotions, it was hard to say.

And yet... close observers would be able to tell that her expression was forced, and her smile was empty. In fact, her eyes seemed as cold as ice. Yet she seemed to be in full anticipation of the wedding. There was no conflict between the iciness and the anticipation. After all, she was not really Spirit Phoenix. The emotions she felt toward Young Lord Aurora were not natural. The anticipation came because, even though history said that the wedding ceremony would never be completed, it would still create karmic connections![1]

In other words, the fact that she had reached this point meant that she had already largely accomplished her goal. All she had to do was continue onward, and it wouldn’t really matter what happened historically speaking. She sped up a bit as she walked.

Meanwhile, the man wore a swirling gown with nine dragons on it. The golden crown on his head reflected the light of the sun, and its jewels glittered. And yet, as he approached his dazzling wife, his heart pounded. The reason was because of his understanding of what happened at this linchpin in history.

Yuanshan Su is playing the part of Spirit Phoenix. I’m acting as Mi Ming. Historically speaking, this is their wedding. And historically speaking, the wedding actually didn’t work out... They never finished the ceremony of kowtowing. Her name... was never added to the marriage contract.

Li Mengtu had explained to Xu Qing what happened in real history, and Zhou Zhengwei had confirmed it so that Xu Qing didn’t misunderstand what was to play out.

The linchpin was the first kowtow! When they kowtowed to heaven and earth, there was a violent reaction. The Immortal Lord rebelled, the Immortal Paragon stepped in, and everyone in the immortal palace... crumbled into ashes, dead. freewebnovel.com

It’s going to happen after enough time passes for an incense stick to burn.

Xu Qing’s heart pounded harder and harder. It wouldn’t be long before the biggest tempest of all would strike this historical space-time.

At the same time, he was ready to make his final salvo. He was on the side that was fighting to change history. He needed that to grow his space-time canon. He had not stopped working toward the effort just because he drove out Sir Star Ring’s consciousness.

After all, expelling Sir Star Ring eliminated all factors of uncertainty for the outsiders. Everything... came down to this very day!

Xu Qing was not pleased with an hourglass that could exist beyond the timescape for only fifteen minutes! He wanted more than that. He wanted to take his space-time canon to the limit that was possible in the fourth world. He wanted his timescape hourglass to last for much longer.

And there were two historical events that, if he could change even just one of them, would fit the bill. Unfortunately, changing either of those things would be so difficult they might as well be impossible.

The first was to save Aurora and everyone else from the fate of death. The second was to change this wedding ceremony into a success.

A failed wedding was second only to death in the regret it would cause.

Xu Qing knew that the first thing was something he had no way to affect or change. But... the second, because of his identity, wasn’t impossible to change. In fact, Xu Qing felt certain... that the imp who had given him those birthdate characters was none other than the discarnate soul of Immortal Lord Aurora. And it seemed very likely that his goal was to make up for past regrets.[2]

Of course, that was mere speculation on Xu Qing’s part, and he had no hard evidence to confirm it. Either way, it didn’t conflict with his own goal here.

And his timescape hourglass was going to be his biggest asset right now! He could use it to buy fifteen minutes for Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, to ensure that, in this reflection of history, their wedding ceremony was not interrupted. This time, they would succeed at completing the ceremony! The resulting space-time waves in this version of history would become a true space-time tempest! That was Xu Qing’s plan.

As things developed, he became more and more certain of what he had to do. He stepped forward without hesitation, until... the two people clad in wedding garments, surrounded by cheering... rose up into the air together. Dazzling, auspicious light shone from heaven, surrounding the bride and groom with a beautiful glow.

Everyone looked on intently. In the crowd, Zhong Chi sighed, the fox maiden snorted coldly, Li the Chosen looked on with cold eyes, and Zhou Zhengli’s eyes shone. Fourth True Monarch was there as well, standing next to Immortal Lord Aurora, looking on with a proud smile.

“Little Junior Brother really has grown up.” Fourth True Monarch turned to look at Immortal Lord Aurora.

Aurora didn’t seem to have heard him. He seemed relieved, and yet, as he looked at the auspicious couple, he seemed to be exuding a black smoke that no one could see.

The master of ceremonies, who was a grand elder in the immortal palace, then spoke in a loud voice.

“The beautiful, auspicious day has arrived. Let the ceremonial performers do their duty. Let the honor guard display the wedding paraphernalia. Let the spectators revel. Drums, flutes, and all manner of musical instruments will bring propitious sounds to our ears.”

Cheering and music filled the air. It couldn’t have been a more optimistic atmosphere. An immortal phoenix flew about, accompanied by a heavenly dragon, carrying a red silk banner in their mouths that supported an embroidered silk ball. As they swirled around Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, the two of them were bound by the silk, with the silk ball between them.

Laughing heartily, the master of ceremonies said, “To respect the ancient etiquette, the couple will first kowtow to heaven and earth! Let the couple begin by prostrating to heaven.”

As his voice echoed out, Xu Qing took a deep breath. Then he and Yuanshan Su both looked up into the sky.

The dome of heaven was filled with dazzling rosy light. The sun and moon were hidden, and the heavenly workings seethed. Time was still slipping away as a new epoch approached. The rosy light and the auspicious glow were symbols....

The master of ceremony’s voice again rang out. “Pay respect to the great heaven. The happy couple are the product of heaven.”

Xu Qing lowered his head and together with Yuanshan Su, prostrated to heaven. The dome of heaven rumbled.

“Pay respect to the wondrous earth. Tie the knot and make the marriage official.”

The two of them prostrated again! The sky trembled, and the glow grew more intense.

“Pay respect to heaven and earth. Endure as long as the earth lasts and heaven exists.”

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Winds kicked up. The sun and moon were completely covered up. It was as if an enormous hand... had plucked them out of the sky! The Aurora Epoch was truly on the way!

Yuanshan Su took a deep breath. She knew that a dramatic event was just about to unfold. The black smoke coming out of Immortal Lord Aurora was about as thick as it could be. The astounding historical event was about to happen!

But then, all of a sudden, an hourglass flew out from Xu Qing.

The moment the hourglass appeared, it shone with stupendous light, like a torch on a dark night, illuminating everything! The sand began to fall, whereupon a majestic and stupefying power spread out within this space-time. It was a flood that could not be stopped.

It was time beyond the timescape. It transcended this space-time. It was fifteen minutes that could not be changed. As it fell, it forced this linchpin of time to continue!

And thus, the light in the sky went still. The quaking lands came under control. Everyone stopped moving. The wind, the spirit energy, the heavenly workings... all froze.

But within the light cast by the sand, Xu Qing and Yuanshan Su were not affected. Yuanshan Su was stunned. Her eyes were wide with incredulity as she turned to Xu Qing and opened her mouth to say something.

But he simply took a breath and growled, “Don’t waste your breath. Continue the ceremony!”

She shivered and slowly closed her eyes. Eyelashes quivering, she quietly said, “According to etiquette, the bride and groom will kowtow a second time, this time to the sun and moon. Pay respect to their brightness, which brings about the good fortune of both yin and yang.”

Xu Qing bowed his head, and together with her, kowtowed!

Voice trembling, she continued, “Pay respect to the red thread of matchmaking, to create a union perfect in heaven.”

As the two of them continued with the ceremony, things were happening in the outside world. Space-time waves were building into a crescendo.

“Now the third kowtow, to the parents.” Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s voice trembled with complex emotions, including reminiscence, but also... boundless anticipation. Her voice came as a surprise to Xu Qing, and he suddenly looked up. What he saw caused his heart to skip a beat.

There was something unusual going on with her. She looked very different compared to before. Her eyes were not cold, and she was clearly not acting. She seemed full of ancient reminiscence, complex emotions... and tenderness. It was as if she had been waiting for thousands and thousands of years, all for this very day and moment. Yuanshan Su’s consciousness had, at some point, simply vanished.

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted. And then he heard a very familiar voice sighing into his mind. It was... the imp! The sigh became a wave that swept through him, taking control of his body away from his consciousness.

Xu Qing’s mind reeled as all of the puzzle pieces clicked together. He’s not the discarnate soul of Immortal Lord Aurora. He’s... actually Young Lord Aurora!!

Young Lord Aurora looked at Spirit Phoenix tenderly. Reaching out, he took her hand and gently said, “Pay respect to the kindness our parents showed in raising us. This emotion is like the East Sea. Pay respect to the kindness our parents showed in educating us. This grace is weightier than a mountain. May our parents experience love and joy, and live lives long and peaceful.”

Tears seeped out of the corners of Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s eyes as she clasped Young Lord Aurora’s hand tightly. Then she looked into the eyes of the person whose life she valued more than all others, and opened her mouth to utter the last part of the ceremonial oath.

“The fourth kowtow is between husband and wife.... One heart. One will. We will grow old together on the same pillow and under the same blanket. We are both willing to experience the love of husband and wife, a happy couple in perfect harmony. The blessing of three lifetimes, cooperating for eternity, always together... in life and in death. We are... husband and wife....” Tears streamed down Spirit Phoenix’s face and fell to the ground below.

“We are... husband and wife!” Young Lord Aurora said, reaching out and wiping her tears away. And then he took out the marriage contract... and wrote Spirit Phoenix’s true name onto it.

Unheard-of space-time waves rolled out. Heaven and earth trembled. A screaming wind created a huge vortex that covered the entire immortal palace. Intense rumbling rocked everything.

1. As is made clear throughout the rest of this chapter, this wedding ceremony is not like a Western wedding ceremony. It’s the traditional Chinese type that involves a series of bows/kowtows. ☜

2. The birthdate characters were first mentioned and explained in chapter 1146 and 1147, and were again mentioned in chapter 1154. Previously, we weren’t 100% sure that the birthdate characters mentioned in 1154 were those provided in 1146 and 1147, but now we do have confirmation. ☜

Love can be both moving and confusing. Countless men and women dream of finding that one special person that will stay by their side through every phase of their life. It is just like the ancient wedding vow: the lovebirds sing in harmony, they stay together forever, they grow old together, and they share life and death.[1]

But sometimes karma plays out in a different way, and despite a sacred promise being made, love letters become very hard to send.[2]

There are always going to be people who live lives full of lamentation and regret. And thus, there came to be a woman who spent millions upon millions of years traversing the God Blood River as a ferry pilot, but clad in a red wedding dress. And thus, there came to be an imp who devolved into desolate madness, who hid his bitterness beneath laughter and cursing.

***

There are few happy couples amongst immortals. In the vast majority of cases, their love becomes a whirlpool of bitterness and struggle. The regrets that come with unrequited love become like stars in the sky that can be seen but not touched, beautiful but sad.

I can only stand in the immortal palace in the timescape, and look at the same old embroidered curtains, musing that there is a person missing. I think back to that day years ago, and how her face was flush in the reflection of the peach blossoms.... And I sigh, thinking about the person I miss, who is oh so far away.

There is bitterness entrenched deeply within me. It goes without saying who that person is, and how things turned out.

A bitter east wind blows, and our happiness is cut short. My mind is steeped in sorrow and gloom.

This is wrong, wrong, wrong.

Peach blossoms fall, and lie idle on the pond and pavilion. We still have our sacred promise, but even a love letter is hard to send.

We have nothing, nothing, nothing.[3]

But... the two ends of the timescape river connect to each other. The road of reincarnation creates an endless loop. If you refuse to forget someone, they’ll eventually speak to you once more. And thus, those words caused waves to flow across the surface of the river of blood.

“You came back....”

She had gone, leaving behind only the peach blossoms laughing in the spring breeze. The scenery stayed the same, but it was empty and meaningless.

Then the spring breeze picked up, and a person stepped out of those memories.

They had waited millions upon millions of years, and were now being reunited beyond the timescape.

On the edge of one small section of time, on this day, Xu Qing was able to tread the timescape and help them continue what had been interrupted.

***

Looking at the young lord, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix softly said, “Over the years, I constantly wondered... if it was fate that I had met someone who touched my heart. Was it a blessing?”

The wind of time was a tempest on the outside. A vortex. But inside... it gently stirred Spirit Phoenix’s hair as she gave voice to her longing. Glittering space-time sand dropped down, surrounding Young Lord Aurora and Spirit Phoenix. From a distance, it was possible to see waves surging around them, almost like a dream.

“The last time this happened,” Spirit Phoenix said, “we didn’t complete the wedding ceremony.... Catastrophe struck, and my father came to take both of us away.

“Because we had not truly become husband and wife, and my name was not written on the marriage contract, you refused to leave with my father. I know why. You didn’t want to drag me into what was happening. Instead, you chose... to stay here and help your father settle his debt. And I chose... to be punished on the river of blood, to help you atone for your crimes.

“So does today count as us completing the ceremony and putting my name on the marriage contract? Does it count as making everything official?” Spirit Phoenix sighed. “The debt has been settled. The crimes have been atoned for... Can we go home now?”

Young Lord Aurora said nothing.

The space-time waves were stronger than ever. They were whipping into a vortex, filling the immortal palace with deafening rumbling sounds. And they were bringing more and more space-time sand.

It surrounded the two of them, gradually accumulating to again form an hourglass that existed beyond the timescape. The limit was not fifteen minutes. There was enough sand to last... for two hours. That was the limit in this reflection of space-time.

Young Lord Aurora didn’t answer Spirit Phoenix’s question. He looked up... in the direction of his father, Immortal Lord Aurora. When he did that, the fifteen minutes that Xu Qing had bought for him... ended.

Rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth. All of the living beings who had frozen in place earlier... went back to normal. The cheering and laughter resumed. It was as if no one had noticed that some extra time had been bought.

The sky was still distorted. The sun and moon were dark. The workings of heaven were at a peak level of chaos. Everything was about to change dramatically!

And then a white light spread out that illuminated the entirety of the Fifth Star Ring. It was like the spreading of an entire sea! The Aurora Epoch arrived, late by fifteen minutes.

A boundlessly mighty force converged, pouring into Immortal Lord Aurora’s life force, and transforming into an imperial robe that draped about him.

Countless people looked on as Aurora put on an imperial crown. Immortal Lord Aurora was ascending the throne! In this next epoch, he was taking over as the ruler of the Fifth Star Ring! The sun and moon, which had reached the epitome of darkness, now blazed with light. Their dazzling brightness shone infinitely.

Then Immortal Lord Aurora’s gaze swept through the world before coming to rest on his son. His eyes were full of warmth, blessing, and... departure. He lifted his foot and stepped... up into the sky.

He strode through the dome of heaven to the sun and moon. The moment he took over as the lord of the star ring, a boundlessly mighty force converged on him, and his hand became infinitely large. It covered the sky, piercing through the highest heavens to reach the sun and moon. The hand pierced through something like a bubble before grabbing the sun and moon!!

Heaven and earth became pitch black. Sunlight and moonlight disappeared, and Aurora’s own light became gloom.

The entire Fifth Star Ring was now without any light! And then Immortal Lord Aurora squeezed down on the sun and moon in his hand, and they were pulled inside of him. It happened very smoothly. The sun and moon merged into him as smoothly as water flowing down a pipe!

And that was because, back when the workings of heaven went into chaos, he had taken away the name of the sun and moon. No one even realized that they had forgotten those names. He had taken the names of the sun and moon and hidden them within the name of his son.

Mi Ming. Seek Brightness.

Seek for what is not seen. The sun and moon are the brightness. That was the meaning of Mi Ming![4]

“Going forward,” Aurora said softly, “you will be the sun and moon of the Fifth Star Ring. You will have boundless light that can never be defiled. The will of the gods is laid bare, and you can be forever free from the godbane! Ming’er, this... is my wedding gift to you. Go now... and live the life you want to live.”

As he looked out at the pitch-black heaven and earth, black smoke exploded from within him and spread out everywhere. At the same time, his voice echoed out into the Fifth Star Ring.

“Of the seven colors in the world, I chose the red! It will become part of my aurora, turning it crimson! Henceforth... I convert to the dao of gods! I hereby change my canon into godhood!”[5]

His voice echoed in the ears of all living beings. It exploded into countless hearts and minds. And then... he extracted the infinite red color and fused it with his light.

It became... a crimson red aurora! It was a mountain-toppling, sea-draining aurora that could crush anything in its path. As it spread out through the canopy of heaven, covering all beings.... It replaced the sky! Going into the future, that crimson aurora would be the only source of light in the sky for the people of the Fifth Star Ring!

However, there was something strange and gruish. A change this drastic had never occurred in the Fifth Star Ring, this land of cultivators. After all, it was something that would affect all living beings. And yet everyone in the immortal palace, even Fourth True Monarch, was smiling.

The dancing continued. The celebration went on. The laughter and chatting did not cease. Apparently, none of them realized what was happening in the outside world. That scene, coupled with the dramatic change in the dome of heaven, was extremely jarring.

When Xu Qing realized what was happening, he looked up at the familiar red aurora, and his mind felt like it was spinning.

Is this what really happened? But why did the Immortal Lord do this? And why... is everyone here acting like this? Also... what is Young Lord Aurora trying to accomplish...?

Gradually, his racing thoughts began to form an answer. Even as it occurred to him, Immortal Lord Aurora spoke again, his voice ringing through the sky. This time, he sounded even more aggressive than before!

“Did you hear that, Immortal Paragon?” freewebnovel.com

As his voice boomed like thunder through the red sky, the response came in the form of an ancient sigh. It came from the dome of heaven, from the land, from the air, from the inanimate objects, from the living things. It came from every corner of the Fifth Star Ring.... It turned into a most ancient voice, resonating everywhere, causing the sky to distort, driving away the aurora, and revealing a glittering starry sky.

The starry sky was also distorted. Countless heavenly bodies rippled, as if they were a host of bubbles, all of them different sizes.

All were different colors, but there were none that were red. There were infinite bubbles, and yet all of them contained various scenes. If you put all the scenes together like a puzzle, they would form... the entirety of the Fifth Star Ring!

An ancient hand appeared along with the sigh. Extending two fingers, the hand reached through the starry sky and touched one of the bubbles.

The bubble popped. It was destroyed. In an instant, the immortal palace was wiped out of existence just like that bubble. All things and all beings were reduced to ashes. It didn’t matter the level of their cultivation base. None could fight back or resist. They dissipated.

Fourth True Monarch. The grand elder. Everyone, even the cultivators who served as hosts to the outsiders. Only Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix remained amidst the crumbling ruins. They were real, living beings!

Up above, Immortal Lord Aurora disappeared. However, his boundless red light converged on him and then shot up into the canopy of heaven. It appeared in the starry sky amidst the countless bubbles, where... it began to fight the ancient hand. Down below in the destruction and ruins, the young lord maintained silence.

He looked at the figure in the starry sky, and then he prepared to take a step forward. He had assumed all along he could do this. After all, he had planned for this moment for millions upon millions of years. The moment he had longed for that entire time was now upon him. He had assumed that he would be able to make the choice.

Except... he couldn’t help but look at Spirit Phoenix, whose hand he held, and who was holding his hand tightly. He knew that she was still waiting for an answer.

She had been waiting for that answer for millions upon millions of years. He could envision her on the God Blood River, piloting a little boat, clad in a woven rush raincoat. And beneath that raincoat was a wedding dress. Wind blew and rain fell. Time passed. Year after year....

Compared to that, all of his talking points seemed meaningless. He couldn’t bring himself to say them. He didn’t have the strength to step forward. He knew that he owed her far, far too much....

After a long moment of silence, he took a deep breath and suppressed the obsession that had driven him for millions upon millions of years. Reaching out, he tucked a stray hair behind Spirit Phoenix’s ear.

“Let’s go home...” he said softly.

Spirit Phoenix had been waiting for him to say that for too many years to count. It had finally happened. She was almost in a daze as she looked at that familiar face from her memories, that person who she could never possibly forget. Tears flowed down her face. She squeezed down tighter on his hand.

And finally, she said, “I know that you can never understand or forgive the Immortal Paragon.... I understand that you want to uncover all the secrets, and find out why this happened. And I know more than anything that you did all of this... to save your father.

“You didn’t set this up for me.... That hourglass creates two hours that exist beyond the timescape. You want to use it to go back to real history, not just a reflection. You want to go back and try to change what happened! But you’re willing to give that up for me. In that case....”

Spirit Phoenix looked at the man she loved, and then she reached toward the hourglass floating off to the side. She grasped it between her fingers, and a popping sound rang out as the hourglass broke open. Countless grains of space-time sand spilled out, forming... a space-time door that led back to real history!

Young Lord Aurora was shaken to the core.

Standing in front of the door, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix said, “I’ll go with you. Let’s... either live or die together.”

1. As far as I can tell, this wedding vow is made up by the author, although it contains some idioms and terms that are common in traditional Chinese wedding vows. I could be wrong. I tend to check these things to see if the poetic sayings are from real-life poems, songs, etc. In this case, nothing popped up right away, so if it is a real-life ancient wedding vow, I think it’s relatively obscure. ☜

2. In this line, the author alludes to a poem by Southern Song Dynasty poet Lu You. Like I’ve said before, I prefer to use existing translations of poetry if they exist and are good quality, and in this case, I found a great translation of the poem by Jean Yuan. The original line in the translation is: “We still have our sacred promise, but even a love letter is hard to send.” The poem is called Phoenix Hairpin. In this case, the translator has a literal translation, a more poetic translation, as well as background information on the poem. If you’re interested, I suggest going to the translator’s website to check out the poem (it’s at the bottom of the page). ☜

3. This is a much longer excerpt from the same poem referenced above. ☜

4. Just a reminder that the character Ming/brightness is made up of the two characters for sun and moon.... ☜

5. The last thing he says is somewhat vague in Chinese, and does not actually say godhood. It uses one of the characters from the terms I’ve been translating as personhood and godhood, and based on the context here and later, it seems clear that the implication is that it's related to gods and godhood. ☜

In the dome of heaven, in the reflected version of history, the starry sky rippled and distorted. Heavenly bodies blurred. Countless bubbles lacked the color red.

But red was in the aurora. The crimson aurora flowed as if to do battle with all the other colors! Within light and shadow, Immortal Lord Aurora and the ancient hand got closer and closer.

As Xu Qing looked on, he was reminded of that monster back in the second world.... Everything that was happening in the sky here was very similar to what happened in the second world.[1]

Meanwhile, the doorway of time stood amidst the ruins, glittering. However, the glow was not colorful. Rather, it was black and white. That doorway of time looked like a door, but it also looked like a mirror. Just like the mirror from the first world.

A ripple of understanding flowed through Xu Qing’s consciousness. At the same time, he realized that the black-and-white glow coming from the doorway of time did not consist of rays of light. Rather, it was light like powder, drifting about. It surrounded Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, and was also pouring into Young Lord Aurora. It was... forming a resonance with his consciousness.

Xu Qing was not surprised at all. He had formed the space-time sand, and he had caused the space-time waves. It made sense that the doorway of time would be connected to him because of his space-time canon. Young Lord Aurora and Spirit Phoenix were borrowing that, and using their memories as a link between the past and the present. As a result, Xu Qing would need to witness their journey back into real history.

“Is that okay, young friend?” Young Lord Aurora said softly, his voice reaching both Spirit Phoenix and Xu Qing’s consciousness. “Will you come with the two of us on a quick trip back?”

Spirit Phoenix’s gaze was kind as she said, “Young friend, you are our benefactor. Regardless of whether we live or die on this trip, we’ll make sure that you get back safely!”

Xu Qing thought about it. He considered what he knew about the young lord and Spirit Phoenix. And then....

“Okay!” he said.

“Thank you...” said Young Lord Aurora. Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix said the same thing. And then the married couple held hands as they walked into the doorway of time.

It was almost like going into the first world. They were going... back into real history!

***

History took place within time. It was ancient time. And it was the sand and silt at the bottom of the river of the timescape. Even more than that, it was a record and a reflection of time.

Fundamentally speaking, time was the backdrop and the framework for the development of history. By means of time, people could organize and interpret past events. But simultaneously, by means of historical developments, time could reveal its flow and its transformations! For most people, that was nothing more than an abstract concept. But to cultivators who could command space-time canon, it could fill in gaps in their understanding, and lead to... astounding destined opportunities!

Imagine taking a mirror and placing it above a river. Obviously, the image formed by the mirror would only reflect one part of the river. That image corresponded to reflected history.

Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix stepped out of the mirror and onto the River of Time.

There, the young lord spoke to Xu Qing. “It’s formed from my canon of the past.”

His words verified Xu Qing’s supposition. And it significantly bolstered the understanding provided by his canon of time. “Everything here is formed subjectively. People believe that time flows like a river, and so it does.”

Young Lord Aurora laughed softly. “That’s what my father said once.”

Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix held hands as they stepped into the river and sank down to the sand and silt. From that point, they began to walk against the flow. With every step they took, the sand and the silt stirred around their feet. It looked at first like they were making changes. But as they passed, nothing behind them was different.

Xu Qing noticed that.

This time, the one to provide an explanation wasn’t Young Lord Aurora. It was Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix.

“My father once explained all of this to me,” she said softly. “Think of the past like pages in a book. Once you turn the page, the past is gone. It doesn’t exist. But it does leave behind evidence of its passage. That evidence becomes hidden secrets, and the hidden secrets naturally form order.”

Xu Qing tried to digest what she was saying.

Immortal Lord Nineshores’ canon was that of secrets. Clearly, that was related to the history he could see. By viewing history and time from different angles, they could be seen more completely.

Walking through the River of Time, and treading on the sand of history, was an astounding destined opportunity. Xu Qing was gaining immense enlightenment, and it was allowing him to extend his space-time canon far out into the River of Time.

Gradually, his space-time canon began to fill with waves. As the waves grew bigger, they made a vortex that absorbed his understanding of space-time. Ultimately, they became a powerful flow that spread out and seemingly stirred the sand. Every single grain of that glittering sand contained images of space-time. All of that shone into his heart.

To Xu Qing, who cultivated the canon of space-time, there could be no good fortune that surpassed the experience of transcending beyond time itself like he was now.

Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix could sense what was happening. They exchanged a glance, and then... they slowed their pace significantly.

They were dead set on reaching their goal, and they wanted it to happen quickly. But... this was an unprecedented destined opportunity and good fortune for Xu Qing, and they wanted him to succeed, just as he had done everything possible to help them succeed.

Xu Qing was experiencing a journey that involved going back into a reflection of the past, and then stepping from that reflection into real history. It went without saying that there couldn’t possibly be a better way to bolster his understanding of space-time.

When he reached his limit, an indescribable cracking sound echoed in his consciousness. It was the sound of a lock on his space-time canon being broken open. The instant it happened, massive amounts of space-time sand began to pour into his consciousness. And it far surpassed the amount that had made the previous hourglass!

Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix were approaching their destination. When they finally stepped onto the origin of their memories... a sigh echoed through time. It kicked up sand and sent waves across the river water. And with the help of Xu Qing’s space-time canon, it formed numerous pages of history for Young Lord Aurora, which spread out in front of them. Soon, it replaced everything they could see.

The River of Time dissipated, and the immortal palace of old appeared in front of them. However, it was as if there was a curtain separating them, making it impossible to see things perfectly clearly....

Within the blur, Xu Qing spotted a person.

It was Immortal Lord Aurora. He wore white clothes and had white hair, and he was standing in front of a mountain of ice. His expression was one of pain, bitterness, and sorrow. Ultimately, all of those emotions blended together to form loneliness.

“From now on, it’s just going to be you and me, son.... I’ll be with you as you grow up.”

There was an infant sealed in the ice mountain. It went without saying who that infant was.

***

The image blurred, as though the pages of time were being flipped. Immortal Lord Aurora was by the infant’s side as he slowly grew. The infant babbled happily as he learned to talk.

His father hugged him and laughed. His father held his hand as they climbed a mountain together. He was eventually a boy, perched on his father’s shoulders as they watched the sun rise.

“Daddy, I want the sun and the moon to be around forever. I love them!”

Immortal Lord Aurora smiled. It seemed that his time spent with his son was healing him. The immortal palace had been empty, but now there were people there. There were attendants, followers, apprentices, and more.

Xu Qing eventually spotted Fourth True Monarch. All of them were smiling. They respected the Immortal Lord, and they loved the young lord. All of them accompanied the young Lord as he grew up.

The immortal palace overflowed with life.

***

Sadly, those beautiful times were only temporary. As the pages of history turned, and as time flowed, the light in the immortal palace dimmed. And then, without warning... it went out.

Darkness spread everywhere, reaching every corner. The Immortal Lord walked through that darkness and gloom, and he no longer wore a white robe. His clothing was black. And his hair was black. His eyes were cold and they seemed full of slaughter.

He personally... killed all of his followers, wiped out all of his attendants, and brutally slaughtered his apprentices. His four apprentices all died miserably. The immortal palace reeked of gore. Blood flowed on the ground. Shredded flesh stuck to all the buildings.

When the immortal palace was quiet, a young man was stranded in the sea of blood, shivering in terror and despair. In front of him, the darkness converged into the form of his father. His father slowly reached out his hand.

The hand was trembling and black. The darkness was rippling, struggling as if it was being restrained, until eventually... he reached down and tousled the young man’s hair.

The light of dawn accompanied the tears that fell onto the young man’s face.

The Immortal Lord’s robe became white. His black hair turned white. Wrapping the young man in his arms, he bitterly murmured, “I’m sorry. I’m so sorry. I’m so sorry....”

Then he erased the young man’s memories and erased the blood in the immortal palace.

When the young man woke up, the sun shone brightly. Everyone was there in the immortal palace, their smiles unchanging. They were not acting strangely at all. Just as they had in life, they happily accompanied the young man.

And yet, it was starting on that day that Immortal Lord Aurora told the young man to never come visit him at night. Beneath the Immortal Lord’s grand hall, a cave came to exist. And in that cave were chains. Every night, that cave was filled with bitter howls that no one could hear.

In that manner, one day turned into another. Years passed....

The young man grew up and gained enlightenment of his canon. It was a special canon. It was that of the mirror.

But then one day his canon... was secretly transformed.

The night Immortal Lord Aurora sensed that his son’s canon had changed, his pain in that cave surpassed anything from before. Until... darkness once again infected the entire immortal palace.

By the time dawn came, everything was back to normal. Normally speaking, time would have passed like that, an illusion that contained only a father and a son.

But one day a very determined woman arrived. And then there were three living people.

And then the wedding day came.

The red curtain of history had been opened wide. Young Lord Aurora’s heart was pounding thanks to the memories that had been hidden away within him.

At the very least, memories that had been waiting countless years to be released were now free. Young Lord Aurora, who had been slowly driven mad as he waited quietly in the immortal palace, finally had an explanation. And yet... personally seeing what had actually happened didn’t enable him to calm down.

Spirit Phoenix gripped his hand even tighter.

Xu Qing and Young Lord Aurora were in a fused state right now, so Xu Qing could clearly sense his agitation. And he understood it. But there was nothing he could say.

A real life, and a fake one. Despair and hope. Weeping and laughter. All of them mixed together until... they revealed a father’s love. Unfortunately, that father eventually disappeared into time, like sand that slipped through the fingers when dredged up from the bottom of a river.

It was only possible to go through time without a fear of death, like a dreaming soul, full of helplessness and sorrow, full of longing. Surpass life and death. Walk through time. To find an opportunity to ask: why?

Xu Qing sighed. He thought back to Peerless City, and the blur of memories, and the image of his parents that could never fade away. He thought back to Seven Blood Eyes, to his Master, to Sergeant Thunder, and to Grandmaster Bai. And then those figures combined into an ancient voice that echoed in his consciousness.

“Don’t stop now! Don’t give up!!”

***

The historical images continued to flow through time. The red curtain had parted, but it didn’t take away the red. The color of the wedding still blossomed within history. Like blood.

In the image, Immortal Lord Aurora laughed gratefully. Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix were kowtowing to heaven.

But then...real history played out, and it was not what had happened in that fifteen minutes beyond the timescape. Heaven and earth transformed. The sea of light rippled, and even as their first kowtow concluded... rumbling descended from above.

The sun and moon were plucked away. Immortal Lord Aurora became red, and the sky... no longer had a sun and moon, but instead a crimson aurora. That was the only source of light. Within that light, countless bubbles appeared.

Along with them came an ancient hand. The bubble popped, and a ripping sound echoed out as he took away all the glory of the immortal palace.... At the same time, the bride and groom stood amidst the ruins, stunned looks on their faces. At least, until their minds blurred.

Neither the Immortal Lord nor the Immortal Paragon wished for the bride and groom to know what had truly happened. They were cut away from it all and rendered unconscious.

Just before passing out, the Young Lord Aurora of the past looked at his father, and watched him rebel. He watched him change his canon into godhood, and shoot out into the starry sky. Even if he lost, he was going to fight the Immortal Paragon! That was the last thing Young Lord Aurora saw before losing consciousness.

But the images of history continued to play out. The Young Lord Aurora and Spirit Phoenix who had stepped out of the mirror and into the past, were watching intently. They wanted to see... what really happened.

And they did.

After Immortal Lord Aurora shot out into the starry sky, he blazed with radiant, crimson light. And yet... he did not have any desire to do battle!

Smiling, and yet with tears flowing down his face, he looked at the ancient hand and shouted, “Kill me, father!”

Those words slammed into the mind of Young Lord Aurora like millions upon millions of lightning bolts. This was not a fight to quell a rebellion. It was....

“Father... asked to die...?” murmured Young Lord Aurora bitterly.

An ancient sigh echoed through history. The bubbles glittered, and light swirled into the shape of a majestic figure. The figure hovered in the starry sky in front of Immortal Lord Aurora, so majestic he became everything. It was as if he was the starry sky. Mixed emotions filled his eyes. Shame. Helplessness. Sorrow.

“Do you blame me?” he asked hoarsely. “For sealing the godbane inside of you...?”

Immortal Lord Aurora looked up at the familiar figure in front of him. It was his father, the most paramount entity in all of the Fifth Star Ring. The Immortal Paragon!

He was the one who had led the cultivators of all the minor worlds in a grand counterattack against the gods! He was the one who had overthrown the dynasty of the gods, and ended the suffering of all living beings. He was the one who had compacted the Fifth Star Ring down and turned it into a land of cultivators. No one had accomplished more in the Fifth Star Ring than him. There were countless people who grew up venerating him as a hero of the ages.

“I don’t blame you,” Immortal Lord Aurora said. “Back during the war with the gods, it seemed like you won. But the truth is that just before death, the God Paragon infected you with the godbane.

“The gods are a fundamental manifestation of the higher star rings. They are a part of the higher star rings. Therefore, a God Lord can never truly be destroyed, not for all eternity. As long as someone remembers a God Lord, then no matter how many epochs pass, that God Lord can be called back. And thus, there’s no need to even mention... a God Paragon.”

Immortal Lord Aurora looked at the Immortal Paragon, and he shimmered with red light as he continued, “The God Paragon used the power unleashed by the destruction of his godhood to gather his boundless godly might and turn it into the ultimate curse. Not even someone as incredibly powerful as you could completely wipe it out of existence. And the bit that remained when you tried became a sealing mark.

“That’s why you went into seclusion after the final battle. You found out that the God Paragon... wanted that curse to be inside of you... so that hē could be resurrected. A resurrection like that would take many, many years. But if the process couldn’t be stopped, then the resurrection was certain to take place. And the moment it occurred, this land of cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring would be reduced to ashes.

“In order to prevent that from happening, you traveled through all the higher and lower star rings, sending out countless clones in the hopes of finding a way to solve the problem. And eventually you did.”

Aurora’s voice faltered a bit, and when he started talking again, there was bitterness in the voice. “And that was to transfer the godbane away and enter a state of slumber! The transfer magic came with extremely strict conditions. You could only pass it on to an only child. Your son. Me. And I could only pass it on to an only child.

“After passing it through 4,900 generations, the curse would be fully dispelled. With each transfer, the curse would weaken until it eventually disappeared. That is why, for the sake of the Fifth Star Ring, you chose to take the godbane and use that magic... to transfer it to me and enter a state of slumber.
