But he knew that if he was fighting when it happened, or if someone interrupted the process, he would have a hard time defending himself.

He hadn’t been planning to interrupt Sir Star Ring’s breakthrough. He figured it would be best for both of them to break through before worrying about fighting. But apparently... Sir Star Ring wasn’t going to let that happen.

“Fine then,” Xu Qing growled, his eyes icy. “I won’t allow you to break through.” Lifting his right hand, he pushed it gently in the direction of Sir Star Ring. “Be expelled.”

The fifth world rumbled loudly, and the wind became a tempest. As the world rumbled, the vortexes all started rotating. It was as if countless eyes had suddenly opened. A terrifying force of expulsion erupted. And it landed... right on Sir Star Ring!

Sir Star Ring was stunned, and he wanted to fight back. But the terrifying power was beyond his ability to resist. An instant later... he started blurring. And then he just vanished. He had been expelled from the fifth world. After he was gone, the force of expulsion went away and everything returned to normal.

As for the Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors, their desire to see a dramatic scene play out in front of them died. All of them suddenly felt the need to take the situation very seriously.

“He owns the place?”

“He has seniority!”

“This guy has power over the immortal palace!”

Xu Qing didn’t have time to judge the reactions. Before leaving, Young Lord Aurora had given him ownership of the immortal palace. Theoretically speaking, he should be able to expel anyone he wanted once he was in a given world. After expelling Sir Star Ring, he sat down cross-legged, closed his eyes, and immersed himself in his ninth extreme.

The ninth extreme was the extreme of parallelism. It seemed to Xu Qing that this extreme was like the primordial sand he had found in the Desert of Time. Each and every movement became individual timelines and instances of space-time. Theoretically speaking, there was no limit to the versions of space-time that could be produced in that way.

They were real. But at the same time, they were unreal. At the same time, they were also doors. By means of those doors, he could connect to versions of himself from different space-times, and could share thoughts with them. Unify them, and that was the ninth extreme.[2]

You could call it the overlapping of parallel universes.

Suddenly, the fifth world rippled as Sir Star Ring appeared, forming out of the void.

“You—” he howled.

He only got out one word. Xu Qing, not bothering to even look at him, waved his hand to repeat the expelling process. Ripples flowed out, and the furious Sir Star Ring, who had just been stepping into the fifth world, was once again thrown out. He left behind only the echoing remains of the one word he had spoken.

Xu Qing closed his eyes and circulated the ninth extreme within him. He linked space-times, expanding the effect, until his ninth world bloomed like a dazzling flower.

Then he unified all the worlds! Nine worlds intersected, and Xu Qing’s cultivation base skyrocketed. His aura and energy shot upward. It caused ripples, which quickly turned into something like a vortex. As it spun and spun, Xu Qing sat cross-legged in the center of it. And his soul... manifested externally!

In the Imperial Sovereign level, one formed an immortal embryo. When it was complete, one became a Quasi-Immortal!

It was divided into three phases, which were the illusory reality, the undying, and the immortal embryo!

In the illusory reality, the soul came out of the body, covering the physical body and becoming what was called the real body. Because it was made of a soul, it was illusory. But because there was also a real body, it was called... illusory reality.

Xu Qing’s entire person radiated dazzling light. As his soul emerged, it looked almost like the statue of a buddha. He sat cross-legged, like a giant, shining with boundless light like a divine being.

Imperial Sovereigns were the cultivator system’s version of the Godfire level. Of course, Xu Qing’s version of the illusory reality was a bit different from other Imperial Sovereigns. It very quickly transformed from being blurry to clear, which was the hallmark of the great circle of illusory reality. At the same time, a majestic power that surpassed Smoldering Gods erupted within him.

He had reached Imperial Sovereign in one step!

***

Outside of the immortal palace, beyond the Fifth Star Ring, and separated by a boundless starry sky was... the Ninth Star Ring!

In the Revered Ancient mainland, in Sea-Sealing County, there was a phoenix palace underground, where Plumdark was in seclusion....

A figure sat cross-legged nearby, surrounded by shocking godly light. It was Xu Qing’s old god clone. The moment his immortal body stepped into Imperial Sovereign, their mysterious connection caused the god clone’s godly authority to glitter. There was a resonance between this god and this immortal!

Off to the side, Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior looked stunned. Inside the phoenix hall, Plumdark’s eyelashes quivered.

In the imperial palace of humankind, Empress Summer Departure looked in the direction of Sea-Sealing County.

Another person looked in that same direction. Beneath Revered Ancient in the ancient world where the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk were sealed, Erniu was frantically running along. His head was currently the size of a small mountain. He looked to be in very bad shape, but his eyes glittered brightly as he ran along and laughed uproariously.

I hit the jackpot. The jackpot! I could tell at a glance that this thingie is delicious. Granted, īt’s a bit tough. I just need to find a good spot to crack īt open.

As he ran along salivating, he was about to check his surroundings to look for a good place to eat the item he had taken. That was when he sensed something strange happening. He looked up, whereupon his eyes went wide.

Holy crap! Little Ah Qing must have eaten something amazing. How could he be breaking through so soon??

1. I have selectively edited out some text here that claimed Sir Star Ring had never seen Xu Qing’s true facial features in the fourth world. Except, he did, in chapter 1171. ☜

2. In English, “space-time” is an uncountable noun, similar to “traffic.” You generally do not use the word “traffics” in English. That is why I have been saying things like “instance/version of space-time.” However, the author uses the term as a countable noun. After a while, it gets tedious to say version/instance of space-time, so going forward, I will use it like a countable noun in many cases. ☜

The Imperial Sovereign level was all about the process of forming the immortal embryo. With an immortal embryo and a corresponding canon, one could step into the level of the Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor. After, the immortal embryo would become a mature immortal, and canon would become a tributary, and the Quasi-Immortal would become a Lower Immortal!

Countless cultivators dreamed of reaching those three levels. But it was extremely rare for people to actually succeed. Every major level was like a brutal elimination process. Each step along the way required destined opportunities and good fortune. You also need to build up impressive reserve powers.

What was more, because the Fifth Star Ring had outlawed gods, cultivators didn’t really have any natural predators. That was why there were more Imperial Sovereigns than in places like Revered Ancient. But if you looked at them as a proportion of the cultivator population in general, they were still rare.

In the Revered Ancient mainland, gods still wreaked havoc. Mutagen was everywhere, and life was hard. Even when it was in its heyday, the cultivator population there didn’t come close to the Fifth Star Ring. As a result, there were very few Imperial Sovereigns there.

The three phases of the level didn’t just require an impressive canon. It also required significant power from the star ring itself to act as nutrients for the immortal embryo to eventually become a mature immortal.

Xu Qing had been aware of that for a while now. Now, as he was breaking through, he was fully aware of the advantages and disadvantages he had. In the Smoldering God level, his canon had been strong, but his fleshly body had been a weakness.... He was now facing a similar situation in the Imperial Sovereign level.

The reason I was able to come into the fifth world, which is normally for Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors, is my canon. The ninth extreme, that of parallel overlapping universes, is comparable to a Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor’s canon in the great circle. But it’s definitely not anywhere close to being a tributary.

As far as I’m concerned, when it comes to the Imperial Sovereign level, and even the Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor level, what I lack... is the immortal embryo, and its eventual mature form. What I have to do next is acquire more star ring power, which is really the origin power of a higher star ring. With that as nutrients, I should be able to rapidly mature my immortal embryo.

As for canon... I can’t give up on that. If I want to become a Lower Immortal, then my canon is lacking. What I need... is the tenth extreme!

As Xu Qing sat cross-legged, he sensed his cultivation base fluctuations, and at the same time, analyzed everything that had happened so far, and used that to speculate about the future. He had no idea what the tenth extreme was going to be. He didn’t even have a direction to pursue. At least he knew where his weaknesses lay.

I’m strong enough to fight a Quasi-Immortal. But because of the process of creating the immortal embryo, my fleshly body is as weak as an Imperial Sovereign. If I actually faced Quasi-Immortal power, it would be a problem.

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment.

An assassin?

Eyes gleaming, he cleared his thoughts and looked off into the void. There were ripples in the spot he was looking at. They were aggressive ripples, and they seemed to indicate that someone was trying to force their way into the fifth world.

Xu Qing knew exactly who it was. But....

He broke through on the outside?

He looked apathetically at the spot with the ripples. Gradually, a shape grew more distinct, and Sir Star Ring appeared. Instantly, the might of a Quasi-Immortal erupted around him.

“Xu Qing!!” he howled furiously. His eyes were completely bloodshot as he glared at Xu Qing. He really had achieved a breakthrough! There hadn’t been any other choice. After being expelled multiple times, he knew that he couldn’t possibly reach his goal of breaking through in the fifth world. He had no choice but to do it outside. Unfortunately, becoming a Quasi-Immortal in that manner was not ideal.

The killing intent within him grew even stronger than before. He wanted nothing more than to slaughter Xu Qing.

Upon sensing the killing intent and seeing Sir Star Ring’s bloodshot eyes, Xu Qing coolly said, “I’ve been waiting for you for a while now.”

As those words swept through the fifth world, a screaming wind kicked up, which sent out space-time fluctuations. The fluctuations reverberated in front of and behind Sir Star Ring, as well as to his left and right. They reverberated in his past, present, and future. They reverberated everywhere!

Xu Qing eyes glittered like heavenly bodies, as if the light of space-time was flowing within them.

To him, Sir Star Ring didn’t look like a single, unique entity. Xu Qing saw... countless versions of space-time, and in every one of them was Sir Star Ring, just in a different state. In some cases he was insane. In others, he laughed coldly. In yet others, he was silent, vicious, or in pain.... There were countless space-times, and countless Sir Star Rings. Xu Qing took them all in.

Of course ‘seeing’ was just the first step. The second was influencing. Xu Qing could clearly sense that he was able to influence, not just Sir Star Ring, but the space-time he was in. If his canon were at a higher level... he could truly erase him from existence. He could erase all versions of him, along with his karma, fate, and reincarnations....

That sensation made Xu Qing think back to what Yu Liuchen had told him about True Gods. The reasons True Gods always came back was because of thēir undying names. Even if thēy were killed, as long as there existed a memory of thēm, thēy could use that as a symbol to return to.[1]

Back then, Xu Qing didn’t quite understand what that meant. He just knew that True Gods were terrifying, and that there were too many unknowns regarding thēm. But now... he understood. When a True God came back, they were not the same as before. And that was because... what came back after thēir death wouldn’t be the actual god, but rather, a manifestation of that god from another space-time.

Sadly, my immortal embryo is still in the illusory reality phase, and my ninth extreme hasn’t reached the limit. So at the moment, I can’t influence all of the space-times.

Xu Qing lifted his right hand, pointed it toward Sir Star Ring, and opened it wide.

Sir Star Ring was currently looking directly at Xu Qing, and his heart was pounding. The look in Xu Qing’s eyes caused him to shiver down to the depths of his being. He even stopped breathing, as a sensation of deadly crisis erupted within him. It felt like someone was seeing every aspect of him. They could see his karma, his fate, his reincarnations, and thus... he instinctively felt immense crisis.

All of a sudden, a host of chains appeared around Sir Star Ring, and the terrifying power of his Quasi-Immortal cultivation base erupted. He was about to launch an attack....

Xu Qing closed his hand. “Infinite Timelessness!”

As the words echoed out and his hand closed into a fist... the various space-times that had appeared around Sir Star Ring rumbled loudly and unleashed an explosion of disorder. The explosions instantly reached a peak of intensity, transforming into a space-time tempest. Xu Qing had used Infinite Timelessness before, but could only unleash disorder. But now... with command of his ninth extreme, things were different.

Next, Xu Qing opened his fist and waved his hand, and the disorderly space-time tempest swept about like an angry wave. And it engulfed... Sir Star Ring and nine of the versions of space-time around him. Nine versions of Sir Star Ring were engulfed by the tempest, causing their fleshly bodies to wither up, and eroding the chains of order around them.

All of this seemed to indicate... that all of those instances of order had become a thing of the past in the timescape. Of the nine Sir Star Rings, three screamed as their bodies collapsed into dust, leaving behind only immortal embryos. They wouldn’t last for long, though, and were currently trembling violently.

The other six versions found the space-time around them crumbling. Their experience was affecting the real world, as Sir Star Ring was currently coughing up blood, and his body was withering.

This was Quasi-Immortal battle prowess! It could influence immortal embryos! No matter how dazzling a canon was, if it couldn’t do anything to an immortal embryo, then it wasn’t considered Quasi-Immortal battle prowess.

Different canons influenced things in different ways. In parallelism space-time, the fluctuations were parallel overlapping universes. It required the destruction of multiple space-times to affect the real world.

For example, if Li Mengtu were in this situation, then after his poison reached a certain level, his attacks would affect the body in the real world.

It was the same with Sir Star Ring. That was especially true considering he had achieved a breakthrough and become a Quasi-Immortal. Although it wasn’t the perfect breakthrough from what he could tell, his battle prowess was definitely extraordinary. He couldn’t see other space-times, but he could sense that his immortal embryo was being damaged. And he... had to launch a counterattack!

Countless chains of order whipped out, glowing with golden light. And they quickly converged into a tool. It was a scale! On one side was Sir Star Ring, while on the other side was Xu Qing! Above order, there was... balance!

The moment it appeared, there was an instant, mysterious connection! When that connection occurred, the intangible tempest Xu Qing had summoned weighed down on the scale, causing it to become unbalanced....

Because of the imbalance, a majestic force swept out of the void, landing on Sir Star Ring, gathering, becoming more boundless, until... balance was restored! It was like he was borrowing power! When Sir Star Ring became a Quasi-Immortal, his canon transformed.

The stronger his enemy was, the more outside power he could borrow. And it would eventually turn into a majestic, crushing force!

This canon caused Xu Qing’s eyes to glitter. “Interesting.... I guess we’ll have to see who reaches their limit first, you or me.”

Inside of himself, he plucked at his ninth extreme like a string on a musical instrument. The infinite timelessness caused by the space-time tempest surged toward the rest of Sir Star Ring’s space-times. In the blink of an eye, it devoured 11 of them. Then 12, 13, 14....

An imbalance resulted, only to be followed by another balance. Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed, and the tempest raged. 18 space-times had now been swept up. He was definitely using this fight to hone his canon.

Sir Star Ring eventually reached his limit when Xu Qing had swept up the 21st space-time. At that point, the scale... collapsed into nothing.

Xu Qing stood. 21 space-times wasn’t his limit. He could now see that if he fully unleashed his ninth extreme, he could cause fluctuations in space-time that would reach the level of about 50.

Sir Star Ring was coughing up blood like mad, and his immortal embryo was covered in wounds. He staggered backward. Inside, he was full of many complicated thoughts. He knew that he was in a disadvantageous position now. For one thing, his opponent’s canon was too strong. But also, he had not achieved a perfect breakthrough.

“Xu Qing, you’re definitely strong. But you have one obvious weakness. Your immortal embryo... is in the phase of illusory reality!”

Sir Star Ring lurched to a halt and looked up, his eyes full of killing intent.

1. Yu Liuchen talked about True Gods coming back in chapter 998. ☜

Outside of the immortal palace, and beyond the Fifth Star Ring’s western region... was the eastern planetary system.

At the highest point there was a collection of 1,000,000 pagodas. Even viewed from a distance, the pagodas seemed to go on forever. The pagodas glittered as if with starlight, and were organized in such a way that they apparently corresponded to actual heavenly bodies in the starry sky. What was more, all of the pagodas were connected to each other by a network of chains that represented order.

Located in the very middle of the 1,000,000 pagodas, there was one specific pagoda that was taller than all the others, whose radiant starlight illuminated the sky overhead. This was one of the most prominent pagodas in the entire star ring.

An old man in a daoist robe stood in that pagoda, his hands clasped behind his back as he stared off in the direction of the west. He had the demeanor of a transcendent being, with flowing white hair and eyes that seemed to contain the cyclings of the universe itself.

He was none other than the Pagoda Lord of the Star Ring Pagoda! And he was the Lower Immortal who was entrusted with guarding the east! He was also... Sir Star Ring’s Master!

“Sir Star Ring is fated to endure the Sun Lord Tribulation! That type of tribulation didn’t exist in the past. But a few years ago, it suddenly appeared.... Like the sudden arrival of an assassin, it restrains the fate of the sun lord. If he passes the tribulation, he will achieve the dao of the great rising sun of the east.”

The old man performed an incantation gesture with his right hand, and then... his eyes glittered. “If there are no twists and turns during the tribulation, then how could good fortune spring from extreme adversity? Sir Star Ring must accept the tribulation!”

***

Tribulation had come!

In the immortal palace’s fifth world, Sir Star Ring shook from head to toe. His five yin organs and six yang organs were in chaos. Coughing up a massive mouthful of blood, he staggered backward seven paces. Every step he took caused starlight to glitter around him.

Within him, determination surged. He was Sir Star Ring, the number one chosen in the eastern planetary system. And he was publicly recognized to be number one in his generation in the entire Fifth Star Ring. It was correct to say that he had lived a life of brilliance and glory. Whether because of his family background or his success in cultivation, he was a superstar.

His Master had arranged for him to inherit the Star Ring name from the Star Ring Pagoda, all to further his dao. And his Master had also arranged for Sir Vilespirit and Zhou Zhengli to be whetstones for him to hone his abilities.

Before meeting Xu Qing, his fate, his destiny, and his path had all been unobstructed. He didn’t have any misfortune to deal with. But then he met Xu Qing, and had been stymied at every turn. It was the case with his attempt to maintain order in the fourth world, as well as his attempted breakthrough in the fifth world. In fact, it had reached the point where he was starting to think that all of it had been foreordained.

And yet, even as that feeling rose within him... Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered with cold light, all as a sharp blade within him cut away such thoughts, smashed any barriers, and destroyed thoughts of foreordination.

I’m in control of my life! he thought. He looked at Xu Qing, and the aura of a Quasi-Immortal built within him. The power of a Grand Emperor surged as countless chains appeared out of nowhere all around him. The sense of order was inimitably intense. He still had one move left....

The moment he stepped into the Quasi-Immortal level, he gained enlightenment of the balance that came when he upgraded his canon of order. And during that process, he had extracted something from within his life force. It was a measure of... law!

And that law had a name.

“Heaven’s principle!” Sir Star Ring said, reaching out with his right hand and making a grasping gesture. When he spoke, his words resonated like the sounds of heaven. “Come here!”[1]

A ripple spread through the fifth world as Xu Qing took a step forward, then stopped in place, his eyes gleaming. He had just sensed that there was something different about Sir Star Ring compared to earlier.

Earlier, he had perceived Sir Star Ring with great clarity. But now... he was blurry. And it wasn’t just Sir Star Ring himself, but also the space-time surrounding him. His past, present, and future, as well as all of his parallels, all became blurry at the same time.

A sense of great danger erupted inside Xu Qing. And the source... was Sir Star Ring’s invisible hand! Astonishingly, there was a mote in that hand, something that resembled a speck of dust! The moment Xu Qing spotted it, his heart raced. He suddenly had the sense that he was facing the entire starry sky. It could not be defied or seized!

The Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors who were watching the events play out were visibly taken aback.

“Is that...?”

“Heaven’s principle??”

“Very impressive of Sir Star Ring!”

The canon of order could be upgraded to balance. By commanding the canon of balance, Sir Star Ring could walk the path of the Quasi-Immortal. But after breaking out of Quasi-Immortal and stepping into Lower Immortal, balance wouldn’t be enough. Sir Star Ring would need to push his canon of order to the highest peak.

After balance came... heaven’s principle!

However, it shouldn’t have been possible for Sir Star Ring to gain sufficient enlightenment of his canon to push it to the level of heaven's principle. Normally speaking, he would seek enlightenment during the process of transforming his immortal embryo into a mature immortal. It wouldn’t be until the very end that he would have a portion of heaven’s principle! That was when he would become a Lower Immortal! That was the path he should tread going forward.

He shouldn’t have been able to do it now. But he was the number one Shining Star. What was more, he was the only one of the Shining Stars who had not relied on the Senior generation to provide his canon. He had relied only on himself to become the most astounding chosen of the generation. And thus, though seeking heaven’s principle had been difficult, in the moment of his cultivation base breakthrough, he had extracted... a mote of heaven's principle!

That mote was the source of the danger Xu Qing sensed. Sir Star Ring waved his hand, and the mote... descended!

An unstoppable force bore down on Xu Qing! This mote of heaven's principle could bury all things. It could reject your ability to even exist! Xu Qing’s pupils constricted, and the sense of danger within him grew to an incredible level. However, there was no time to formulate a complicated plan.

As the mote descended, it entered Xu Qing’s world and appeared in front of him. It looked like a mote of dust, but it was almost infinitely heavy, and nothing Xu Qing did would enable him to defend against it. Rumbling sounds filled his mind. His fleshly body, unable to sustain the force, began to crumble. The same thing happened to his soul as the mote continued to fall.

Xu Qing struggled to breathe as a sensation of impending death swept over him like tide waters. There was no time for thought or planning. Lunging backward, he left the fifth world, and in fact, he left the immortal palace entirely.

When he reappeared, he was out on the Fallen Immortal Moors. And yet... he was still sinking into death. His life was still draining away. His fleshly body couldn’t last any longer, and it exploded. He existed only in drifting soul form as he shot across the Fallen Immortal Moors along with his canon.

Unfortunately, heaven's principle just couldn’t be stopped. An instant later... Xu Qing’s soul exploded.

As it dissipated, he bitterly thought about the life he had lived. And he thought about how things had gone so poorly in the fourth world. But at least working together with Sir Star Ring, he had managed to maintain order. And that had earned him the right to enter the fifth world. Unfortunately, the destined opportunity he had encountered in the fifth world gave him no choice. Sir Star Ring, who he had considered a friend, ultimately became his greatest enemy.

That was fate. Xu Qing sighed and dispersed into nothing. The space-time around him crumbled before being erased out of existence.

Astonishingly, as that space-time collapsed, another Xu Qing appeared in the immortal palace’s fifth world, and he was currently falling back at high speed. There was still a mote falling down toward him. In the end... he was destroyed in body and soul. Yet the battle still went on. A third Xu Qing appeared, also falling back.

As these scenes played out, the Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors who were watching the fight reacted with strange expressions.

“This person... has space-time canon!”

“He’s taken his space-time canon to such a high level that it’s manifesting as law.”

“He’s using space-time selves to substitute for his true body in death!”

As they saw Sir Star Ring’s mote falling, and Xu Qing using substitutions to meet it, something astonishing suddenly happened. A host of space-time fluctuations suddenly appeared, along with numerous instances of different space-times. And all of those space-times began to eat away at the mote of heaven's principle.

In the blink of an eye, three space-times collapsed. After that, seven of them collapsed. Next, a total of twenty collapsed. As one space-time after another collapsed, the mote of heaven's principle got lighter and lighter. It got blurrier and blurrier. Finally, after forty-six space-times had been destroyed... the mote collapsed into ashes.

The remaining space-times glittered, and within one of them, Xu Qing looked up at Sir Star Ring, his eyes shining.

“This heaven's principle is very impressive....” His heart was already starting to pound from the thought of it.

A bitter look appeared on Sir Star Ring’s face as he heard Xu Qing’s words. He was currently looking at the area surrounding his opponent. Endless space-time fluctuations rolled out. He had no idea how many space-times there were, so he had no idea of what limits his opponent had. What was more, he had no way to know who he was talking to. Was it someone from a different space-time, or was it his true body?

This was the canon of parallelism. The magic of overlapping universes ensured that whenever Xu Qing faced an opponent, he could use a version of himself from another space-time to substitute for him in death.

In theory, he could do it endlessly. But in reality, he had a limit. He was hindered because of his immortal embryo, as well as his opponent’s command of canon. Because of that, he couldn’t go past 54 right now!

What was more, there were downsides to his death substitution magic. The versions of himself from other space-times were actually connected to his true self. They were like secondary versions. And therefore, when they died, it did have an effect on his true body in the real world. He could deal with those effects, and they wouldn’t do anything to his foundation.

But what it meant was that the key to killing Xu Qing was... to destroy all of the space-times he was using, and kill all of the space-time selves. Only then could an opponent truly put an end to Xu Qing.

Speaking calmly from within that instance of space-time, Xu Qing said, “What I’m wondering now is if killing you would allow me to extract that mote of heaven's principle from your life force....”

He extended his hand, and astonishingly, an overflow of sword will spilled out, transforming into... The Emperor’s Sword! I wasn’t just a single version of The Emperor’s Sword. All of the Xu Qing’s in the other surrounding space-times also extended their hands and summoned the sword. Then all of them slashed forth!

It was impossible to tell which of them was in the real world. And it wasn’t possible to identify which stream of sword energy was real and which was illusory. The streams of sword energy slashed out of their respective space-times, then converged in the fifth world, forming an astonishing and deadly sword that shot toward Sir Star Ring.

In the blink of an eye, they slashed right through him! After going through him, the remaining sword energy tore open a huge hole in the air behind him. As for Sir Star Ring, he shivered from head to toe, and then his body... collapsed and turned into ashes.

All of the space-times began to vanish, and all the other versions of Xu Qing, including the one who had just been speaking, blurred.

That was when the real Xu Qing stepped out of the depths of one of the space-times, and hovered in front of the spot where Sir Star Ring had died. His gaze hardened. He did not sense any change to his Immortal Capital permission medallion.

Not dead?

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed, yet he didn’t look very surprised. This was the number one Shining Star, and he had just experienced a breakthrough. It was no stretch of the imagination to assume he would have astonishing life-saving abilities.

But I still want that mote of heaven's principle....

He reached out and made a grasping motion backed by space-time. The spot where Sir Star Ring had died rippled, and then a stream of energy flew from it into Xu Qing’s hand.

It was a scrap of energy, evidence left behind by Sir Star Ring that could be used to track him. After taking a moment to study it, Xu Qing’s eyes flashed coldly.

“He’s not far off!”

1. The term “heaven’s principle” or perhaps “heavenly principles” is a real-life term used by Neo-Confucian philosophers to explain the universe. Another dictionary definition is “natural order,” and I was even tempted to translate it as that. Considering that Sir Star Ring was on the side of “order,” it makes sense. However, the characters are completely different from those I’ve been translating as “order,” and I don’t want to create a false character connection. So I will stick with ‘heaven’s principle.’ ☜

Sir Star Ring really wasn’t very far away. The moment Xu Qing cut down Sir Star Ring in the fifth world, a blurry figure appeared at the entrance of the immortal palace, right past the immortal foyer. This was one of the three paths leading to the immortal palace. Back at the beginning of the event, Xu Qing had looked at this location and just barely seen the bridge in the mist. The mist was currently seething as the figure staggered back from that spot and onto the immortal foyer.

Staggering, he coughed up a massive mouthful of blood onto the limestone. His chest heaved as he struggled to breathe. He looked like someone who had just barely escaped from catastrophe with his life.

He was none other than Sir Star Ring. His aura was in shambles, and he looked extremely weak. In fact, it seemed that nearly half of his body existed in a state between real and illusory.

“Xu Qing...” Sir Star Ring’s expression was grim as he sped toward the exit. He was leaving the immortal palace.

The moment he appeared in the Fallen Immortal Moors, he saw a host of people seated cross-legged in the area. Glancing at them, he spotted Li Mengtu as well as Zhou Zhengli.

The seated cultivators sensed his gaze. That was especially true of Li Mengtu and Zhou Zhengli, who looked up at him. Li Mengtu’s gaze hardened. Zhou Zhengli looked thoughtful.

Sir Star Ring didn’t hesitate for an instant. He walked out, flew up into the air, and raced toward the horizon. He held nothing back in terms of speed. When he reached the border of the Fallen Immortal Moors, he turned to look back at the immortal palace. His body was already reverting from its state of half-illusory into being fully real.

That was the result of the lifesaving skill he had used, which was a secret magic of the Star Ring Pagoda. By sacrificing some of his dao, he could create a version of the Star Ring Pagoda to substitute for him in death. In that way, he could avert deadly crises. Over the years, he had made seven Star Ring Pagodas to serve in that capacity.

I can’t believe I had to waste one just now....

When he thought back to what had played out in the fifth world, he felt fear inside of him, and had to admit that his opponent’s understanding of canon... surpassed his own by a lot.

Whether in terms of deadliness or stealthiness, his canon is terrifying! If I want to crush him, I need to improve my own canon to the point of being able to destroy all of his space-times. Otherwise... it would be just too difficult to kill him. Unless....

Sir Star Ring’s eyes glittered. The only other option would be to figure out how to crush his true body with heaven’s principle! His biggest weakness... is definitely his true body! He has an Imperial Sovereign cultivation base, and his immortal embryo is still forming. That means that the best option is to figure out how to identify his true body amidst the various space-times.... In other words, there definitely is a way to kill him!

Ultimately, Sir Star Ring shook his head. Theories were, in the end, nothing but theories. Besides, Sir Star Ring knew... that he wasn’t in the position to succeed right now.

He took a deep breath and then vanished into thin air. He had no idea of knowing whether his opponent would try to track him down, but he still felt a sensation of danger. He needed to get out of the western planetary system as quickly as possible and get back to the east. Only there would he truly be safe.

***

Meanwhile, in the immortal palace’s fifth world, Xu Qing looked at the scrap of energy in his hand. After a moment, he squeezed it into another instance of space-time, then looked at the surrounding Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors.

Without a word, he took a step forward. He blurred. But then he reverted back to being clear.

I can’t get into the sixth world.

Although he knew that no one with battle prowess weaker than a Lower Immortal was supposed to be able to get into the sixth world, he figured he might as well do a test. After confirming that he couldn’t get into the sixth world, he took another step forward... but not to try to get into the sixth world. He was going back outside. He vanished, and when he reappeared he was on the immortal foyer.

At the moment, there are no more destined opportunities for me in the immortal palace.

As he stood on the immortal foyer, he looked back at the immortal palace. A host of images played out in his memories. It was as if the River of Time was rumbling past, sweeping up the sand from the bottom of the river.

For a moment, Xu Qing felt like he could see a young man in white clothing. He stood at the very end of that river of the timescape, a marriage contract in his hand. Standing next to him was a young woman in a wedding dress. Both of them looked at him, smiled, and then held hands as they bowed to him.

Their smiles contained indescribable reminiscence. Perhaps they were smiles of youth. Or maybe they were smiles of bitterness, or beauty, or pain. The froth of the raging river filled the image.

Xu Qing turned his head and saw himself standing at the end of the timescape river. He smiled and bowed. The wind and rain from yesterday echoed into today. The flowing river, and the sand that glittered like starlight, eventually dissipated.

Xu Qing straightened from his bow, turned, and walked off of the immortal foyer... and out of the exit.

Out in the Fallen Immortal Moors, he looked up into the sky and saw the crimson aurora. Because of the aurora, the scenery in the area was red, just like before. However, something about it seemed different now. In the past it had been many-colored, but now it was just red. However, the light seemed to be gentler. It seemed to contain the love of a father.

Xu Qing closed his eyes to experience the feeling. When he opened his eyes shortly after, he saw the crowd that was gathered outside the immortal palace. He saw Patriarch Diling, Li Mengtu, Zhou Zhengli, and other cultivators he recognized.

Most of the people who had come out of the immortal palace had chosen to stay behind until the immortal palace event concluded. The receding of the spirit tide that would mark the end of the event would provide opportunities to further their cultivation and seek enlightenment. After all, most of them were only able to operate in the third world, and though most had benefited in some way, their gains were limited.

Clearly, everyone present was hoping to benefit additionally, including Li Mengtu and Zhou Zhengli.

Li Mengtu had a complicated expression on his face, and it looked like he wanted to say something to Xu Qing. The events of the fourth world had affected him deeply, and at the moment, he wasn’t sure if he was himself or Zhong Chi....

Zhou Zhengli looked a lot more calm and collected than Li Mengtu. He was not thinking about the reflected version of history and how it related to the real world. To him, the most important thing was to take advantage of the moment to continue his relationship with Xu Qing, and make sure that it developed into the future. That was truer than ever considering he had seen how badly Sir Star Ring was injured when he came out. And he had noted how Sir Star Ring fled so quickly.

Therefore, when Xu Qing looked at him, he hurried forward. When he reached Xu Qing, he acted in the same manner he had in the fourth world.

Bowing very respectfully, he said, “Young Lord, congratulations on your cultivation breakthrough. In one fell swoop, you have become the number one Shining Star!”

Xu Qing looked at Zhou Zhengli. “This isn’t the reflection of history.”

Zhou Zhengli shook his head. “The person who won me over wasn’t Young Lord Aurora.”

Xu Qing looked deeply at Zhou Zhengli.

Meanwhile, Patriarch Diling flew over, bowed deeply, and excitedly said, “Welcome back, Senior! I was waiting in anxious anticipation this whole time. After all the kindness you showed me, I was very worried about your safety in the fourth world. Sadly, my cultivation base is too weak, so I couldn’t go to the fourth world to help you. Now that you’re back safely, I can finally rest at ease.

“Now I can see that you are truly a genius among geniuses, someone who plans out everything meticulously in advance. Presumably, you had already considered all of the challenges you would face in the fourth world. And thus, I had to wait out here, wondering how things would turn out. Clearly, things went very smoothly for you!

“Finally, Senior, I would like to thank you for saving my life. Your actions in the immortal palace are going to make you extremely famous. Congratulations on the glory you will enjoy going forward as one of the Shining Stars!”

Off to the side, Zhou Zhengli looked on with raised eyebrows. Even the shadow beneath Xu Qing’s feet seemed shaken by Patriarch Diling’s praise.

Before anything else could happen, ripples flowed through the sky above. The crimson aurora glittered more brightly than ever, and thunderous sounds as if from beyond the heavens rang out.

It wasn’t just the sky over the immortal palace that was affected.... The sky over the west filled with rumbling. The same happened in the east, south, and north. It was as if some enormous, invisible hand had lifted back the sky over the Fifth Star Ring, revealing a huge starry sky. Some of the stars were bright, others were dim. And that was because each star corresponded to a specific cultivator in the Fifth Star Ring. They were... reflected versions of the Immortal Capital permission medallions!

All of the cultivators in the Fallen Immortal Moors looked up in surprise. They weren’t the only ones. Vast numbers of cultivators throughout the Fifth Star Ring also looked up. It was because....

Zhou Zhengli’s eyes glittered as he said, “The third and final phase of the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt is going to start!”

This phase was about fighting, and it was an elimination phase! The arrival of the third phase meant that the final rankings were going to be established! All cultivators with permission medallions found that their medallions were shining brightly.

Xu Qing was no exception. At the same time, the sound of killing drums echoed through heaven and earth. The thumping was like heavenly thunder.

The cultivators who had been working on their cultivation outside the immortal palace all got to their feet and began to leave.

Zhou Zhengli took a deep breath and bowed to Xu Qing again. “Young Lord, it’s a foregone conclusion that you’ll make it to the Immortal Capital. But I have a lot of work to do if I want to catch up and make it there with you! Going forward, everyone with an Immortal Capital permission medallion needs to focus fully on the trial.”

With that, Zhou Zhengli shot up into the starry sky above.

Zhou Zhengli was gone, as was almost everyone else. At that point, Li Mengtu finally approached.

Sounding somewhat awkward, he said, “Er... when Hordeslayer and Rampart came out, they were both trying to flee faster than the other.... But based on what I could sense, their auras weren’t much different than they were in the fourth world. I suspect the events there affected them out here in the real world.

“As for me, I’ve experienced some changes to my canon. I never saw Sir Vilespirit. I think he was one of the first to come out, and he left immediately. Yuanshan Su had a strange look on her face when she left. I... have to go do some training. I definitely need to improve my permission medallion ranking. Young L... er, would you like to come along?”

Xu Qing smiled and shook his head. Lifting his hand, he revealed the swirling scrap of Sir Star Ring’s energy.

Li Mengtu’s gaze hardened. “Are you going—?”

“Sir Star Ring has something of mine. I’m going to go retrieve it.” With that, Xu Qing shot toward the horizon.

The spirit tide in the Fallen Immortal Moors had not yet fully disappeared. And that was because the good fortune and destined opportunities of the immortal palace were not over. It was only over for the first five worlds. The Quasi-Immortals were still attempting to get into the sixth world.

Therefore, when Xu Qing reached the horizon, he hovered in the air looking back at the immortal palace. He could just barely make out a sound like crashing waves. A tremor passed through him. Because of his ownership of the immortal palace, he knew what had just happened.

Someone just entered the sixth world!

His eyes glittered brightly. Only someone with Lower Immortal battle prowess could step into the sixth world. There were destined opportunities for Lower Immortals in the immortal palace.

Either some unknown Lower Immortal got into the immortal palace, or... one of the Quasi-Immortals experienced a breakthrough. It’s too bad that, though I own the immortal palace, my cultivation base limits me, and my canon isn’t sufficient. I really have no way to get into the sixth world.

He shook his head sadly, but at the same time, wasn’t anxious. Now that he owned the place, all he had to do was wait until he did qualify, and he could come back and enter.

Once my immortal embryo is complete and I’ve gained enlightenment of my tenth extreme, I can return. I wonder what the sixth world is like....

Taking a deep breath, he shot off into the distance. Soon he was outside of the Fallen Immortal Moors.

The star chart in the sky that showed all the Immortal Capital permission medallions was gone. The crimson aurora was back. However, because the third round of the trial had begun, cultivators with permission medallions could now sense each other even more keenly than before. What was more, it was now possible to access the star chart in the permission medallion at any time!

It was now the perfect time to fight and rob others! That was why the third round was such a brutal affair. Of course, there were ways of masking one’s permission medallion, though not many people knew how. Clearly, Sir Star Ring was one of them.

Xu Qing found that out quickly when he sent his divine will into the medallion and couldn’t find the star representing Sir Star Ring anywhere on the star chart. It actually wasn’t a big surprise to him. Sir Star Ring wouldn’t make a mistake as obvious as that.

Xu Qing, meanwhile, could use the aura of the violet crystal to cover his permission medallion and keep it hidden. That would ensure that things would go smoothly.

And now to start tracking him down....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. He lifted his hand, and the scrap of Sir Star Ring’s energy that Xu Qing had extracted from space-time appeared. It seemed to pulse as he absorbed it into his divine will. A moment later, he knew which direction to go in, and he flew off.

Time went by. Xu Qing could move very quickly. Unfortunately, so could Sir Star Ring. Sir Star Ring’s cultivation base surpassed Xu Qing’s. However, using his substitution secret magic to avoid death had weakened him. As a result, Sir Star Ring was limited, and couldn’t put very much distance between himself and Xu Qing. Nor could he prevent Xu Qing from locking onto him and tracking him down. Thus, three days passed.

As Xu Qing continued his pursuit, a majestic desert eventually appeared within his senses.

It was... the Desert of Time. This was his third time seeing this desert. The first was when he had been traveling with Yunmen Qianfan. The second time was in the reflection of history, when he was with Immortal Lord Aurora. This was his third time.

Xu Qing landed at the edge of the desert, his heart astir as he stared at it for a short time. Then he walked inside. The sandy wind screamed along, as if it were telling an ancient story. The sand churned as if it were preparing to open the curtain.

As Xu Qing walked through the desert, he could sense the space-time fluctuations, and could hear the story being told. He proceeded on his way. His canon was now advanced enough that he could clearly see the space-time in the desert.

In fact, he was easily able to find the exact spot that Immortal Lord Aurora had taken him to. He stopped walking. He gazed about....

In the reflected history he had experienced, this place had once been the location of a beautiful, colorful sea of flowers. The flowers looked like dancing butterflies, or perhaps like graceful immortal cranes. And every single one exuded a fragrance like perfume.

They... had been planted personally by Immortal Lord Aurora. It was because his wife... had loved orchids. On this very spot, Immortal Lord Aurora had told his son... that he should come back every year to plant more flowers. Eventually, the entire Desert of Time would become a sea of flowers. But now....

Xu Qing saw no life here. The sea of flowers had long since ceased to exist. Yet Xu Qing smiled. And that was because he saw more than the lack of life. Right in the middle of the spot where the sea of flowers had long since withered away, he could see two little flowers that had been planted recently.

The two little flowers were alive and growing. They swayed in the wind, and when they rubbed against each other, they let off a fragrant aroma. Xu Qing could envision Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, right here, planting the two flowers. And he could hear the voice of Immortal Lord Aurora, echoing out of the reflection of history, and drifting along with the wind into Xu Qing’s ears.

“Remember to come back here every year and plant some more orchids for your mother. Let’s make sure this place always stays a sea of flowers.”

Xu Qing squatted down, extracted a flower seed from space-time, and planted it. He bowed.

He was certain that more flowers would appear in the years to come. And eventually, the sea of flowers would come back, and the Desert of Time would become the Flower Sea of Time. The gentle light from the crimson aurora shone down onto the orchids. The light from above wasn’t golden like it had been when Xu Qing visited as Young Lord Aurora. But there was still a dreamlike romance to the place.

And there was a fragrance that lingered on Xu Qing. Perhaps that fragrance provided a blessing, because only three days after leaving the desert, Xu Qing found a cave in the wilderness where the wounded Sir Star Ring was hiding.

Sir Star Ring was hurt so badly that he couldn’t keep up a sustained flight from Xu Qing. He had eventually been forced to hole up in this place, surrounded by protective spell formations, and focus on healing. Sadly for him, Xu Qing showed up and interrupted him. And thus, fighting broke out in the wilderness.

Xu Qing had been able to ‘kill’ Sir Star Ring even when he was at his peak, so there was little need to mention how it turned out now that Sir Star Ring was so badly wounded. The fight was quick and violent. It didn’t last long. And it ended with Sir Star Ring dying a second time!

But this time, it caused Xu Qing to frown deeply as he looked at the spot where Sir Star Ring was crumbling into ashes.

He came here and purposely waited to die.... He wanted to use this opportunity to prevent me from tracking him.

The energy Xu Qing had taken from him was now gone. And there was nothing left in space-time for him to make up for it. He now had no way to lock onto Sir Star Ring, and no way to track him down.

Well, that’s just what I would expect of the number one Shining Star. Despite the predicament he’s in, he managed to shake my pursuit.

Xu Qing looked off into the distance.

However.... He still needs to get back to the east. And if he wants to leave the western planetary system, he can pick from different paths. But there’s only one that could be considered the safest....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he looked in the direction of the God Blood River. One of the unique things about the God Blood River were the ferry pilots. If you could get onto a ferry boat, then according to the rules of the ferry pilots, you were completely and utterly safe. And the person responsible for your safety was the ferry pilot.

It didn’t matter who was chasing you, once you were under the protection of a ferry pilot, no one could do anything to you. At the same time, you could use the time spent on the journey to focus on healing and recovery. For the most part, it was only possible to cross the river three times in your life. For the majority of cultivators, crossing one or two times was the limit of what they could accept.

If I can realize that, so can others.

After some thought, Xu Qing started moving in the direction of the God Blood River. One reason was that he was convinced Sir Star Ring was going in the same direction. Since he had lost track of his quarry, it seemed logical to try to intercept him. If it didn’t work... he would just have to wait until later to kill him. They would definitely run into each other eventually.

Another reason he wanted to go to the God Blood River was that Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix had mentioned leaving a gift for him there. Xu Qing had some speculations about what that gift was. But he wasn’t completely sure.

If I’m right about the gift... it’ll be kind of funny if Sir Star Ring actually does choose the river.

With his decision made, he sped off into the distance.

Half a month passed.

Soon Xu Qing arrived at the banks of the God Blood River. The God Blood River was very long, but there was actually only one spot on this branch of it where you could board a ferry boat.

For aeons, the banks of the river had been in contact with the water, and thus, the river banks were as red as blood. It was for the same reason that the wooden pier was also red and corroded. The wind itself sounded like moaning ghosts that could shake one down to the soul.

Xu Qing walked down the crimson river bank and onto the rickety pier. He heard the sound of the wind, and smelled the blood on the air. The river looked like a huge sea of blood. It wasn’t possible to see the other side of the river. All he could see was endless waves, and the river glittering beneath the light of the aurora.

Beneath the crimson sky, and surrounded by what sounded like the wailing of ghosts and howling of wolves... an ancient, pitch-black boat floated across the ghastly river of blood toward him.

The seething river became calm for the boat. The raging wind became docile. It approached as silently as an evil ghost. It neared the pier, and neared Xu Qing.

It was a lone ferry boat. And in the ferry boat... there was no ferry pilot. There was only a woven rush raincoat, a bamboo hat, and a jade slip.

When Xu Qing looked at the jade slip, it shattered, and the voice of Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix filled the area.

“This is my gift to you. There is no karma. There are no restrictions. I have already severed all the karma and removed all the restrictions. I’ve also assumed responsibility for the ferry pilot mission. This ferry boat was constructed personally by my father, and it belongs to you. With it, you can cross the river... without giving up any longevity.”

The God Blood River was made from the blood of all the gods that had been killed in the Fifth Star Ring. It contained the blood of Godfire Gods, Altar Gods, and even quite a few True Gods. There were even multiple God Lords whose blood ended up in the river!

Thus, it was no surprise that the river had very intense mutagen levels, as well as an intense aura of death filled with the rage of gods. The banks of the river suppressed all of that with magical barriers. As a result, the mutagen and rancorous energy couldn’t really spread out into the world.

However... cultivators who entered the water would be infected. If the body and soul were contaminated, then the karma of gods could cause major problems down the line.

It was only Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors who qualified to cross the river without using a ferry boat. Of course, just because they qualified didn’t mean that they would take the risk. The risk was twofold. One part was the possibility of getting contaminated by the mutagen in the river. The other was because there were grues in the river. Over the countless years that had passed, it was impossible to count how many dead gods had contributed to the river, and as such, no one really knew what vile, god-like beings or terrifying entities might exist there. That was why even Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors would be very careful if they had to cross the river.

And unless there was some dire reason, they simply wouldn’t do it on their own. It was almost always best to use a ferry boat. And that was where the ferry pilots came into the picture. Though it seemed like they merely ferried people across the river, the reality was that they also had the job of patrolling the river.

The ferry boats were their main tools! Each boat was a precious treasure specifically designed to deal with gods. Thus, it was only natural that they would be able to suppress the aura on the river. Because of how they operated the boats, patrolled the river, and dealt with the godly entities, the ferry pilots were obviously an integral part of the river. Their work was also part of what they did to atone for the crimes they had committed.

The boat that came to Xu Qing was a gift to him from Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. And it had been specially crafted for her by her father, Immortal Lord Nineshores.

Xu Qing looked at the boat, his eyes gleaming. He knew full well why Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix had given him this boat.

It gives me an avenue of retreat....

The ferry boat gave him a new identity, as a ferry boat operator and someone atoning for crimes. Although he was not a ferry pilot, if he ever did commit some big crimes in the Fifth Star Ring....

Well, this ferry boat crafted by Immortal Lord Nineshores would definitely provide him an avenue of retreat that he could use to save his own life. After some thought, Xu Qing took a deep breath and bowed deeply to the dome of heaven.

Walking forward, he stepped onto the ferry boat. The moment he did, the boat trembled, and a black energy swept out to cover Xu Qing. After enough time had passed for an incense stick to burn, he and the boat had become one. He put on the woven rush raincoat and the bamboo hat.

He sat down cross-legged. An aura of time emanated from the raincoat and hat, which fused with the black energy and completely masked Xu Qing. From a distance, he looked exactly like a ferry pilot.

There he remained in place, completely motionless. He was waiting to see if he really would be able to hook the fish he was after. At the same time, he studied the deepest structures and elements of the boat with his senses.

Xu Qing, of course, was familiar with boats.[1]

In that manner, time passed. Ten days.

All of a sudden, an astonishing streak of light appeared on the horizon, which raced toward the shore. Within the light was a young man. His face was pale, and he looked very weak. He was none other than... Sir Star Ring!

He really had chosen to come to the God Blood River. There had been other options he could have picked from besides the river. But he had come to the conclusion that the God Blood River was the safest option. Thus, he came.

As he neared, a sensation of safety and stability blossomed within him. That was especially true when he saw the ferry boat next to the shore. He could finally breathe a sigh of relief. His long flight had left him weary in body, mind, and cultivation base. He had died twice, and though he had his Star Ring Pagodas to substitute for him in death, each time he woke up afterward he was weaker.

That was especially true considering he had died intentionally the second time. He had suspected that Xu Qing had some way to track him, so he had decided to pay the price of a life to sever any karma and wipe away any evidence that could be used to find him.

He had paid a huge price just to be sure. Ten days had passed since then, and he had not yet fully recovered.

Given the level of my cultivation base, I actually qualify to cross the river myself. But I’m very weak, so I couldn’t resist the infection, and that’s not to mention that I’m not strong enough to deal with any denizens of the river. Taking a ferry boat is the best option. Thankfully, I’ve never actually taken a ferry boat before.

Without slowing down at all, he shot through the air until he appeared right on the little pier. With a single leap, he jumped onto the ferry boat. As soon as he was on board, he felt a sensation of ultimate safety covering him. He sighed, long and hard. He bowed respectfully to the figure clad in the rush raincoat and wide bamboo hat that sat in front of him, surrounded by swirling black energy.

“Well met, Senior. Could you please cast off?”

The figure in the rush raincoat didn’t say anything, but the boat quickly slid away from the pier and started moving across the river of blood. It soon left the pier behind. They got so far along the river that the shore wasn’t visible anymore.

As the waves crashed and the mutagen-filled wind blew, Sir Star Ring gradually began to relax. Sitting down, he looked back at the western planetary system, and his eyes flashed aggressively.

“Xu Qing,” he growled, “our fight is not over yet.”

“You got that right,” said the figure in the raincoat.

Stunned, Sir Star Ring slowly turned his head, his face falling and his eyes shining with incredulity. All of a sudden, his heart was racing. He shot to his feet. “Y-your voice. Y-you... you....”

The figure in the raincoat took off his bamboo hat, and roiling black energy parted to reveal his face. “I’ve been waiting for you a while now.”

Sir Star Ring forgot all about the sound of the waves and wind. His mind filled with so much rumbling it was like the thunder of 10,000,000 lightning bolts. He couldn’t believe it. He wouldn’t believe it. It seemed completely and utterly absurd. freewebnovel.com

The person in front of him was Xu Qing!

All of a sudden, he felt the same premonition he had felt during his long journey, that he was heading toward complete safety. Except... as the feeling occurred to him, he also heard a familiar old voice echoing in his mind.

“Accept the tribulation.”

***

A month later....

On the shore of the God Blood River in the southern planetary system, a battered black ferry boat quickly approached the pier. The only person to disembark was Xu Qing.

It was just barely possible to see a mote orbiting around him. It was... a mote of heaven’s principle.[2]
