Waves raced across the surface of the God Blood River, and the wind carried the stench of gore across the shore of the southern planetary system. It seemed connected to the blood-red aurora in the sky overhead.

Within all of the redness was a ferry boat with no one on it, slowly drifting into the depths of the river, never to be seen again. Xu Qing stood on the pier, looking at the ferry boat disappearing into the distance. The gift from Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix was not something he could take with him. It had to stay on the God Blood River. However, it would be waiting there for him if he ever called out to it.

After a while, Xu Qing looked down at the mote floating above his palm.

“Heaven’s principle....” he murmured. That was the item he had taken from Sir Star Ring’s body after killing him!

It seems like canon or law. But at the same time, it doesn’t. It’s more like something that came out of imagination. It exists, but also doesn’t exist.

He looked at the mote thoughtfully. He had not absorbed it, as he intended to use it externally. And he had spent his time on the river studying it.

As for Sir Star Ring.... Because of the unique properties of the God Blood River, whenever he came back to life after dying, he was still on the ferry boat. And he got weaker each time. All Xu Qing had to do was wait for him. After dying the seventh time, he was truly destroyed in body and soul.

Although I did get Sir Star Ring’s Immortal Capital permission medallion, his death served another purpose. After all, the fact that I was able to just sit around waiting for him to show up was a clue in and of itself.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he put away the mote of heaven’s principle, then walked off the pier. With the wind against his face, he proceeded into the southern planetary system.

After a while, he ceased to mask his permission medallion, whereupon a terrifying stream of energy emerged from him, becoming a red pillar of light that shot up into the sky. When it reached the aurora above, it became a swirling vortex that was visible to the naked eye. Rumbling sounds echoed out as Xu Qing’s aura surged to an astonishing level, causing everything around him to ripple and distort.

Some of it came from him, but some came from the Immortal Capital permission medallion. As a result, the star chart in the sky over the south became clear and visible. Instantly, it was obvious that there were three stars in the south that were brighter than all the others.

One belonged to Xu Qing, and the other two... were the other two Shining Stars from the south! They were Jiang Fan and Yuanshan Su!

Sir Star Ring obviously hadn’t taken many other permission medallions. After killing him, my ranking only rose to 73. At least I’m in the top 100, though.

Xu Qing was certainly surprised to find his ranking so low, although he had some ideas about the reason for it. It was most likely that Sir Star Ring had been focused on cultivation rather than going around collecting medallions. He had probably intended to focus on the medallions after he went to the Aurora Immortal Palace and became a Quasi-Immortal.

Xu Qing looked up at the sky.

Those two clearly did things differently than Sir Star Ring. They worked hard to collect medallions earlier, and they’re continuing to do that now that we’re in the third round.

There are two ways for Fifth Star Ring cultivators to get into the Immortal Capital. One is by means of the Trial of the Hunt. As long as you can get into the top 100, you’re almost certain to get in. The other way doesn’t require participating in the trial. However, it’s harder. After reaching Quasi-Immortal, you have to get to Lower Immortal within 500 years!

Obviously, I’m not going to use that second method. And that means my only option is the first....

Xu Qing’s narrowed eyes gleamed. Getting into the top 100 virtually guarantees that you’ll get to the Immortal Capital. However, your exact ranking determines the resources you’re given when you arrive!

Xu Qing was fully aware that, going forward, his cultivation focus wouldn’t be just on improving his canon. He needed to acquire ringsource!

With enough ringsource, I can form my immortal embryo more quickly. And ringsource is also the key to fully completing my immortal embryo! This makes it obvious that my true goal... is to take 1st place! I’ll step into the Immortal Capital as the winner of the trial!

Having made his decision, his aura surged, and he shot off into the distance. He appeared to be going in the direction of Grand Immortal Mountain. That was where one of the south’s two Shining Stars called home. And that person was... Jiang Fan!

If I eliminate all of the other Shining Stars, and take their permission medallions one by one, then I’ll definitely be able to take first place. And I’ll start with ‘Li the Chosen.’

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he raced toward Grand Immortal Mountain.

***

Ten days later, he appeared in the central region of the southern planetary system. From a distance, he could see an endless mountain range filled with rising and falling mountains that numbered in the hundreds of thousands at the very least.

The place was filled year-round with white mist that seemed filled with occasional drifting forms of immortal beings. Sometimes the wind would blow, thinning the mist and revealing spectacularly beautiful palaces and temples crafted from the finest jade.

It really did seem like an immortal paradise. The immortal spirit energy here surpassed any other area in the south, as this place was the capital. This place was the main orthodox organization in the southern planetary system, Grand Immortal Mountain. And it was Jiang Fan’s sect!

Xu Qing did not just barge into the mountains. Though his battle prowess was considered incredible in his own generation, and he could even fight a Quasi-Immortal... the reality was that Grand Immortal Mountain had many Quasi-Immortals. There was even an aura that was far more terrifying than that. It was the might of a Lower Immortal.

That said, according to the rules of the Trial of the Hunt, Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors cannot participate or interfere. The same goes for Lower Immortals. This fight... will be fair and aboveboard.

Xu Qing let his energy surge and unleashed the aura of the permission medallion. Combined, it formed a heaven-shaking, earth-shattering battle spirit. It was also a battle challenge issued to Grand Immortal Mountain!

“Will you fight me, Jiang Fan?” he said in a cold voice that thrummed with the desire to do battle.

Numerous streams of divine will issued forth from Grand Immortal Mountain, locking onto Xu Qing to inspect him. Among those streams of divine will were several from Quasi-Immortals. None of them did anything to oppose him.

Xu Qing had issued a challenge in a fair and honest way. There were countless people who could bear witness, and the rules set forth by the Immortal Capital were inviolable. This was the Trial of the Hunt, and it was a struggle to get to the Immortal Capital!

Xu Qing’s expression remained neutral as the divine will inspected him. He simply hovered in place as he waited for Jiang Fan’s response.

***

In a hall in Grand Immortal Mountain, Jiang Fan sat cross-legged and silent. He could sense Xu Qing’s energy, and had heard him clearly. He knew that Xu Qing was challenging him to fight. No one in the sect would push him to accept the challenge. If he wanted to, he could simply hide and refuse to fight. After all, he knew that he wasn’t a match for Xu Qing.

And yet, he rose to his feet, his eyes gleaming and his energy building. Then he walked out of the hall, whereupon he found someone standing outside.

Jiang Fan ducked his head and bowed. “Master.”

Standing there was an impressive middle-aged man with handsome facial features and a robe embroidered with a cloud motif. In Grand Immortal Mountain, he ranked second only to Immortal Monarch Vastpeak. His name was... Lan Yun. And he was Jiang Fan’s Master.[1]

“You’re not a match for him,” Lan Yun said coolly. “Given your ranking, you can just stay here in the sect. When the third round is over, you’ll definitely get into the Immortal Capital.”

Jiang Fan thought for a moment and then shook his head. “Master, I don’t mind losing. And I won’t refuse a challenge. Although it’s very important to me to get to the Immortal Capital... shrinking from a fight is not something I’ll ever do!”

With that, he bowed to his Master, then floated up into the air and off Grand Immortal Mountain. Shortly after... he appeared in front of Xu Qing!

When Jiang Fan looked at Xu Qing, he thought back to the fourth world of the immortal palace, and everything that had played out there. Taking a deep breath, he waved his right hand. Using his canon, he sent his Immortal Capital permission medallion flying off to the side.

“Beat me and you can have it!”

Jiang Fan began to power up, causing swirling mist to build up around him. It covered the area, and then spread out as if to weigh down on all creation. And it bore down on Xu Qing. Jiang Fan’s canon had clearly improved since his time in the immortal palace. The mist seemed mighty enough to devour anything in its path, and to cover over all things and beings. Xu Qing was quickly surrounded by it, and it began to permeate the space-time around him.

But then... before Jiang Fan could even launch an attack, he stopped in place, a bitter feeling rising in his heart. He could see... that the sky, the land, and everything around him was filled with numerous instances of Xu Qing’s space-time.

It was like looking at a kaleidoscope. Of those innumerable space-times, there was only one that had his mist in it. In all the others, Xu Qing was simply staring calmly at him.

Then one version of Xu Qing walked over to him, reached out with his right hand, and patted Jiang Fan on the shoulder. There was nothing Jiang Fan could do to stop him. Rumbling sounds filled Jiang Fan, and a loud cracking sound rang out. That sound didn’t come from the air or the ground, but rather... the space-time he was in. There was no need for Xu Qing to do anything other than that.

Walking past the immobilized Jiang Fan, he picked up the Immortal Capital permission medallion, then waved his hand to dispel all the space-time instances. He walked away without saying a word.

***

On the highest peak of Grand Immortal Mountain, there was a holy throne in a hall filled with silver light. There was currently a performance going on including singing and dancing. Some sandalwood incense was burning, the smoke curling through the hall and making everything seem hazy and mysterious.

Seated in the position of honor was an old man wearing a silver robe.

“He first understood space-time, and then parallelism. While only an Imperial Sovereign, he developed canon befitting of a Grand Emperor. This kid... is nothing short of spectacular. No wonder the Immortal Paragon has taken a liking to him.”

***

Jiang Fan hovered there quietly. He knew that he was no match for Xu Qing. But he hadn’t realized that he was so far beneath Xu Qing that he couldn’t even put up a fight. It filled him with bitterness.

Some time passed, whereupon his Master, Lan Yun, stepped out of thin air. Hovering next to Jiang Fan, he looked at Xu Qing disappearing in the distance.

“There’s nothing embarrassing about losing to him,” he said calmly.

1. Lan Yun was introduced in chapter 1100 and mentioned again in chapters 1102 and 1136. Immortal Monarch Vastpeak was introduced in chapter 1120. ☜

The Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt was divided into three rounds.

In the first round, a total of 10,000 permission medallions were distributed, and the countless cultivators in the four planetary systems would fight over them. That first round was brutal, and involved a lot of medallions changing hands. That said, cultivators could choose whether or not to participate.

Then came the second round, in which the four Immortal Monarchs would distribute their legacies for everyone to seek enlightenment of. The second round was an indication that the trial would soon speed up. During that round, cultivators with an advantage would get a big boost, while cultivators who had no advantage would be whittled out of the competition. The participants were still allowed to kill each other to take permission medallions during the second round, and at the same time, could get stronger thanks to the legacies. The enticement of the legacies and the medallions made the second round very intense.

Now the third round had come. This was the round in which the final eliminations and selections would take place. It was all about hunting down other participants, and either killing them or robbing them of their medallions. By the time the third round ended, all of the previous fighting and killing ensured that there were far fewer than 10,000 cultivators with medallions.

Only someone with complete canon could unfuse with their permission medallion. Those without complete canon could not get rid of their medallion unless they died first.

When the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt began, people who chose to participate knew there was no turning back. Either you got to the Immortal Capital, or... you died trying and became fodder for other participants. If you got very, very lucky, you could theoretically lose your medallion and live to tell the tale, although that went against the spirit of the competition.

Right now, it was a nearly daily occurrence in the southern planetary system for permission medallions to change hands. There were currently less than 500 medallions left. At that moment, the cultivators who had those medallions suddenly sensed something shocking, and they quickly took out their medallions to check the star chart.

In the chart that showed the southern region, the star that represented Jiang Fan, which shone brightly at Grand Immortal Mountain, suddenly went dim. Its brightness was being gobbled up by another star. And then, that other star became brighter than all the other stars in the planetary system. The only star who could compare to it was a star in the Yuanshan Clan.

All of the cultivators who had permission medallions were astonished.

“Jiang Fan was defeated?”

“He’s the top Shining Star in the south! Who could beat him?”

“It wasn’t Yuanshan Su. Don’t tell me one of the Shining Stars from one of the other three planetary systems came over here!”

Then the cultivators witnessed something even more shocking, as the star that had just defeated Jiang Fan was now moving with astonishing speed in the direction of... the Yuanshan Clan!

Bedlam ensued in the Yuanshan Clan. They were the top clan in the south, and they had no shortage of powerful experts. But according to the rules of the Trial of the Hunt, none of those experts had the right to challenge the trial participants. As anxiety built in the clan, Yuanshan Su walked out.

Clad in a white gown, she stood atop Mount Skyspirit and looked off into the distance. Surrounding her were other clan cultivators, all with serious expressions on their faces. At first, she hadn’t been completely certain who that third star on the star chart was. But after watching that star go to Grand Immortal Mountain and defeat Jiang Fan... she could guess who it was.

There are only two people who could do that. The first would be Sir Star Ring, and the other is... him. According to the news coming out of the east, Sir Star Ring already perished. And that makes it clear who this person is.

She had a complicated expression on her face. When the events in the fourth world came to a conclusion, she was one of the first people to leave the immortal palace. After returning to her clan, she had thought constantly about everything that happened in the immortal palace. And there was one person who occupied her thoughts more than anyone else.

She had achieved her goal, benefited greatly, and improved her cultivation base a lot. But that person continued to weigh down on her with pressure like a mountain. It made things very complicated.

After all, she had completed an official wedding ceremony with him. Though it had been a requirement in that reflection of history, the ramifications could still affect the real world. With such thoughts filling her mind, she looked at the sky as the wind wailed in the sky and churned the clouds. A person appeared on the horizon.

He wore black garments and had long violet hair, and as he approached, it was like he was walking through waves of time itself. He was none other than Xu Qing.

As he neared, the other cultivators of the Yuanshan Clan looked shocked. There were even some Quasi-Immortal patriarchs who unleashed their energy, causing the surroundings to ripple as if they were facing a major enemy.

Xu Qing didn’t pay any attention to the pressure weighing down on him. He simply proceeded, his expression neutral. He passed the Yuanshan cultivators, ignored the gazes of the patriarchs, and landed on Mount Skyspirit in front of Yuanshan Su. He extended his hand.

“Hand it over,” Xu Qing said quietly. He didn’t say much, but he spoke in a way that indicated he wouldn’t take no for an answer.

Yuanshan Su said nothing. The fluctuations from the surrounding patriarchs grew more intense, and their eyes were as cold as ice. But after a moment passed, Yuanshan Su sighed. She reached up and, to the astonishment of the clan cultivators around her, she placed her palm onto her forehead. A popping sound rang out as she stripped her own Immortal Capital permission medallion outside of herself. With the wave of her hand, she sent the brightly shining medallion over to Xu Qing.

It landed on his palm. Not even glancing at it, he gave Yuanshan Su a meaningful look. “Is there a third way to get to the Immortal Capital?”

The indifference with which Yuanshan Su gave him the medallion led Xu Qing to the conclusion that there was likely another way to get to the Immortal Capital.

“Yes,” she said. “If I become a Quasi-Immortal during the trial, I can also go there. It’s a special right given to the eight Shining Stars.”

Xu Qing nodded. He could tell that Yuanshan Su’s aura was just on the verge of being that of a Quasi-Immortal. She had clearly benefited a lot in the immortal palace.

However, that had nothing to do with him. He closed his fist over the medallion, and it disappeared. Dazzling light shone up from him and into the sky. A moment later, the star chart once again appeared overhead in the south.

The star that represented Xu Qing was now brighter than all others, making it completely unique. He was number one in the south! Of course, his own permission medallion told him his rank in the Fifth Star Ring as a whole.

5th!

He didn’t care who it was that ranked higher than him. If things went according to plan, then no one would be able to stop him from taking 1st.

“Well then,” he said, “see you at the Immortal Capital.” With a final look at Yuanshan Su, he turned and left.

The Yuanshan Clan cultivators could do nothing but watch him go. Shortly after, the patriarchs landed on the ground next to her.

Yuanshan Su bowed her head. “I’ve let you down, Patriarchs. I don’t even qualify to make a move on him.”

A few breaths of time passed, whereupon one of the patriarchs sighed. “Su’er, the truth is... not even we could be fully confident in beating him in a fight. How does he compare to Sir Star Ring?”

Yuanshan Su shook her head. “Sir Star Ring perished. Although I can’t be sure if he’s truly dead or not, I’m fairly certain he was the one who did it.”

The patriarchs all sighed.

“People like that sometimes don’t come around for generations....”

Yuanshan Su smiled. “It just makes things more interesting.”

***

In the northern planetary system of the Fifth Star Ring was the Sword Immortal School!

As an organization, it was very different from Grand Immortal Mountain in the south or the Starry Quarter in the east. The most orthodox organization in the north was built atop a gargantuan meteor. It was surrounded by a permanent tempest of sword energy, and the sound of swords rose up from it into the highest heavens. The meteor itself was shockingly large, like a mountain. If you stood at the bottom and looked up at it, you wouldn’t even be able to see the top.

There were various legends about where the rock came from. Some people said it wasn’t native to the Fifth Star Ring. They claimed it came from outside of the star ring, and that Sword Immortal Blue Mallard had acquired it, gained enlightenment from it, and used it to found the sect. Other people say that it was left over from the days when the starry sky of the Fifth Star Ring was compacted to make the current geography. And there were many other stories.[1]

But the fact remained that the Sword Immortal School really was built on top of the gigantic meteor. On the exterior of the meteor, in the central square of the Sword Immortal School, Hordeslayer and Rampart were carefully erecting a host of warding spells. As they worked, they communicated via divine will.

“He put Sir Star Ring to death!”

“He took Jiang Fan’s medallion!”

“That shrew Yuanshan Su was the biggest pushover of them all. She didn’t even try to fight!”

“He’s on his way here to the north right now....”

“I have the feeling he’s after more than just our medallions....”

“You’re right! He wants to subjugate us!” freewebnovel.com

“Being forced to bond with him in the fourth world was the biggest humiliation imaginable!”

“We can’t let this matter drop!”

“We can’t let this matter drop!”

“So the plan is to make him pay as soon as he shows up!”

Gritting their teeth, they continued setting up all sorts of warding spells as fast as they could. A few days later, they finally breathed sighs of relief and sat down cross-legged.

“Now we just wait!”

***

Above them, in the sky over the Sword Immortal School, a person rested within the endless tempest of sword energy. He wore blue clothing and had gray hair. Orbiting around him was an ancient blue sword. The sword’s name was Blue Mallard, and as a result, he was known as Sword Immortal Blue Mallard.

As he rested within the sword energy, he sipped alcohol and looked down at his two apprentices. A moment later, he sighed.

I was so blind back then. Why did I pick these two talentless hacks as apprentices? They can’t even beat him two versus one? They have to set up warding spells as well? And they’re planning an ambush?

The Fifth Star Ring was divided into east, west, south and north.

The north there was unlike the north in the Revered Ancient mainland. There was no snow in the northern planetary system. It was quite the opposite. Most locations there were very hot. Of course... when big events played out that got all the cultivators in the north talking, then it wasn’t just the weather that heated up.

In a small town not far from the Sword Immortal School, a local teahouse buzzed with conversation.

“This area has become one of the busiest locations imaginable recently.”

“The big sects, clans, and tribes have all sent direct bloodline elites and core disciples here.”

“The two Shining Stars from the Sword Immortal School achieved major success in the dao of the sword. It’s only natural that the north is all stirred up because of the upcoming Sword Activation Ceremony.”

“They’re the most dazzling chosen in the north! All cultivators of this generation basically worship them!”

“The Sword Activation Ceremony is definitely going to be watched by everybody.”

“Seems to me that their trip to the Fallen Immortal Moors was really a success. They made some shocking gains.”

“I heard that when they were at the Fallen Immortal Moors, both of them managed to form immortal wills in their sword spirits!”

Everyone in the teahouse was talking about Hordeslayer and Rampart.

Xu Qing sat next to a window in the teahouse, his expression neutral as he smelled the aroma of tea wafting up from his cup and listened to the chatter. Northern cultivators didn’t usually drink alcohol. They were fonder of spirit tea. As a result, cities usually had a lot of teahouses.

Those two swords are very interesting.

Xu Qing took a sip of tea. There was something uniquely bitter in the tea, but when the tea passed along your tongue, it changed into something sweet.

It was Xu Qing’s third day in the northern planetary system. Because of his lack of familiarity with the north, he had masked the aura of his permission medallion, thus removing himself from the star chart.

It was only after arriving that he heard about the upcoming Sword Activation Ceremony for Hordeslayer and Rampart. The ceremony was to start in three days, and was supposed to last for two months. It would end at the same time as the third round of the Trial of the Hunt.

Are they... scared?

Though news about what Xu Qing had done in the south had not spread very much, he was certain that Hordeslayer and Rampart knew about it.

Why are they so confident that they’ll be safe for the next two months during their ceremony? It can’t be the sect. The trial rules prohibit that. They must have things set up as part of the ceremony. Or are they waiting for me to go find them?

After some thought, Xu Qing finished the rest of his tea in one gulp.

***

Three days later....

More and more cultivators were gathering around the meteor where the Sword Immortal School was located. All sorts of organizations from the north were present, and the atmosphere was very lively. Everyone was waiting for the ceremony.

The atmosphere was similarly lively inside the Sword Immortal School. Whether it was cultivators who were members of the Sword Immortal School, or representatives from other places, they were all gathered around the central square, chatting and laughing as they waited for the formalities to begin.

Eventually, the auspicious hour arrived, and rumbling sounds filled heaven and earth. Two astonishing beams of light rose up from the central square. They reached the aurora in the canopy of heaven, and crimson light spread out like a vast sea.

Two huge vortexes formed. As the rumbling sounds grew more intense, the meteor was affected, and sent out streams of blue light. The blue light rose up and connected to the red above. And thus, the entire Sword Immortal School was bathed in a combination of blue and red light.

Everyone observing from outside the sect looked on intently. Everyone observing from inside the sect watched happily, their hearts filled with anticipation.

However, as the crowds looked on and the sword energy raged, Hordeslayer and Rampart were feeling surprised. They were still communicating via projection.

“He didn’t come after all?”

“I thought for sure he would come before the ceremony, but as it turns out, he didn’t!”

“Don’t tell me he’s planning to show up during the actual ceremony.”

“It doesn’t matter. We’re prepared. If he’s so scared he doesn’t come, then fine. But if he does show up, then today—”

“Will be the day we get revenge!”

“But... what if we can’t beat him?”

“Then we just surrender! If that happens, we won’t be the ones to lose face. It’ll be Master! If he, an immortal monarch, can’t even protect his two apprentices when they’re in the middle of seeking enlightenment, then just imagine the humiliation he’ll experience!”

“You’re right, brother!”

Hordeslayer and Rampart exchanged a look, and both could see the bravado in each other’s eyes. Taking a deep breath, they each took a step forward and unleashed their sword energy. As they absorbed the blue and red light, two streams of immortal will surged within them.

Astonishingly, two blurry swords appeared over their heads! The swords seemed extremely ancient, as if they contained an aura of time itself. The moment the swords appeared, they attracted the attention of everyone in the area.

If any of the other Shining Stars were present, they would recognize the swords immediately. They were... the very same immortal swords that had come out of the sword furnace in the fourth world.

Next, the blue light and the light from the aurora acted like sharpening sand that flowed back and forth across the blurry immortal swords. It was as if the swords were being sharpened, causing their sword energy to grow stronger and more incisive! It was the same with the sword light.

The ceremony involved this sharpening process going on for two months. During that time, the immortal swords would grow increasingly dazzling, and the sword will they emanated would provide the onlookers with a chance to seek enlightenment.

Hordeslayer and Rampart sat there cross-legged, their eyes closed and their minds focused.

Exclamations of admiration could be heard everywhere. All of the onlookers were paying very close attention.

Meanwhile, in the Sword Pavilion elsewhere in the Sword Immortal School, someone was speaking sarcastically.

“Brother Blue, those two apprentices of yours are truly extraordinary.” The speaker was a middle-aged man clad in red, who was currently watching the scene in the central square.

Seated next to him was Sword Immortal Blue Mallard. At the moment, Sword Immortal Blue Mallard was shaking his head helplessly. “Extraordinary my ass! Those two are gutless cowards! I bet that if something goes wrong, they’ll spout some bullshit excuse and blame me for everything.”

The man in red chuckled. Looking down into the crowd, he saw someone that seemed to both exist and not exist at the same time. It was correct to say that he didn’t exist, because none of the other cultivators in the crowd seemed to notice him. But it was also correct to say that he existed, because there were certain people who could see him with absolute clarity.

“So they’re scared of that guy? No wonder the Immortal Paragon has taken a liking to him. You know what? His canon reminds me of... Immortal Lord Aurora from back in the day.” The man in red seemed wistful. “Brother Blue, now that I think about it, weren’t you the apprentice of the top-ranking true monarch from the Aurora Immortal Palace back then...?”

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard sighed. “Technically speaking, yes. But my Master was cheap. He only came to see me a few times, and he never took me to the immortal palace. If he had, I’d be long gone. I guess—”

“I guess it all comes down to karma,” the man in red said softly.

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard sighed again. “You know what annoys me most about you?”

“Yes.”

“It’s annoying that you always say what I’m about to say, before I say it!”

“I said I know! Oh, hey, that fellow is looking at us.” Smiling, he pointed down.

***

Down in the crowd in the Sword Immortal School, Xu Qing looked up at the tallest building present. He could just barely sense an aggressive aura there. Though he couldn’t see who it came from, he could guess.

After a moment of consideration, he clasped hands and bowed. Then he strode forward.

He made his way through the crowd, across the square, and then flew right up to the two pillars of sword energy.... He was now hovering right in front of the two immortal swords that were being sharpened.

He waved his hand. That simple gesture caused the swords to vibrate. An instant later... to the absolute shock of the crowd, the swords seemed to seethe with excitement, and then, they turned and shot toward Xu Qing.

Hordeslayer and Rampart suddenly opened their eyes. They were instantly inclined to feel excited, but they quickly suppressed the sensation.

“He’s here!”

“Those are our swords!”

“We have to go all out!”

Without any hesitation, and ignoring the fact that so many people were watching, Hordeslayer and Rampart both performed incantation gestures and then smacked their hands onto the ground. Numerous halos of light instantly rose up from the ground, hundreds of them, and each of them pulsing with terrifying mightiness. They all shot toward Xu Qing.

Then Hordeslayer and Rampart shot to their feet, performed an incantation gesture, and grimly shouted, “Rising Sword. Sword Falls!”

A massive, illusory sword rose up from the square, shining with dazzling light and pulsing with magnificent sword energy. It instantly slashed upward toward Xu Qing.

At the same time, a giant sword emerged from the sea of light and slashed toward Xu Qing from above.

Things weren’t over yet. As the hundreds of halos and double swords closed in on Xu Qing, Hordeslayer and Rampart moved as one, performing another incantation gesture and then spitting out mouthfuls of blood.

“Meteor Swords!”

The meteor that the Sword Immortal School was built on erupted with blue light. And within that light were thousands of long, blue swords, all of which shot toward Xu Qing and then started orbiting around him in a huge sword formation. That, combined with the halos and double swords, were bringing a torrent of death.

These were the warding spells that Hordeslayer and Rampart had prepared to deal with Xu Qing.

After doing all that in one short moment, their eyes shimmered with determination. With yet another incantation gesture, they blurred into motion, superimposing over each other as they fused into one! They became one person! Blood oozed out of their eyes, ears, nose, and mouth. They drained their ringsource. And they performed a double-handed incantation gesture and pointed toward the excited immortal swords orbiting around Xu Qing.[1]

The two swords vibrated, and their excitement seemed to be quashed. Thrumming aggressively, they spun to point at Xu Qing. All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but it happened at the exact same moment that Xu Qing revealed himself.

In response to all of that, Xu Qing’s expression remained neutral. He waved his hand, and a mote like a piece of dust flew out. It began to fall. The sky rumbled. Heaven and earth shook. The air trembled. Space-time oscillated.

It was... a mote of heaven’s principle.

1. Although it says they “became one person,” the author then goes on to refrain from using pronouns at all, which is easy to do in Chinese. In other words, he doesn’t call the fused version “he” or “them.” He just uses their names. This continues into the next chapter. Unfortunately, that gets clunky real fast in English, especially in a fight scene, so I’m just going to refer to them with plural pronouns. It’s not as if they became a new individual entity when they fused. They’re just occupying the same body. Or something like that. ☜

The moment that dust mote appeared, the heaven and earth of the Sword Immortal School began to shake. A terrifying pressure began to weigh down, like the might of heaven itself. The world stilted. The air shattered.

The countless cultivators present were all reacting with visible shock. In fact, they were so terrified that they immediately turned and fled. In the face of that mote, all things and beings had no choice but to flee. It could not be defied!

After order came balance. And from that came this, which was part of the power of an immortal!

The former number one Shining Star, Sir Star Ring, had relied on a lifetime of resources and destined opportunities, as well as reserve powers from the Star Ring Pagoda, to acquire this precious treasure at the moment he became a Quasi-Immortal! You could even call it a corroboration of Sir Star Ring’s dao of immortals.

There weren’t even enough words to describe its grandeur. As it fell, it was only natural for dramatic things to happen!

All onlookers felt like they were looking at an entire starry sky! That was especially true considering that nothing like it had ever appeared in the north before. Actually, the only people who had ever seen it were the Quasi-Immortals in the fifth world of the immortal palace, who had witnessed the fight between Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring.

But now, it was here in the north, at the Sword Immortal School, right above Hordeslayer and Rampart. And thus, it was an absolutely astonishing development that shook everyone down to their soul.

That was particularly true of Hordeslayer and Rampart. All of their advance preparations were child’s play. The trap they had laid was nothing more than a joke.

The two enormous swords that had appeared, one above and one below, couldn’t continue to exist. Their sword might was broken. The swords... trembled and emitted sounds that resembled wailing. After that, the two enormous swords... crumbled into pieces. The cloud of thousands of storms whipping around Xu Qing also collapsed.

When facing a mote of heaven’s principle, sword energy ceased, and sword light went dim. The tempest of swords... disappeared. None of it existed any longer.

As for the two immortal swords by Xu Qing, which Hordeslayer and Rampart had tried to seize back control of, as they inched closer to Xu Qing, they began to tremble violently. And then, they tumbled away.

Hordeslayer and Rampart in fused form were bleeding profusely, and finally, their killing intent turned into nothing as they tumbled backward.

This level of force was unstoppable! A dust mote might not seem like something very heavy, but to Hordeslayer and Rampart, this dust mote was as heavy as the entire starry sky. The terror they felt had reached a peak.

And yet, in the face of a mote of heaven’s principle, fleeing was useless. Heaven’s principle could bury anything and cause it to cease to exist!

As they reeled mentally, their combined fleshly body couldn’t stay together any longer, and they exploded apart. After separating, blood sprayed out of their mouths like mad, and their bodies were disintegrating. Their souls were also starting to fall apart. A sensation of death slammed into them like a wave.

However, just as the mote was about to completely wipe Hordeslayer and Rampart out of existence... a sigh drifted out of the tallest building in the Sword Immortal School.

“Could you give me some face....?”

Along with the sigh flew a stream of sword energy that appeared beneath the mote. Because of the sword energy, the mote stopped in place.

Taking advantage of that moment, Hordeslayer and Rampart fled with all the power they could muster toward the tall building. They had recognized their Master’s voice, and were now convinced that he was interfering on their behalf. They had been terrified out of their minds by the sensation of impending doom, and knew that their only hope of survival lay with their Master.

Though they fled at top speed... space-time ripples suddenly appeared in front of them, blocking their path. And that tall building became like something that didn’t even exist. The space-time ripples overlapped, creating a space-time tempest. Then time flowed like a river, and a time wave swept over Hordeslayer and Rampart.

When the foam cleared, the two of them were gone. They had been swept up by the wave and sent into a time that wasn’t the present!

Then Xu Qing stepped forward onto the wave before disappearing without a trace. He... was entering the same space-time where he had sent Hordeslayer and Rampart. Xu Qing had appeared, Hordeslayer and Rampart had launched their trap, then tried to flee. Then Xu Qing sent them into space-time and followed with the intent to kill....

All of that happened in only a few short breaths of time!

All of the organizations in the north were shaken to the core. This was an unforgettable event the likes of which rarely occurred.

For one thing, Hordeslayer and Rampart alone were very famous, so to see the tables turned on them was shocking. Even more shocking was that nobody knew who attacked them. All they knew was that he had terrifying canon.

This battle between Shining Stars surpassed the Imperial Sovereign level. Even Quasi-Immortals were shocked by what they were seeing. In fact, it was no surprise that some people even assumed that Xu Qing was actually Sir Star Ring.

“Who was that guy...?”

“Sir Star Ring?”

“It didn’t seem like it....”

Inside the Sword Immortal School, in the Sword Pavilion, Sword Immortal Blue Mallard sighed, took a step forward, and seemed about to say something.

Before he could, the man in red chuckled and said, “Oh, kids. They’ll surpass us in time, I’m sure. Not even willing to give face to a Lower Immortal.”

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard stopped in his tracks and looked at the man in red who annoyed him so much. After a moment of thought, he was about to say something, but again, the man in red spoke first.

“But since they’re your apprentices, it would be reasonable to step in at least to save their lives. And you could also make sure that lad understands that face should be given to Lower Immortals.”

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard said nothing. This person was being more annoying than ever. He really was just blurting out everything before Sword Immortal Blue Mallard could say it, leaving him somewhat at a loss for words. He was currently frowning, and was so irritated he was about to let loose a harrumph.

The man in red snorted coldly.

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard snapped at that point. “This is ridiculous! I can’t even snort coldly without you beating me to the punch!”

The man in red laughed quietly.

Fuming, Sword Immortal Blue Mallard took a step forward and vanished.

***

Meanwhile, in another space-time was a desert.

Hordeslayer and Rampart were fleeing wildly in the hopes of finding their way out of it. A space-time wave had swept them up and taken them away from the real world, delivering them to this space-time. When they popped out, they had no idea where they were or if it was real. This space-time, and this desert, seemed real.

But the intense sensation of deadly crisis in the two brothers made it impossible for them to analyze the situation. They were overwhelmed with anxiety and bitterness.

“Dammit, dammit, DAMMIT! This is all your fault!”

“What are you blaming me for? You were the one who came up with that idiotic plan. You wanted to lay a trap and ambush him. Now how stupid do you feel, huh??”

“Me? Stupid? It was all because you said nobody could help us, not even Master. You said to lure him out and kill him to negate the karma that resulted from bonding with him!”

“You make it sound like I’m the only one who got bonded. You did too!”

“It’s all your fault!”

“It’s all your fault!”

As the two brothers raced along, they were arguing with each other so heatedly they were yelling.

“Master’s also a useless piece of trash!”

“That old codger! He’s an actual immortal and he just sat around watching us about to get killed!”

“That’s right. That guy obviously doesn’t care about giving face to Master!”

“That’s why Master has always been so shameless!”

“You are absolutely, positively correct. Now, if he was the Immortal Paragon, then maybe that guy would give him some face.”

“And that means...”

“It’s all Master’s fault!!”

Now that they had found a way to vent together, they were back to being in each other’s good graces. After venting for a while, they felt better, and even managed to speed up a bit. It looked like they were about to break free of the desert.

But that was when a wind kicked up. Sand grains flew through the air, filling the world, and buffeting the fleeing brothers and slowing them down to a standstill. No matter how they launched attacks or howled in rage, they were helpless. Eventually, the sand formed a huge face that filled half the sky.

It was Xu Qing. He opened his mouth to devour them.

Hordeslayer and Rampart shared a despairing glance. Then they gritted their teeth, and their eyes shone with defiance. Then they quickly communicated with each other via divine will.

“I’d rather die than surrender, lil’ bro!”

“Even if it means dying while standing up, big brother, I refuse to bend the knee!”

“Let’s just fly up there and self-detonate!”

“Okay, sure. We’ll fly up and detonate at the same time!”

Howling, they were about to fly up into the air when... they simultaneously dropped to their knees.

“Young Lord....”

But then they sensed something had changed. The two of them instinctively looked up, whereupon shocked expressions appeared on their faces. They opened their mouths to speak... but before they could, brilliant blue light appeared in the sky.

It was like a raging sea that spread out rapidly, and caused the huge face of Xu Qing to hesitate for a moment. An enraged voice echoed out from the blue light.

“You disgraceful fools!”

Hordeslayer and Rampart were delighted, and quickly jumped to their feet as Sword Immortal Blue Mallard appeared out of the blue light. Not interested in hearing anything from them, Sword Immortal Blue Mallard slapped both of them hard. The brothers shivered as their Immortal Capital permission medallions were ripped away from them.

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard threw the medallions up into the sky. Then he waved his hand, and an indescribably terrifying energy surged off him, causing the surrounding space-time to shatter.

Ripples spread through all of the space-time instance. All it took was a single thought, and he could reduce the space-time to ashes.

Having accomplished that, he coolly said, “Can you give me some face, lad?”

Xu Qing stepped out into the open, put away the two permission medallions, and then bowed at the waist.

“I’m happy to comply with your orders, Senior.” With that, Xu Qing took a step back and vanished. The instance of space-time also vanished.

Everything blurred, and when it became clear again, the surroundings had once again become the Sword Immortal School. They weren’t in the central square, but rather, in the Sword Pavilion.

Hordeslayer and Rampart looked around, stunned. Then, they jubilantly prepared to bow to their Master.

However, Sword Immortal Blue Mallard just glared at them and then kicked each of them, sending them flying over to the corner of the room. As the two of them howled in grief, he walked over and proceeded to kick them several more times.

“Disgraceful moron! Shameless fool! I must have been drunk back when I said you had amazing potential. You don’t have any freaking preheaven sword bodies! You have preheaven whored bodies!”[1]

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard gave a cold snort, and then looked at the man in red without saying a word.

The man in red also didn’t say a word.

Sword Immortal Blue Mallard frowned and waited a bit longer. “Why aren’t you saying what I’m about to say?”

“I don’t feel like it,” said the man in red, smiling.

Sighing helplessly, Sword Immortal Blue Mallard said, “Elder Brother... these two imbeciles are your Sect Nephews. You have the right, so why not... give them two new permission medallions?”

1. In Chinese, there is a character that means many things, including inexpensive, lowly, base, whore/whorish, slut/slutty etc., and has the exact same pronunciation as sword. By chance, the word whored rhymes with sword, so I used it. In reality, this joke wouldn’t work in spoken Chinese dialogue, as the pronunciation of the two is exactly the same. The English equivalent would be something like “they weren’t bred bears they were bread bears.” It only works when you can see the character/word, so it’s a “written” joke. Although, to be fair, most TV shows and movies in China have subtitles anyway, so I guess it could work visually as well. But it definitely wouldn’t work in audiobook format. I supposed I could have done something with “sored/sword,” but the slutty/whore aspect is what makes it really funny in Chinese, so I’d rather go with something like that. ☜

The third round of the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt was about killing and plunder. There was no set time limit. On some occasions in the past, the third round lasted for a long time, while in other cases it ended quickly.

The reason was that the end of the round was determined by a number. Of the 10,000 Immortal Capital permission medallions that were given out, when only 1,000 remained... a one-month countdown would begin. At the end of the month, the Trial of the Hunt was over.

In terms of the ranking list, it was publicly displayed at all the major orthodox organizations in the Fifth Star Ring. In other words, it was visible to participants and non-participants alike.

As of now... there were 1,000 people with permission medallions. The countdown had begun.

As it did, the rankings became public, and the Fifth Star Ring was shaken. That list contained the combined results of all of the four major planetary systems, and if there were no unexpected changes, it was likely to be the final ranking list.

The most important thing about the list was the top 100. Going back through many Trials of the Hunt, everyone in the top 100 ended up going to the Immortal Capital. Exceptions were exceedingly rare. The top 10 were considered the chosen ones, and they were always the elites of the current generation in the star ring.

After scanning the top 100, just about everyone would focus on the top 10!

To the surprise of everyone, there were only three of the Shining Stars in the top 10. The others... weren’t even on the list! By now, it was no secret why this was the case.

Whether it was the big event in the north or the news from the south, just about everyone had heard about Xu Qing! Other people just tried to snatch whatever permission medallions they could. But he was hunting the Shining Stars.

Jiang Fan had lost to him. Yuanshan Su had chosen to bend the knee. Hordeslayer and Rampart had ultimately given him their medallions. With their light added to his, the star that represented Xu Qing was glittering more brightly than ever. When those Shining Stars were eliminated, they dropped from their high spots on the list, and cultivators that few people had heard of replaced them. But eventually, a familiar name popped into the top 5. freewebnovel.com

Li Mengtu took 5th place! As the lone Shining Star from the west, he had always been on an upward trajectory.

Above him was Sir Vilespirit, who was in 4th. There was no consensus on whether it was a good or bad thing for him to have such a high rank. At the very least, people agreed that he had earned his place there.

In 3rd place was Xu Qing! Opinions about him were mixed. Although he had collected some medallions from other Shining Stars, there were others on the list who had many more medallions than he did. Everyone was still trying to take advantage of every moment to rise in the rankings. That was why Xu Qing wasn’t in 1st place.

Above him was Zhou Zhengli, who was in 2nd! People weren’t sure what to think about Zhou Zhengli. He had always maintained an image of being kind, charitable, righteous, and strict. But he didn’t have a very impressive presence. For the most part, he always came up in the context of Sir Vilespirit, as if he was predestined to oppose him.

As for 1st place... it was occupied by a name that the vast majority of cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring had never heard of.

Chen Batian! It was a rather inelegant name, so it went without saying that people were taken aback to see it in 1st place.[1]

Because few people were familiar with this person, more people were talking about him than about Xu Qing and how he was hunting Shining Stars. Unfortunately, there was hardly any reliable information about him. Everything was rumor.

Some people claimed he hailed from the eastern planetary system. Others said he had an extreme personality, and that he was both ruthless and lascivious. There were people who said that he had ranked very low in the first and second rounds, and had suddenly risen to the top in the third, for unknown reasons. Yet others claimed that he was bloodthirsty, and had killed every opponent he ever fought. But in the end, those were all just rumors. As a result, the mystery surrounding him grew deeper.

Meanwhile, after the ranking list went public, there was something else that led to widespread astonishment.

Sir Star Ring wasn’t on the list! He was the number one chosen in the Fifth Star Ring, yet he wasn’t in the top 10. In fact, he wasn’t even in the top 100. He wasn’t there at all! A lot of people had speculations.

However, it wasn’t until a Quasi-Immortal finally emerged from the fifth world of the Aurora Immortal Palace that an explanation was provided. The fight between Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring in the fifth world was like a breeze that had long since passed. But now, that breeze returned and became a tempest that raged near and far. At that point, everybody started talking about Xu Qing.

As rumors raged, Xu Qing left the north. By the use of several long-distance teleportation portals, he reached the eastern planetary system on the seventh day of the countdown. There were now only 735 permission medallions left.

He went directly to Mount Taia.[2]

Expression placid, he stepped onto the mountain. Mount Taia was the ninth of the most prominent mountains in the eastern planetary system. It towered majestically into the clouds, its surface pitch black, making it look like a dark blade stabbing up into the sky.

If you looked at it closely, you would see a network of red filaments running through the mountain, almost like blood vessels. According to legend, this mountain... was actually a horn! Supposedly, it was the horn of God Emperor Starhorn, who had served as one of the nine generals of the Fifth Star Ring’s God Paragon! That particular god emperor’s godhood was related to stars, and he was known as the number one God Lord serving under the God Paragon. Of course, very few people knew whether or not that legend was true.[3]

At the moment, someone was seated cross-legged at the very peak of Mount Taia. He was a young man clad in black. There was a grave and stern look to him, as well as some sort of wretched energy. He seemed to exude killing intent. Stabbed into the ground in front of him was a broken sword. His aura was so interconnected with the sword that it was impossible to distinguish between the two of them.

He was none other than Sir Vilespirit. All of a sudden, his eyes opened, and he looked at Xu Qing approaching him.

Xu Qing’s expression was neutral as he took a step forward, placing him about a tenth of the way up the mountain. He stopped walking.

Sitting on a boulder just ahead of him was a small white bottle. The bottle was open, and it exuded an aura that seemed like that of an immortal, but wasn’t. It also seemed like that of a god, yet wasn’t. Swirling within it was some sort of liquid.

When Xu Qing looked at it, the illusory reality emanating from his soul rippled. Obviously, the contents of the bottle were something that could be very beneficial to an immortal embryo.

“Ringsource...” Xu Qing murmured.

Ringsource was the most fundamental power in the thirty-six higher star rings. It formed the origin of gods and the structure of the star rings. Whether it was the godly authority of the gods, or the cultivator authority of the cultivators, substructurally speaking, they all came from ringsource. It was the same with both godhood and canon. It was something higher star rings literally could not be without. When cultivators formed an immortal embryo and then upgraded it to become a mature immortal, they absolutely had to use ringsource!

When all was said and done, if a cultivator was working on converting an immortal embryo into a mature immortal, it was necessary to acquire ringsource, even if it was by stealing it! This bottle could help Xu Qing take his immortal embryo a step further. Although he couldn’t reach the undying level yet, it would still be immensely helpful.

“Well, isn’t this interesting.” Xu Qing waved his hand and collected the bottle. Looking up at the peak of the mountain, he took a second step forward and vanished. When he reappeared... he was in the middle of the mountain.

There on a boulder in front of him was a green bottle. Inside it was a fist-sized clump of crimson clay. It was called god clay, and it was one of the tools Fifth Star Ring cultivators would use to control gods. By molding it into the shape of a god, you could control that god. It went without saying that it was astonishingly valuable.

Xu Qing took it and then stepped forward a third time. When his foot fell, he was near the top of the mountain. Lying in front of him was what appeared to be the stalk of a plant. However, it glittered with faint starlight. Xu Qing was familiar with this type of plant.

“Star ring hemp!” Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Star ring hemp grew in the far reaches of the outer sea in various star rings, and it was exceedingly rare. If you burned it, you could open a passageway between star rings. Star ring hemp was how Xu Qing had originally come to the Fifth Star Ring.[4]

It was smaller than the piece he had used in the past, but it was still extremely valuable. After a long moment, Xu Qing picked up the hemp and took a fourth step forward. When he appeared again, he was at the very top of the mountain, right in front of Sir Vilespirit!

Sir Vilespirit reached out, grabbed his broken sword, and yanked it out of the ground. The entire mountain trembled. Countless red filaments then flowed up the mountain and converged at the peak. It was as if they were being absorbed by the broken sword. Eventually, the sword was pure red. And then, that redness converged on the tip of the sword, where it emerged... as a drop of blood!

The moment that blood appeared, the sky trembled, the winds seethed, and rumbling as loud as heavenly thunder echoed out. Everything in the area rippled and distorted. The rest of the red filaments on the mountain quickly turned dark, and eventually disappeared, as if their last power had been drained away. That drop of blood on the sword became the only color in all heaven and earth!

When Xu Qing looked at the blood, he heard the sound of heavy breathing in his mind. It was Starfire, who seemed very excited.

“That’s the blood of a God Lord! And it’s a God Lord with godly authority similar to mine!! Xu Qing, I must have that drop of blood! If I absorb it, then I’ll not only be able to reach the Altar God level very quickly, but it would make it vastly more possible for me to eventually become a True God!”

Just as Starfire seemed to be on the verge of speaking out loud, Sir Vilespirit waved his hand. The drop of blood flew off the broken sword toward Xu Qing.

“Fellow Daoist Xu, you helped me a lot in the fourth world. The three gifts you took on your way up the mountain are repayment for that. As for this drop of God Lord blood... I broke my promise regarding the fox madam, and am offering this as compensation.”[5]

With that, Sir Vilespirit got to his feet and bowed to Xu Qing.

Xu Qing didn’t respond.

Sir Vilespirit turned and flew off the mountain. The broken sword followed. Once in the air, he bowed again, then became a bright streak of light that shot off into the distance.

Xu Qing watched him go and did nothing to stop him. The four gifts were given in thanks and compensation. But Xu Qing knew that they were also the price Sir Vilespirit was willing to pay to keep his Immortal Capital permission medallion.

“I can’t take all these gifts and then demand the medallion,” Xu Qing murmured, shaking his head. However, he didn’t leave. Instead, he looked at the horizon in the opposite direction. “Isn’t that right, Zhou Zhengli?”

As his words echoed out, ripples flowed over the horizon as Zhou Zhengli appeared. He happened to be carrying an unconscious, burly man. The man was criss-crossed with bloody wounds, and pulsed with an aura of death. He almost seemed like a puppet and not a person.

Zhou Zhengli neared, landed on the mountain in front of Xu Qing, and then tossed the burly man onto the ground. Clasping hands, he bowed respectfully.

“Well met, Young Lord.” He pointed at the burly man. “That guy’s name is Chen Batian. After I left the Fallen Immortal Moors, I tracked him down here in the east. He’s my personal gift to you. Take him. You can then be the number one Shining Star, and you can also take 1st place in the Trial of the Hunt!”

1. Chen Batian: Chen is listed #5 on the list of the 100 most common surnames. Ba means “tyrant, lord, rule by force, usurp” and Tian means “heaven/sky.” I guess you could interpret it to mean something like “lording it over heaven” or something similar. Madam Deathblade’s reaction upon seeing the name was, “this is the name of a bully.” Her reaction conforms to what it says in the paragraph that his name is “inelegant.” ☜

2. I’m transliterating this name as that seems to be the intent of the author. In other words, there is no meaning to the name. Taia in Chinese seems to be an alternate set of characters to describe a sword named Tai E, which was a real sword from ancient Chinese history. Here is a link to an article that mentions it. I also clipped that section of the article to save as an image, because you never know how long websites like that will keep articles up. ☜

3. The term ‘god emperor’ came up previously in chapters 808, 963, 966, 967, and 1007. Back then and now, it is not treated as a cultivation level. God Lord is a cultivation level, and as you can see in this passage, it seems to indicate that this ‘god emperor’ was in the God Lord cultivation level. And if you go back to 1007, you will see that same information stated outright. In other words ‘god emperor’ is a title used by God Lords. ☜

4. Xu Qing used star ring hemp to open the way to the Fifth Star Ring in chapter 1089. ☜

5. Sir Vilespirit uses a slightly different and more respectable form of address than the one used back in the immortal palace, which I’ve reflected by calling her fox madam instead of fox maiden. ☜

Xu Qing had never heard of Chen Batian before. After all, this Chen Batian had only jumped in the rankings when the one-month countdown began. Though he was the focus of a lot of attention, few cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring knew anything about him.

As time passed, more and more rumors spread about him. As it turned out, not one of the dramatic and fanciful rumors proved to be true. In the end... how could anyone guess that the top contender in the Trial of the Hunt had been prepared as a gift?

It was a gift that had been created out of nothing. At the moment, the person who had created this gift out of nothing was bowing deeply and smiling humbly.

That was the most terrifying thing about Zhou Zhengli. He had been very careful when dealing with the menacing Sir Star Ring. He didn’t reveal how dangerous he could be. And Xu Qing got the feeling that the conflict and grudge between him and Sir Vilespirit was a facade.

In all likelihood, Zhou Zhengli and Sir Vilespirit were doing it all on purpose. And was all done... to please people far more important and powerful than them. Those important people were interested in watching the show, and the willingness of Zhou Zhengli and Sir Vilespirit to go along with it was a way of showing subservience.

Xu Qing knew that he wasn’t one of those ‘important people,’ and he didn’t think Sir Star Ring was one of them either. He didn’t make demands of subservient people. To him, both the Fifth Star Ring and the Immortal Capital were just stops along a very long journey.

Since it was just a stop on the journey, he would be cautious... but do as he pleased. In other words, he didn’t care about Zhou Zhengli’s ulterior motives. Vipers were fine as long as they didn’t bare their fangs. But if the fangs came out, well, Xu Qing had already explained to Zhou Zhengli what would happen then. He liked to eat snakes. And venomous snakes tasted the best.

Besides, after everything he had experienced in his youth, plus his journeys in the Revered Ancient mainland, as well as the teachings of his Master and the tutelage of Erniu, Xu Qing... was far more venomous. Therefore, he only glanced at Zhou Zhengli before turning to look at Chen Batian.

“I selected Chen Batian very carefully,” Zhou Zhengli said in a soft voice. “I wanted to make sure he had no deep karmic ties. Incidentally, you could say that he’s evil through and through. Also given to lust.”

Zhou Zhengli knew that he had to make sure Xu Qing was comfortable accepting his gift. Therefore, he had picked someone without any karmic connections, and could thus be killed without worry about the consequences. That was the way to make sure his gift could be accepted without worry.

To further achieve that end, he bowed and backed away from Xu Qing and Chen Batian.

That was because Chen Batian was gasping for breath. The flame of his life force was just about to go out. Zhou Zhengli had taken measures along the way to ensure that Chen Batian would actually die of natural causes. And it would happen... very soon.

That way, there would be no misunderstandings. No one would believe that he had booby-trapped his gift. He had indirectly killed him in a way that had nothing to do with the person he was giving his gift to.

When a cultivator died in that way, their Immortal Capital permission medallion would automatically go to the person closest to them. That was why he had backed away.

Xu Qing said nothing. A few dozen breaths of time passed, and Chen Batian breathed his last.

The instant it happened, an Immortal Capital permission medallion flew out of him, dazzlingly bright. It shot toward Xu Qing, fused with him, and then the star chart appeared in the sky again. This time, the ranking list had changed.

1st place was now occupied by Xu Qing!

Zhou Zhengli again bowed to Xu Qing. Then he backed away before leaving Mount Taia and flying off into the distance.

Xu Qing didn’t stop him. After Zhou Zhengli disappeared over the horizon, Xu Qing blurred and stepped into space-time. Using space-time that way left no traces of his passage, and made it impossible to track his karma.

Shortly after, ripples spread out in the dome of heaven, and Zhou Zhengli appeared again. He looked down thoughtfully at Mount Taia.

Definitely very different from Sir Star Ring. If it had been Sir Star Ring, and he had such an advantage and such strength, he would definitely be a lot less cautious. In fact, he would probably stay around here until the trial was over.

But this Xu Qing... has the advantage, and even crushed all the Shining Stars. Yet even after getting gifts from both me and Sir Vilespirit, he still acts very cautiously. And it’s not something done with purpose. It’s actually... an instinct for him!

Zhou Zhengli sighed softly. Definitely not to be trifled with!

With that, he turned and vanished again.

***

There were only seven days left in the countdown. Thanks to the change to the ranking list, everyone in all the sects and organizations in the Fifth Star Ring knew about Xu Qing. And of course, it caused quite a shakeup.

Chen Batian disappeared and Xu Qing was in 1st place! More and more rumors were spreading about Xu Qing now. Him taking 1st place had a big effect on the various cultivators he had interacted with.

In the western planetary system, Li Mengtu was working harder than ever. Of course, since he was in fifth place, it was inevitable that he would reach the Immortal Capital. But when he saw the rankings list, he decided that he would still try to get more permission medallions.

I might not be able to surpass him, but at least I won’t fall behind.

There were similar sentiments in the southern planetary system. They existed in the Yuanshan Clan. They existed at Grand Immortal Mountain.

Yuanshan Su was in seclusion. She needed to achieve a cultivation base breakthrough before the end of the Trial of the Hunt. If she could become a Quasi-Immortal, then she would be able to get to the Immortal Capital. “I know I can do it!”

Jiang Fan chose a similar route to Yuanshan Su, and was working hard to that end.

In the northern planetary system, Hordeslayer and Rampart, thanks to how connected their Master was, had things a lot easier than Jiang Fan and Yuanshan Su. Both of them got new permission medallions and started over from the beginning. Given the level of their cultivation base and battle prowess, it wasn’t a very difficult task. All they had to do was fight enough people. However, given the limited time frame, the two of them were very busy. Whenever they rose through the rankings, they would see Xu Qing’s name and curse him. But at the same time, they would work harder.

Things were different in the eastern planetary system.

Sir Vilespirit and Zhou Zhengli both had stable spots on the ranking list, being in 2nd and 3rd place respectively. They had given up on trying to improve their ranking, and were simply waiting until the Trial of the Hunt ended.

What Sir Vilespirit and Zhou Zhengli were actually most focused on was... the Star Ring Pagoda! As far as they were concerned, that was the biggest variable in the entire trial!

***

Amidst the countless towering pagodas that made up the headquarters of the Star Ring Pagoda, there was one pagoda that was taller than all the others, and it shone with dazzling starlight. At the moment, that starlight was all pouring into a complicated spell formation.

A young man was seated cross-legged in the formation. The starlight flowed through the rotating formation into the young man and through his meridians. Thanks to the process, his body had become completely fused with the pagoda.

A strong immortal aura pulsed from him, and if you looked closely, it came from... his immortal embryo! After experiencing the illusory reality and the undying, it was possible to form the immortal embryo. It was the hallmark of Quasi-Immortals. That was why the starlight acted as meridians, the pagoda as his bones, and the immortal embryo as his fleshly body. It was turning into...

Sir Star Ring!

Within the pagoda, someone spoke in a raspy voice.

“If there are no twists and turns during the tribulation, then how could good fortune spring from extreme adversity? My apprentice, you have already accepted the tribulation, and perished in the process. That was simply your destiny. As your Master, I have remolded your body, and thus, you can achieve ultimate balance and continue on the path of the immortal!”

As the words echoed out, Sir Star Ring’s eyes suddenly opened, and boundless starlight spilled out of them, making the pagoda even more dazzling.

“He’s out there, waiting for you,” the raspy voice said.

After a moment of silence, Sir Star Ring shook his head. “No.”

“Why not?”

“I can’t defeat him. If I fight him now, I’ll lose the name Star Ring. There’s no rush. I can fight him... at the Immortal Capital!”

“Well said!”

***

Outside of the Star Ring Pagoda there was a mountain called Ninth Heaven. At the peak of Mount Ninth Heaven, Xu Qing sat cross-legged, staring at the boundless Star Ring Pagoda headquarters. The crimson aurora made the starlight of the towers especially prominent. And the spot where the starlight was gathering was the same spot Xu Qing was staring at.

He was waiting for Sir Star Ring. The moment he arrived in the eastern planetary system, he had sensed Sir Star Ring’s aura. It was obvious that Sir Star Ring... had returned. Thus, he had come here to wait for Sir Star Ring to come out and fight.

Sadly, even after waiting for quite a while, Sir Star Ring never came out. Xu Qing’s facial expression remained the same as usual. He wasn’t inclined to force the issue.

He closed his eyes. Days passed. Eventually, there was only one day left in the countdown. Then one hour. Then one second.... It passed!

Rumbling sounds could be heard in the sky over the Fifth Star Ring. They grew louder and louder, filling the east, and ultimately, the entire Fifth Star Ring. Countless cultivators, regardless of what they were doing, all went silent and looked up into the sky.

A voice rang out.

“The Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt is over. Now, the top 100 will enter the Immortal Capital!”

Innumerable cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring were filled with excitement, and looked on in envy as numerous seven-colored beams of light descended from the aurora. There were a total of ninety-nine, and they were distributed among the qualified trial-takers in all four planetary systems. They were like shining roads of light leading upward.

All Fifth Star Ring cultivators dreamed of stepping on the road that led to the Immortal Capital. These prismatic beams of light were why the participants had gone through so much hardship. It was why they had shed so much blood and killed so many enemies. Now, their hearts were racing. This was the moment they had been fighting for!

One by one, they prepared to step into the light. But just before they did, more thunderous rumbling sounds issued forth above to fill the Fifth Star Ring.

Countless individuals looked on as a beam of light far brighter and more colorful than all of the others descended, almost like a river. Compared to this beam of light, the others were like little streams. It was a majestic and boundless river that shone with blinding light. It descended from above and landed in the east, at Mount Ninth Heaven.

Everyone was shaken.

Xu Qing opened his eyes and looked at the bright path of light. He rose and stepped into the light. The moment he did, he was whisked upward.

Meanwhile, other cultivators in other areas were also flying upward. All were heading toward what lay beyond the dome of heaven... the supreme Immortal Capital.

It was a most holy occasion during the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt! It was a moment that countless cultivators dreamed of. Countless living beings would witness the moment in which the qualified participants ascended to the Immortal Capital!

Xu Qing was in the brightest beam of light that advanced ever upward. Behind him, ninety-nine beams of light rose from the four planetary systems, all of them bearing cultivators who were going to the Immortal Capital.

As of this moment, they were the center of all attention in the four planetary systems. As of this moment, they were entirely worthy of being called stars. As of this moment, the four planetary systems were all peaceful and quiet as the scene played out in the canopy of heaven.

Of course, the vast majority of people could only see some of what was happening. But the truly powerful experts in the four planetary systems could see how unique the most brightly shining of the light was. As everyone watched, the people in the beams of light rose higher and higher, getting closer and closer to the aurora. And finally... they turned crimson as they entered the aurora, one after another.

***

There was no starry sky above the aurora. There was only a foggy haze.

Within the haze were a hundred four-sided pillars, all of them very ancient and weathered. They were terraced, so that the tallest pillar was in the very middle, with pillars stretching out almost in a triangular shape on either side, with each successive pillar shorter than the one before it. As a whole, they looked like the character for ‘person’: 人.

All of the pillars glittered with seven-colored light. They seemed to have existed for countless years, to have witnessed innumerable magnificent things, and now pulsed with infinite majesty.

The light they exuded turned into numerous prismatic beams. They dropped down below the aurora and into the four planetary systems. They became the subject of all attention there.

The light coming from the central pillar was the brightest as... Xu Qing rose through the aurora within it! He was the first of the hundred cultivators to emerge from the aurora. As the aurora flowed around him, he seemed almost like something going from the bottom of a river up to the surface of the water.

Upon breaking the surface, he saw the infinite haze, as well as the one hundred seven-colored pillars. He didn’t hesitate. He approached the pillars and alighted on the tallest of them, the one in the center.

There he stood. Turning, he looked down. The vast aurora was like a crimson sea. Inside of it, ninety-nine beams of light contained more cultivators who were ascending to their corresponding pillars.

Among the crowd, Xu Qing spotted Zhou Zhengli, who smiled humbly. freewebnovel.com

He saw Sir Vilespirit, who bowed his head.

He saw Yuanshan Su, who avoided his gaze.

He saw Li Mengtu, who looked excited.

He saw Hordeslayer and Rampart. They usually acted proud and arrogant, but now they seemed to shrink in on themselves.

Xu Qing studied the group. The majority of the faces were unfamiliar to him, but there were some he recognized. Jiang Fan wasn’t there. But what was shocking was... a young man in black! He exuded a sensation of order, and was orbited by chains of starlight. Almost as soon as Xu Qing looked at him, he looked back.

Sir Star Ring!

Xu Qing remained completely calm. He was not surprised to see all of these people here. And he had long since come to sense that Sir Star Ring had awoken. He had gone to the Star Ring Pagoda sometime earlier and waited for a while, but Sir Star Ring never came. As a result, Xu Qing wasn’t taken by surprise at all to see him here. He quickly looked away from him.

Ignoring all the cultivators landing on the pillars, Xu Qing looked up at the haze. He had always felt that the Fifth Star Ring wasn’t very big. He had come to that conclusion after comparing it to the Revered Ancient mainland. It wasn’t that Revered Ancient was larger. It was a fact that the four planetary systems of the Fifth Star Ring were vast in size. Even just a single one of them would surpass Revered Ancient. Most cultivators could fly for an entire lifetime and never leave one of the planetary systems. Despite that, Xu Qing still felt that the Fifth Star Ring was small.

Based on the star ring map he had seen years ago that depicted the thirty-six higher star rings, he knew that a star ring should be incredibly large. But that was not what he had experienced in the Fifth Star Ring.

Of course, he knew that some of it was because of how the Fifth Star Ring had been compacted. It made sense considering that the various layers of a starry sky were all the same instance of space. After being compacted, the Fifth Star Ring turned into a landmass, and therefore, the way one perceived it with the senses would be different.

But when all was said and done, that was only one factor, and there was definitely a much more relevant explanation. It was a theory Xu Qing had developed after traveling to all four planetary systems. Yet now....

As he stood atop the ancient pillar looking at the haze, Xu Qing’s thoughts went wild. He was struck with a sudden premonition that the real Fifth Star Ring... was what he was looking at right now.

Anticipation filled him. The other cultivators in the area felt similarly. They didn’t have to wait long. Soon, the final person stepped onto the pillar, and the haze began to seethe. An indescribably heavy force was clearing the fog, as if an invisible hand were waving it away. And then... the haze that had been blocking their view vanished without a trace.

A majestic starry sky was now visible to them! Within the infinitude was a huge whirlpool that occupied about ninety percent of the starry sky. It seemed still, but if you looked closely you would realize it was rotating.

Xu Qing and the other cultivators on the pillars were minuscule in comparison. Everyone could sense that the astonishing whirlpool was full of a massive amount of heavenly bodies, and all of them had life on them as well as the aura of immortals. And yet, as everyone soaked in the astonishing sight... it was as if some immense power shrank that starry sky down. The whirlpool also shrank down rapidly.

And as it shrank down, an even more majestic whirlpool of stars appeared within the starry sky. The whirlpool from before wasn’t visible. But it hadn’t disappeared, it had shrunk down, revealing that it was one of millions upon millions of whirlpools.
