His mind spun. Yet things weren’t over. The giant whirlpool of stars shrank down again. Xu Qing and the other cultivators saw countless astonishing whirlpools of stars forming together into a huge star chart. Or, put more precisely, it was a star domain!

If the first thing they had seen was the star domain, they wouldn’t have been able to grasp how large it was. But after seeing everything shrink down, it was obvious that it was so immense it defied description.

And yet... things still weren’t over.

The star domain shrank down, revealing a host of innumerable star domains, an infinitude that became a complete universe! Yet even as the universe became visible, the starry sky blurred, and... countless universes appeared to them. Then the universes shrank.

The starry sky trembled. Ultimately... an immense figure became visible in front of them. It was not a true body. Instead, it was made of countless planetary systems, galaxies, star domains, and universes! This person’s features were indistinguishable, but he was surrounded by the most paramount of sensations.

This figure was not the Immortal Paragon of the Fifth Star Ring! And that was because as the figure made up of countless universes appeared, the starry sky shrank again, revealing that, astonishingly, there were ten other such figures!

There were a total of eleven! They were like heavens beyond heaven! They were the eleven Immortal Lords of the Fifth Star Ring!

Each one was magnificent.

Xu Qing and all of the other hundred cultivators felt like they were being battered by waves of astonishment. Rumbling sounds filled Xu Qing’s mind and heart as he looked at the eleven figures.

One of the figures, despite having indistinguishable facial features, was immediately recognizable to Xu Qing thanks to his experience in the immortal palace.

That person was... Immortal Lord Nineshores! There was something unique about Immortal Lord Nineshores compared to the others. In front of him was a ring made of starlight.

As soon as Xu Qing saw the ring, he realized what it was. It was the ring of the epoch. It was currently... the Nineshores Epoch!

Xu Qing took a deep breath and suppressed the excitement in his heart as he looked at the other Immortal Lords. He was hoping to spot... Grandmaster Bai! Eventually, his gaze settled on the ninth of the Immortal Lords. It was a majestic figure who seemed to be an old man. It wasn’t possible to see his face clearly, but he had a medicinal decocting pot in his hands that immediately struck Xu Qing with a sense of familiarity.

The old man looked down at Xu Qing, and a very faint smile appeared on his lips. Xu Qing smiled back and then bowed.

After that, the starry sky blurred again, and the sensation of shrinking occurred again. And then, the heavens beyond heaven that were the eleven Immortal Lords shrank down. Behind them was an even more majestic figure who seemed unsurpassably holy, and who was mighty enough to occupy the entire starry sky.

This was the origin of all immortals! This was the paragon of the Fifth Star Ring. This was he who had crushed the gods. He was... the Immortal Paragon!

The eleven heavens beyond heaven all orbited around him. This was the true Fifth Star Ring!

After being taken over by cultivators, it was compressed, and that process caused the different parts of it to occupy heavens beyond heaven.

As for the four great planetary systems of east, west, south and north, they were the original homeland! They were where everything had started.

Fundamentally speaking, there wasn’t actually an Immortal Capital. The original homeland was the Immortal Capital. That was where the Fifth Star Ring’s pureblooded humans existed.

All of the fighting, killing, and bitterness was designed to raise pureblooded humans. It was all for the future of the Fifth Star Ring. The cultivators who came from there all had politically correct family backgrounds and educations. In the future, they would be tasked with an important mission.

As for the lives of those in the heavens beyond heaven, in some ways, they were simply collateral relatives. In fact, most of them weren’t even human, but instead, had just been blessed with human bloodlines. All of these things did not need to be conveyed with words. As soon as Xu Qing and the other cultivators saw the majestic scene in front of them, they understood.

“Now I get it....” Xu Qing murmured.

And then, among the eleven heavens beyond heaven, Immortal Lord Nineshores, whose turn it was to oversee the epoch, opened his eyes.

“Ascendees, you will now enter my own heaven beyond heaven.”

From the land of origin, a hundred ships had sailed into the Immortal Capital. It was the grand, majestic tradition of the four great planetary systems of east, west, south and north.

What they found out after arriving wasn’t necessarily top secret. After all, there were immortals in all four of the orthodox organizations, as well as some core Quasi-Immortals, who knew the truth.

The Immortal Capital was actually a project being carried out by cultivators after taking over the Fifth Star Ring. It was a project designed to nurture pureblooded humans. The project had gone on in the past, and it would continue to go on in the future.

To the upper echelons of leadership in the Fifth Star Ring, cultivators weren’t nourished and nurtured. They were born out of struggle. They went against the stream and fought to survive. It reflected how the cultivators from a minor world had eventually fought their way to the point of overthrowing the gods that had ruled the Fifth Star Ring.

They did not want to lose that spirit! They did not want greenhouse flowers. They wanted like-minded people who never let go of their killing intent and their determination to strive forward. Only cultivators like that counted as being pureblooded humans that could be responsible for the future, and could survive in the higher star rings, surrounded by gods.

Low-level cultivators might need special circumstances to develop such qualities. But it was built into these cultivators who had just ascended. The cultivators who had reached this point were resolute individuals who had developed their own ways of understanding and perceiving things. Those with similar ideals could walk together. Those with dissimilar ideals would not be forced to stay. It was a demonstration of the confidence of the Fifth Star Ring cultivators.

Unfortunately, the rest of the thirty-six higher star rings were lands occupied by gods, so those with dissimilar ideals... would have to become gods if they wanted to go somewhere else. The factions had long since been determined. freewebnovel.com

That was why the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt was held over and over again. It was also why Immortal Lord Nineshores had called them ascendees! They had ascended from their homeland.

The rules of the Fifth Star Ring stated that whichever Immortal Lord was reigning over the current epoch would accept all of the ascendees into their immortal palace. It was currently the Nineshores epoch. Therefore, Xu Qing and the rest of the cultivators responded to the voice of Immortal Lord Nineshores by flying off the pillars.

They shot... right toward Immortal Lord Nineshores’ heaven beyond heaven made of countless planetary systems, galaxies, star whirlpools, star domains, and universes.

The instant Xu Qing entered, a plethora of stars appeared before his eyes, like infinite star charts. There was no limit. There was no end. It was so vast, and the cultivators were so insignificant, that they felt like ants.

Then, someone spoke in a majestic voice.

“This, which occupies only a small percentage of the Fifth Star Ring, is... the Nineshores Heaven!”

It was not Immortal Lord Nineshores. The owner of the voice appeared in front of Xu Qing and the others, and he was an old man in a white daoist robe. He had the demeanor of a transcendent being, like someone who could tread through starry skies and universes.

“I am Xu Daoyun, a reception elder here in the Nineshores Immortal Palace. I am tasked with receiving you and offering a bit of an explanation along the way.”

His gaze swept over them, and all of them trembled inwardly. Those who had canon treasures felt such treasures dimming as if they were being suppressed. Those with true canon had it slightly better off, but still felt as if the gaze were weighing down on their canon and making it difficult to operate. It was a gaze that pierced into the depths of even Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring, and left them feeling powerless to resist.

Xu Qing had experienced something like this before. Back in Revered Ancient, he had stood with Grand Emperor Swordsage and faced a Lower Immortal who wanted to enter the mainland. The feeling was similar. The difference was that the feeling now was far more intense.[1]

Immortal...!

Xu Qing took a deep breath. Sir Star Ring also bowed his head. To him, this old man was giving him a sensation similar to his Master. If the two strongest members of the group of one hundred felt that way, there was little need to mention the others. All of them quickly bowed.

The old man’s expression remained the same as he continued, “There is no end to the heavenly bodies in the Nineshores Heaven. New heavenly bodies are born constantly, and old ones fall. The orbits are not eternal. The star domains are not fixed in place. The universes rise and fall.

“Assuming there are no setbacks, then this is where you will practice cultivation going forward. Furthermore, as cultivators who have ascended from the homeland, you will now be given a reward!

“Everyone here will be given a universe in the Nineshores Heaven to serve as your mansion grotto! All of the star domains, star whirlpools, galaxies, and planets within it belong to you!”

All hearts surged with excitement.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered at the generosity of the Fifth Star Ring, and the importance with which it treated ascendees! All the resources of a universe were being given to help one person grow stronger! It could well be imagined that even a relatively barren universe would still have vast amounts of immortal energy in it. That wasn’t to mention all of the other items and resources it would contain.

It was definitely proper to say that whoever got this reward would be... paramount in the universe they were given!

Even Xu Qing was moved by this reward. Yet the anticipation he felt in his heart continued to grow more intense. And that was because he had taken 1st place. It went without saying that his reward wouldn’t be limited to this.

The white-robed old man once again spoke. “The universe is only the first reward. But before moving onto the second, I need to address the 1st place ascendee....” His gaze shifted to Xu Qing. “There are certain special universes in the Nineshores Heaven, and each one is considered a strategic resource. Since you took 1st place... you are hereby rewarded with a first-class universe. The Inksun Universe! Later on, you can discover for yourself what’s so special about it.

“Now, as for the second reward.... Everyone will receive a treasure or canon augmentation. For those of you who have magical treasures with no canon, you can have canon added to them. Those who already have canon in a magical treasure can have it improved. Or you can request to have the canon taken out of the treasure and put inside of you! It will be your choice how to use this reward.

“In addition, those who made it into the top 10 will be given the chance to have a Lower Immortal personally forge you a piece of equipment. To take advantage of this reward, you can go to the Daoforge Universe! Few people can ever get a destined opportunity like this, so treasure it, all of you.”

At this point, the old man’s gaze shifted from the top 10 in general to once again focus on Xu Qing. “Since you took 1st place, you will be given one opportunity to visit the Heroic Immortal Tombs. Here in the Nineshores Heaven, the Heroic Immortal Tombs have served for countless years as a place to inter the bodies of Lower Immortals who fell in battle. There, you can find canon and immortal treasures, all of which can be acquired based on your own good fortune.”

As the old man spoke, Xu Qing could feel everyone else looking at him. Clearly, their gazes were full of envy. That was especially true of people like Hordeslayer and Rampart, who had once been in the Shining Stars, and had benefited from help and equipment provided by Lower Immortals.

Other than the universe, the other rewards weren’t very enticing to them. But when they heard about the Heroic Immortal Tombs, they couldn’t help but fill with longing. After all, though they might have benefited from the help of a Lower Immortal, there was no way that such a Master would pass on canon to them unless it was unneeded. And they wouldn’t give up their most powerful and useful canon treasures. After all, they were still alive.

But the Heroic Immortal Tombs were different. They contained the remains of dead Lower Immortals, and the canon there would be masterless. And any treasures they left behind... as long as they hadn’t been destroyed in the battle that led to their death, would definitely be spectacular.

Any other type of good fortune would be similar. The destined opportunities in the Heroic Immortal Tombs were like true legacies! Even Sir Star Ring was sighing inwardly.

It was only natural that Xu Qing understood how precious of an opportunity he was being given, so he ducked his head and bowed.

Looking away from him, the old man continued, “The Nineshores Heaven isn’t just the location of your mansion grotto going forward. You will also be given an official assignment here. However, you will be given some time to rest and enjoy your rewards. One year. A year from now, you will be summoned to the Reception Universe, where the relevant personnel will make arrangements for your assignment. And now, you’re all dismissed.”

The old man waved his hand, and a host of wooden immortal slips flew out toward the hundred cultivators.

In the vast majority of cases, each cultivator got two immortal slips. One was a teleportation talisman leading to the universe that they had been rewarded with, while the other would augment a treasure or canon. A handful of people got three immortal slips, with the extra one being the opportunity to have equipment forged by a Lower Immortal. Xu Qing was the only one who got four!

After distributing the immortal slips, the old man said nothing more. He simply faded away into nothing.

After he was gone, some people left excitedly. However, most of them didn’t leave. Instead, they hurried over to Xu Qing. They had all arrived together, and no one knew what post they would be assigned to. For all anyone knew, they might end up working together. And since Xu Qing had taken 1st place, he would surely start out with an important position. Obviously, the smartest thing to do was try to befriend him.

As people clustered around Xu Qing and made small talk, Sir Star Ring flew off looking proud and aloof. He soon disappeared. Yuanshan Su hesitated for a moment before making the choice to leave.

It almost wasn’t necessary to mention Hordeslayer and Rampart. They rushed away at the earliest possible moment, worried that if they didn’t get away quickly enough, Xu Qing might order them to come over to him. They definitely did not want everyone seeing them being under his control, or possibly rushing over to him excitedly.... The mere thought of such a scene left them feeling uncomfortable.

Xu Qing paid little attention to them as he exchanged words with the other ascendees. Then, after they had given each other transmission jade slip contact information, the ascendees began to depart.

Now that Zhou Zhengli and Sir Vilespirit had ascended to the Nineshores Heaven, it seemed that their previous violent animosity for each other had changed. Though they hadn’t been standing next to each other, it spoke volumes that they stayed behind after everyone else had left.

“See you in a year, Brother Xu!” Sir Vilespirit said, clasping hands before leaving.

Zhou Zhengli and Li Mengtu were the last to leave. The former smiled in the same self-deprecating way as always.

“Young Lord, my guess... is that a year from now, the whole lot of us are going to get the same assignment.” With that, he respectfully departed.

Sighing inwardly, Li Mengtu exchanged a glance with Xu Qing, then turned to leave. Just before departing, he said, “Any time. Just say the word. I owe you my life. And more.”

Xu Qing watched them all leave. Then he smiled and, eyes gleaming with anticipation, made his way off into the distance. Then he sent his divine will into the teleportation slip and... vanished.

He was heading to his very own... Inksun Universe!

1. Grand Emperor Swordsage and Xu Qing faced the Lower Immortal in chapter 1086. Remember that in Chinese, Lower Immortal and Summer Immortal are pronounced exactly the same. ☜

How big was the Inksun Universe...? Xu Qing wasn’t actually sure. True, he was the paramount entity in the Inksun Universe, and could destroy the entire system with a thought. Unfortunately, the range of his divine will wasn’t sufficient to encompass the entire universe.

That said, when being teleported inside, he was able to see it in its entirety on the approach.

The Inksun Universe resembled the two curved horns of a goat, composed of innumerable galaxies and whirlpools of stars. They were connected at the bottom, so that the entire structure looked like an irregularly shaped ellipse. Taken as a whole, it also looked like a fish. To be most precise, the Inksun Universe looked like a big fish with the horns of a goat.

It was majestic. When it came to the planets, star systems, star whirlpools, and star domains, they were densely packed.... And there was shining light everywhere. They were... suns. Some places had life, some had death.

That was all Xu Qing could take in before he got too close to take in its entirety.

The teleportation abilities in the Nineshores Heaven surpassed anything Xu Qing could perceive or comprehend. Clearly, they were the result of extensive research carried out in the cultivation system in the Fifth Star Ring. These teleportations could cover multiple universes to send a person to a specific starry sky. It definitely surpassed the normal limitations of space. It was something beyond description.

This is what civilization feels like.... It’s a civilization of immortals.

On the way inside the Inksun Universe, Xu Qing wondered what was special about it. Given what the reception elder had said, he needed to explore it to find out. Considering that the Inksun Universe was of special strategic significance, he got the feeling that the high-level living beings inside it would probably have a good idea of its unique nature.

It was still getting bigger and bigger from his point of view. Galaxies flowed past him like rain water, until he saw his destination!

It was an immortal hall! Crafted from a pitch-black asteroid, it looked big, but compared to the starry sky in general, it was minute. That said, the size of a structure in this universe was unrelated to the power and status it represented. It could be tiny, and all living beings would still prostrate in worship to it!

In the Inksun Universe, this was the most holy location in existence. It was ancient, archaic, and magnificent.

Surrounding it... were countless figures, all of them bowing. Most of them were humanoid in appearance, although there were small differences between them and ordinary humans. There were some that were very obviously nonhuman. There were even some that emanated terrifying beastly auras. There seemed no end to them, and when it came to their cultivation base, there were Smoldering Gods and even Imperial Sovereigns. These were the lords of the various star domains in the Inksun Universe.

The Fifth Star Ring was huge, and though humans had started out as a minority there, considering it was a civilization of cultivators, it was little surprise that they had proliferated so dramatically. But compared to a magnificent conglomeration of many universes, it was like a drop of water in the ocean.

And yet the humans that made up that drop of water had ultimately become the rulers of all the other species in the Fifth Star Ring!

These nonhumans were really the progeny of the gods. That was where they had come from. But they had been forced into servitude, and after many generations had passed in the Fifth Star Ring, the blood of the gods in them had long since been sealed. As a result, there was a limit to how much they could grow, and they had to treat humans as their lords.

In other words, they had no choice but to walk the same path as the cultivators. Because of their blood being sealed, they could rise no higher than the Imperial Sovereign level. People who were not human could not become immortals!

The only exception... were individuals of strategic importance. Only then could the seals be removed, allowing them to fight and die for the Fifth Star Ring.

The end result was that the ascendees who had just come from the original homeland were like royalty to these nonhumans! Xu Qing was the lord of this universe, so when he came, all its servants would come to worship.

As the powerful experts prostrated, the immortal hall atop the asteroid began to shine with dazzling immortal light. All nine colors shimmered, creating a flowing sea of light that swept throughout the surrounding starry sky.

The starry sky trembled. All heads were bowed. The door of the immortal hall opened.

Xu Qing stepped out. At the same time, he absorbed the immortal slip that had just teleported him here. Of course, that slip didn’t just function as a teleportation device. More so... it was a symbol of the highest level of power in the Inksun Universe. It created a resonance with the immortal hall, with the starry sky, with all the countless star domains, and with the entire universe.

The countless nonhuman cultivators all bowed lower.

“Greetings, Your Majesty!”

“Greetings, Your Majesty!”

“Greetings, Your Majesty!”

A chorus of voices swept out into the starry sky with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. The momentum of the combined voices grew more and more intense.

Xu Qing looked around with a calm expression. As he stood at the door of the hall, he closed his eyes. After arriving, opening the door of the immortal hall, and absorbing the immortal slip, he became recognized as the lord of the Inksun Universe. After that, the entire universe existed in his mind.

And thus, he sent his thoughts out like an unstoppable wave through all the star domains, galaxies, and planets. The entire place was full of strong immortal energy. Some of that immortal energy was emanating from the planets. Surprisingly, some of it... existed in the living beings, and came from their life force. This was what it meant to use a universe to nurture a chosen!

Xu Qing opened his eyes. He retracted his divine will, and then over a thousand of the nonhumans flew up to the immortal hall and lined up to speak respectfully to him.

“Your Majesty, the Inksun Universe contains 700,000,000,000,000 galaxies. Every galaxy contains....”

“Your Majesty, the total number of species in the Inksun Universe is....”

“Your Majesty, there are many resources in the Inksun Universe, but the most abundant are the black suns....”

“Your Majesty, there are a number of pocket realms and treasure lands in the Inksun Universe. Specifically....”

Xu Qing received a full report of everything in the Inksun Universe.

As he was listening, he suddenly turned his head to look off into the distance. Interrupting the report that was being given, he pointed and said, “There’s a cultivator right there. Who is it?”

He was pointing in the direction of the spot where the two fish horns connected at the fish’s head. By means of divine will, Xu Qing could see that there was an area of darkness there, a spot cut off from divine will that contained terrifying mightiness. Though it was cut off from senses, it seemed like there was an incomparably massive black sun there, emanating infinite black light and fire. Either that, or it was a black hole inside that could devour anything and everything. It was extremely unique.

But when he sent his divine will to examine it further, the stream of divine will vanished. What made it vanish wasn’t the strange heavenly body that resembled a black sun or a black hole. It was a figure hovering cross-legged next to the black hole. That person seemed to be emitting Quasi-Immortal cultivation base fluctuations, and was able easily crush Xu Qing’s divine will out of existence.

In response to Xu Qing’s question, the cultivators who had gathered outside the immortal hall exchanged awkward glances.

Then one of them spoke in a trembling voice. “Your Majesty, that area is the Inkland, which formed after this universe’s very first sun was extinguished. It’s also been named a restricted area by the immortal palace. We’re not allowed to even get close to it. As for the person guarding it....”

The cultivator hesitated. Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed.

Bowing his head, the cultivator continued, “It’s the exalted Kun Wu. Just like Your Majesty, he’s human. Before you came along, the exalted Kun Wu was the acting lord here. He’s the only one who has the right to practice cultivation in restricted areas.”[1]

“Acting lord?” Xu Qing’s gaze turned cold.

1. Kun Wu. Kun is not a common surname. It’s most commonly known as the Chinese character from Kun Lun. The meaning of the term ‘acting lord’ was self-evident. This person was temporarily in charge. He was a human with a Quasi-Immortal cultivation base, which was befitting of such a position.

“Your Majesty, the likes of us can only speculate about your identity. Presumably, the Nineshores Immortal Palace decreed that this universe was to be your personal property....” A nonhuman cultivator stepped forward who looked like an old human man, except that he had a third eye. Bowing respectfully, he continued, “From ancient times until now, the only people rewarded with this glory are pureblooded ascendees from the Immortal Capital. This seems to indicate that Your Majesty is an ascendee from the Immortal Capital.

“As for the exalted Kun Wu... well, he’s similar to yourself, Your Majesty. Supposedly, he was an ascendee from the Immortal Capital who had his own universe. But this place was apparently more suitable for his style of cultivation. So he came over here about a thousand years ago and never left.... He’s human, and the Nineshores Heaven is just so huge....”

At this point, the old man looked up hesitantly at Xu Qing in the immortal hall. “In the Nineshores Heaven, any universe with no lord in its immortal hall is considered unoccupied. And thus, human cultivators will often go into them to practice cultivation. Before the exalted Kun Wu came to the Inksun Universe, there were other humans who had settled down here. But they were all driven away when the exalted Kun Wu showed up.”

The old man was being very careful with his words. He clearly didn’t want to offend either Kun Wu or the new lord in the immortal hall.

Xu Qing thought about that for a moment. “In other words, you call him the acting lord, but that’s just a form of address, and not an official position?”

The old man hesitated but ultimately nodded. “Yes. The Inksun Universe’s immortal hall has been without a lord for many years until now. Because of that, a lot of humans have come and gone.... And so, for the past thousand years, we’ve just gone along with whatever the exalted Kun Wu told us to do.” He smiled wryly. “Truth be told... there are so many universes in the Nineshores Heaven that the likelihood of an ascendee being given the Inksun Universe was always remote. In fact, we were surprised when we found out Your Majesty was coming here. Presumably, the exalted Kun Wu is also surprised.”

Xu Qing’s gaze turned even colder. Now he understood some of the unstated rules in the Nineshores Heaven. The Nineshores Heaven was a huge place and had many, many universes. It wasn’t possible for all of them to have official lords ruling over them. As a result, many were unoccupied. The unoccupied universes would naturally be attractive to cultivators. And any human who entered one of them could basically do anything they wanted with them.

Perhaps the Nineshores Immortal Palace tacitly approves. After all, the Fifth Star Ring seems to foster intense competition to identify who’s strongest! It’s natural selection.

Xu Qing looked at the strange area known as the Inkland. If these nonhumans know about my arrival, there’s no way this human doesn’t know. Given that he hasn’t left, and even went so far as to destroy my divine will, I guess I have to treat him as a squatter. And the only thing to do with squatters is drive them away.

Paying no further attention to the nonhumans, he strode out of the immortal hall, left the asteroid, and made his way into the starry sky. Space-time flowed beneath his feet, and the void rippled. To the astonishment of the nonhuman leaders, he used his divine will as a guide to step onto the thread of the timescape in the Inksun Universe as if it were a string on an instrument.... There was a twang. He vanished.

The bowing nonhuman cultivators were all astonished to the core. That was especially true of the peak Imperial Sovereigns. These were extraordinary individuals. In fact, if they weren’t being restrained by the Fifth Star Ring, they would already have reached immortal ascension. It was only natural that they were extremely knowledgeable. And the more knowledgeable one was, the more astonished they would be by what they had just seen.

“Space-time?”

“His Majesty’s canon... is that of space-time??”

“He’s only an Imperial Sovereign, and his immortal embryo is still only in illusory reality. But just now, he didn’t give off the sensation of being a mere Imperial Sovereign!”

“I wonder... how did he rank among the other ascendees?”

In the depths of the Inksun Universe, where the fish head was, in the location that could not be penetrated by divine will, just on the border of the area that seemed to contain a black hole like a sun... a middle-aged cultivator sat cross-legged.

He wore an embroidered robe, had flowing, blue hair, and though his eyes were closed, his facial expression was cold. Astonishingly, he had a fishing pole in his hand! And the fishing line went right down into the black hole!

Frowning, he opened his eyes and looked at the starry sky in front of him. To him, it looked like the starry sky in front of him was being folded. It was like a piece of paper being folded over many times. It soon looked like a door, out of which Xu Qing emerged.

Xu Qing looked expressionlessly at the fishing cultivator, then looked at the fishing line going down into the Inkland black hole. Behind him, the starry sky went back to normal.

Ringsource? Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Previously, he had only sent a bit of divine will here, and it had been shattered very quickly. And since he had been focused on the squatter, he hadn’t had a chance to study the mysterious black hole. Now that he was here in person, he could sense that it contained the power of ringsource.

Perhaps because of the unique nature of the Inkland, or maybe the gravitational force from the black hole itself, the ringsource couldn’t get out. The only way to get it out was to fish it out.

Even still, Xu Qing couldn’t help but be a bit excited. Although the ringsource was trapped and not easy to get out, that didn’t change the fact that ringsource was the foundation of the higher star rings, and was considered the most elemental type of power.

It was also absolutely critical to forming the immortal embryo! This type of power was extremely precious!

Is this why the Inksun Universe is said to be of strategic importance?

Xu Qing decided that he would look further into the situation. Looking away from the black hole, he turned to the middle-aged cultivator.

“Leave this place,” he growled.

The middle-aged cultivator was, of course, Kun Wu. Looking up at Xu Qing with a grim expression, he coolly said, “So you’re a new ascendee?”

Xu Qing didn’t answer the question. He just looked calmly at Kun Wu.

Kun Wu’s eyes narrowed as he sized up Xu Qing. Although he couldn’t see every detail, he was able to determine that Xu Qing wasn’t a Quasi-Immortal, but did have Quasi-Immortal battle prowess. And he could sense the space-time fluctuations around him. His guard went up.

After a moment of thought, he said, “Did you know that I’m originally from Grand Immortal Mountain. This universe of yours used to be special, but it’s degraded into something ordinary.... I’ll be making use of it for a short time longer. No more than three hundred years. In terms of compensation—”

Before he could finish speaking, Xu Qing extended his right hand and unleashed his space-time canon. He seized control of the time of all living beings and things in the Inksun Universe! In any other universe, Xu Qing would not have been able to do such a thing with his current cultivation base. After all, even just a single universe was immeasurably large.

But the Inksun Universe was different. From the moment he arrived and became the lord of the immortal hall in this universe, the karma of the Inksun Universe became like a servant to him. This place... was his personal property. It was similar to the god cultivation system in which gods had god kingdoms of their own.[1]

Earlier, his divine will could make use of karma to spread throughout the universe. Now, he was doing the same thing with his space-time canon. All of the time in the entire Inksun Universe surged, and under the direction of Xu Qing’s canon, it swept toward him.

A sound echoed out like the water of a river. Crashing waves could be heard. A majestic, flowing body of water appeared, growing larger and larger. Eventually... this universe’s River of Time appeared in Xu Qing’s right hand!

The astonishing river contained projected images of all the living beings here. It was like an ancient cradle of civilization that contained everything and everyone from throughout the starry sky.

It was all under the control of Xu Qing’s canon. Xu Qing dropped his right hand. The starry sky shook, and everything distorted.

All of the nonhuman cultivators who could sense what was happening were astonished.

Kun Wu with his fishing pole was also visibly taken aback. An intense sensation of danger filled him. There was no time to offer explanations, so he unleashed his Quasi-Immortal cultivation base. Instantly, he was surrounded by flowers, plants, and trees. Infinite vegetation sprang up, surrounding him and growing out into the void. It was as if a primeval jungle had suddenly come to exist in the starry sky.

And the vegetation rushed toward the River of Time. When it reached the river, it grew in and around the water, until the River of Time seemed like it was just part of the jungle! The jungle wanted to completely cover it.

This was Kun Wu’s canon, mastery of vegetation!

Xu Qing’s face remained completely expressionless as he performed an incantation gesture with the right hand that he had just lowered. Instantly, innumerable planets in the Inksun Universe trembled, and the time that belonged to them was extracted and turned into... sand in the River of Time!

Every single grain of sand was a planet. With planets as sand, the river had a “foundation” as well as “weight.”

It crushed downward. The vegetation in the river collapsed. The jungle outside of the river began to wither up.

However, Kun Wu was an extraordinary Quasi-Immortal. The collapsed vegetation began to grow again, and the withering reversed. Kun Wu himself was on his feet and backing up, his eyes glittering coldly. He could tell that Xu Qing was no simpleton.

“You have an Imperial Sovereign cultivation base but Quasi-Immortal battle prowess. No wonder you don’t want to let me borrow this place. But... in the end you’re just not a Quasi-Immortal!”

Kun Wu’s eyes shone with an aggressive light as he threw both of his hands out in front of him.

“Cosmic Reversal!”

Instantly, all of the vegetation collapsed, and this time it didn’t return. The withering did not reverse. Instead, everything destroyed itself. In the blink of an eye, the endless vegetation died. As a result of the vegetation dying, a powerful aura of death built up within Kun Wu’s words.

“Borrow the canon of death to slay the living!”

The aura of death converged, becoming a gray image that contained an outline of Xu Qing. The image was like a death seal, and the person within it would have their life severed. This was Kun Wu’s trump card, and was an expansion on his vegetation canon that he himself had created.

Xu Qing’s eyes shone coldly as a sensation of danger exploded within him. The River of Time rumbled as it changed shape. It turned into a vortex, and as it spun, a wind kicked up. It had turned into... a space-time tempest! Infinite Timelessness had appeared.

Thanks to Infinite Timelessness, Kun Wu’s image trembled and collapsed into chaos. The image of Xu Qing flew out, and then there was no outline.

The tempest formed by Infinite Timelessness swept toward Kun Wu. Seeing that his killing move had been negated, his face fell and he shot backward with shock in his eyes.

“You can control your canon to that level? What was your ranking among the ascendees?”

Xu Qing didn’t respond. Although he hadn’t fought very many Quasi-Immortals, he knew that each Quasi-Immortal had areas of strength. What was more, the one he was facing had come from an earlier batch of ascendees, and could very well be a chosen. A Quasi-Immortal like this had to be very powerful.

The canon of parallelism stirred within him. Different layers of space-time descended. It was like a kaleidoscope!

Heaven’s Principle also appeared!

Kun Wu’s pupils constricted as the sensation of danger within him grew explosive. Without a moment of hesitation, he pulled out the immortal slip for his own universe and began a teleportation. He was done fighting!

He had managed to stick around the Inksun Universe as a squatter thanks to the level of his cultivation base. What was more, he knew that the majority of the ascendees would be mere Imperial Sovereigns. Back when he had been an ascendee, he had ranked in the 60s. But now he was a Quasi-Immortal, and for people like that to pick on newbies wasn’t anything out of the ordinary. In fact, it had happened to him back then. He had intended to just rely on force to get what he wanted.

All in all, the Inksun Universe had been special in the past, but was now considered ordinary. Yet little did he know that the person who had been given this universe actually had stupefying battle prowess. What was more, that kaleidoscope imparted a sensation of imminent and intense peril to him. If he moved even an instant too slowly, he would die.

In his astonishment, he began to blur as the teleportation began. Then he vanished! Unfortunately, Heaven’s Principle went with him.

Xu Qing looked on coldly. Eventually, he waved his hand, and Heaven’s Principle returned, stained with blood.

All of the nonhumans who had been watching were shaken to the core, and prostrated even lower to Xu Qing. What was more, all of them had been wondering the same thing that Kun Wu had wondered just before he left. But now... they were starting to get an idea of just what ranking Xu Qing had among the ascendees.

Time passed, slowly but surely.

A month of in-universe time passed in the Nineshores Heaven. That month was relevant to the universes in the Nineshores Heaven, not the star domains, star whirlpools, and galaxies. The reality was that in the massive Nineshores Heaven, the way time flowed in the endless universes changed depending on what civilizations and species were there, and how they recorded history.

In the end, that wasn’t important. Any given species in the Nineshores Heaven would usually have multiple ways of recording the passage of time. After all, they would have records of their own planet, but also records of the galaxy they were in. Some large species would have records of the star whirlpools, star domains, or even of the entire universe.

The month that passed for Xu Qing in the Inkland was different for the species that lived in the multitude of other locations. To them, it might have been dozens of years or even hundreds. More time would pass the smaller the galaxy was. It could also reflect incomplete or damaged natural and magical laws, or low levels of immortal energy.

The beings that lived amidst such slow passage of time would often be incomplete or damaged in some way. It could be their soul, or their bloodline, or their karma. Because of that, such species might not develop much even after the passage of hundreds of years. Things were always balanced out in some way.

Xu Qing got a clear sense of all that as he sat in the same spot as Kun Wu had occupied in the Inkland. He was also fishing. By means of his space-time canon, he had come to a much deeper understanding of his universe during the last month.

He had attempted to enter the black hole, but could only descend about 30 meters. After that, a terrifying power of rejection stopped him. He had eventually given up, sat down cross-legged and started using the fishing pole.

Although his divine will couldn’t go very far inside, and given how difficult it was to get the ringsource out, Xu Qing felt like he was sitting on top of a mountain of treasure, only for the treasure to be extremely difficult to take. That said, he could tell that practicing cultivation here would give faster results to his immortal embryo than anywhere else.

The ringsource doesn’t come out easily, but there are still bits and pieces to be had. At the same time... Kun Wu’s fishing method is worth studying.

That old man from the immortal palace said the Inksun Universe is a strategic resource. There must be something special about it....

First of all, he said that the universe had degraded, and was now considered ordinary. Second, Kun Wu had been unaware of Xu Qing’s ranking. Based on the clues, Xu Qing had come up with a theory. Kun Wu didn’t think that the Inksun Universe was a strategic resource, not even considering the fact that it had ringsource. In other words, it hadn’t occurred to him that this universe would be given to the 1st place ascendee!

So, he didn’t truly understand this universe. But what exactly is it about the Inksun Universe that’s special?

Xu Qing looked at the Inkland black hole and something suddenly occurred to him. Maybe the answer is in the black hole! What if there’s something inside it other than ringsource.... Unfortunately, I can only go down 30 meters into it. Unless some Quasi-Immortal came along to help, I’m not going to have any luck.

Xu Qing kept on fishing as he planned out what he would do going forward. My short-term goal is to go to the Reception Universe in a year and get an assignment here in the Nineshores Heaven.

But my long-term goal is to gather lots of ringsource. With it, I can form my immortal embryo and become a Quasi-Immortal. After that, I need even more ringsource to complete my immortal embryo. Then, I can gain enlightenment of the tenth extreme and reach immortal ascension! And that’s when I can go back to Revered Ancient! I only have twenty years to work with.... I wonder if that’ll be enough time.

Xu Qing looked off into the distance. It hardly seems like it, but I’ve already been in the Fifth Star Ring for about ten years.

Revered Ancient was a very long way away. In fact, Xu Qing didn’t even know how far away it was. But he felt like he could sense where it was. Regardless of anything, when the time comes, I’ll go back. If I can reach immortal ascension beforehand, great. If not... at least I can lend some strength to the fight! One thing I need to do is fix my Sageheaven Pagoda. Maybe I can use my reward for that.

Having reached this point in his train of thought, Xu Qing cleared his mind and focused on the ringsource. Ringsource was the key to improving his cultivation base.

Actually, there’s another way to get ringsource....

Xu Qing’s narrowed eyes glittered with a mysterious light. And that’s gods.... Gods are in the majority in the higher star rings, and ringsource forms the basis of thēir life force. Thēir entire growth is based on gathering ringsource.

Because thēy are born in the higher star rings, it’s much easier for thēm to gather ringsource than it is for cultivators. Thēy are essentially collections of ringsource!

Devouring gods is that other way! The downside is that they aren’t pure, so devouring them is dangerous and can have side effects. But, it’s the fastest method. That’s especially true considering I have a god clone with me. In other words... I can probably get around some of the downsides.

All of a sudden, Xu Qing thought back to the god prison he had ended up in when he first arrived in the Fifth Star Ring.[1]

In that prison of gods, there were spell formations that would extract and purify thēir spirit energy. In that manner, it could be used for cultivation purposes by low-level cultivators. The more cultivators that were part of the process, the more spirit energy would be produced, in an endless cycle.

Once there was enough spirit energy, it would be converted into immortal energy. I bet that’s the same function served by the nonhumans in this universe. The nonhumans are used as nutrients for the path of the cultivators. Meanwhile, the further a cultivator gets along that path, and the longer they live, the stronger they get.

Xu Qing felt like he was experiencing sudden enlightenment.

But the god prisons in the four great planetary systems all contain low-level gods. But the high-level gods... must have special prisons of thēir own. And I bet those prisons are used to extract ringsource. If I pursue this path further, I need to find an opportunity to do some tests of my own. But right now, my most important focus is right in front of me. The Inkland!

Xu Qing looked down at the black hole in front of him. As for the ringsource in there....

Xu Qing looked hesitant, but he had an idea, so he closed his eyes to think.

When he opened them again, they shone with determination. Waving his left hand, he produced a green bottle. Within it was a fist-sized clump of clay. It was crimson.

Fifth Star Ring cultivators had different ways of controlling gods, and in this one, they formed the clay into the image of a god that they could control. The blood-red clay floated out in front of Xu Qing, and then he used his divine will to change its shape.

Starfire gasped excitedly.

Starfire was clearly moved, but still let loose a cold snort. “Call me big sis. Then I’ll obey.”

They all had different facial features, but there was something about the temperament that seemed similar. It was... a feeling like that of a jackal. In terms of cultivation base, two of them were peak Imperial Sovereigns, while the one standing in the middle was a Quasi-Immortal. In response to Hordeslayer and Rampart yelling at them, they merely grinned nonchalantly.

As for the Quasi-Immortal, he dug into his ear with his pinky finger, blew the tip of his finger clean, and chuckled. “Of course I’m aware that you’re ascendees. Unfortunately... who around here isn’t an ascendee? Guess what? We also ascended, only a few times ago.

“Furthermore, while it’s true that the sects from the Immortal Capital have connections here... that counts for everybody. Besides, we just want to have a little talk with the two of you. We want to buy those swords. That’s all. If you don’t want to sell, that’s fine. We’re not going to force you.

“That said... we have a big responsibility. And we do have the right to conscript people into our forces. I’m just asking you two to cooperate. Unfortunately, you don’t have the option of refusing.”

Hordeslayer and Rampart scowled.

Quite a few cultivators in the area were looking on and discussing the scene playing out.

“Look at the clothes those three are wearing. They’re obviously a bunch of greedy Acquisitioners!”

“Hmph! The Department of Acquisitions is full of jackals. They run amok in universe after universe under the guise of collecting funds for the war. They’re hated wherever they go!”

“What’s worse is that the envoy squadrons usually have dozens or even hundreds of cultivators in them. They’re all corrupt scumbags, but they’re also very united. Ordinary folk like us don’t dare provoke them.”

“That’s exactly what’s happening right here. Those three jackals took a liking to those two brothers’ swords. Except, the brothers won’t sell. And since they’re new ascendees, the Acquisitioners are going to conscript them.”

“If they get conscripted, they probably won’t be killed outright. But they won’t be able to keep their immortal swords.”

It was obvious from the chatter that the Department of Acquisitions had a horrible reputation, and that no one was willing to step in.

Hordeslayer and Rampart were very nervous. They had just arrived here, and hadn’t had time to connect with any fellow disciples who were also ascendees. And they knew that if they left the Nineshores Heaven, it would be like going from the river out into the sea.

In the Fifth Star Ring, fighting was permitted according to the law. If they weren’t strong enough to defend their immortal swords, then it would be a simple case of the weak falling prey to the strong. At the moment, it would be hard for them to feel more anxious.

Xu Qing could see that the swords were drawn and the arrows were nocked, and that conflict would break out any moment.... As he stood unnoticed in the crowd, he considered the situation and tried to decide whether or not to interfere. After all, those two swords were, at least in some way, his.

Before he could make a decision, a domineering beam of light appeared from off in the distance. Within the beam of light was a young man wearing a black robe, with flowing black hair. He had a cold facial expression, and pulsed with the aura of a Quasi-Immortal. Surrounding him were numerous chains of order. He immediately attracted a lot of attention.

He was Sir Star Ring. His purpose in coming was not to provide assistance. He had come to get his magical treasure, and just happened to be passing by.

As he neared, his domineering aura, which he made no effort to conceal, caused the eyes of Hordeslayer and Rampart to shine. Without any hesitation, they started calling out to him.

“Greetings, Eldest Brother!”

“Eldest Brother, we need your help!”

The use of the address “Eldest Brother” was forced but appropriate.

As the anxious Hordeslayer and Rampart bowed formally, Sir Star Ring stopped in place. He frowned. This matter had nothing to do with him. At a glance, he could tell what was happening, and he had no intention of interfering. But before he could do anything, Hordeslayer and Rampart flew over and cowered behind him. If he left now, it would come across as him being scared.

Sir Star Ring felt a bit irritated, but his eyes remained cold as he looked at the three cultivators in hundred-pocket robes who were now rushing after Hordeslayer and Rampart. He suddenly surged with a Quasi-Immortal aura.

The three Acquisitioners stopped in place. The two who were Imperial Sovereign had serious looks on their faces, but the Quasi-Immortal’s eyes were narrowed. They didn’t advance any further.

Seeing that, Sir Star Ring looked away from them and flew off into the distance. Hordeslayer and Rampart breathed sighs of relief as they followed. The three of them soon disappeared in the distance.

Everyone else present looked on with glittering eyes.

As for the Quasi-Immortal Acquisitioner, he suddenly said, “He must be the 1st place ascendee! I guess we underestimated this group. They have some really impressive people. Let’s go figure out who that guy is!”

What Xu Qing saw on his way out of the Daoforge Universe was a little interlude and nothing more. Sir Star Ring showed up, and thus, Xu Qing didn’t end up revealing himself. Hordeslayer, Rampart, and even Sir Star Ring himself, were merely passing travelers to him. At the very most, he might end up taking the two swords if the need arose one day.

However, the three evil cultivators Hordeslayer and Rampart had run into were of note to Xu Qing. Two were Imperial Sovereigns, and one was a Quasi-Immortal. It was obvious how greedy and domineering they were.

Xu Qing had never been under the illusion that everyone with a high cultivation base had some sort of transcendent personality. In the chiliocosm of worlds, there was no end to the cultivators that existed. Powerful experts were as numerous as clouds in the sky, and it was only natural that they would have all sorts of personalities.

And of course, they would act differently and hold themselves to different standards. Some people were sinister, some were extraordinary. There were broad-minded people like Grand Emperor Swordsage, and of course, there would be greedy and evil people like those he had just seen.

It was the same even in the Quasi-Immortal level. People were people, and they all had different personalities. There were many Quasi-Immortals in the Fifth Star Ring, largely because of the different environment.

It wasn’t like the Revered Ancient mainland, where life was tough and the resources were scarce. In Revered Ancient, Quasi-Immortals and even Imperial Sovereigns were as rare as phoenix feathers or qilin horns. The higher you climbed, the more mountains you encountered. The further you traveled, the more scenery you saw.

It was just how things worked. When all was said and done, personality was largely the result of one’s experiences. There were some people who lived for thousands or tens of thousands of years, and who experienced all the joy and sorrow of life, that eventually became numb, blank, and returned to their primal state. Otherwise, it would be hard to escape the colorful reality of human nature.

Of course, in some cases, one couldn’t just take things at face value. In the end, Xu Qing wasn’t surprised at all to find some powerful experts, and even a Quasi-Immortal, who would try to rob others in public. But what he did find surprising was who those three people were.

Acquisitioners... for some war...?

Xu Qing was lost in thought as he left. What was especially noteworthy was the mention of war.

They acquire resources for war...? What war is the Fifth Star Ring fighting? Maybe with another star ring?

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment. There were some things that you wouldn’t be able to see clearly until you reached the proper vantage point and had a wide view. Up to this point, Xu Qing had not been aware of any war being fought by or in the Fifth Star Ring. However, listening to the conversations of the other cultivators had given him an idea of what was going on.

“I suppose things will be made clear in the Reception Universe.”

With such thoughts in his mind, he crushed the immortal slip for the Heroic Immortal Tombs, and vanished in a teleportation.

The starry sky blurred.

***

The Heroic Immortal Tombs didn’t just exist in the Nineshores Heaven. Similar things existed in all of the heavens beyond heaven. From ancient times until now, whenever immortals fell in battle, they would be buried somewhere. In some cases, their corpses were interred intact. In the vast majority of cases, their remains were mangled. In some cases, the only thing left behind was a grave marker.

The Heroic Immortal Tombs were located in the Heroic Immortal Star Domain in the Immortal Eulogy Universe. It was isolated by unique barriers, and the only entrance was an immense ancient door made of bronze. Outside of the door was a black stone staircase of the most ancient construction.

Seated right in front of the door at the top of the staircase was an old man in a black robe. He was nothing special to look at, and his aura was imperceptible as he sat there motionless.

When Xu Qing materialized, he was on the stairs outside the door. He looked up at the huge door, and then at the old man, and his heart trembled. There was a strong feeling of death coming from the old man, as well as a sensation of lonely bleakness.

The sight caused his canon to ripple, as if it were being drawn to the old man. At the same time, a host of information filled him. He suddenly got the feeling that this old man shouldn’t exist, and yet did exist. The feeling grew very strong before vanishing.

After hesitating for a moment, he bowed. Then he walked up the stairs and disappeared into the door.

After Xu Qing was gone, the old man opened his eyes. He lifted a flagon of alcohol and took a drink. Looking at the door, he hoarsely murmured, “Nobody has come for a while now. That’s good. There have been few memorial services, but that just means not many people have died in the war recently. That’s excellent.... All of you are long gone. Why did you leave me behind guarding your tombs here in the mortal world...?”

The old man’s eyes seemed to fill with reminiscence.

Upon stepping through the door, the starry sky again blurred to Xu Qing, and when things became clear, he was looking at a host of galaxies. They were tombs!

In the Heroic Immortal Star Domain, each galaxy was a tomb. Each one had a stone stele above it inscribed with writing. In some cases, the writing told the life story of the individual interred therein. In other cases, there were only a few words written down. In the case of the latter, it was usually an epitaph explaining the ideals of the buried individual.

There weren’t many galaxies; there were only a bit more than a hundred. That said, this was a place of buried immortals. In other words, from ancient times until now, there had only been a bit more than a hundred Lower Immortals who had perished in battle in the Nineshores Heaven.

Xu Qing knew that history went back for countless years. But to walk through that huge door and see all these galaxies, and the stone steles above them, left him feeling deeply shaken.

He could just barely make out a sound like a sigh, echoing through the starry sky. It was like the battle cry of a valiant warrior, drifting amongst the galaxies. It was like a blessing from the aeons, lingering among death.

They had defended their home. They had defended their people. They had fought heroically for humankind and their star ring! They risked life and limb with no thought given to their personal interest.

Even though Xu Qing wasn’t native to the Fifth Star Ring, he felt his mood sinking. He couldn’t help but feel deep reverence for the heroism these people had shown. The stone steles he was looking at became inscribed on his heart.

After a moment passed, he began to pass amidst the swirling stars and look at the stone steles.

“I practiced cultivation for 9,000 years. I hailed from Grand Immortal Mountain, practiced cloud cultivation, and when I became an immortal, I was given the title immortal monarch. During my life, I cut down seven True Gods. I couldn’t be prouder.”

“I was a rogue cultivator who refused to give up. I eventually rose to the level of immortal, and in the star ring war, I participated in the God Lord Siege. Though I died, I had no regrets.” freewebnovel.com

“Spirits become gods. Beasts become specters. Ghosts become freaks. In that case... what is an immortal? When a human becomes a mountain, all to defend humankind, well that person is an immortal!”[1]

“I lived for too long and began to lose my humanity. I could not kill any True Gods, but I wanted to accomplish something, so I went hunting. I planned to kill as many Altar God chosen as I could, and sever the lineage of whatever gods I found!”

“Later generations of cultivators shall not come to offer respects empty-handed. I require the blood of gods! Offer some to me!”

As Xu Qing went from stone stele to stone stele and read the script, he felt like he heard people laughing heartily. In other cases he heard weeping or even insane babble. It was like a great river of history flowing past him.

The stone steles and their inscriptions linked past, present, and future into an indelible marking. Anyone who came here would be moved.

It was pure poetry. The green mountains are full of loyal bones, the annals of history record the mighty deeds. The spirit of the heroes fills heaven and earth. The illustrious names will be spoken of throughout the ages.[2]

Eventually, Xu Qing settled down cross-legged in the middle of the starry sky and looked around at all the stone steles.

“Seniors, I am Xu Qing. I’m not a native of the Fifth Star Ring. But I promise I won’t let you down. Is there any of you willing to give me some of your inheritance? I promise to never give up on my ideals.”

The response was silence. Nothing stirred.

Xu Qing settled his energy, cleared his mind, and began to seek enlightenment. Nothing happened. He frowned, and after some thought, decided not to seek enlightenment. Instead, he let his thoughts expand. Gradually, he began to recall the past.

His youth had been a struggle. After growing up, he faced endless slaughter. He faced the evil of the gods. He encountered the wrath of the gods. But when the empress reached godly ascension, he gained an understanding amidst the confusion.

And that was when he realized what the real question was. It was as if a voice was asking him.

What are the gods?

In the past, Xu Qing had been able to answer succinctly. But now that he thought about the question again, and considered Empress Summer Departure, he suddenly spoke in a calm voice.

“The vast majority of gods are sons of bitches like they’ve always been! But there are some of them who are still human!”

The stone steles began vibrating.

1. This entire passage is full of wordplay that doesn’t translate perfectly. He basically takes two-character descriptions of things like gods, ghosts, etc. and breaks them up into their component characters to describe them. The point of the last part is something Er Gen readers have seen before in other novels. The character for immortal 仙 has the character for person/man/human on the left 人 and the character for mountain on the right 山. In this particular passage, the 人 character is associated specifically with the word for humankind or humans as a species. ☜

2. As far as I can tell, this poem is an invention of the author, although it contains some common poetic phrases. ☜

It wasn’t just the stone steles that reacted. The more than one hundred galaxies began to shine with dazzling light. Apparently, the sentiment Xu Qing had just expressed was not considered enlightened in the Fifth Star Ring. Streams of divine will emerged from the stone steles, along with voices.

“Preposterous!”

“Gods are just gods!”

“How could they be human?”

“It doesn’t matter if you’re talking about preheaven gods, or all of those postheaven gods. Anyone who chooses the path of the gods has forfeited their humanity!”

“What you have seen and felt is simply a part of the process of god cultivation. The gods are more than willing to fool you to make progress easy!”

“You are not the first to be scammed by the gods, nor will you be the last.”

“Young one, take some advice... don’t let them fool you!”

“From ancient times until now, all who befriend the gods end up regretting that decision. There are no exceptions!”

“Now, take back what you said, and I’ll give you some of my inheritance!”

The streams of divine will echoed in the star domain, entering Xu Qing’s heart and mind.

Xu Qing didn’t say anything. His eyes contained reminiscence. After some more thought, he made his decision.

The remains of the immortals here had no souls. And what he was hearing wasn’t actual divine will. It was more like the lingering obsession of the immortals who had died in battle. They had fought gods their entire lives. From birth to death, they had stood in opposition to them. And thus, from their point of view, gods... really were all the same.

Xu Qing used to think in the same way. But then he had witnessed Empress Summer Departure reach godly ascension. And that had changed his worldview!

“Seniors,” he said calmly, “where I come from, there are things called holy lands. When the gods wreaked havoc, my people, even the children, were infected by the mutagen of the gods.... And you know what the humans in the holy lands did? They didn’t care about us. They left. They abandoned humankind.

“They were so high and mighty that it didn’t bother them at all that other humans were dying. And then their descendants came back and continued to exploit and manipulate things from behind the scenes.

“Over time, humans fell into decline. One emperor after another shed blood, sweat, and tears to keep humans safe. And then there was Grand Emperor Swordsage, who sacrificed everything to defend us.

“Despite all that, humans struggled to survive, much less rise to prominence. Countless humans... became food for nonhumans. They suffered in bitterness. I have seen things worse than even cannibalism. Our species struggled in the darkness, gradually losing touch with our humanity, until we were on the verge of being wiped out.

“But then someone came along within that tribulation and destruction. She was the empress of the humans back at my home! Unfortunately, her ideals were vanquished, and in the end, she had only two choices. Either let humans be wiped out. Or become a god!

“In the end, she chose godly ascension! Was it rebellious? Heretical? Did it besmirch the ancestral edicts? Maybe. But she chose to shoulder the responsibility!

“She said that she didn’t care if the holy lands were populated by humans. She was going to do everything to make sure that the joss flame of humankind still burned in Revered Ancient! She said that humans deserved to be happy. And if heaven and earth wouldn’t do it for humankind, she would. So she would bring peace to humans in Revered Ancient!

“She said that she didn’t care about living forever. She just wanted humans to have a chance to flourish, and once again be glorious in Revered Ancient. She said that she wasn’t becoming a god for her own sake. And she brought all of the old emperors with her to also reach godly ascension.

“She said that the five old emperors would be zombie gods. They would lack thinking faculties, but they would have godly might. And then she drew on the destiny aura of humankind to defend the last bastion of humankind, and strike fear into the hearts of the nonhumans.

“She said she would become a human god, to safeguard humankind and bring peace for generations to come! And lastly, she said that she knew her actions would result in karma that would bring catastrophe and tribulation. But she... would bear sole responsibility!”[1]

Xu Qing’s words echoed out into the star domain. They contained all of his reminiscence, and all of the emotions he felt. He used his words and voice to paint a detailed picture of the heroic spirits, describing how and why Empress Summer Departure became a god. In the end, he looked around at the stone steles.

“As far as I’m concerned, a god like that is more human than many humans! I also know that not all gods are like that. But humans can also be good and evil. It’s the same with gods. It doesn’t matter how many there are that are good. They do exist. And that’s why I’m not going to change my mind!”

Ducking his head, Xu Qing clasped hands and bowed.

Afterward, the galaxies in the star domain all seemed to emanate pure coldness. The stone steles didn’t vibrate, and the words on them disappeared from view. As for inheritances and legacies... not one came out! They did not agree with Xu Qing’s opinion, and thus... they had nothing further to say.

Xu Qing quietly turned. He was not disappointed at the results. One needed to walk one’s own path in life. And the scenery one would inevitably encounter on the way would mold one’s way of thinking. It would mold one’s view of life, one’s understanding of the world, and one's perception of things living and inanimate. All of that would converge into a unique way of thinking. That was what it meant to be human.

Going forward, Xu Qing would still kill gods. He would still rob them and treat them cold-bloodedly. But there were some gods, such as the empress, whom he would fight for! Because he knew that, in her heart, the empress was not a god. She was human. And she was more human than many humans.

It was with such thoughts, and without any regrets, that Xu Qing calmly walked toward the door. He was ready to go back to the Inksun Universe and wait until the time came for his formal reception into the Nineshores Heaven.

But as he neared the door, and just before he stepped through it... the door trembled loudly. A somber, killing aura began to pulse from it.

Xu Qing stopped in place, his gaze hardening. Someone was coming through the door. In fact, it wasn’t a single person. It was over a hundred.

They all wore unique suits of armor that were stained with blood, both the blood of gods, and their own blood. They looked exhausted, and deep down inside, full of sorrow. They approached silently. Amidst this procession were a dozen or so cultivators carrying... a huge coffin. Draped atop the coffin was the flag of the Fifth Star Ring.

Xu Qing quietly stepped to the side to make way.

None of the cultivators paid any attention to him. They sorrowfully made their way off into the distance.

As Xu Qing watched them pass, he could sense sorrow, but more than that, desolation. That desolation didn’t come when cultivators fought and killed each other. It was something Xu Qing was familiar with. It was the powerful desolation that built up on soldiers when they spent time on the field of battle! These people had come from the war!

As for who rested in the coffin... Xu Qing could guess who it was. It definitely contained the remains of an immortal. An immortal had died on the field of battle and was being sent here for a hero’s burial!

Xu Qing felt more somber than ever.

Off in the stance, the procession stopped. They all bowed as the coffin was sent forth. And they began to sing an ancient song of mourning. The lyrics seemed to tug at the soul. It was a eulogy. And as the lyrics drifted out, stars appeared, like sand or dirt that covered the coffin. Soon it wasn’t visible.

The sand of stars then turned into a galaxy, and a stone stele appeared above it.

The cultivators stood, and the leader amongst them saluted.

“Rest in peace, Immortal Monarch!”

After the soldier passionately bade farewell, they turned somberly and left.

After all of this happened, Xu Qing didn’t just leave. He went over to the galaxy where the heroic immortal had just been laid to rest. After bowing, he looked at the inscription on the stone stele.

“Life is like a dream, and time is like a song. The starry sea eventually comes to an end. I am Immortal Monarch Spirit Jade. I eradicated a True God and drank hīs blood. I wiped out hīs mark like the turtledove occupying the magpie’s nest. Let’s see what happens in the future.... Will it be hē who returns, or me? If hē returns, my corpse will emanate golden light, and later generations can erase the True God from existence. But if it’s me... then silver light will shine, and I will slay gods again!”

This immortal seemed different than the others. He seemed to be attempting to use the natural laws governing gods to effectuate his own return!

Eyes shining, Xu Qing was about to investigate further when he heard a sigh from behind him. Looking over his shoulder, he saw a stooped old man, who was the guard from outside.

The old man approached and stood in front of the stele.

“We’ve reached the next stage of the war. There are going to be a lot more heroic spirits here soon. According to what I heard, this one had been searching his whole life for an explanation about why True Gods are undying.”

The old man sighed.

Xu Qing backed up a few steps, then bowed thoughtfully. “Senior, what’s the war about?”

The old man turned and looked at him deeply. “When the rain falls, it falls on everyone equally. But if one party doesn’t feel the rain, it indicates that someone has gone out of their way to prevent the rain from falling on them. Immortal Lord Deepgloom is that person. He is stationed on the border, preventing the Fourth Star Ring from invading. It’s a star ring war, but also, a war between gods and immortals.”

The old man looked off into the distance. He lifted his hand, within which was a bell that lacked a bell clapper. It seemed ordinary in nature, but its mere presence caused colorful ripples to spread through the starry sky.

“I had a good friend who died in the war, killed by a God Lord. Though he perished, and this treasure of his was damaged, it survived in this state. It contains the might of a God Lord. He wanted me to find someone connected to him by destiny, and pass it on to them.”

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as he looked at the old man.

The old man waved his hand, and the bell floated over to Xu Qing. He turned and started walking off.

“I heard what you said, and I greatly admire that empress you mentioned. We live in a complicated world. And human nature is complicated. Don’t care too much what others think.

“I’m confident that if these old friends of mine were actually alive, they would understand. Unfortunately, all that’s left behind here are remnants of their obsession, and their will to defy the gods. An outstanding person like you shouldn’t leave here empty-handed. Take that as a gift from me.”

The old man disappeared, leaving behind a few words. “I’ve met gods like those you described... those who are more human than many humans.”

Upon leaving the Heroic Immortal Tombs, Xu Qing listened to his heart and gazed in the direction he imagined was where the Ninth Star Ring lay. It was a haze of stars, and truth be told, he had no idea if the Ninth Star Ring really was in that direction. He had a clone in Revered Ancient, and he could sense it, but it was so incredibly far away that it was little more than a vague feeling.

But though he couldn’t see anything, or even be certain that he was looking toward the Ninth Star Ring, he knew why he felt inclined to do this. He missed home. He missed the Revered Ancient mainland, he missed the people there, and the things there, and everything....

The day is going to come when Revered Ancient is like here in the Fifth Star Ring. The mutagen will be gone, and immortal energy will fill the place. The gods there will change their dao, and abandon the cultivation of gods!

Eventually, he looked away. It wasn’t time to leave yet. He still needed to get stronger. He had not yet reached the point where he could go back to keep anyone safe, or change anything.

“Soon...”

Collecting his thoughts, he took out his Inksun Universe immortal slip and squeezed it. Everything blurred, and ripples spread out as the teleportation began.

Majestic spatial power was required to perform inter-universe teleportations. It also required the support of high-level canon. Neither could be lacking. When both qualifications were met, cultivators in the Nineshores Heaven could go through with such teleportations.

Given the current level of Xu Qing’s cultivation base, he did have a good understanding of space, but his view was limited. He had no way to see into the deeper levels.

There are mysteries at play here.... I suppose it has something to do with Immortal Lord Nineshores.

Immortal Lords were currently unfathomable to him. As a result, he could only vaguely make out bits and pieces of the whole. His vision blurred, and the void around him changed. The starry sky... slowly transformed.

When everything went back to normal, Xu Qing was no longer at the Heroic Immortal Tombs. Instead, he was in his immortal hall on the asteroid in the Inksun Universe!

When he opened the doors of the hall, the Inksun Universe stretched out in front of him. He took a step forward and vanished. When he reappeared, he was outside the Inkland black hole.

He saw Starfire lying there on a divan, enjoying life and surrounded by a host of dancing, chatting maidens.

Upon noticing Xu Qing, shē first looked surprised, and then shē pouted slightly. “Back so soon, you devil? Why didn’t you let me know you were coming? I could have gotten ready. Xu Qing had long since become immune to Starfire’s flirting. “Very smoothly. You can carry on.”

Xu Qing sat down cross-legged. Ignoring Starfire, he took out the gift the old man had given him and sent his divine will inside to study it.

Seeing that Xu Qing was ignoring hēr caused Starfire to chuckle softly. Shē wasn’t offended. He was used to dealing with hēr, and shē had long since become used to dealing with him. Shē loved flirting, and shē loved how he refused her.

Thus, shē chose to ignore hēr godly nature and immerse hērself in human nature. As the beautiful maidens around hēr danced, shē glanced at Xu Qing sitting there. Shē smiled. This is the beautiful scenery I’ve built for myself!

Starfire ate an immortal fruit, and hēr eyes narrowed into crescent moons of happiness and comfort.

Starfire felt wonderful that entire time.

Not even his canon of parallelism would work on it. It could not be sent to other space-times! There was some sort of force surrounding it that prevented it from leaving its own space-time!
