His eyes glittered brightly.

Though he had not been able to leave even a tiny mark on the bell using external force, by means of his immortal embryo, he was able to make a connection to the bell by nourishing it. At first, the connection wasn’t very strong. The bell was masterless, and though it didn’t exactly reject the nourishment he offered, it also didn’t cooperate. It wasn’t like parched dirt thirsty for even a drop of dew.

But Xu Qing was cautious in the way he treated it. As he slowly provided nourishment, he gradually reached the point of being able to exercise some ownership over it. And when that happened, he seized that control and didn’t let go. If he made the slightest mistake, the connection would sever.

It seems to me that the key to unleashing the power of this treasure is going to be sound!

Xu Qing waved his hand, and the iron skewer he had acquired in the Daoforge Universe flew out, bright and glittering. Xu Qing had a good idea of how to deal with the bell.

After reviewing his thought process to make sure he hadn’t forgotten anything important, his face flashed with determination, and he sent the iron skewer to hit the side of the ball. The moment they made contact, the bell vibrated. The crisp but ethereal sound of a chiming bell echoed out.

The cup of fine wine that Starfire had lifted to hēr lips suddenly collapsed into nothing. So did all the dancing maidens around hēr.

Starfire leaped up, only to stagger backward, hēr body blurring, revealing hēr god altar. Shocked, shē said, “What is this thing?!”

Starfire wasn’t the only one to react in that way. The entire starry sky shook. The bell echoed out infinitely, reaching into the minds of all living beings, and echoed into all objects. The entire Inksun Universe filled with the sound of the bell, and nothing else. Within that silence, all illusions ceased to exist. All magical techniques collapsed, and all divine abilities shattered.

Xu Qing was visibly moved. Now he knew what this bell treasure could do!

It prohibits all magical arts! And given what just happened to Starfire, it seems gods fall under the umbrella of the prohibition as well!

Unfortunately, once the sound of the bell vanished, everything went back to normal. The dancing and bustle around Starfire came back. The immortal fruit that had vanished once again appeared in hēr hand. At the moment, shē wasn’t interested in eating it.

Looking seriously at Xu Qing, shē said, “That treasure... can prohibit gods!”

Xu Qing nodded. “It’s actually a deadly weapon!”

Face filling with concentration, he continued studying the bell.

After a long moment passed, Starfire sighed. Here in the Fifth Star Ring, shē had really come to understand what it meant to be terrified.

Once he finishes his studies here, the kid’s gonna go back to Revered Ancient and shake things up among the gods there. Well, who cares? What’s that got to do with me?

Starfire went back to enjoying hērself. Time continued to pass.

Xu Qing spent a few months in study, and then he focused on cultivation. He stabilized his immortal embryo, and began laying the foundation for his next breakthrough. He was currently very stable in his existing state.

Before long, the one-year deadline approached. The day of reception was nearing.

When the day came, a dignified voice drifted out from his universe’s jade slip.

“All ascendees have twenty-four universe-hours to check in at the Reception Universe and receive your new orders. You will be given permanent assignments in the Nineshores Heaven, and will begin to truly assimilate here.”

The voice didn’t just echo in Xu Qing’s mind. It reached all of the ascendees. It didn’t matter what universe they were in or what they were doing. All of them looked up with expressions that were both serious and full of anticipation.

Xu Qing opened his eyes and stood. “The time is here. Finally.”

Starfire retracted all hēr magical arts, strolled over to Xu Qing, and stretched. “I’ve been idle for too long. Time for excitement. I’ve really been looking forward to this!”

All of the new ascendees were given universes after entering the heaven beyond heaven, as well as a year to rest. That year was intended to give the new ascendees time to get familiar with the heaven beyond heaven, as well as their personal universe. They also had time to get their rewards.

When the rest period ended, they were then summoned to the Nineshores Heavens’ Reception Universe. There, they would be told about the assignment that had been arranged for them.

By the time Xu Qing got the message, he was already back at the Inksun Universe’s immortal hall. Without any hesitation, he stepped onto the immortal hall’s teleportation portal and began the teleportation. Starfire was now a special symbol sealed onto his arm.

The immortal hall trembled as terrifying teleportation fluctuations rolled out through it. This teleportation took much longer than any Xu Qing had experienced before. Clearly, the Reception Universe was a great distance away from the Inksun Universe. He wasn’t sure exactly how long it took, as the process was like a mottled dream. Within that dream, everything was blurry and colorful.

Eventually, the distorted glow faded away, and he could see clearly again. Stretching out in front of him was a vast golden river. The river was made of innumerable star domains, countless star whirlpools, and uncountable planets.

The planets all emanated a unique golden light. They didn’t move. Rather, starlight flowed around them, which made it seem like they were in motion. It was Xu Qing’s first time seeing a golden river of stars like this.

This place was the Reception Universe!

It was also one of the seventy-two centers of government in the Nineshores Heaven, which were second only to the immortal palace in terms of power and authority. It controlled general operations in the Nineshores Heaven, and during this epoch, it was the headquarters that oversaw the reception of visitors from other heavens beyond heaven.

It didn’t just receive new ascendees. It provided direction to the minor worlds under the Fifth Star Ring, as well as the nonhumans in all the star ring’s various universes. It was like a military command center, and at the same time, a personnel coordination department. It went without saying that a lot of Lower Immortals were stationed there.

As Xu Qing looked in astonishment at the majestic golden river, a stream of starlight emerged from it and shot toward him. The golden light was insignificant in comparison to the river as a whole, but as they neared, they seemed similarly majestic. The stream swirled around him and began to draw him toward the river.

The golden starlight that had come out to receive Xu Qing originated in... a location in the lower reaches of the golden river, to a specific planet in a star whirlpool in a star domain.

Streams of starlight were drawing people in from all over the Reception Universe. It happened to all cultivators who had teleported there. And depending on why they had come here, the light would lead them to different places.

As the light tugged at Xu Qing, he shot toward the planet. He was moving so fast that he felt like he was being stretched out like a shooting star.

In the shortest of moments, he was pulled from outside the star river to its interior. He entered a group of planets, and eventually neared the one that he was being pulled toward. His view rapidly transformed. Everything started rumbling.

And then he dropped onto a huge sea on the planet. The sea was black and viscous, almost like gelatin. And he had been tugged toward it at such incredible speed that he hit it with a great amount of force.

Given the level of Xu Qing’s cultivation base, he could deal with the force. However, a lower-level cultivator who experienced that impact would lose their soul and find their fleshly body crumbling. Of course, though his cultivation base was sufficient to avoid injury, when he hit the surface of the sea, he slammed down into it, all while creating a huge crater above him.

A short time later, he struggled out of the crater and looked around. The sky was golden, and the black, viscous sea around him stretched on forever.

Up in midair were other beams of golden starlight bringing other cultivators. Booms rang out on the surface of the sea. Soon, there were dozens of craters. Some of the cultivators slammed into the sea and then emerged looking bedraggled. A few even had to wipe blood from their mouths, and had looks of lingering fear in their eyes.

Xu Qing spotted Zhou Zhengli in the crowd, as well as Sir Vilespirit, Li Mengtu, Yuanshan Su, Hordeslayer, and Rampart.

Sir Star Ring was also there, who looked to be in much better shape than the other fellow ascendees. Almost as soon as Xu Qing looked at him, he turned and looked back. Their gazes met. Both remained expressionless.

Time passed as more people arrived. Some people stuck to themselves, while others gathered in groups. People had obviously begun to form into factions over the past year, based on their experiences.

Sir Vilespirit was still operating alone. Yuanshan Su had originally planned to stick to herself, but had been unable to avoid some of the other female ascendees, who had chosen to ally themselves with her. Hordeslayer and Rampart were sticking close to Sir Star Ring, as were a group of a few dozen other cultivators.

The biggest group had gathered around Xu Qing. He had taken 1st place, so many people, upon spotting him, came over and cheerfully offered greetings. Zhou Zhengli and Li Mengtu were among them.

The former was acting like usual. Smiling, he offered an obsequious bow.

The latter had a serious look on his face. Keeping his voice low, he said, “Brother Xu, it looks like eleven from our group have gone missing. I just counted, and there are only eighty-nine people present!”

Xu Qing nodded.

Zhou Zhengli chuckled. “Dead, I suppose. We were given a year to rest and acclimate. But our star ring has always focused on raising venomous bugs in a jar. And thus....”

Zhou Zhengli looked at Xu Qing. The truth was that Zhou Zhengli had learned a lot about this heaven beyond heaven in the past year, and was on guard about what was to come. More than ever, he felt that it was important to maintain a good relationship with Xu Qing.

Therefore, he opened his mouth and said, “Things aren’t just brutal in the four great planetary systems. This entire heaven beyond heaven is very intense. To the higher-ups, only people who are truly important are those who have, at the very least, Quasi-Immortal battle prowess. In other words, you, Young Lord, as well as Sir Star Ring and Yuanshan Su. But that’s it. Just you three. Imperial Sovereigns... well, the higher-ups don’t care much about them. So, unless you have very good connections, advancing to a better position requires having a lot of resources and allying with a Quasi-Immortal.”

Zhou Zhengli didn’t bother to lower his voice when he said these things. The other ascendees in the area all heard him very clearly. All of them suddenly seemed very thoughtful.

Xu Qing looked at Zhou Zhengli. Zhou Zhengli smiled back obsequiously.

Xu Qing looked away and thought back to what Zhou Zhengli had said to him the previous year.

“My guess... is that a year from now, the whole lot of us are going to get the same assignment...”

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment. Time passed as everyone waited. There were no other cultivators atop the vast sea. No one had come to receive them.

But these were all extraordinary individuals, so none of them were going to get impatient being asked to wait. One by one, many of them sat down cross-legged.

Another two hours went by.

Eventually, a loud wind picked up, whereupon Xu Qing and Sir Star Ring both seemed to sense something. They looked up into the sky. Yuanshan Su was the third to notice what was happening. Everyone else, noticing the reaction of those three, did the same.

The sky was rippling, and golden light had appeared. It was the same type of light that had drawn them to this planet. There were a total of seventy or eighty streams of it, with a handful of them in front of the others. Heaven and earth began to tremble.

Only some of the cultivators in the group slammed into the surface of the sea and made craters. Most of them alighted stably on the water. They had been to this place before, and had the skill to maintain control.

All of these people were dressed the same way. They had on the same clothes that Xu Qing had first seen in the Daoforge Universe.... Each wore a gray hundred-pocket robe! Those robes were the signature clothing of the notorious Acquisitioners!

There were eight who were Quasi-Immortals, and they were obviously the leaders.

After they landed, Xu Qing’s expression didn’t change, but many of the other ascendees suddenly looked very serious.

The new arrivals looked at the gathered ascendees, particularly Xu Qing and the people surrounding him. Their gazes were like those of jackals. They seemed indifferent to life and full of unfeeling callousness. None of them said a word. Then their leaders shot off into the distance, followed by the others.

“Young Lord,” Zhou Zhengli said in a low voice, “they’re Acquisitioners.... Presumably, we’ve been drawn to this planet because of them.”

Xu Qing nodded.

However, things weren’t over yet. After the time it takes an incense stick to burn, more golden light appeared in the sky. Again, dozens of cultivators arrived in hundred-pocket robes. After landing on the sea, they raced away.

In that manner, time passed. Group after group of Acquisitioners arrived. None of them paid any attention to Xu Qing and the other ascendees.

After observing them, Xu Qing realized that they all had cold, greedy auras. And the higher their cultivation base, the more obvious it was that they had corpse energy and death auras. The reek of gore was especially prominent. Clearly, these people had long-term contact with corpses and death.

Eventually, when the golden light in the sky started to dim, another several dozen beams of light shot down and resolved into figures in front of them.

The one in the lead had an extremely terrifying aura. He was an old man who resembled a vulture, and his immortal embryo was at the great circle. He was just a step away from being an immortal! Upon landing, he turned to lead everyone away. But then....

A middle-aged cultivator in the group behind the old man stopped in place. Turning, he looked at Xu Qing and the others. And then... he looked behind Sir Star Ring, Hordeslayer, and Rampart. He smiled.

Xu Qing had seen this person before. He was the very same Quasi-Immortal cultivator who had caused trouble for Hordeslayer and Rampart back in the Daoforge Universe! His gaze came to rest on Sir Star Ring. Meanwhile, some of his fellows had stopped in place just like him.

Hurrying over to the terrifying old man, the middle-aged cultivator said a few words. The old man frowned, but eventually nodded. With the old man’s approval, the middle-aged Quasi-Immortal looked at Sir Star Ring and smiled.

“I’ve lost a few members of my squadron in the war. I need to make up some numbers, so as of this moment, you three are conscripted!”

Hordeslayer and Rampart were visibly taken aback!

Sir Star Ring frowned. Eyes cold, he looked at the people approaching and growled, “Screw off!”

His words were like an icy wind, filled with killing intent. That was just how Sir Star Ring acted. Though Xu Qing had killed him, he had been born again, and his personality hadn’t changed. He was arrogant and ice-cold down to his soul. It didn’t matter if he was facing a Quasi-Immortal just like himself, who had a lot of friends with him, and even a peak Quasi-Immortal backing him up. He cultivated order, and would rather break than bend!

The middle-aged cultivator laughed. “You’ve got quite a temper.”

Eyes flashing, he turned to his leader and bowed. The old man frowned, but yet again nodded.

The middle-aged cultivator’s aura flared. He seemed to be borrowing outside power! He waved his hand, then pushed down, and ripples flowed out over the surface of the black sea.

Astonishingly, a host of flying black insects emerged. They were extremely vicious and ugly. What was more, they were not corporeal. In the shortest of moments, there were so many of them they were impossible to count. After rising up from the black sea, they charged toward Sir Star Ring.

Sir Star Ring’s eyes flashed coldly as a host of chains materialized around him. Clanking sounds could be heard as they swirled into a vortex. The might of order could suppress all. The dao of balance could eradicate anything. Hordeslayer and Rampart cooperated smoothly, as both of them unleashed sword energy that bolstered Sir Star Ring.

In the face of their divine abilities, the black insects began to collapse en masse. Sir Star Ring’s vortex of order chains was whipping up into a tempest. From a distance, it looked as if the black insects would be routed in one move.

However, the collapsing insects didn’t completely disappear. Instead, the resulting black ash and dust became a cloud that spread out rapidly. At the same time, the middle-aged cultivator performed an incantation gesture and pointed out. The black cloud swept around him, surrounding him in layer after layer, even covering his face. It was almost like it was molding him a new body.

In the blink of an eye, the middle-aged cultivator’s face disappeared, to be replaced by a featureless mask. Moments later, the face blurred, and a new set of facial features became visible. They were different from before! They were the facial features of Sir Star Ring!

His facial expression, aura, and soul now seemed to be exactly the same as Sir Star Ring! Next, black smoke converged on either side of his head, where it formed two additional heads. They looked like Hordeslayer and Rampart.

The other ascendees’ hearts sank.

Next, the middle-aged cultivator in his terrifying three-headed giant form looked at Sir Star Ring and the others and laughed loudly. Then he simply ignored them and walked back to his companions. His companions didn’t seem to find this unusual at all, as if it happened all the time. And their leader, without so much as a backward glance, started to walk away. The entire group was clearly going to leave.

But then, a very strange event unfolded. The departure of the middle-aged cultivator seemed to do something to Sir Star Ring, Hordeslayer, and Rampart. The three of them... started trudging forward as if they had lost control of their own bodies.

Hordeslayer and Rampart had completely blank looks on their faces, as if their souls had been extracted. Though Sir Star Ring continued forward, his eyes shone with an aggressive light, and creaking sounds echoed out with every step he took. The control exerted over him was clearly crumbling.

The middle-aged cultivator made an exclamation of surprise. Even the old man looked over his shoulder at Sir Star Ring.

“Impressive,” the old man said. “Go get him.”

Three members of the squadron walked out and flew toward Sir Star Ring.

Zhou Zhengli looked on thoughtfully, all while Sir Vilespirit licked his lips. Yuanshan Su frowned. The other ascendees said nothing, but some seemed to be bristling aggressively. These were cultivators who had risen through slaughter to become ascendees, so they were a proud lot. Even though they weren’t necessarily friends with these people... it didn’t sit right with them to see their fellows being treated like this and not interfere.

Unfortunately, these Acquisitioners were clearly stronger than them, having several Quasi-Immortals and the old man who was stronger than anyone else. There was a big disparity between the two groups. So though they were agitated, no one dared to step forward.

This didn’t sit right with Xu Qing either. Those two swords belonged to him. As for Sir Star Ring....

After a bit of thought, Xu Qing came to the conclusion that something fishy was going on. If this were happening elsewhere, it might make sense. But this was the Reception Universe. The new ascendees were supposed to be getting their permanent assignments. For them to be conscripted by the Department of Acquisitions at this moment seemed to indicate that the so-called ‘reception’ they were being given was nothing more than a joke.

Something out of the ordinary is going on!

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed, and he casually stepped forward. As he did, his aura erupted. The canon of space-time filled heaven and earth, and a bell flew out from his forehead. The bell chimed. The sound echoed out ethereally, filling the hearts and minds of everyone present.

All faces reacted with shock. That included all of Xu Qing’s fellow ascendees and the members of the Acquisitioner squadron. The bell entered their ears like thunder, shaking them inside and out. Their cultivation bases went still, and all of their magical techniques... stopped working! Some people even fell out of midair and crashed onto the ground.

The three cultivators who had been flying toward Sir Star Ring shivered, and their eyes filled with shock as they realized they couldn’t advance any further. freewebnovel.com

The brothers Hordeslayer and Rampart also shivered. But when the bell chimed, they suddenly felt very clear-headed. Sir Star Ring, whose head had already been starting to clear, completely woke up! Killing intent blazed in his eyes.

But the person affected the most was the middle-aged cultivator. His three heads all exploded, and the fleshly body of black ash collapsed. Black smoke poured out in all directions as his true body was revealed. His pupils were constricted as he looked in Xu Qing’s direction. He looked very serious, as if he was facing an arch-nemesis. At the same time, he was filled with a sensation of having barely escaped a big catastrophe.

And that was because, at some point in the past few moments, an iron skewer had come to appear right in front of him! The skewer was incredibly sharp and emanated a cold aura that clamped down on the middle-aged cultivator’s soul. He really had no idea when that skewer had come to be in front of him, but he knew that he had somehow barely avoided having it stabbed into his forehead.

In fact, there were two fingers holding onto the skewer and preventing it from hurting him. The person holding the iron skewer was his leader, the old man who was indescribably close to the peak of Quasi-Immortal!

The old man turned and looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing did nothing to avoid his gaze. Voice cool, he said, “Those are my swords. And my people.”

The old man looked deeply at him for a moment. Then he looked up into the sky, clasped hands, and bowed. “Arch-Immortal, my squadron has already finished the extra mission you assigned us. May we leave?”

Astonished, everyone looked up into the sky. Xu Qing did as well.

Ripples spread out in the previously calm dome of heaven, as the previously dim sky suddenly started to fill with color. It was a dazzling assortment of colors that gathered together into a patch of absolute brilliance. The outline of a figure appeared, walking through the brilliance.

He was an unprepossessing old man. He wore rough, hemp garments that made him look like a fisherman. And in one hand he held a roughly-carved walking stick. The walking stick was covered with cracks, much like the wrinkles on his face.

The moment he appeared, the old man who was nearly at the peak of Quasi-Immortal bowed his head. All of the members of his squadron followed his lead.

The moment Li Mengtu saw the new arrival, his expression flickered dramatically. His eyes went wide with disbelief, and he exclaimed, “Master!”

It was hard to tell how sincere he was in his excitement.

Xu Qing, meanwhile, was shaken to the core. There was something very familiar about this old man. It was his canon that Xu Qing had ultimately abandoned. He was Li Mengtu’s master, and he was the immortal from the Dao Immortal Sect in the western planetary system!

Poison Monarch!

Xu Qing’s guard immediately went up. He knew full well that Poison Monarch was not a virtuous person. He had provided his canon, not out of good intentions, but because that canon contained karma that he could lend out and take back.

If Xu Qing had not gained enlightenment of his space-time canon, then the other canon would have caused him immeasurable harm. It was a dao that could be given and taken. That was why he had ultimately chosen to abandon it.

Right now, Xu Qing couldn’t fathom why this person... would appear right here and now.

What was more... he didn’t just serve as Poison Monarch. He wasn’t just a heavenly inspector in the Dao Immortal Sect. He also had another post!

Looking around at everyone, Poison Monarch spoke in a raspy voice. “I am the director of the Department of Acquisitions.”

As Poison Monarch spoke, his voice transformed into numerous five-colored butterflies that appeared in front of Xu Qing and the other ascendees. They were very unique jade slips. As they flapped their wings, they transmitted information directly into the minds of everyone present.

The Department of Acquisitions was one of the 324 departments in the Reception Universe. The director was tasked with providing special materials for the war. Usually, the department was sent to a specific area with a specific deadline to acquire funds and provisions. They would then be sent back to the Reception Universe, where the profits would be transferred to the Department of Transportation, and beyond that, to the front lines. Because of the wartime situation, everything the Department of Acquisitions did was centered around the acquisitions.

In terms of what the department sought to acquire... it boiled down to one thing! It was something that all Imperial Sovereigns and higher desperately needed: ringsource! Unfortunately, the ringsource needs of the war effort surpassed those of individual cultivators. As a result, there was no way they could go about acquiring ringsource in the way Xu Qing had done in the Inksun Universe, in other words, by fishing.

The focus of the Department of Acquisitions... were the nonhuman universes in the heavens beyond heaven in the Fifth Star Ring. It was extracted from their blood and their life force. That included... the various god prisons located in large numbers in the various heavens beyond heaven.

Of course, there were different types of prisons. Some were operated on the universe-level, some belonged to the heavens beyond heaven. Others were run by clans, and were considered private ventures. The gods held in the prisons served as the origin of ringsource.

As the information poured into Xu Qing’s mind, his gaze hardened. Now he understood why the Acquisitioner squadrons had such strong auras of death. Their main job was killing and extracting! What was more, they did things in a very domineering fashion. After getting used to acting in that way, it was only natural that they would be filled with perverse energy.

The information also provided a clear explanation of who Poison Monarch really was. Poison Monarch had long since performed amazing services. Though he was indeed in charge of the Dao Immortal Sect in the western planetary system of the Immortal Capital, he was also the director of the Department of Acquisitions.

Thanks to the information from the butterflies, everyone now had a much better understanding of the Department of Acquisitions. Up in midair, Poison Monarch looked at the squadron that had clashed with Xu Qing and the ascendees.

“The lot of you go turn in your ringsource.”

The old leader of the squadron bowed along with the other cultivators, and then they flew off into the distance.

The cultivator who had very nearly been stabbed in the forehead by Xu Qing’s iron skewer stopped in the distance and looked back at him. His eyes flickered with both fear and defiance.

Xu Qing could sense that, and committed the man to memory.

After they were gone, Xu Qing and the other ascendees were left alone on the black sea, digesting the information about the Department of Acquisitions.

Xu Qing’s guard was up, and Li Mengtu was feeling nervous. But no one else had ever dealt with Poison Monarch, so as far as they were concerned, he was just an immortal and their future commanding officer. Regardless of the level of their cultivation base, the ascendees all bowed respectfully. After all, failing to respect immortals was a grave crime in the Fifth Star Ring.

“Starting on this very day—” started Poison Monarch, but he paused after only five words. All of a sudden, great pressure swept over the group. He didn’t pay any attention to his own apprentice, Li Mengtu. Nor did he seem to care about Xu Qing. He wasn’t concerned about things that had happened in the past. His previous actions had been little more than a standard test. But as he looked around, everyone bowed their heads.

A moment later, Poison Monarch continued in a raspy voice. “This group of ascendees is all being assigned to posts in the Department of Acquisitions. Since you all have the same assignment... then you might as well be a squadron of your own. As for the captain....”

Poison Monarch looked at Xu Qing, then Sir Star Ring and Yuanshan Su, as well as... Zhou Zhengli.

Of those four, two had Quasi-Immortal cultivation bases, one had Quasi-Immortal battle prowess, and as for Zhou Zhengli... when he realized he was being looked at, he stepped back, seemingly terrified and deferential.

Sir Star Ring looked surprised. Clearly, he had just come to the realization that everything that had just played out was a test. And more importantly than that... someone had been trying to split them up! But thanks to Xu Qing interfering, that effort had failed. It was easy to imagine that if they had been split up, then they wouldn’t have ultimately been put into one squadron. They would have been split up into two or more groups.

It had never occurred to Sir Star Ring that Xu Qing would help him. After a moment of silence, he said, “I’m not interested in the position of captain.”

At almost the same time, Yuanshan Su quietly took a step backward. Her personality had changed. After everything that happened in the Aurora Immortal Palace, she had come to truly revere Xu Qing. One reason was because of his methods. The other... as one of the very last Shining Stars to leave the immortal palace, she knew a lot more than many of them. She also had certain speculations.

For instance, she was certain she knew who had taken the identity of Young Lord Aurora. And she was fairly certain... that the real Young Lord Aurora wasn’t dead. She was also convinced... that the identity she had taken was also still alive! Given all that, she didn’t want to be the leader of their squadron.

Face completely expressionless, Poison Monarch looked at Xu Qing. “Xu Qing.” freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing looked up with clasped hands. The more he was convinced Poison Monarch had sinister intentions, the more he knew that he couldn’t reveal any weaknesses. That included failing to show respect to immortals.

“You are assigned to be the leader of this squadron. You will leave immediately for your appointed destination to carry out resource acquisitions. Your deadline... is in five months!” He waved his hand, and a ring of holding flew over and hovered in front of Xu Qing. “In there you’ll find your Acquisitioner uniforms, identity medallions, and also the information about your mission.

“And now, all of you can go out and wait outside the Reception Universe, with the exception of you, Xu Qing. You stay behind.”

Poison Monarch flicked his sleeve. Heaven and earth trembled, and everything blurred as all the other ascendees except for Xu Qing vanished. They had been teleported away by an incredible force.

Xu Qing’s pupils had constricted slightly, though it wasn’t easy to tell. He just stood there looking as respectful as possible.

Poison Monarch hovered in the air. He stood on the sea. The atmosphere became as still as death.

Neither of them spoke. A long moment passed, and then Poison Monarch took a step forward, blurring slightly as he appeared in front of Xu Qing.

An immortal filled with evil intentions stood right in front of Xu Qing. The pressure he felt was incredible. Especially noteworthy was the fact that Xu Qing could sense that this was no ordinary immortal. Even though he was a Lower Immortal, it was obvious that he ranked near the very top among that group.

Someone like that could obviously kill Xu Qing with a thought. Thankfully... this was the Reception Universe, in the Nineshores Heaven, a heaven beyond heaven in the Fifth Star Ring. As long as Xu Qing had not committed any crime, then he would be safe. That was why he was making sure to maintain a very respectful attitude.

“You’re clearly an extremely vigilant person,” Poison Monarch said. “You’re uneasy, but aren’t showing it at all. Xu Qing, though this is my first time meeting you in person, I have to admit that you’ve surprised me.”

“I’m grateful for your approval, Arch-Immortal,” Xu Qing said in a tone that was neither supercilious nor obsequious. “Your humble servant is honored to receive such praise.”

Poison Monarch looked at him deeply, then started walking across the black sea. Xu Qing hesitated briefly and then followed. The wind blew, stirring the sea.

A short time passed, and then Poison Monarch said, “Xu Qing, I previously wanted to take your dao to break through into the Immortal Lord level.”

Xu Qing didn’t say anything.

“Many, many years have passed here in the Fifth Star Ring since Immortal Lord Aurora perished. During that time, not a single new Immortal Lord has risen up. The pace of the war is speeding up. Momentum is increasing....” Poison Monarch’s voice seemed to drift along like a helpless sigh.

“The main reason that’s happening is that a new God Lord has appeared in the Fourth Star Ring! That God Lord’s overall strength has pushed us to a point of life or death in this war between star rings! Do you understand, Xu Qing? It is vital for everyone involved... that the Fifth Star Ring get a new Immortal Lord! As for myself....”

Poison Monarch stopped walking. “I am the person in the Fifth Star Ring who is in the best position to break through and become an Immortal Lord among Lower Immortals!”

Xu Qing somberly clasped hands and bowed. “Your humble servant offers congratulations, Arch-Immortal. I hope that your breakthrough comes soon, and that you quickly rise to the glorious position of Immortal Lord!”

Poison Monarch turned to look at him.

Xu Qing’s expression was sincere.

Eventually, Poison Monarch shook his head and laughed softly again. “Although I failed to take your dao, you’re still connected to me by destiny.... I kept you behind today because I have an errand for you to handle for me.

“A few years ago, Immortal Lord Nineshores gave the Department of Acquisitions a mission. We were tasked with finding a mysterious piece of nine-colored ice that was capable of extinguishing the fire of a God Lord. I’ve been looking this entire time for that nine-colored ice, but have failed to find it. I have never entrusted the task to anyone else. But today, I’m giving you a chance. Are you willing to look for it?”

Poison Monarch looked over at Xu Qing. He wanted to see if Xu Qing understood the implications of this offer.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered, and his impression of Poison Monarch suddenly improved. The meaning in the words was obvious.

He was being given a good opportunity!

There was a tacit understanding among Acquisitioners. As long as they met their acquisition quota... anything left over could be kept for personal use. As long as the Acquisitioner didn’t get too greedy, they could benefit a lot.

What was more, it was a mission from an Immortal Lord... and not just any Immortal Lord, but Immortal Lord Nineshores himself. Given that, Xu Qing would have major protection in carrying out the assignment! With that protection... and his status as an Acquisitioner, he could do just about anything he wanted, and most likely make out like a bandit. In just about any circumstance that arose, he could just say that he was looking for that nine-colored ice at the behest of the Immortal Lord. This also meant he could fast-track his cultivation!

At the same time, it was a double-edged sword. After all, there could be some severe downsides. For example, failing! Poison Monarch could punish him at any time for failing to acquire the object in question.

If he accepted the mission, he would be under the complete control of Poison Monarch.

This entire thing was both a covert conspiracy and an overt conspiracy. If he said he understood, it would be an overt conspiracy. If he said he didn’t understand, it would be a covert conspiracy.
